TAFSEER-E-SURAH ALE IMRAN

Compiled by Syed Shoeb Raza Abdi Nauganvi (Bombay)

(These are regular daily post on Social Media)

SHIA CHANNEL WELCOMES YOU
***********************************
     ♦QUR'AN - MUQATTA'AT♦
As-salamu alaikum wa  Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (279)

(بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ)

(بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ
الم * اللَّهُ لَا إِلَٰهَ إِلَّا هُوَ الْحَيُّ الْقَيُّومُ * نَزَّلَ عَلَيْكَ الْكِتَابَ بِالْحَقِّ مُصَدِّقًا لِمَا بَيْنَ يَدَيْهِ وَأَنْزَلَ التَّوْرَاةَ وَالْإِنْجِيلَ)

"Us Khuda ke naam se jo Maherban aur Bakhshnewala hai."
Alim, Laam, Meem!"
"Khuda e yakta ke alawa koi ma'bood nahi, Woh Zinda wa Paidar aur Nigehbani karne wala hai."
(Wohi zaat hai) jisne tum par Haq ke sath Kitab nazil ki. Ye Kitab guzishta Kutub ki nishaniyon par muntabiq hoti hai aur isse qabl tauret aur Injeel ko logon ki Hidayat ke liye utara gaya. Nez Haq o Batil mein tameez karnewali Kitab (Qur'an) ko nazil kiya."
(Surah Aal-e-Imran: 1 - 3)
📖 ⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜
👉 Tafseer:
Aaj se surah Ale Imran ki suruat ho rahi hai. Imran janabe Abu Talib (as) ka naam tha. Ale Imran means Khandane Abu Talib (as)
Means Ahlul Bait (as). Qur'an ka zyada hissa fazilate Ahle Bait (as) hai.
Is surah mein Janabe Maryam binte Imran ka waqea hai, isliye surah ka naam Ale Imran. Janabe Esa (as) se koi nasl age nahi chali, aur woh abhi zinda hain. Lekin Janabe Abu Talib (as) (Imran) ki nasl (Ale Imran) aaj tak maujood hai.
📖 ⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜
Qur'an ka Moajeza:
Mashhoor Egyptian Magazine: "آخرساعةAkheri Sa'ah" ke auther Teacher of Chemistry, ustad Dr. Reshad Khalifa ne ek Computer Research ki aur bataya:
Qur'an mein 114 surah, 86 Makki, 28 Madani. 29 Surah
Huroof e Muqattaat حروف مقطعات se shuru hote hain, jis 14 huroof (letters) hain out of 28 Arabic Abjad letters. Aur wo ye hain: ا، ح، ر، س، ص، ط، ع، ق، ك، ق، ك، ل، م، ن، ه، ى.
Computer calculation se ye paya gaya ke jo surah in letters se start hota hai in mein is letter ki ta'dad doosre surah se zyada hai. Ye calculation jab sahi hoga jab word ko sahi likhe. E.g. agar زكواة ko زكات likhen to calculation ghalat ho jayega. Isse ye natija nikalta hai ke Qur'an mein koi tehreef (changes) nahi hue.

Rivayat ye bhi hai ke Alif Lam Meem se murad Ale Muhammad (as) hain. Phir bhi in short code ka asli ilm sirf Allah ko hai.

Ye ek Qur'an ka moajza hai.
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜
----------------------------------------------

MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!
🙇 📖
Rasule Khuda (saww):
"Dua maangne wale ka aur Aamin kehne wale ka; Quraan padhne wale ka aur Quraan sunne wale ka; Aalim ka aur Taalib e Ilm ka, Sawaab equal hai."
(Nahjul Fasaha)

       ♦AASMANI KITABEN♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (280)

(بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ)

(مِنْ قَبْلُ هُدًى لِلنَّاسِ وَأَنْزَلَ الْفُرْقَانَ ۗ إِنَّ الَّذِينَ كَفَرُوا بِآيَاتِ اللَّهِ لَهُمْ عَذَابٌ شَدِيدٌ ۗ وَاللَّهُ عَزِيزٌ ذُو انْتِقَامٍ)

"Nez Haq o Batil mein tameez karnewali Kitab (Qur'an) ko nazil kiya. Jo log Ayate Ilahi ke munkir hu gaye hain unke liye sakht Azaab hai aur Khuda badkaron aur sarkash Kafiron ko Azaab dene ki qudrat rakhta hain aur woh inteqam lenewala hai."
(Surah Aal-e-Imran: 4)
📚📖
👉 Tafseer:
Some Points:
1. HAQ: Haq k asil meaning hai 'mutabiqat' aur 'ham ahangi' 'Harmony'. Ham Khuda Ta'ala ko Haq kahte hain isliye ke Uski Zate Muqaddas Azim tareen waqeiyyat hai jo qabile inkar nahi.
2. Taurait: توارئة Ibrani zaban ka lafz hai. Means "Shariyat aur Qanoon". Ye lafz (word) Hazrat Musa bin Imran par nazil hone wali Kitab ke liye bola jata hai. Ab ye Old Testament ka hissa hai.
3. Injeel (Bible): Ye Unani (Greek) word hai. Means "Basharat" (Glad Tidings) ya "Jadeed Taleem" (Modern Knowledge). Ye Kitab Hazrat Esa (as) par nazil hui.

Ye original kitaben Allah ki taraf se nazil hui, lekin at present maujood The Holy Bible jis mein Old Testament aur New Testament hai. New Testament mein 4 Injeel hain: Luke, Mark, Mathew, John.
Ye sab Nabiyon ke chale jane ke baad logon ki likhi hui hain. Ye aasmani kitaben nahi hain.
Qur'an ne jis aasmani tasdeeq ki hai woh original kitabon ki ki. Qur'an ko Furqaan kaha gaya jo achhe bure mein tameez karta hain.
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜
----------------------------------------------

MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!
🙇
Imam Sadiq (as):
"Taurait Maahe Ramzan ki 6th ko Naazil huwi, Injeel is mahine ki 12th ko, Zaboor is maah ki 18th ko aur Quran Shab e Qadr mein."
(40 Hadith - Quran)

Rasule Khuda (saww):
"Jisne apne waaledain ko takleef di (dil dukhaya) usne mujhe takleef di aur jisne mujhe takleef di usne Allah ko takleef di aur jisne Allah ko takleef di uspar Tawrat, Injeel, Zabuur aur Quran mein la'nat hai."
(Family Life of Islam)
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜

***********************************
       ♦QUDRAT-E-KHUDA♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (281)

(بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ)

(إِنَّ اللَّهَ لَا يَخْفَىٰ عَلَيْهِ شَيْءٌ فِي الْأَرْضِ وَلَا فِي السَّمَاءِ *
هُوَ الَّذِي يُصَوِّرُكُمْ فِي الْأَرْحَامِ كَيْفَ يَشَاءُ ۚ لَا إِلَٰهَ إِلَّا هُوَ الْعَزِيزُ الْحَكِيمُ)
👉
"Zameen o Aasmaan mein koi cheez bhi Khuda par makhfi (hidden) nahi rahti (isliye unki tadbeer karna bhi uske liye mushkil nahi hai.)"

"Wo wo zaat hai jo mao (Mother) ke rahem (womb) mein jaisi chahta hai tumhari surat banata hain (isliye) Us Tawana (Mighty) aur Hakim (Wise) Khuda ke alawa koi ma'bood nahi hai."
(Surah Aal-e-Imran: 5 - 6)

📚📖
👉 Tafseer:
Knowledge of Embryology mein pata chalta ke kaise ek qatre se alag shakl ke insaan paida hote hain, maa ke rehm ke kaise bachcha parva chadhta hai. Researchers ne rehme madar ki film tak bana li. Ye sab dekh kar Khuda ki Qudrat hi nazar aati. Ye koi by-chance amal nahi hai, na koi coincidence hai. Kiyon ye sab ek baar hote hai. Ek systematic nizam ko dekh kar pata chalta hai is Kaynat ka chalana wala koi hai, aur woh Khuda hai. Aur Detail ainda ayaton mein ayegi.
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜
----------------------------------------------

MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!
🙇 😫
Imam Baqir (as):
"Jab rehm (womb) mein beej girta hai, 40 din tak wahin muqarrar rehta hai, 40 din munjamid taur rehta hain (clot), aur agle 40 din Mudghama ki surat mein. Phir Allah 2 Farishton to uski aisi takhleeq ke liye bhejta hai jaisa Allah chahta hai. Chahe male hota hai ya female (muzakkar ya moannas). Wo usko shape dete hain aur uski Zindagi ki Muddat, maut ka waqt, nasibwar ya bad nasib sab likh dete hain. Uski dono ankho ke darmiyan Dono wo uska woh AHD likhte hai jo usne Alam-e-Zar mein halaf liya tha. Jaise hi uska maa ke pet se nikalne ka waqt qareeb aata hai, Allah ek Farishta bhejta hai jo nasihat karnewala hota hai,  jab woh usko nasihat karta hai to usko shock mein dal deta hai. Farishte ki nasihat par woh Ahd bhool jata hai aur rote rote zamin par aa girta hai."
(Kafi, Chap 6, H 7, H10290)
👰🏻
﻿Imam Sadiq (as):
ne ek aurat se kaha "Kya tu chaahti hai ke tere chehre ki raunak laut aaye to Khana pet bhar kar NA khaya kar. Zyada khana chehre ki raunak bigaad deta hai."
(Tehzibul Islam)

♦RASEKHOONA FIL ILM♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (282)

(بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ)

(هُوَ الَّذِي أَنْزَلَ عَلَيْكَ الْكِتَابَ مِنْهُ آيَاتٌ مُحْكَمَاتٌ هُنَّ أُمُّ الْكِتَابِ وَأُخَرُ مُتَشَابِهَاتٌ ۖ فَأَمَّا الَّذِينَ فِي قُلُوبِهِمْ زَيْغٌ فَيَتَّبِعُونَ مَا تَشَابَهَ مِنْهُ ابْتِغَاءَ الْفِتْنَةِ وَابْتِغَاءَ تَأْوِيلِهِ ۗ وَمَا يَعْلَمُ تَأْوِيلَهُ إِلَّا اللَّهُ ۗ وَالرَّاسِخُونَ فِي الْعِلْمِ يَقُولُونَ آمَنَّا بِهِ كُلٌّ مِنْ عِنْدِ رَبِّنَا ۗ وَمَا يَذَّكَّرُ إِلَّا أُولُو الْأَلْبَابِ)

"Wo Zaat Wo hai ke jisne tum par Kitab nazil ki jis ki baaz aayaat Muhkam (Clear) hain jo is Kitab ki buniyad hain (aur jo pecheedgi deegar aayaat mein nazar aaye woh inki taraf rujoo karne se bartarf ho jati hai) aur kuchh aayaat Mutashabeh hain (ye woh aayaat hain jin mein buland sateh ke matalib bayan kiye gaye hain aur kuchh deegar pahloo bhi hain jinke bayes pahli nazar mein in mein mukhtalif ehtemali maani dikhayi dete hain lekin Muhkam aayaat ki Tafseer ki taraf tawajjah karne se ye aayaat bhi ahle nazar par wazeh ho jati hain) lekin jinke dilon mein kaji hai woh mutashabehat ke pichhe pade rehte hain taake Fitna angezi karte rahen (aur logo ko gumrah karen) aur iski (ghalat) tafseer karna chahte hain halanke unki tafseer Allah aur Ilm mein rasikh logon ke alawa koi nahi janta aur ye (rasikhoona fil ilm) wohi hain jo (fahm o idraak rakhte hai, tamam Aayaate Qur'ani ke asraar (secrets) wa rumooz se aagah hain aur Ilahi Ilm o danish ke sabab kahte hain ke ham un sab par Imaan rakhte hain, sab kuchh hamare Parwardegar ki taraf se hai aur danishmand logon ke siwa koi tazakkur nahi karta (aur inke alawa koi idraake haqiqat nahi kar sakta.)"
(Surah Aal-e-Imran: 7)

📚📖
👉 Tafseer:
Imam Sadiq (as):
"Rasoole Khuda (sa) rasekhoon fil ilm (Profound in Knowledge) mein sabse buland the. Allah Ta'ala ne jo kuchh bhi Aap par farmaya Aap uski Taweel o Tanzeel se waqif the. Khuda ne Aap par koi aisi cheez nazil nahi ki jiski taweel Apko na sikhai ho aur Aapke Awsiya bhi Qur'an ki sab taweel o tanzeel ko jante hain."
⚜
Mohkam Aayaat: Woh clear aayaat jin ke zahiri meaning clear hote hain aur sabki samajh mein aa sakte hain.
⚜
Muhtashebat: Woh aayaat jin ke meaning sab nahi samajh sakte siwae Rasekhoona fil Ilm ke aur woh Rasoole Khuda (sa) aur Ahle Bait (as) hain. Lekin kaj dil afraad Mutashabehat par amal karte hain taake us aayaat ka ghalat meaning nikal kar fitna paida karen. Isliye sirf Qur'an kafi nahi hai. Book ke sath uska teacher hona zaroori hai jo har lafz ka meaning aur tafseer batay. Rivayaat ke mutabiq Aimma e Masoomeen (as) ke alawa Rasekhoona dil ilm aur koi nahi ho sakta. Unko chhod kar kisi aur ke dar se asli Ilm nahi mil sakta.  
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜
----------------------------------------------

MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!
🙇
Imam Ali (as):
"Aalim jaahil ko samajh sakta hai kyun ki wo pehle kabhi jaahil tha. Jaahil aalim ko nahi samajh sakta kyun ki wo pehle kabhi aalim na tha."
(Tajalliyaat e Hikmat)

                   ♦DUA♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (284)

(بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ)

(رَبَّنَا لَا تُزِغْ قُلُوبَنَا بَعْدَ إِذْ هَدَيْتَنَا وَهَبْ لَنَا مِنْ لَدُنْكَ رَحْمَةً ۚ إِنَّكَ أَنْتَ الْوَهَّابُ *
رَبَّنَا إِنَّكَ جَامِعُ النَّاسِ لِيَوْمٍ لَا رَيْبَ فِيهِ ۚ إِنَّ اللَّهَ لَا يُخْلِفُ الْمِيعَادَ)

"(Rasekhoona fil ilm kahte hain): Palnewale hamare dilon ko seedhe ko rahne ki Hidayat ke baad munharif na karde aur apni taraf se ham par rehmat farma kiyonki Tu hi Bakhshnewala hai."
"Aye hamare Parwardegar! Tu logon ko us din jama karega jis mein koi shak o taraddud nahi hai kiyonki Allah apne wade ki khilafwarzi nahi karta (ham tujh par, teri Rehmat be payan par aur Hashro Nashr aur Qayamat ke wade par imaan rakhte hain.)"
(Surah Aal-e-Imran: 8 - 9)
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜
----------------------------------------------

MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!
🙇 📖 🙏 👐 🙌
Rasekhoona fil ilm is tarah dua mangte hain. Inhi logon ne hame dua mangne ka tariqa sikhaya.
🙏
Imam Sajjad (as):
"Aye Rab! Jab mujhe aamaal ki achchaai buraai mein ishtebaah (dhoka / confusion) pad jaaye to Behtareen kaam ki taufeeq de."
(Dua e Makaarimul Akhlaaq)
🙏
Imam Sajjad (as):
"Aye Rab! Jab mujhe aamaal ki achchaai buraai mein ishtebaah (dhoka / confusion) pad jaaye to Behtareen kaam ki taufeeq de."
(Dua e Makaarimul Akhlaaq)
🙏
Imam Sajjad (as):
"Aye Rab! Mujh par ehsaan kar balaa se pehle salamati dekar, maangne se pehle ataa farma ke, gawaahi se pehle hidaayat deke."
(Dua e Makaarimul Akhlaaq)

               ♦_AZAAB_♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (285)

(بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ)

(إِنَّ الَّذِينَ كَفَرُوا لَنْ تُغْنِيَ عَنْهُمْ أَمْوَالُهُمْ وَلَا أَوْلَادُهُمْ مِنَ اللَّهِ شَيْئًا ۖ وَأُولَٰئِكَ هُمْ وَقُودُ النَّارِ)
♨
"Jo log Kafir ho gaye hain unhe maal o daulat aur aulad Khuda se beniyaz nahi kar sakte (woh unhe uske Azaab se nahi chhoda  sakte) aur woh (Jahannam ki) aag  ka eindhan (fuel) hain."
(Surah Aal-e-Imran: 10)
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜
----------------------------------------------

_*MORAL OF THE DAY* ....!!!!!!!!_
🙇 🔥♨
Imam Ali (as):
"Aisi AAG (Jahannum) se bacho jis ki cheekh o pukaar sakht hogi, jikse sholay (flames) shadeed (extreme) honge aur jiska Azaab hamesha NAYA hoga."
(Meezan ul Hikmah, v2)
♨
Imam Ali (as):
"Tumhe maalum hona chahiye ke ye naazuk jild (chamdi / skin) Jahannum ka Azaab bardaasht NAHI kar sakti, lihaza tum apne aap par Rahem karo."
(Meezan ul Hikmah, v2)
♨
Rasule Khuda (saww):
"Allah kisi Ummat pe Gazab-naak ho magar Azaab naazil na kare uski nishaaniya'n: MAHENGAAI,
KAM-UMR,
DHANDE ME NUKSAAN…
BAATILO'N KA UNPAR HAAWI HONA."
(Tuhaf ul Uqool)

***********************************
       ♦ _*INKAR-E-AYAATULLAH*_ ♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (286)

(بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ)
📚
(كَدَأْبِ آلِ فِرْعَوْنَ وَالَّذِينَ مِنْ قَبْلِهِمْ ۚ كَذَّبُوا بِآيَاتِنَا فَأَخَذَهُمُ اللَّهُ بِذُنُوبِهِمْ ۗ وَاللَّهُ شَدِيدُ الْعِقَابِ)

"(Inkare Haqaeq aur tahreef mein) inki aadat Ale Firaun aur unse pahle logon ki tarah hai. Unhone Hamari Aayaat ki takzeeb ki aur Khuda ne unke gunahon ke bayes unki giraft ki aur Khuda Shadeedul Eqaab hai."
(Surah Aal-e-Imran: 11)
📚📖
👉 _* Tafseer:*_
' _Dab_' داب means seerat o harkat ke daem o qaem rakhna. Jo bhi kisi ko koi aadat ya lat lag jaye.
Yahan Allah ne Kafiron ki apni hat dharmi par rahna Ale Firaun se mushaheba kiya hai. Yani Ale Imraan bamuqabil Ale Firaun. Firaun ki life zulm o sitam se bhari hui thi jo Aayaate Ilahi ka inkar karte the. Paighambare Islam ki Ummat mein bhi jin logon ne Haqeeqi Rehbar ( _Ayatullah_) (Ale Imran) ko jhootlaya woh misle Ale Firaun hain. In logon ke liye Khuda tanbih kar raha hai ke Woh unko giraftar karega aur is mamle mein Allah Shadeedul Eqaab (severe in punishment) hai.
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜
----------------------------------------------

_*MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!*_
🙇 📚
Imam Sadiq (as):
"Jahannumi jahannum me HAMESHA is liye rahenge ke duniya me unki NIYYAT ye thi ke agar wo duniya mein hamesha rahe'n to hamesha Allah ki na-farmani karte rahenge."
(Al Kaafi, v3)
📚
Rasule Khuda (saww):
"Agar Jahannum walo'n se ye kaha jaaye ke unhe wahaan utne din rehna hai jitney is duniya mein reyt / zarre (sand particles) hain, to wo bahut khush honge; aur agar yehi baat Jannat walo'n se kahi jaaye, to wo ghamgeen (sad) ho jaayenge. Magar Allah ne Jannatiyo'n ko abdi (endless) zindagi di hai."
(Nahjul Fasaha)
📚
Rasule Khuda (saww):
"Agar koi shakhs Haraam kaam ko Khauf e Khuda ki wajah se NA kare to Allah (bhi) Jahannum ki aag uspar Haraam kar deta hai."
(Rehmat Aagosh e Tauba)

       ♦ _*FATAH KI UMEED*_ ♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (287)

(بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ)

(قُلْ لِلَّذِينَ كَفَرُوا سَتُغْلَبُونَ وَتُحْشَرُونَ إِلَىٰ جَهَنَّمَ ۚ وَبِئْسَ الْمِهَادُ)

"Jo log Kafir ho gaye hain unse kah dijiye Jange Uhud ki waqti fatah par khush na ho jao, anqareeb tum maghloob (overcome) ho jaoge. (Aur phir Akherat mein) Jahannam ki taraf mahshoor (gather) honge aur woh kis qadr buri jagah hai."
(Surah Aal-e-Imran: 12)
🏹⚔🗡
👉 _* Tafseer:*_
Ye Ayat Jange Uhud ke baad nazil hui jis mein Musalmano ko nuqshan uthana pada tha woh bhi is wajah se ke kuchh ne Rasool (sa) ke pairavi nahi ki. Allah ne agli Fatehyabi ki peshengoi ki yani Jange Khaibar. Jange Uhud mein jo Musalman bhage the woh munafiqeen the, aur inhi munafeqeen ki wajah se Islam ko nuqsan pahuncha. Lekin Muhafezin e Islam ne Islam ko bachane mein koi kasar nahi chhodi. Karbala ka maarka iski ek misal hai. Shaam mein Janabe Zainab (sa), Imran ki poti ne jo kirdar nibhaya uski misal nahi milti. Aaj jo Islam zinda hai woh inhi hastiyon ki wajah se, warna Yazid ke darbar mein ye dam tor raha tha. Ale Imran ka Islam ahm role raha. Aaj bhi unke rozon par munafeqeen ke hamle ho rahe hain. Ye zulm ki inteha hai. Parda ghaib se wo bhi dekh raha hai, woh din qareeb nahi jab woh ayega aur ye zulm ka khatma hoga. Yehi Allah ki peshengoi hai.
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜
----------------------------------------------

_*MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!*_
🙇
زينب بنت على (ع):
من أراد أن يكون الخلق شفأء إلى الله فليحمده ألم تسمع إلى الله قولهم سمع الله لمن حمده فخف الله لقدرته عليك و استح منه لقربه منك.

Zainab binte Ali (as):
"Jo koi chahta hai Allah ki Shafa'at hasil ho, use chahiye ke Uski Hamdo Sana kare, kiya tumne nahi suna ke Allah ke bare mein unka qaul: Jo koi Uski Hamdo sana karta, Allah ki Qudrat se darta hai, Uski qurbat hasil karta hai, Allah uski sunta hai."
(Balaghatun Nisa, Page 62)
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜

***********************************
       ♦ _*FATHE BADR*_ ♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (288)

(بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ)

*(قَدْ كَانَ لَكُمْ آيَةٌ فِي فِئَتَيْنِ الْتَقَتَا ۖ فِئَةٌ تُقَاتِلُ فِي سَبِيلِ اللَّهِ وَأُخْرَىٰ كَافِرَةٌ يَرَوْنَهُمْ مِثْلَيْهِمْ رَأْيَ الْعَيْنِ ۚ وَاللَّهُ يُؤَيِّدُ بِنَصْرِهِ مَنْ يَشَاءُ ۗ إِنَّ فِي ذَٰلِكَ لَعِبْرَةً لِأُولِي الْأَبْصَارِ)*

"Jab do giroh (Jang-e-Badr mein) aamne samne aaye to is mein tumhare liye nishani aur dars o ibrat tha. Ek giroh rahe Khuda mein Jang kar raha tha aur doosra kafiron giroh tha (jo Shaitan aur Buton ki rah mein mashgoole jang the.) Un (Kafiron) ko (Mo'monin) apni ta'dad se dugna nazar aa rahe the (aur ye bhi unki wahshat o shikasht ka ek aamil (cause) ban gaya) aur Khuda jise chahta hai (aur ahel samajhta hai) apni Madad se uski Taeed (support) karta hai aur us mein sahebane nazar ke liye Ibrat (Lesson) hai."
(Surah Aal-e-Imran: 13)

⚔🐎🗡🐪🏹🐎🐪
👉 _* Tafseer:*_
Jange Badr mein Musalmano ki ta'dad 313 thi, in mein 77 Muhajir aur 236 Ansar. Muhajirin ke Alambardar Hazrat Ali (as) the, aur Ansar ka parchambardar Saad bin Abadah. Unke pas Sirf 70 oont (camel) 2 ghode (horse), 6 zireh aur 8 talwaren thi. 1000 Kafir aur ke pas, zyada weapons, 100 ghode the. 22 Muslim Shahid hue jis mein 14 Muhajir, 8 Ansar. Dushman ke 70 mare gaye, 70 qaedi bane. Musalmano ki ye kam ta'dad hote hue pahli Fateh hui.
Is jang se ye Lesson milta ke ta'dad aur fateyabi ka koi relation nahi hai. 313 Mukhlis new Muslim the aur Khuda ki madad thi. Woh jante the ke Haq ja muqabala Kafiron (Haq ko chhupane walon) se tha. Alambardar Khadane Ale Imran ka ek fard Ali (as) the. Isi tarah Karbala mein mein mukhtasar Ale Imran ka muqabla kasir ta'dad Ale Sufyan se hua aur Islam ke Fateh aisi hui ke jis ki wajah se Islam aaj tak baqi hai. Rasool (sa) ki rehlat ke baad Jange Jamal mein mukhtasar Ale Imran ki Shakhsiyat Ali (as) jinko us waqt Khalifa maan rahe the kasir ta'dad musalmano se muqabla hua jin alambardar ek zauja-e-Rasool thi. Ale Iman har tarah se Islam ki muhafezat ki.
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜
----------------------------------------------

_*MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!*_
🙇 😟
Imam Ali (as):
Main tumhare baare me 2 chizo'n se bahut darta hu'n: (1) Khawisho'n ki pairawi
     - jo Haq se rok deti hai,
(2) Lambi Aarzoo
    - jo Aakherat ko bhula deti hai.
(Guftaar e Dil Nasheen)
🕌
Imam Ali (as):
"Hargiz (munafiq) logo'n ki Masajid ki tadaad aur (namaz e ba) jamaat se dhoka NA khao; inke jism ikatthe lekin dil bikhre huwe hain."
(Meezanul Hikmah, Vol 7)

       ♦ _*DUNIYAWI ZEENAT*_ ♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (289)

*(بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ)*

*(زُيِّنَ لِلنَّاسِ حُبُّ الشَّهَوَاتِ مِنَ النِّسَاءِ وَالْبَنِينَ وَالْقَنَاطِيرِ الْمُقَنْطَرَةِ مِنَ الذَّهَبِ وَالْفِضَّةِ وَالْخَيْلِ الْمُسَوَّمَةِ وَالْأَنْعَامِ وَالْحَرْثِ ۗ ذَٰلِكَ مَتَاعُ الْحَيَاةِ الدُّنْيَا ۖ وَاللَّهُ عِنْدَهُ حُسْنُ الْمَآبِ)*

"Maddi cheezen (Material) mein se aurten, aulad aur maal jo sone chandi ke dheron par mushtamil ho, muntakhab ghode, janwar aur zara'at (kheti) logon ki nazar mein pasandeedah bana diye gaye hain (taake unke zariye unki azmayish (Test) aur tarbiyat (training) ho lekin) ye cheezen (agar insaan ke asli maqasid ke liye zariya bane phir bhi) past (low) maddi Zindagi ka sarmaya hain aur anjaame nek (aur aali zindagi) Khuda ke paas hain."
(Surah Aal-e-Imran: 14)

📚📖 👨‍👩‍👧‍👦 💰💵 🐎 🌾🍃
👉 _* Tafseer:*_
Duniya ki Maal o Daulat, Biwi, Aulad, behtareen sawari, kheti badi sab ko Allah ne hamare liye fitratan Zeenat banaya taake Wo hamara in cheezon ke zariye test le sake. Duniya ko har shakhs pasand karta aur yehi uska zariya hayaat hai, lekin asal maqsade hayaat Akherat hai.
Aaj Wiladat Imam Husain (as) hai Ale Imran ki ek kadi, Karbala mein inhone apne 72 sathiyon ke sath bata diya maqsade hayaat kiya hai. Agar Maqsad Duniya hoti to maarkaye Karbala na hota. Karbala mein ek taraf Yazeed ki misali Duniya thi, doosri taraf Islami Maqsade Hayaat tha. Duniya Fani hai, Akherat ki Zindagi la mahdood hai.
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜
----------------------------------------------

_*MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!*_
🙇  👨‍👩‍👧‍👦 💰💵 🐎 🌾🍃
Imam Husain (as):
"Agar GAREEBI, BEEMARI aur MAUT na hote, to aadmi kisi ke aage JHUKTA NAHI."
(Hadees of Imam Husain (AS) www.aimislam.com)
🌍
Imam Husain (as):
"Tum Jannat ke haqdar ho. Apne aap ko is se kam me mat becho. Wo jo duniya ki lazzat pe raazi hai usne bahut neech aur ghatiya par itminaan kiya."
(aimislam.com)
🌍
Imam Husain (as):
"Qayamat ke din SIRF wohi shakhs DARR se mehfooz hoga jo Duniya mein Allah se darta raha."
(Meezan ul Hikmah, v3)
💰💵
Imam Husain (as):
"Agar Maal ka jamaa karna chhod jaane ke liye hai to phir sharif aadmi chhode jaane wale maal ke liye KYON KANJOOSI KARTA HAI."
((Bihaarul Anwaar 44/374)

               ♦ _*JANNAT*_ ♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (290)

*(بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ)*

*(قُلْ أَؤُنَبِّئُكُمْ بِخَيْرٍ مِنْ ذَٰلِكُمْ ۚ لِلَّذِينَ اتَّقَوْا عِنْدَ رَبِّهِمْ جَنَّاتٌ تَجْرِي مِنْ تَحْتِهَا الْأَنْهَارُ خَالِدِينَ فِيهَا وَأَزْوَاجٌ مُطَهَّرَةٌ وَرِضْوَانٌ مِنَ اللَّهِ ۗ وَاللَّهُ بَصِيرٌ بِالْعِبَادِ)*

"Kah dijiye: kiya tumhe aisi cheez se aagah karun jo is (maddi sarmaye) se behtar hai jinhon ne Parhezgari ikhtiyar ki hai. (Aur Material wealth, maddi sarmaye se sharaii tariqe se aur Haq o Adalat ko malhooz rakhte hue istefada (use) kiya hai). Unke Parwardegar ke paas (doosre jahan mein) aise baghaat hain jinke niche nehren bahti hai, woh hamesha un mein rahenge aur pakeeza biwiyan (jo har napaki se munazzah hain) aur khushnoodiye Khuda inhe naseeb hogi aur Khuda (bando ke umoor ko) Dekhnewala hai."
(Surah Aal-e-Imran: 15)

📚📖
👉 _* Tafseer:*_
Taqwa wa Parhezgar logon ke liye Jannat ki khushkhabri Allah ne di hai. Akherat mein Jaza wa saza jismani hogi. Jannat mein baghaat honge jis mein naheren bahti hongi. Hauze Kausar hoga jahan Rasoole Khuda (sa) aur Ali (as) honge, Sardare Jawanan Jannat Hasan wa Husain (as) aur Khatoone Jannat Jb Fatema Zehra (sa) hongi. Jo inse doori ikhtiyar karega ghate mein rahega Jannat ke qareeb bhi nahi ja sakega.
Aaj Wiladat hai Ale Imran ki ek aur hasti Hazrat Abbas (as) ki, jo wafaon ke sardar, apne Maula ke mutee o farmabardar, Abdus Saleh hain.
Yehi log is Jannat ke misdaq hain jinke liye Jannat banayi gayi. للذين اتقوا jo Muttaqi the. Muttaqi ki sifat Surah Baqarah ke shuru bata di gayi hai. Inhe qamare Bani Hashim kaha gaya, ye Ale Imran ke chaand the, jo chaand Karbala mein chamka, jinki wajah se aaj tak Islam roshan hai.
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜
----------------------------------------------

_*MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!*_
🙇
Imam Sadiq (as):
Rasulullah (saww) ne farmaya:
"Meri Ummat mein Jannat mein daakhil hone wale zyadatar log Muttaqi (Parhezgaar) aur Achche Akhlaaq wale honge."
(Al Kaafi, v3)

Imam Sadiq (as):
"Khush-naseeb hai wo shakhs ke jo andekhi (unseen) Jannat ke badle mein Duniya ki shehwato'n (desires) ko tark (avoid) kare."
(Sharh Dua e Kumail)

Imam Sadiq (as):
"Mein gawahi deta hun, Aye Abbas, tum Raza bar Razai Ilahi, Wafa o Ita'at mein Kamal ki choti par pahunch gaye."

       ♦ _*MUTTAQEEN*_ ♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (291)

*(بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ)*

*(الَّذِينَ يَقُولُونَ رَبَّنَا إِنَّنَا آمَنَّا فَاغْفِرْ لَنَا ذُنُوبَنَا وَقِنَا عَذَابَ النَّارِ*
*الصَّابِرِينَ وَالصَّادِقِينَ وَالْقَانِتِينَ وَالْمُنْفِقِينَ وَالْمُسْتَغْفِرِينَ بِالْأَسْحَارِ)*

"Wohi jo kahte hain: Ay hamare Parwardegar! Ham Imaan le aye hain, pas hamen bakhsh de aur aag ke Azaab se bacha le."

"Wohi jo (mushkelat ke muqabele mein, ita'at ki raah  mein aur tarke gunah ke raaste mein) pamardi aur isteqamat dikhate hain (Sabir- Patient), Sach bolte hai (Truthful), (Khuda ke huzoor mein) Khuzoo karte hain (humbleness), (Uski rah mein) kharch karte hain (Charity), aur auqate saher mein (dawn, aur Ibaadat akhire Shab mein) istighfar karte hai (Forgiveness)."
(Surah Aal-e-Imran: 16 - 17)

📚📖
👉 _* Tafseer:*_
Pichhli Ayat mein Allah ne un logon ke liye Jannat ki Basharat di thi jo log Muttaqi o parhezgar hain. Allah unki sifat yahan bayan kar raha hai. Jo sifat yahan bayan ki gayi woh yeh hain.
(1) Sabr o Isteqamat.
(2) Sachchai
(3)Khuzoo wa inkisari
(4) Infaq
(5) Namaze Shab mein Istighfar.
🌻
Ale Imran mein ye sari khusoosiyaten payi jati hain, jabke woh in sab mein hamare liye Namoona e Amal hain. Karbala mein Imam Husain (as) ne ek raat ki muhlat sirf Ibaadat ke liye maangi thi, khemon mein se raat bhar aisi awazen aa rahi thi jaise makhiyan bhinbhinati hain. Us raat ye sari 5 sifat zahir ho rahe thi. Ali Ibnul Husain Akbar, Ausat o Asghar sab ne in sifat ka muzahera kiya. Janabe Ali Akbar ham shakle Shabeeh e Rasool, Ali Awsat Imam Zainul Abdin, Sajjad, Ali Asghar jazba e sabr o isteqamat. Shaban mein Farzandan e Ale Imran ki aamad hai, Karbala ke kirdar Shabaan mein tayyar ho rahe hain. Aur isi Shaban mein Muntaqime Karbala ki bhi amad hai. Jinke Rahnuma aise hon unke pairokar ko bhi aisa banne ki koshish karni chahiye. Ahdenas Siratal Mustaqeem.
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜
----------------------------------------------

_*MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!*_
🙇 🌻
Imam Sajjad (as):
"Momin ki 5 nishaniya'n hai: (1) Tanhaai me Taqwa,
(2) Gareebi me Khairaat,
(3) Musibato'n me Sabr,
(4) Gusse ko bardaasht karna aur
(5) khauf ki haalat me (bhi) sach kehna."
(A Bundle of Flowers)
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜
_*AL MAHDI (atfs)*_ (1)
The Lineage of Imam al-Mahdi (Nasle Imam)

قَالَ رَسُولُ اللٌّهِ :الْـمَهْدِيُّ مِنْ وُلْدِيْ وَجْهُهُ كَالْقَمَرِ الْدُّرِّيِّ.
Rasoole Khuda (sa):
"Al Mahdi Meri Aal se hai, unka chehra Roshan chamakta Chand hai."
🌻
“Al-Mahdi is from my progeny; his face is like the brightly illuminated moon.”
(Biharul Anwar, Volume 51, Page 85; Kashful Ghammah
🌻
Imam Ali (as):
"Sabse behtareen ibaadat hai _*Sabr*_, Khamoshi aur Imam e Mahdi (atfs) ki aamad (zahoor) ka _*intezaar karna.*_"
(Islamic Morals)

              ♦ _*TAWHEED*_ ♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (292)
🕌
*(بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ)*

*(شَهِدَ اللَّهُ أَنَّهُ لَا إِلَٰهَ إِلَّا هُوَ وَالْمَلَائِكَةُ وَأُولُو الْعِلْمِ قَائِمًا بِالْقِسْطِ ۚ لَا إِلَٰهَ إِلَّا هُوَ الْعَزِيزُ الْحَكِيمُ)*

"Khuda (jahane hasti ke akele nizam ko ijad karke) gawahi deta hai ke Uske alawa koi Ma'bood nahi hai aur _*Farishte aur Ahle Ilm o Danish (Ale Imran)*_ (sab ek tarah, gawahi dete hain, is Aalam mein ke Khuda Ta'ala Aalam hasti mein) Adalat qaim kiye hue hai (aur ye Adalat bhi Uski Zaat ki Yaktai (Oneness) ke liye nishani hai, isliye tum bhi un sab ke sath ham awaz hokar kaho ke) Uske Alawa koi Ma'bood nahi jo Ghalib o Tawana (Mighty) aur Hakim o Dana (Wise) bhi hai."
(Surah Aal-e-Imran: 18)

📚📖 🕌
👉 _* Tafseer:*_
Is ayat mein Allah ki Wahdaniyat ki gawahi di ja rahi hai. Allah khud is ki gawahi de raha hai. Iski daleel ye hai ke Allah ki Adalat puri Aalam mein qaim hai. Ye gawahi Fe'li hai (practical) na ke iqrari. Allah ke sath Farishte aur Ulool Ilm bhi gawahi de rahe hai. Yani Masoom ki gawahi ho rahi hai kiyonki Ulool Ilm ko Farishton ke ham palla bayan hua hai.  Pas Ulool Ilm (Master of Knowledge) ka bhi Masoom (infallible) hona zaroori hai. Ghair Masoom ki gawahi etebar ke laeq nahi rahegi. Isliye pata chalta hai hai ke Ulool Ilm Ale Imran mein Masoom Imams ke siwa aur koi nahi. Sab jante hain Ahle Bait (as) Masoom the, unki baat koi inkar nahi kar sakta. Isse wazeh ho gaya ke Aima Tahereen ka rasta tawheedi rasta tha. Is ayat par Rasoole Khuda (sa) ne khusoosi nazar rakhi. Zuhair bin awam ka bayan hai ke Arfa ki raat Aap (sa) bar bar is ayat ko daurah rahe the.
Phir Allah hukm deta hai ke ham sab bhi unke sath wahi gawahi den. Means Kalma La ilaha Illa Allah ki gawahi den.
Ye pura surah Ale Imran ki fazilat mein hai jis ki taraf ham roz ishara karte hain.
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜
----------------------------------------------

_*MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!*_
🙇 🕌
Rasoole Khuda (sa):
*ساعة من عالم يتكى على فراشه ينظر فى علمه خير من عبادة العابد سبعين عاما.*
"Aalim ki ek lamha jisme wo apne ilm mein fikr o nazar karne ke liye bistar par takiya lagai, ek aabid ki 70 saal ki Ibaadat se behtar hai."
(Tafseer Majmaul Bayan- Tabarsi under this ayat)
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜
_*AL MAHDI (atfs)*_(2):
The Most Beloved to the Prophet (‘s)
💐
*قَالَ رَسُولُ اللٌّه: طُوبـى لِمَنْ أَدْرَكَ قَائِمَ أَهْلِ بَـيْـتِيْ وَ هُوَ مُقْتَدٍ بِهِ قَبْلَ قِـيَامِهِ. يَتَوَلَّـى وَلِـيَّهُ يَتَبَرَّأُ مِنْ عَدُوِّهِ وَ يَتَوَلَّى الأَئِمَّةَ الْهَادِيَةَ مِنْ قَبْلِهِ. أُولٌئِكَ رُفَقَائِيْ وَ ذُو وُدِّيْ وَ مَوَدَّتِيْ وَ أَكْرَمُ أُمَّتِيْ عَلَـيَّ.*
💐
Rasoole Khuda (sa):
"Mubarak ho us shakhs ko jo mere Ahle Bait mein se Qaim se mulaqat karega aur unke Zahoor se pahle un par poori aqeedat rakhta hoga. Wo unke doston se Muhabbat rakhega aur unke dushmano se bezari, aur unke pahle Aimmatal Al hadi se Muhabbat karega. Yaqeenan ye mere haqeeqi dost jin se mein Muhabbat o muwaddat rakhta hun, aur ye meri ummat ke Shurafa hain."
💐
“Congratulations to the person who meets the Qa’im [one who will rise] from my Ahlul Bayt and has firm belief in him before his advent. He will have love for his friends, and will distance himself from his enemies and will have love for the leaders of guidance (the Imams) who came before him. Indeed these are my true friends, those whom I have love and affection for and (they) are the noblest of people from my nation.”

(Biharul Anwar, V 52, P-129; al-Ghaybah of Shaykh Tusi)

   🌹 *WILADAT MUBARAK*🌹

                ♦ _*ISLAM*_ ♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (293)

*(بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ)*

*(إِنَّ الدِّينَ عِنْدَ اللَّهِ الْإِسْلَامُ ۗ وَمَا اخْتَلَفَ الَّذِينَ أُوتُوا الْكِتَابَ إِلَّا مِنْ بَعْدِ مَا جَاءَهُمُ الْعِلْمُ بَغْيًا بَيْنَهُمْ ۗ وَمَنْ يَكْفُرْ بِآيَاتِ اللَّهِ فَإِنَّ اللَّهَ سَرِيعُ الْحِسَابِ)*

"Allah ke nazdeek Deen-e-Islam (aur Haq ke samne sar tasleem kham karna) hai. Jinke pas aasmani  kitab thi unhone ilm o agahi ke baad bhi ikhtelaf paida kiya. Aur woh bhi apne darmiyan zulm o sitam ki bena par aur Ayate Khuda se Kufr ikhtiyar kare (to Khuda iska muhaseba karega kiyonki) Khuda Sariul Hisab hai (Ready Reckoner)."
(Surah Aal-e-Imran: 19)

📚📖
👉 _* Tafseer:*_
Deen ke literal meaning hai: 'Jaza', 'Reward'.
Islam mean "Submission", 'Haqiqat ke samne jhuk Jana."
Allah ko Islam pasand hai. Doosri ayat mein jab Imran (Abu Talib) ke Farzand Ali (as) ko Rasool ne apne Janashin ka ailan kiya to Allah Quran declare kiya ke Islam Complete hua. Quran sirf Ale Imran ka fard hi samjha sakta hai.
Imam Ali Ibne Imran (Abi Talib) (as):
*"لا نسبن الاسلام نسبة لم ينسبها احد قلبى:*
*الاسلام هو التسليم، و التسليم هو اليقين، و اليقين هو التصديق، و التصديق هو الاقرار، و الاقرار هو الآداء، و الآداء هو العمل.*

"Mein chahta hun Islam ki aisi Tafseer bayan karon jo kisi ne na ki ho."
Iske baad aap (as) Islam ke 6 marhale bayan karte hai:
(1) Islam Haq ke samne sar tasleem kham karna. (Complete Submission)
(2) Tasleem Yaqeen ke baghair mumkin nahi. (Certainty)
(Kiyonki Yaqeen ke baghair Tasleem andha dhond hogi, alemana nahi.)
(3) Yaqeen Tasdeeq ka doosra naam hai.
(Confirmation or Verification)
(4) Tasdeeq hi Iqrar hai. (Dil se)
(Acceptance by heart, affidavit)
(5) Iqrar Zimmedari ko puri karna.
(Fulfilment of duties)
(6) Zimmedari puri karna hi
Amal hai. (Action)
(Ref: Nahjul Balagha)

Ab sab Ilm o danish zahir hone ke baad bhi Haq mein ikhtelaf karen to ye jahiliyat nahi. Ahle Bait o Ale Imran (as) ki manzelat kaun nahi janta. Sab hi inke fazael bayan karte hain, lekin phir bhi inko apna Rehbar tasleem nahi karte, ye jihalat nahi, ta'ssub hai. Ye silsila Hazrat Adam (as) se aaj tak chala aa raha hai. Sare Anbiya, Aimma Shaheed hue kiya wajah thi. Yahan ayat mein Christian ke misal di hai ke Haq itna zahir hone ke bawajood phir bhi unhone inkar kiya. Dua hai ke Allaj ham sab ko in ikhtelafat se door rakhe.
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜
----------------------------------------------

_*MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!*_
🙇
_*AL MAHDI (atfs)*_ (3):
None Shall be Saved, Except…

*قَالَ الإِمَامُ الْحَسَنُ بْنُ عَلِيٍِّ الْعَسْكَرِيُّ : ... وَ اللٌّهِ لَيَغْيِبَنَّ غَيْـبَةً لاَ يَنْجُوْ فِيهَا مِنَ الْهَلَكَةِ إِلاَّ مَنْ ثَـبَّتَ اللٌّهُ عَزَّ وَ جَلَّ عَلـى الْقَوْلِ بِإِمَامَتِهِ وَ وَفَّقَهُ (فِيهَا) لِلدُّعَاءِ بِتَعْجِيلِ فَرَجِهِ.*

Imam Hasan ibn ‘Ali al-’Askari (as):
"Khuda ki Qasam wo (Imam Mahdi) ghaibat ikhtiyar karenge, is tarah ke sab halal ho jayenge siwai uske jisko Allah azza wa jallah (Imam Mahdi) ki aqeeda e Imamat ko sabit qadam rakhega, jisko Woh unke Zahoor ke jaldi ke dua ki taufeeq deta hai."

“… I swear by Allah that he (Imam al-Mahdi) shall go into an occultation such that none shall be saved [during that period] from destruction, except the person whom Allah, Glorious and Grand is He, makes firm on the belief of his Imamate [of Imam al-Mahdi] and whom He grants the Divine ability(tawfiq) to supplicate for his speedy advent.”
(Kamalud-Din, Vol 2, P-384
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜
----------------------------------------------
7th Shaban 1437
15th May 2016, Sunday,

                ♦ _*DEBATE*_ ♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (294)

*(بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ)*

*(فَإِنْ حَاجُّوكَ فَقُلْ أَسْلَمْتُ وَجْهِيَ لِلَّهِ وَمَنِ اتَّبَعَنِ ۗ وَقُلْ لِلَّذِينَ أُوتُوا الْكِتَابَ وَالْأُمِّيِّينَ أَأَسْلَمْتُمْ ۚ فَإِنْ أَسْلَمُوا فَقَدِ اهْتَدَوْا ۖ وَإِنْ تَوَلَّوْا فَإِنَّمَا عَلَيْكَ الْبَلَاغُ ۗ وَاللَّهُ بَصِيرٌ بِالْعِبَادِ)*

"Agar woh tumse guftugu aur jhagde ke liye uth khade hon (to unse mujadela na karo) aur kah do! Mein aur mere pairokar Khuda ke (aur iske farman ke) samne tasleem hain aur jo Ahle Kitab (Jew & Christian) hain aur jo anpadh jahil (Mushrekin) hain, unse kahdo kiya tum bhi tasleem hue ho? Agar wo (farmane Khuda aur Mantiqe Haq ke samne) dar Tasleem Khan kar den to Hidayat pa len aur agar rugardani (turn away) karen (to tum pareshan na ho kiyonki) tum par to iblaghe risalat ki zimmedari hai aur Khuda bando ke (aqaed o Aamaal) dekhta hai."
(Surah Aal-e-Imran: 20)

📚📖
👉 _* Tafseer:*_

1. Ayat se zimni taur par maloom hota hai ke aise hat dharm afraad se bahes mubahesa avoid karna chahiye.
2. 'Ummi' se murad mushrekin hain kiyonki inke pas koi aasmani Kitab nahi thi. Isliye wo jahil the.
3. Paighambare Islam ne jo 40 saal tabhleeg ki usme kisi par unhone apne nazarya ya aqeeda jabran nahi thoonsa. Balke unki apne amal se koshish ye rahi ke haqaiq ko samjhen. Unhone na koi daleel pesh ki na koi bade bade tableeghi program ya ijtema rakhe. Bas sirf Rasool kahte rahe aur log sun kar ghaur karte rahe.
Yehi ravish Rasool (sa) ke ausiya m, Ahle Bait (as), Ale Imran ki rahi. Karbala ke waqea ke baad Ahle Bait (as) ki khamosh Zindagi ek namoona hai. Ye khamoshi isliye thi kiyonki unke chahnewalon ki qillat thi, aur unhone ne zabardasti ki par apne aqaid thope nahi. Jisne  Haq ko pahchan liya woh unki taraf chala aya.
Imam Mahdi (as) bhi pardae ghaib mein apne chahnewalo ke muntazir hain, jab 313 afraad ho jayenge tab Zahoor karenge.
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜
----------------------------------------------

_*MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!*_
🙇
*الإمام علي (ع): إياكم والجدال؛ فإنه يورث‏الشك.*
Imam Ali (as):
"Hujjat o bahes na karo kiyonki ye shak mein mubtela karta hai."
(al-Khisal, p. 615, no. 10)
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜
_*AL MAHDI (atfs):*_ (4)

Absolute Obedience to the Imam

*قَالَ الإِمَامُ مُحَمَّدُ بْنُ عَلِيٍّ الْجَوَادُ : ... إِنَّ الْقَائِمَ مِنَّا هُوَ الْمَهْدِيُّ الَّذِي يَجِبُ أَنْ يُنْـتَظَرَ فِي غَيْـبَتِهِ وَ يُطَاعَ فِي ظُهُورِهِ وَ هُوَ الثَّالِثُ مِنْ وُلْدِي ...*

Imam Muhammad ibn ‘Ali al-Jawad (as):
" ...... Yaqeenan Al-Qaim ham (Ahle Bait)  mein se hain, aur woh hain Al-Mahdi, jinki ghaibat mein Intezar aur zahoor mein ita'at wajib hai aur wo meri nasl mein teesre hain."

“… Indeed al-Qa’im is from among us (the Ahlul Bayt) and he is al-Mahdi - the one whom it is obligatory to wait for during his occultation and obey during his advent, and he is the third from my progeny …”
(Kamal ad-Din, Volume 2, Page 377)
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜

***********************************
          ♦ _*NA-HAQ QATL*_ ♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (295)
🐾
*(بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ)*

*(إِنَّ الَّذِينَ يَكْفُرُونَ بِآيَاتِ اللَّهِ وَيَقْتُلُونَ النَّبِيِّينَ بِغَيْرِ حَقٍّ وَيَقْتُلُونَ الَّذِينَ يَأْمُرُونَ بِالْقِسْطِ مِنَ النَّاسِ فَبَشِّرْهُمْ بِعَذَابٍ أَلِيمٍ **
*أُولَٰئِكَ الَّذِينَ حَبِطَتْ أَعْمَالُهُمْ فِي الدُّنْيَا وَالْآخِرَةِ وَمَا لَهُمْ مِنْ نَاصِرِينَ)*
🐾
_"Jo log Ayat-e-Khuda se Kufr karte hain (Haq ko chhupate hain), Anbiya ko na-Haq qatl karte hain aur Adl ka hukm dene walon ko bhi qatl kar dete hain. Inhe dardnak Azaab ki Basharat dijiye."_
_"Wo aise log hain jinke nek Aamaal (in azeem gunahon ki wajah se) Duniya aur Akherat mein tabah ho gaye hain aur unka koi yawar o madadgar (aur Shafa'at karne wala) nahi hai."_
(Surah Aal-e-Imran: 21 - 22)

📚📖 ⚔ 🗡 🔪
👉 _* Tafseer:*_
🐾🐾🐾🐾🐾🐾🐾🐾
Is ayat mein jis ke liye dardnak Azaab ki basharat di gayi hai uske liye 3 Azeem gunah hain:
(1)  Aayaat-e-Ilahi se Kufr.
(2) Anbiya ka na-Haq Qatl.
(3) Adalat qaym karne walon  ka bhi qatl.
Qatl gunahe kabira nahi balke Azeem gunah hai. Aur woh bhi aisa hai ke agar usne nek Aamaal bhi kiyon ho to sab mit jayenge.
Shaitan bhi pahle sab se bada aabid tha, lekin usne Ayaat-e-Ilahi (Hazrat Adam) ka Kufr kiya, Jannat se nikal diya gaya. Shaitan ne challenge kiya ke mein Admi (nasle Adam (as) ko bhatkaonga. Allah na kaha uske mukhlis bande uski baaton mein nahi ayenge. Yehi kaam Shaitan ne shuru kiya, pahla qatl Habeel ka hua. Phir Anbiya ke qatl ka silsila chala. Lekin Allah ne bhi Hidayat ke Chirag ko bhujne na diya. Silsila e Nabuwwat Hazrat Rasoole Khuda (sa) par khatm hua. Phir unke baad Imamat o Wilayat ka silsila shuru hua, Shaitan ke pairokar ne bhi apna kaam jari rakha. Qatil bhi aise jinke matho par sajdon ke nishan, zaban par Allah o Akbar, Aasteen chadhi hui payjama chadha hua, ba wuzu, Namaz ke paband lekin Allah ke Mehboob bande ke qatl par amadah. Karbala mein ye muqabala urooj par pahuncha. Shahadaten par shahadaten waqae hoti rahin, Ahle Bait, Ahle Imraan Shaheed hote rahe. Phir Shaitan ke parokaron ne Ale Payambar ke chahnewalon ko bhi nahi chhoda. Allah ne apne akheri Hidayat ke Chirag ko parde mein mehfooz rakh diya taake woh apni Adalat qayem kar sake kiyonki unke Adalat qayem karne walon ko bhi nahi chhoda. Islam aaj mazloom hai, woh bhi intezar mein hain kab woh is sare khoon ka inteqam lene wala Zahoor kare aur in zalimo se qabron se nikal kar badla le. Allah ne in ayaat mein isi baat ki taraf ishara kiya hai.
🐾🐾🐾🐾🐾🐾🐾🐾🐾
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜
----------------------------------------------

_*MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!*_
🙇 🐾🗡
Imam Ali (as):
Teen cheezein halaak kar dene waali hai -
(1) _*TAKABBUR (Pride)*_ - Jisne Iblees (Shaitaan) ko apne martabe se gira diya,
(2) _*LAALACH (Greed)*_ - Jisne Adam ko Jannat se nikalwa diya, aur
(3) _*HASAD (Jealousy)*_ - Jisne Adam ke bete ko apne bhai ke qatl par aamaada kiya.
(Tajalliyate Hikmat)
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜
_*AL MAHDI (atfs):*_ (5)

Tears of Separation

*قَالَ الإِمَامُ جَعْفَرُ بْنُ مُحَمَّدٍ الصَّادِقُ : وَ اللٌّهِ لِيَغِيبَنَّ إِمَامُكُمْ سِنِينَ مِنَ الدَّهْرِ ... وَ لَتَفِيضَنَّ عَلَيْهِ أَعْـيُنُ الْمُؤْمِنِينَ.*

Imam Ja’far Sadiq (as):
"Khuda ki qasam , tumhara Imam barson tak ghaib rahenga........ (us darmiyan mein) mukhlis mo'menin ki aankhen aansuon se bhar jayengi (apne Mehboob ke firaaq mein)."

“I swear by Allah that your Imam will go into an occultation for a number of years … [during that period] the eyes of the true believers shall be filled with tears [due to being separated from him].”

(Biharul Anwar, Vol 51, P-147; al-Ghaybah of al-Nu’mani)
😢😭😢😭😢😭😢😭😢😭😢

17th May 2016, Tuesday,

*SHIA CHANNEL WELCOMES YOU*
***********************************
       ♦ _*FAISLA*_ ♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (297)

*(بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ)*

*أَلَمْ تَرَ إِلَى الَّذِينَ أُوتُوا نَصِيبًا مِنَ الْكِتَابِ يُدْعَوْنَ إِلَىٰ كِتَابِ اللَّهِ لِيَحْكُمَ بَيْنَهُمْ ثُمَّ يَتَوَلَّىٰ فَرِيقٌ مِنْهُمْ وَهُمْ مُعْرِضُونَ*

_"Kiya tumne un logo ko nahi dekha jinke pas (Aasmani) Kitab ka kuchh hissa hai. Aur un mein faisle ke liye unhe Kitab e Khuda ki taraf dawat di gayi hai lekin (ilm o agahi ke bawujood) un mein se ek fariq ne roogardani (turn away) ki jabki wo (quboole Haq se) palte hue the."_
(Surah Aal-e-Imran: 23)

📚📖
👉 _*�Tafseer:*_
Ibne Abbas ki rivayat:
Rasoole Khuda (sa) ke zamane mein Khaibar ke Yahoodiyon mein se ek aurat aur ek mard zina e muhassana (dono hi shadi shuda) ke murtakib hue. Dono Ashraf khandan mein se the. Taurait ke mutabiq saza sangsar (stoning) tha. Is ki saza mein un logon ne delay kiya aur Faisle ke liya Rasoole Akram (sa) ko rujoo kiya. Wo samjhe ye kam saza sunaynge lekin Rasoolullah (sa) ne bhi wohi saza ka hukm diya. Is faisle par Yahoodi do hisso mein bat gaye ek ne object kiya to doosre ne support kiya. Rasool ne farmaya yehi Taurait faisla karegi. Unka sab se bada Alim Ibne Soorya ko bulaya gaya. Rasool ne usse kaha ke in logo ko Taurait ka woh hissa suna do jis mein Sangsar ka hukm hai.
Ye sab dekh kar Abdulla bin Salam jo Yahoodi tha Musalman ho gaya. Aur unki Kitab ke mutabiq saza di gayi.
_(Tafseer Majmaul Bayan)_

Is waqea mein Rasool ko isliye bulaya tha ke wo samajhte the ke Rasool ko unki Kitab ka Ilm kam hoga aur woh bhi ke Rahmatullil Alamin hain isliye saza maaf kar de ya kam kar den. Means unki Kitab mein jo likha hai usko chhupana chahte the.
Shuru se ajtak Haq ko chhupaya gaya. Ale Rasool wa Ale Imran ke sath kuchh aisa hi pesh aya.
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜
----------------------------------------------

_*MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!*_
🙇
AL MAHDI (atfs): (7)
🌻
People with the Highest Rank

*قَالَ الإِمَامُ عَلِيُّ بْنُ الْحُسَينِ السَّجَّادُ : إِنَّ أَهْلَ زَمَانِ غَيْـبَتِهِ الْقَائِلِينََ بِإِمَامَتِهِ الْمُنْـتَظِرِينَ لِظُهُورِهِ أَفْضَلُ أَهْلِ كُلِّ زَمَانٍ لأَِنَّ اللٌّهَ تَعَالـى ذِكْرُهُ أَعْطَاهُمْ مِنَ الْعُقُولِ وَ الأَفْهَامِ وَ الْمَعْرِفَةِ مَا صَارَتْ بِهِ الْغَيْـبَةُ عِنْدَهُمْ بِمَنْـزِلَةِ الْمُشَاهَدَةِ.*
🌻
Imam ‘Ali ibnil Husain al-Sajjad (as):
_"Yaqeenan, jo log zamana ghaibat mein rahenge, unki (Imam Mahdi) ki Imamat ke qael aur unke Zahoor ke Muntazir honge, har zamane se woh behtareen honge, jaisake Allah Ta'ala ne, ke Zikr mein hai, unko aql o shuoor o Ma'arefat se aisa nawaza hai jiske zariye wo ghaibat mein is tarah zindagi guzar saken jaise wo Zahoor ke waqt guzar rahe hon."_
🌻
_“Indeed the people who live during the time of his occultation, have firm belief in his (the 12th Imam’s) Imamate and are awaiting his advent are the best people of every age since Allah, Great is His Mention, has granted them from the intellect, understanding and cognizance needed which would permit them to live during the period of the occultation, as if they were living during the time of his advent.”_
(Biharul Anwar, Volume 52, Page 122; al-Ihtijaj)

                 ♦ _*AZAAB*_ ♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (298)

*(بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ)*

*(ذَٰلِكَ بِأَنَّهُمْ قَالُوا لَنْ تَمَسَّنَا النَّارُ إِلَّا أَيَّامًا مَعْدُودَاتٍ ۖ وَغَرَّهُمْ فِي دِينِهِمْ مَا كَانُوا يَفْتَرُونَ)*

_"(Cont'd..) (Unka) ye (amal) is bena par tha ke woh kahte the ke chand din ke siwa (Jahannam ki) Aag ham tak nahi pahunchegi. (Aur doosri qaumon se hamare imtiyaz ki wajah se hame bahut hi mahdood saza milegi) aur (Khuda par band he gaye) is iftera (gharhi hue baten) ne unhe bahut maghroor kar diya tha."_
(Surah Aal-e-Imran: 24)

📚📖
👉 _* Tafseer:*_
Yahoodi ghalat aur batil fikr rakhte the. Apni nasl parasti par naaz karte. Wo apne aap ko par ghamand karte aur kahte 'wo Allah ke bete aur khas dost hain. Isliye wo aisa sochte the ke wo kuchh bhi karen unhe kuchh muddat ke liye saza milegi.
Aisa aqeeda Musalmano mein bhi paya jata hai ke kuchh ko kuchh muddat ke liye saza milegi aur phir Jannat mein entry milegi. Shia jo ye dawa karte ke ham koi bhi gunah karen aur Aimmah hamari shafa'at kardenge aur ham sab Jannat mein jayenge. Hamare aanso Jannat mein le jayenge. Baat sahi hai par kiya Aimma masoomin (as) gunehgar ko pasand karenge? Shafa'at usi ki hogi jis ko Imam chahenge ke anjane mein koi ghalti ho gayi aur phir pur khuloos tauba o isteghfar karega.
Islam mein logon ne bahut si chizen ghadi gayin aur log dhoke mein rahe. Jinhon ne Ahle Bait (as) ka rasta chhoda woh dhoke mein rahe aur gumrahi ke raste par gamzan hain.
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜
----------------------------------------------

_*MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!*_
🙇
Imam Ali (as):
"Jhoote aadmi ki sabse pehli sazaa to ye hai ke uski sach baatein bhi thhukra di jaati hai."
(Tajalliyate Hikmat)
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜
_*AL MAHDI (atfs):*_  (8)
Greeting Imam al-Mahdi

"Ek Shakhs ne ek bar Imam Jafar Sadiq (as) se poochha ke woh kaise Imam Al Qaim (atfs) par apna Salam bhejen to Imam ne farmaya:

_"Taqool: Asslamo alaika ya Baqiyatullah_
(Kaho: Salamti ho aap par, aye Allah ke baqi manda.)"

"A man once asked Imam Ja’far ibn Muhammad as-Sadiq (as) how he should send his salutations upon Imam al-Qa’im (may Allah hasten his advent) and the Imam replied:

*تَقُولُ: السَّلاَمُ عَلَيْكُمْ يَا بَقِيَّةَ اللٌّهِ.*

”Say: Greetings be upon you, O’ Remnants of Allah"

( _*Dua-e-Nudba*_ )
(Biharul Anwar, Vol 52, P-373, Tafsir Furat ibn Ibrahim)

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

*(بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ)*

*(فَكَيْفَ إِذَا جَمَعْنَاهُمْ لِيَوْمٍ لَا رَيْبَ فِيهِ وَوُفِّيَتْ كُلُّ نَفْسٍ مَا كَسَبَتْ وَهُمْ لَا يُظْلَمُونَ)*

_"(Cont'd) Pas us waqt kiya haalat hogi jab us (Qayamat ke) din jis mein koi shak nahi (sab jama honge), Ham unhe aur har shakhs ko jo kuchh unhone apne Aamal ke zariye kamaya hai, diya jayega aur un par zulm nahi hoga (balke wo apne Aamaal ki fasal katenge.)_
(Surah Aal-e-Imran: 25)

(http://al-islam.org/al-tawhid/kafi/)

_*AL MAHDI (atfs):*_ (9)
Testimony to Islam over the Entire Earth

قَالَ الإِمَامُ جَعْفَرُ بْنُ مُحَمَّدٍ الصَّادِقُ: إِذَا قَامَ الْقَائِمُ لاَ يَبْقـى أَرْضٌ إِلاَّ نُودِيََ فِيهَا شَهَادَةُ أَنْ
*لاَ إِلٌهَ إِلاَّ اللٌّهُ وَ أَنَّ مُحَمَّداً رَسُولُ اللٌّهِ.*
Imam Ja’far Sadiq (as):

_“When al-Qa’im makes his advent, not a single place of land will remain except that the call to the testimony of, ‘There is no creature worthy of worship except for Allah and indeed Muhammad is the Messenger of Allah’ will be given (there).”_

(Biharul Anwar, Volume 52, Page 340; Tafsir al-’Ayyashi)

            ♦ _*HUKUMAT*_ ♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (300)

*(بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ)*

*قُلِ اللَّهُمَّ مَالِكَ الْمُلْكِ تُؤْتِي الْمُلْكَ مَنْ تَشَاءُ وَتَنْزِعُ الْمُلْكَ مِمَّنْ تَشَاءُ وَتُعِزُّ مَنْ تَشَاءُ وَتُذِلُّ مَنْ تَشَاءُ ۖ بِيَدِكَ الْخَيْرُ ۖ إِنَّكَ عَلَىٰ كُلِّ شَيْءٍ قَدِيرٌ*
*تُولِجُ اللَّيْلَ فِي النَّهَارِ وَتُولِجُ النَّهَارَ فِي اللَّيْلِ ۖ وَتُخْرِجُ الْحَيَّ مِنَ الْمَيِّتِ وَتُخْرِجُ الْمَيِّتَ مِنَ الْحَيِّ ۖ وَتَرْزُقُ مَنْ تَشَاءُ بِغَيْرِ حِسَابٍ*
_"Kahiye, Bare Ilaha! Hukumaton ka Malik tu hai, Tu hi jise chahta hai ke Hukumat bakhshta hai aur jis se chahta hai Hukumat le leta hai, jise chahta hai Izzat deta hai aur jise chahta hai Zillat deta hai. Tamam Khoobiyan Tere Hath mein hain kiyonki Tu har cheez par Qadir hai."_
_"Raat ko Din mein aur Din ko Raat mein dakhil karta hai, Murdeh se Zindah ko aur Zindagi se Murdeh ko nikalta hai aur jise chahta hai be hisab Rozi deta hai."_
(Surah Aal-e-Imran: 26 - 27)
📚📖
👉 _*�Tafseer:*_
Ayat ke mutabiq Allah hi kisi ko bhi Mulk Ata karta hai ya chhin leta hai. Sab Allah ke hath mein hai.
Lekin kiya Zalimon ko  bhi Allah ki hukumat ata karta hai. Ye is tarah hai ke jab Allah pani barsata hai to sab faizyab hote hain Zalim ya Aadil.
Lekin doosri ayaton par ghaur karne se maloom hota hai Allah awamil o asbab (causes) paida karta hai. Ab in wasail ka kaun kaise istemal karta hai ye insaan par munhasir hai.
Yazid ne bhi apne istedlal mein isi ayat ka istemal kiya. Means Allah ke lutf o karam se. Baqaul Yazid ke jo bhi wo zulm kar raha tha wo Allah ki di hui hukumat ke zariye.
Ye ghalat hai. Allah Zalim nahi hai. Allah dono ka imtehaan leta hai. Kisi ko hukumat de kar, kisi ki le kar.  Zalim ko hukumat banane ka mauqa tab milta hai jab awam bhi uske sath de. Kahawat hai: _"har qaum usi hukumat ki layeq hai jo us par qaim hai"_. To jaisi qaum hogi waisi hi badshah hoga. Lekin Duniya ki history mein dekha ke har jagah jab bhi Zalim hukumat ke khilaf inqilab aya zalim ki hukumat ko ukhad pheka. British ki puri duniya mein hukumat thi phir zawal aya. Logon ki awaz ka natija tha. Agar log khamosh rahte to hukumat baqi rahti.
Allah ne Misali hukumat Nabiyon ko bhi di jaise Hazrat Dawood wa Sulaiman (as). Aur Hazrat Ali (as) ki 4 saal ki adalati hukumat.
Ab zamana Intezar mein hai us Mahdi Mawoood ka jo yahan par Insaaf wa Adle Ilahi Hukumat qaim karega. Jab duniya zulm o jaur se bhari hogi. Lekin us hukumat ke qayam ke liye sathi o nasiron ki zaroorat hogi. Ye hukumat bhi ba sababe insaan hi hogi. Jab 313 mukhlis bande tayyar ho jayenge tab Imam Mahdi (atfs) ka zahoor hoga. Isliye deri hamari taraf se hai. Jab ham chahenge tab aisa hoga.
_Allahumma Ajjil le waliyekal faraj._
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜
----------------------------------------------

_*MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!*_
🙇
Imam Ali (as):
_"Jis par tum Ehsaan karoge, uspar tumhari hukumat hogi. Jis se tum apni Haajat bayaan karoge, tum uske qaidi ban jaoge. Jis se tum beniyaaz (needless) rahoge, to uske baraabari waale ho jaaoge."_
(Meezan ul Hikmah, v1)
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜
_*AL MAHDI (atfs)*_ (10)
Ruling with Justice

*قَالَ الإِمَامُ مُحَمَّدُ بْنُ عَلِيٍّ البَاقِرُ :*
*إِذَا قَامَ قَائِمُ أَهْلِ الـْبَيْتِ قَسَمَ بِالسَّوِيَّةِ وَ عَدَلَ فِي الرَّعِـيَّةِ فَمَنْ أَطَاعَهُ فَقَدْ أَطَاعَ اللٌّهَ وَ مَنْ عَصَاهُ فَقَدْ عَصى اللٌّهَ وَ إِنَّمَا سُمِّيَ الْمَهْدِيَّ لأََِنَّهُ يَهْدِي إِلـى أَمْرٍ خَفيٍّ.*

Imam Muhammad Baqir (as):
_"Jab Ahle Bait ke Qaim (atfs) Zahoor karenge wo (Maal o Daulat) ko insaaf se taqseem karenge aur apni riaaya (parja) mein ADLALAT se pesh ayenge. Pas jis ne unki ita'at ki Allah ki ita'at ki aur jis ne unki mukhalefat ki Allah ki mukhalefat ki. Yaqeenan Al Mahdi isliye naam diya kiyonki wo khufiya Umoor ki Hidayat karenge."_

_“When the Qa’im of the Ahlul Bayt makes his advent, he will divide (the riches) with equity and will show justice among the people. So whoever obeys him, has obeyed Allah; and whoever goes against him, has gone against Allah. Indeed al-Mahdi was named as such because he will guide to the hidden affairs.”_

(Biharul Anwar, Volume 97, Page 117)
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜
----------------------------------------------
*14th Shaban 1437*, 22nd May 2016, Sunday,

BAZM-E-ADAB WELCOMES YOU*
***********************************
     ♦ _*DOSTI - TAQAYYA*_ ♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (302)

*بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ*

*لَا يَتَّخِذِ الْمُؤْمِنُونَ الْكَافِرِينَ أَوْلِيَاءَ مِنْ دُونِ الْمُؤْمِنِينَ ۖ وَمَنْ يَفْعَلْ ذَٰلِكَ فَلَيْسَ مِنَ اللَّهِ فِي شَيْءٍ إِلَّا أَنْ تَتَّقُوا مِنْهُمْ تُقَاةً ۗ وَيُحَذِّرُكُمُ اللَّهُ نَفْسَهُ ۗ وَإِلَى اللَّهِ الْمَصِيرُ*

_"Ahle Iman (Shia Mo'min) ko chhod kar Kafir ko apna dost aur sarparast na banal aur jo shakhs aisa karega uska kisi cheez mein Allah se koi rabt nahi hai. (Yani uska (connection Parwardegar se bilkul toot chuka hai) magar ye ke unse (aur ahmtar maqasid (Important Aim) ke liye) Taqayya karo aur Khuda tumhe apni nafarmani se darata hai aur (tumhari) bazgasht (return) Khuda ki taraf hai."_
(Surah Aal-e-Imran: 28)

📚📖 👥
👉 _* Tafseer:*_
_*Dosti*_
Ayat mein اوليآء wali ولى ki jama hai. Is ke maani dost aur sarparast dono hote hain. Allah ki ye advice hai ke Shia Momin ya Musalman ke hote huwe Kafir ko apna dost ya Wali na banayen. Lekin jab koi important kaam ho to unko contact mein rakha ja sakta hai. Yahan Allah ne Taqayya karne ki ijazat di hai.
_*Taqayya:*_
Taqayya تقيه ka root word hai وقى means to protect, bachana, hifazat karna. Is Ayat mein تقاة ka istemal hua hai.
Jab jan o maal, izzat khatre mein ho to Haq ke izhar ki zaroorat nahi. Yani apne aqeede ko chhupaya ja sakta hai. Is mein apne faraez makhfi taur par ada kiye jate hain. Tarikh mein waqeat bahut hain jab hukmuran ke khauf se log apne aqeede ko chhupa kar anjam dete the. Is ka istemal jab hota hai jab hamare aqeeda zahir hone se nuqsan zyada aur fayda kam hoga. Ammar ke maan baap ne Kafir ke samne izhar kiya to qatl ho gaye. Ammar ne zaheran unke aqeeda ka izhar kiya to bache rahe. Ammar ne is problem ko Rasool (sa) ke samne pesh kiya to Rasool (sa) ne farmaya ke jab tumse poochha jaye to wohi aqeeda zahir karna.
Taqayya ke hukm kabhi wajib, kabhi Haram to kabhi Mubah hai.
Jahan Taqayya se Batil ki tarweej ho wahan Haram hai. Is mein mauqa mahal dekha jata hai ke fayda kis mein hai. Isliye Janabe Zainab (sa) Imame Sajjad (as) se Kheme jalne ke baad pooch tha ke ab kiya karen, yani chadaren chhin rahi hain aseer kiya ja raha hai, Imam ne kaha jaisa wo kar rahen hain karne de. Yahan apni personal izzat important nahi thi, usse badhkar Islam ko bachana zyada important tha. Ye ek tarah ka safety weapon hai, jahan ek shakhs underground mein kaam karta hai. Ye na munafeqat hai na jhoot. Balke is ke peechhe Deeni fayda ahm hai.
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜
----------------------------------------------

_*MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!*_
🙇
_*AL MAHDI (atfs):*_ (12)
Anticipate the Advent of the Imam
*قَالَ الإِمَامُ جَعْفَرُ بْنُ مُحَمَّدٍ الصَّادِقُ : ... فَعِنْدَهَا فَتَوَقَّعُوا الْفَرَجَ صَبَاحــاً وَ مَسَــاءًا ...*

Imam Ja’far Sadiq (as):
_".... Ghaibat ke zamane mein (Imam Mahdi) ke Zahoor ka Intezar subah shaam karen...."_

_“ … During that time (the period of the occultation), await the advent (of the Imam) every morning and evening … ”_
(Usul al-Kafi, Vol 1, P-323)

BAZM-E-ADAB WELCOMES YOU*
***********************************
        ♦ _*TAQAYYA*_ ♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (303)

*بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ*

*قُلْ إِنْ تُخْفُوا مَا فِي صُدُورِكُمْ أَوْ تُبْدُوهُ يَعْلَمْهُ اللَّهُ ۗ وَيَعْلَمُ مَا فِي السَّمَاوَاتِ وَمَا فِي الْأَرْضِ ۗ وَاللَّهُ عَلَىٰ كُلِّ شَيْءٍ قَدِيرٌ*

_"Kahiye ke jo kuchh tumhare seeno hai use chhupaye rakho ya aashkar karo (hide or disclose), Khuda (behar haal) use janta hai aur Jo kuchh aasmano mein hai aur jo kuchh zameeno mein hai, Wo usse Aagah hai aur Khuda har cheez par Qadir hai."_
(Surah Aal-e-Imran: 29)

📚📖
👉 _* Tafseer:*_
Pichhli ayat mein Taqayya concept ki wazahat ki thi. Lekin kuchh log sahi cheez ka bhi ghalat fayda ya misuse karte hain. Means kaha gaya tha sirf Momin se dosti karen. Lekin exception case mein yani Taqayya ke taur karni ki ijazat di gayi thi. Lekin kuchh log bina koi wajah ke unse janboojh kar talluqat rakhen jis se Deen ko nuqsan ho. Aise logon ke liye ye ayat hai. Means bhale logon ko unke milne ka raz pata na ho lekin Allah sab ke razon ko janta hai. Iska fayda Munafeqeen ne uthaya. Ale Imraan ko bhugatna pada. Ali (as) wa Imam Hasan (as) ko munafeqeen ki wajah Bani Umayya se sulah karni padi. Kuchh ka nashta dushman ke yahan aur wafadari yahan par jatate the. Isse Islam ko bahut nuqsan pahuncha. Aise logon se badla lene ke liye abhi Ale Imran ki akhri kadi baqi hai, lekin intezar hai yawar o madadgar ka. Zaban par Al ajal, dil mein kuchh aur, ye sab Imam bhi jante hai aur unka Khuda bhi. To phir kaise zahir honge ye unke chahne walon ke liye lamhe fikriya hai.
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜
----------------------------------------------

_*MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!*_
🙇
_*AL MAHDI (atfs):*_ (13)

Felicitations are for…

*قَالَ رَسُولُ اللٌّهِ :*
*"... طُوبـى لِمَنْ لَقِيَهُ وَ طُوبـى لِمَنْ أَحَبَّهُ وَ طُوبـى لِمَنْ قَالَ بِهِ ..."*

The Messenger of Allah (sa):
_"Tuba ke haqdar hai wo shakhs jo unse (Imam Mahdi (as) mulaqat karega, jo unse Muhabbat karega, jo unki Imamat ka qael hoga."_

Note: Tuba Jannat mein ek darakht ka naam hai. (شجر طوبى).

_“… Paradise is for that person who meets him (al-Mahdi), and paradise is for to that person who loves him, and paradise is for that person who has belief in him (and his Imamate).”_

(Wasa’il ash-Shi’a, Vol 7, P-327, H-1)
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜
----------------------------------------------
*17th Shaban 1437, 25th May 2016, Wednesday,
🔸🔸🔸🔸🔸🔸🔸🔸🔸🔸

BAZM-E-ADAB WELCOMES YOU*
***********************************
           ♦ _*AAMAAL*_ ♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (304)

*بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ*

*يَوْمَ تَجِدُ كُلُّ نَفْسٍ مَا عَمِلَتْ مِنْ خَيْرٍ مُحْضَرًا وَمَا عَمِلَتْ مِنْ سُوءٍ تَوَدُّ لَوْ أَنَّ بَيْنَهَا وَبَيْنَهُ أَمَدًا بَعِيدًا ۗ وَيُحَذِّرُكُمُ اللَّهُ نَفْسَهُ ۗ وَاللَّهُ رَءُوفٌ بِالْعِبَادِ*

"Wo din ke jab har shakhs apne anjam diye hue nek kaam ko maujood payega aur khwahish karega (kash) uske aur uske bure Aamaal ke darmiyan zyada zamani fasla hota aur Khuda tumhe (apni nafarmani se) darata hai aur (iske bawajood) Allah tamam bando par Maherban hai."
(Surah Aal-e-Imran: 30)
📚📖
👉 _* Tafseer:*_
Ayat mein bataya gaya hai ke insaan ke Aamaal Qayamat ke din mujassam taur par uske samne dikhay denge.
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜
----------------------------------------------

_*MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!*_
🙇
Imam Sadiq (as):
_"Agar ek shakhs APNI POORI ZINDAGI raat bhar namaaz padhta hai aur din me roze rakhta hai TO BHI uske aamaal usay koi faayda NAHI pahunchayege AGAR WO APNI ZINDAGI KO Allah ke muqarrar kiye huwe Haadi (PAIGAMBER AUR IMAM) ki taalimaat aur hidaayat ke hisab se NAHI DHAALTA."_
(Agha Pooya Commentary, Surah A'araaf (7:6))
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜
_*AL MAHDI (atfs):*_ (14)

The Ornament of Paradise

قَالَ رَسُولُ اللٌّهِ : اَلْـمَهْدِيُّ طَاوُوْسُ أَهْلِ الْجَنَّةِ.
Rasoole Akram (sa):
_"Al-Mahdi Ahle Jannat ke Mor (Peacock) (zewar) hain."_

_“Al-Mahdi is the peacock [ornament] of the people of Paradise.”_

(Biharul Anwar, Vol 51, P-105; Tara’if)
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜

*18th Shaban 1437*, 26th May 2016, Thursday,
🔸🔸🔸🔸🔸🔸🔸🔸🔸🔸

BAZM-E-ADAB WELCOMES YOU*
***********************************
       ♦ _*MUHABBAT*_ ♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (305)

*بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ*

*قُلْ إِنْ كُنْتُمْ تُحِبُّونَ اللَّهَ فَاتَّبِعُونِي يُحْبِبْكُمُ اللَّهُ وَيَغْفِرْ لَكُمْ ذُنُوبَكُمْ ۗ وَاللَّهُ غَفُورٌ رَحِيمٌ*
*قُلْ أَطِيعُوا اللَّهَ وَالرَّسُولَ ۖ فَإِنْ تَوَلَّوْا فَإِنَّ اللَّهَ لَا يُحِبُّ الْكَافِرِينَ*

_"Kah dijiye! Agar Khuda ko dost rakhte ho to Meri pairavi karo taake Khuda bhi tumhe apna dost bana le aur tumhare gunah bakhsh de aur Khuda Bakhshnewala, Meherban hai."_

_"Kah dijiye! Khuda aur (uske) Rasool ki ita'at karo aur agar roogardani (turn away) karen to Khuda Kafiron ko dost nahi rakhta."_
(Surah Aal-e-Imran 31-32)

📚📖
👉 _* Tafseer:*_
Ayat ke mutabiq Muhabbat ek qalbi talluq hai. Jo Muhabbat ka dawa kare uska taqaza ye hai ke wo uski ita'at bhi kare. Haqeeqi Muhabbat insaan ko Mehboob aur uski khwahishat ki taraf khechti hai. Muhib o Mehboob ka talluq unke amal par asar andaz hota hai. To jahan Muhabbat hai wahan Deen hai. Deen Muhabbat ka doosra naam hai.
Rasool Khuda (as):
*هل الدين الا الحب؟*
_"Kiya Deen Muhabbat ke siwa kuchh hai?"_
Phir Rasool (sa) se doosri ayat mein Khitab hota hai:
*قُلْ لَا أَسْأَلُكُمْ عَلَيْهِ أَجْرًا إِلَّا الْمَوَدَّةَ فِي الْقُرْبَىٰ ۗ*
(Surah Ash-Shura: 23)
_"Kah do aye Rasool mein tumse koi ajre risalat nahi mangta siwa mere qarabatdaro (Ahle Bait as, Ale Imran) se Muhabbat karo."_
Natija ye nikla Allah, Rasool, Ahle Bait (as) se Muhabbat hi Deen hai. Inki ita'at wajib hai. Jis ne inse moo pher liya wo kafir hai, ayat ki roo se.
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜

----------------------------------------------
_*MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!*_
🙇
Imam Jafar Sadiq (as):
*ما احب الله من عصاه.*
_"Jo gunah karta hai wo Khuda ko dost nahi rakhta."_
Phir Imam ne ye mashhoor ashaar padhe:
*تعصى الا له و انت تظهر حبه*
             *هذا لعمرك فى الفعال بديع*
*لو كان حبك صادقالا طعته*
             *ان المحب لمن يحب مطيع*
_"Tu Khuda ki nafarmani karta hai aur iske bawajood Uski Muhabbat ka Izhar karta hai._
_Mujhe apni jaan ki qasam ye badi ajeeb o ghareeb baat hai._
_Agar teri Muhabbat sachchi hoti to tu Uski ita'at karta._
_Kiyonki jo kisi se Muhabbat karta hai wo uske hukm ki pairavi karta hai."_
(Ma'anil Akhbar)
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜
_*AL MAHDI (atfs):*_ (14)
Imam Ali (as):
_"Sabse behtareen ibaadat hai Sabr, Khamoshi aur Imam e Mahdi (atfs) ki aamad (zahoor) ka intezaar karna."_
(Islamic Morals)
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜
----------------------------------------------
*19th Shaban 1437*, 27th May 2016, Friday,
🔸🔸🔸🔸🔸🔸🔸🔸🔸🔸

BAZM-E-ADAB WELCOMES YOU*
***********************************
♦ _*ALE IBRAHIM & ALE IMRAN (as)*_♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (306)

*بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ*

*إِنَّ اللَّهَ اصْطَفَىٰ آدَمَ وَنُوحًا وَآلَ إِبْرَاهِيمَ وَآلَ عِمْرَانَ عَلَى الْعَالَمِينَ * ذُرِّيَّةً بَعْضُهَا مِنْ بَعْضٍ ۗ وَاللَّهُ سَمِيعٌ عَلِيمٌ*

_"Allah ne Adam (as), Nooh (as), Ale Ibrahim aur Ale Imran (as) ko sab jahano par muntakhab kar liya."_

_"Wo aise farzand (aur khandan) the jo (Pakeezgi, Taqwa aur Fazilat ke aitbar se) aise the ke baaz ko baaz mein intekhab kiya gaya aur Khuda Sunnewala aur Jannewala hai (aur apni risalat ki rah mein unki kavishon se bhi aagah hai.)"_
(Surah Aal-e-Imran: 33 - 34)

📚📖
👉 _* Tafseer:*_
Deen ka Rehbar sirf Allah hi muntakhab karta hai. Jo ke Masoom, Ilme Ghaib, Moa'jza jaise sifat rakhte hain. Agar bande apna Rehbar chune to wo in sifat ke hami na honge, isliye agar wo khata karenge to unke pairokar bhi khata karenge. Achhe aur bure ka Imtiyaz karna mushkil ho jayega.
Allah Ta'ala ne Anbiya ko muntakhab kiya aur unki Aal (children) mein se kuchh ko Chuna. Ale Ibrahim aur Ale Imran ka zikr hai. H Moosa (as) ke Walid ka naam Imran tha aur H Maryam (as) ke walid ka bhi. Yahan zikr H. Maryam ke Walid ka hai kiyonki iske baad unka zikr aya hai.
Aal آل aur اهل Ahl  mein farq hai. Ahl ke general meaning hain. Aulad ke liye bhi istemal hota hai aur qaum ya abadi ke liye bhi. Jaise ham kahte Ahle Madina means Madina wale. Ale Madina nahi kahte. Isliye Aal ka meaning sirf aulad ke liye makhsoos hai. Ham Ahle Bait kahte Ale Bait nahi. Kiyonki Ahle Bait (as) mein Rasool (sa) ki beti aur Janabe Abu Talib (as) ke bete shamil hain.
Allah ne na Ale Adam, na Ale Nooh ka zikr kiya. Allah ne sirf do Nabi ki Aal ka zikr kiya hai. H. Ibrahim (as) ki aulad mein do farzand H. Ishaq (as) aur H. Ismael (as). H. Ishaq (as) ki aulad se kai Anbiya (as) hue aur H. Ismail (as) se sirf ek Akhri Nabi H. Muhammad (sa).
Ayat mein Ale Imran ka bhi zikr hai. Janabe Maryam (sa) jo ke Masooma thi, unke Walid Imran, H. Esa (as) ke nana. H. Esa (as) H. Ishaq Ibne Ibrahim (as) ki nasl se Akhri Nabi. H. Muhammad (sa) H. Ismael (as) ki nasl se Akhri. Rasoole Akram (sa) ko Janabe Abu Talib (as) ne pala posa, jinka naam Imran tha. Yahan tak ke Rasoole Akram (sa) ka Nikah bhi Janabe Imran ne padha.
Dekha jaye to H. Ibrahim (as) nasl se Ale Imran common len to ek Ale Imran mein H. Esa  (as) to doosri taraf Ale Imran mein Janabe Abu Talib (as) ki aulad. Jo unki Aulad mein Ali (as) se Imam Mahdi (as) tak 12 Imam hain.
Allah ka bayan hai ke inko poori Alamin par chuna. Aur Allah ghair Masoom ko nahi chun sakta.
Isliye Sura Ale Imran, Ale Imran ki fazilat mein nazil hua.
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜
----------------------------------------------

_*MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!*_
🙇
_*AL MAHDI (atfs):*_ (16)
Brotherhood During the Imam’s Advent

*قَالَ الإِمَامُ مُحَمَّدُ بْنُ عَلِيٍّ البَاقِرُ :*
*... إِذَا قَامَ الْقَائِمُ جَـائَتِ الْمُزَامَلَةُ (الْمُزَايَلَةُ) وَ يَـأْتِي الرَّجُلُ إِلـى كِيسِ أَخِيهِ فَـيَأْخُذَ حَاجَتَهُ لاَ يَـمْـنَعُهُ!*

Imam Muhammad ibn ‘Ali al-Baqir (as):
_"Jab Al Qaim ka Zahoor hoga to dosti wa ittehad is tarah Qaim hoga ke ek shakhs apne brother e Imani ke jeb mein hath dalega aur jo chahega nikal lega baghair uski rukawat ke."_

_“ … When al-Qa’im makes his advent, at that time, friendship and unity will be established to such a degree that a person will be able to put his hand in his brother-in-faith’s pocket and take whatever he needs without his brother preventing him from doing so!”_

(Wasa’il ash-Shi’a, Vol 7, P-324, H-3)
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜
----------------------------------------------
23rd Shaban 1437, 31st May 2016, Tuesday,
🔹🔹🔹🔹🔹🔹🔹🔹🔹🔹

BAZM-E-ADAB CONGRATULATES WILADAT OF JANAB-ABU TALIB (as)*
🌹🌹🌹🌹🌹🌹🌹🌹🌹🌹
***********************************
       ♦ _*ALE IMRAN (as)*_ ♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (369)
🌻
*بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ*

*إِنَّ اللَّهَ اصْطَفَىٰ آدَمَ وَنُوحًا وَآلَ إِبْرَاهِيمَ وَآلَ عِمْرَانَ عَلَى الْعَالَمِينَ * ذُرِّيَّةً بَعْضُهَا مِنْ بَعْضٍ ۗ وَاللَّهُ سَمِيعٌ عَلِيمٌ*
🌻
_"Allah ne Adam (as), Nooh (as), Ale Ibrahim aur Ale Imran (as) ko sab jahano par muntakhab kar liya."_

_"Wo aise farzand (aur khandan) the jo (Pakeezgi, Taqwa aur Fazilat ke aitbar se) aise the ke baaz ko baaz mein intekhab kiya gaya aur Khuda Sunnewala aur Jannewala hai (aur apni risalat ki rah mein unki kavishon se bhi aagah hai.)"_
(Surah Aal-e-Imran: 33 - 34)

📚📖 🌻
👉 _* Tafseer:*_
Allah Ta'ala ne Anbiya ko muntakhab kiya aur unki Aal (children) mein se kuchh ko Chuna. Ale Ibrahim aur Ale Imran ka zikr hai. H Moosa (as) ke Walid ka naam Imran tha aur H Maryam (as) ke walid ka bhi. Janabe Abu Talib (as) ka asl naam bhi Imraan tha.
Majmaul Bayan wa Tafseer Ali ibne Ibrahim qummi mein marqoom hai ke _"qarate Ahle Bait (as) mein و ال محمد على العالمين ke alfaz se Marvi hai. Ale Ibrahim se murad Ale Muhammad (as) hain. Khuda ke muntakhab bande hain. Jise Khuda chun le woh Masoom hota hai, har burai se paak hota hai, kiyonki Khuda kisi badkar gunahgar ko muntakhab nahi karta. Khuda ke muntakhab bando ke liye zaroori hai ke woh Zahir wa Batin mein bhi Tayyab o Tahir hon."_
(Tafseer Noorus Saqlain)

Aal آل aur اهل Ahl  mein farq hai. Ahl ke general meaning hain. Aulad ke liye bhi istemal hota hai aur qaum ya abadi ke liye bhi. Jaise ham kahte Ahle Madina means Madina wale. Ale Madina nahi kahte. Isliye Aal ka meaning sirf aulad ke liye makhsoos hai. Ham Ahle Bait kahte Ale Bait nahi. Kiyonki Ahle Bait (as) mein Rasool (sa) ki beti aur Janabe Abu Talib (as) ke bete shamil hain.
Allah ne na Ale Adam, na Ale Nooh ka zikr kiya. Allah ne sirf do Nabi ki Aal ka zikr kiya hai. H. Ibrahim (as) ki aulad mein do farzand H. Ishaq (as) aur H. Ismael (as). H. Ishaq (as) ki aulad se kai Anbiya (as) hue aur H. Ismail (as) se sirf ek Akhri Nabi H. Muhammad (sa).
Ayat mein Ale Imran ka bhi zikr hai. H. Muhammad (sa) H. Ismael (as) ibne Ibrahim ki nasl se Akhri Nabi. Rasoole Akram (sa) ko Janabe Abu Talib (as) ne pala posa, Islam ke rah mein pura taoon kiya, jinka naam Imran tha. Yahan tak ke Rasoole Akram (sa) ka Nikah bhi Janabe Imran ne padha.
Dekha jaye to H. Ibrahim (as) nasl se Ale Imran common len to ek Ale Imran mein H. Esa  (as) to doosri taraf Ale Imran mein Janabe Abu Talib (as) ki aulad. Jo unki Aulad mein Ali (as) se Imam Mahdi (as) tak 12 Imam hain.
Isliye Sura Ale Imran, Ale Imran ki fazilat mein nazil hua.
Aaj Hazrat Ali (as) ke walid Janabe Imran (as) ki wiladat hai. Sabko Mubarak.
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜
----------------------------------------------

_*MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!*_
🙇 🌻
Riwayat:
Ek baar Jibreel (as) Rasule Khuda (saww) ki khidmat mein haazir huwe aur kaha, _"Ya Muhammad (saww)! Aap ka Parwardigaar tohfa e Durood o Salaam ke baad farmata hai ke As'haab e Kahf ne Imaan ko chhupaya aur shirk ka izhaar kiya is liye Khuda ne unko 2 baar Ajr o Sawaab ataa farmaya. Aur J. Abu Talib (as) ne bhi Imaan chhupa kar shirk ka izhaar kiya is liye Khuda ne aap ko 2 baar ajr ataa farmaya aur wo oos waqt tak duniya se nahi nikle jab tak allah ki taraf se unke liye jannat ki bashaarat nahi aayi"._
(Wasaail ush Shia, v11, p364)
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜

*29th Shawwal 1437, 3rd August 2016, Wednesday,

BAZM-E-ADAB WELCOMES YOU*
***********************************
♦ _*JANABE MARYAM (sa)*_♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (307)

*بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ*

*إِذْ قَالَتِ امْرَأَتُ عِمْرَانَ رَبِّ إِنِّي نَذَرْتُ لَكَ مَا فِي بَطْنِي مُحَرَّرًا فَتَقَبَّلْ مِنِّي ۖ إِنَّكَ أَنْتَ السَّمِيعُ الْعَلِيمُ*
*فَلَمَّا وَضَعَتْهَا قَالَتْ رَبِّ إِنِّي وَضَعْتُهَا أُنْثَىٰ وَاللَّهُ أَعْلَمُ بِمَا وَضَعَتْ وَلَيْسَ الذَّكَرُ كَالْأُنْثَىٰ ۖ وَإِنِّي سَمَّيْتُهَا مَرْيَمَ وَإِنِّي أُعِيذُهَا بِكَ وَذُرِّيَّتَهَا مِنَ الشَّيْطَانِ الرَّجِيمِ*

_"(Wo waqt yad karo) jab Imran ki biwi ne arz kiya: Khudawanda! Jo kuchh mere rahem mein hai mein use teri nazr karti hun taake woh (Tere Ghar ki khidmat ke liye) Muharrar (aur Azad) ho aur Tu ye mujh se qubool farma le ke Tu Sunnewala aur Jannewala hai."_

_"Lekin jab use janm diya (to dekha to wo ladki thi) arz kiya: Khudawanda! Meine ladki ko janm diya lekin Khuda isse aagah tha ke usne kiya janm diya hai (phir usne kaha) ladka ladki ki tarah nahi hota (aur ladki Ibaadatgah ki khidmat ki zimmedari ladke ki tarah anjam nahi de sakti) aur meine uska naam Maryam rakha hai. Use aur us ki aulad ko Shaitan Mardood (ke waswason) se Teri panah mein deti hun."_
(Surah Aal-e-Imran: 35 - 36)

📚📖
👉 _* Tafseer:*_
*"Wiladat of Janabe Maryam (sa):*
Rivayat ke mutabiq _Husna_ aur _Ashya_ do bahne (sisters) thi. Husna Imran ki zauja aur Ashya Hazrat Zakariya (as) ki zauja. Imran Bani Israel ki Important personality the. Chunke Imran ko wahi nazil hui ki unko ek babarkat ladka ata  kiya jayega. Jo Mareezon ko shifa dega, Murdon ko zinda karega, Paighambar hoga. Isliye Imran ki zauja ne nazr ki jo ladka hoga usko Baitul Muqaddas ki khidmat ke liye de diya jayega. Lekin unko ek ladki ka janm hua. Isliye Janabe Maryam ko Baitul Muqaddas mein chhod diya gaya. Wo Janabe Zakariya (as) ki nigrani mein rahi. Janabe Maryam Masoom thi unko Allah ki taraf se ghaza muhayya hoti thi.

Lekin Rasool Khuda (sa) ke zamane mein us waqt ke Imran ko jo beta hua wo direct Allah ke Ghar se namoodar hua. Jo jis sifat ka hamil tha wo misle Esa Ibne Maryam (as) tha. Wo the Ale Imran ki pahli kadi Ali (as) the.
(To be Cont'd ....)
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜
----------------------------------------------

_*MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!*_
🙇
_*AL MAHDI (atfs):*_ (17)
Perfection of the Intellect and Moral Traits

*قَالَ الإِمَامُ مُحَمَّدُ بْنُ عَلِيٍّ الْبَاقِرُ :*
*إِذَا قَامَ قَائِمُنَا وَضَعَ يَدَهُ عَلـى رُؤُوْسِ الْعِـبَادِ فَجَمَعَ بِهِ عُقُوْلَهُمْ وَ أَكْمَلَ بِهِ أَخْلاَقَهُمْ.*

Imam Muhammad Baqir (as):
_"Jab hamare Qaim ka Zahoor hoga, tab woh apne ghulamon ke saro par haath pherenge, to unki aqlen jama ho jayegi, aur unke Akhlaq mukammal ho jayenge."

_“When our Qa’im makes his advent, he will place his hand over the heads of the servants and their intellects will join together and their ethical traits will be perfected.”_

(Biharul Anwar, Vol 52, P-336, Kharaij of al-Rawandi)
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜

*24th Shaban 1437*, 1st June 2016, Wednesday,

BAZM-E-ADAB WELCOMES YOU*
***********************************
  ♦ _*JANABE MARYAM (sa)*_♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (308)

*بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ*

*فَتَقَبَّلَهَا رَبُّهَا بِقَبُولٍ حَسَنٍ وَأَنْبَتَهَا نَبَاتًا حَسَنًا وَكَفَّلَهَا زَكَرِيَّا ۖ كُلَّمَا دَخَلَ عَلَيْهَا زَكَرِيَّا الْمِحْرَابَ وَجَدَ عِنْدَهَا رِزْقًا ۖ قَالَ يَا مَرْيَمُ أَنَّىٰ لَكِ هَٰذَا ۖ قَالَتْ هُوَ مِنْ عِنْدِ اللَّهِ ۖ إِنَّ اللَّهَ يَرْزُقُ مَنْ يَشَاءُ بِغَيْرِ حِسَابٍ*

_"Uske Parwardegar ne usko (Maryam) khushi se qubool farma liya aur uske wujood (ke paude) ko khoob achhi tarah parwan charhaya. Zakariya ko unka kafil banaya. Jab Zakariya wahan dakhil hote to khas ghaza wahan maujood pate. Usse poochhte: 'ye kahan se layi ho?' Woh kahti: 'ye Khuda ki taraf se hai.' Khuda jise chahta hai be hisab rizq deta hai."_
(Surah Aal-e-Imran: 37)

📚📖
👉 _* Tafseer:*_
Imam Baqir (as):
"Ek roz Paighambar e Akram (sa) Janabe Fatema Zehra (sa) ke ghar tashreef laye. Haalat ye thi ke kai roz se unke haan theek se khana bhi mayassar na tha ke achanak Aap (sa) ne unke pas makhsoos ghaza dekhi to Aap (sa) ne poochha:
'Ye khana se aya hai?'
H. Fatema (sa) ne arz kiya:
'Khuda ke haan se, kiyonki wo jise chahta hai be hisab rizq deta hai.'
Ispar Paighambar Akram (sa) ne farmaya:
'Ye waqea to Hazrat Zakariya (as) ke waqea ki tarah hai, wo Janabe Maryam (sa) ke Mehrab ke pas aye the, wahan khane ki koi khas cheez dekhi to poochhne lage ye khana kahan se aya hai to unhone jawab mein kaha ke Khuda ke haan se aya hai."
(Tafseer Noorus Saqlain, Vol 1, Tafseer Ayyashi, Tafseer Namoona)

Dono Ale Imran mein ek hi shabahat hai. Maryam (sa) ke Ibaadat khane mein to Janabe Fatema (sa) ke ghar mein Khuda ki taraf se khane nazil hote the.
Qur'an ki har ayat Ahle Bait (as) ki fazilat mein hai.
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜
----------------------------------------------

_*MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!*_
🙇
_*AL MAHDI (atfs):*_ (18)

The Completion of Knowledge

*قَالَ الإِمَامُ جَعْفَرُ بْنُ مُحَمَّدٍ الصَّادِقُ : اَلْعِلْمُ سَبْعَةٌ وَ عِشْرُونَ حَرْفاً فَجَمِيعُ مَا جَــائَتْ بِهِ الرُّسُلُ حَرْفَانِ فَلَمْ يَعْرِفِ النَّاسُ حَتَّى الْيَوْمَ غَيْرَ الْحَرْفَينِ. فَإِذَا قَامَ قَائِمُنَا أَخْرَجَ الْخَمْسَةَ وَ الْعِشْـرِينَ حَرْفاً فَـبَثَّهَا فِي النَّاسِ وَ ضَمَّ إِلَيْهَا الْحَرْفَينِ حَتَّـى يَـبُثَّهَا سَبْعَةً وَ عِشْـرِينَ حَرْفاً.*

Imam Ja’far Sadiq (as):

_"Ilm 27 huroof (hisson) ka majmua hai. Har woh cheez jo (pichhle) Rasool laye wo in mein se sirf 2 harf the. Pas jab hamare Qaim Zahoor farmayenge to baqi 25 huroof bhi le ayenge and isko logon mein phaila denge aur pichhe 2 huroof ko bhi is mein is tarah mila denge jaise unhone (ilm ke) 27 huroof ko ata kiya."_

_“Knowledge is contained in twenty-seven letters (parts) and everything which all of the (previous) messengers brought was merely two of these letters and until the day (when al-Mahdi makes his advent), the people will not be given knowledge except of these two letters. So then when our Qa’im makes his advent, he will bring with him the other twenty-five letters (of knowledge) and he will spread these among the people and add these to the previous two letters (parts) such that he will have imparted the twenty-seven letters (of knowledge) to them.”_
(Wasa’il ash-Shi’a, Vol 7, P-326, H-10)
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜
----------------------------------------------
*25th Shaban 1437*, 2nd June 2016, Thursday,
🔹🔹🔹🔹🔹🔹🔹🔹🔹🔹

BAZM-E-ADAB WELCOMES YOU*
***********************************
       ♦ _*JANABE YAHYA (as)*_ ♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (309)

*بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ*

*هُنَالِكَ دَعَا زَكَرِيَّا رَبَّهُ ۖ قَالَ رَبِّ هَبْ لِي مِنْ لَدُنْكَ ذُرِّيَّةً طَيِّبَةً ۖ إِنَّكَ سَمِيعُ الدُّعَاءِ*
*فَنَادَتْهُ الْمَلَائِكَةُ وَهُوَ قَائِمٌ يُصَلِّي فِي الْمِحْرَابِ أَنَّ اللَّهَ يُبَشِّرُكَ بِيَحْيَىٰ مُصَدِّقًا بِكَلِمَةٍ مِنَ اللَّهِ وَسَيِّدًا وَحَصُورًا وَنَبِيًّا مِنَ الصَّالِحِينَ*

_"(Jab Maryam mein ye liyaqat o ahliyat dekhi) us waqt Zakariya ne apne Parwardegar se dua ki aur arz ki: Khudawanda! Apni taraf se mujhe (bhi) pakeeza farzand ata farma ke Tu Dua Sunnewala hai."_

_"Jab woh Mehrab mein Mashgoole Ibaadat the to Farishton ne use pukar kar kaha: Khuda tumhe Yahya ki basharat deta hai ke woh Khuda ke Kalme (Maseeh) ki tasdeeq karega, hawa o hawas se door hoga, Paighambar hoga aur Saleheen mein se hoga."_
(Surah Aal-e-Imran: 38 - 39)

📚📖
👉 _* Tafseer:*_
Yahan ayat ek lafz hai حصور jis ka root hai حصر jis se meaning nikalta hai محاصره Muhasera. Kuchh mufasserin ne iska meaning liya hai Shaadi na karna. Lekin Shaadi na karna ek to fitratan ghalat hai aur Deen ke mutabiq shaadi se adha Imaan mukammal hota hai. Isliye in matalib ke liye Aimma (as) ki zaroorat hai. Rivayat ke mutabiq is ka meaning hai ke woh is tarah apne aap ko muhasre mein rakhenge ke hawa o hawas se door rahenge. H Yahya (as) bhi H. Esa (as) ki tarah har waqt safar mein rahte isliye zyada tar mujarrad zindagi guzarni padi lekin aisa nahi hai ke unhone Shaadi nahi ki ho.
(To be Cont'd .... )
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜
----------------------------------------------

_*MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!*_
🙇
_*AL MAHDI (atfs):*_ (19)

No Oppression or Tyranny

*قَالَ الإِمَامُ عَلِيُّ بْنُ مُوسى الرِّضَا :*
*... فَإِذَا خَرَجَ أَشْرَقَتِ الأَرْضُ بِنُورِ رَبِّـهَا وَ وَضَعَ مِيزَانُ الْعَدْلِ بَيْنَ النَّاسِ فَلاَ يَظْلِمُ أَحَدٌ أَحَداً ...*

Imam Ali Raza (as):
_"Jab woh (Imam Mahdi (atfs)) Zahoor karenge, ye zameen apne Rab ke Noor se jagmaga uthegi aur aisa Insaaf ka tarazoo tainat kiya jayega koi bhi ek doosre par zulm nahi karega."_

_“ … So when he [Imam al-Mahdi] will make his advent, the Earth with radiate with the celestial illumination of its’ Lord and the scale of justice will be positioned among mankind such that not a single person will oppress another individual …”_
(Biharul Anwar, Vol 52, P-321; Kamal ad-Din)
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜

*26th Shaban 1437*, 3rd June 2016, Friday,

        ♦ _*JANABE YAHYA (as)*_ ♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (310)

*بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ*

*قَالَ رَبِّ أَنَّىٰ يَكُونُ لِي غُلَامٌ وَقَدْ بَلَغَنِيَ الْكِبَرُ وَامْرَأَتِي عَاقِرٌ ۖ قَالَ كَذَٰلِكَ اللَّهُ يَفْعَلُ مَا يَشَاءُ*

_"Us (Zakariya as) ne arz kiya: 'Mere haan ladka kaise ho sakta hai, jabke mujhe budhape ne aa liya hai aur meri biwi banjh hai.' Farmaya: 'Isi tarah Khuda jo kaam karna chahta hai anjam deta hai."_
(Surah Aal-e-Imran: 40)

📚📖
👉 _* Tafseer:*_
'Yahya' (يحيى) hayaat se akhaz kiya hai jis matlab hai zinda rahna. Esa (as) wa Yahya (as) dono ek hi sifat ke malik the. Dono Paighambar the. Beizne Khuda logon ko zindagi bakhshte the. Yehi sifat Imran ke bete H. Ali (as) mein bhi payi gayi.
Is mein shak nahi hona chahiye ke woh Paighambar hote hue Allah se aise sawal kiyon kiya. Ilm ke kai darje hote hain. H. Ibrahim (as) ya H. Zakariya (as) ek hi sawal ke Khuda ye sab kaise karta hai. Ek to ye ke woh logo ko Khuda ki Qudrat batana chahte the ya aisa karke wo Shuhood ki manzil hasil karte.
(To be Cont'd ..... )
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜
----------------------------------------------

_*MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!*_
🙇
Hazrat Ali (as):
*اذا كنت فی ادبارو الموت فی اقبال فما اسرع الملتقی.*
_"Chunke tum umr ke Akheri hisse ki taraf ja rahe ho aur Maut tumhari taraf badh rahi hai."_
(Nahjul Balagha, Hikmat 28)
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜
_*AL MAHDI (atfs):*_ (20)
A Servant of the Imam for Life

*قَالَ الإِمَامُ مُحَمَّدُ بْنُ عَلِيٍّ البَاقِرُ : ... إِنِّـي لَوْ أَدْرَكْتُ ذٌلِكَ لأَََبْقَيْتُ نَفْسِيْ لِصَاحِبِ هٌذَا الأَمْرِ.*

Imam Muhammad Baqir (as):
_"Yaqeenan! Agar mein (Zahoor e Imam Mahdi) ka zamana dekh paon, to mein apne aap ko (zindagi bhar) is Sahabe Amr ki khidmat mein laga dunga."_

_“ … Indeed if I were to live to see that (the advent of Imam al-Mahdi), then I would have availed myself to serve the Sahib al-Amr (for life).”_

(Biharul Anwar, Vol 52, P-234; al-Ghaybah of al-Nu’mani)
