BAZM-E-ADAB WELCOMES YOU*
***********************************
   ♦ _*JANABE ZAKARIYA (as)*_ ♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (311)

*بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ*

*قَالَ رَبِّ اجْعَلْ لِي آيَةً ۖ قَالَ آيَتُكَ أَلَّا تُكَلِّمَ النَّاسَ ثَلَاثَةَ أَيَّامٍ إِلَّا رَمْزًا ۗ وَاذْكُرْ رَبَّكَ كَثِيرًا وَسَبِّحْ بِالْعَشِيِّ وَالْإِبْكَارِ*

_"(Hazrat Zakariya (as) ne) arz kiya: Parwardegar! Mere liye koi nishani muqarrar farma. (Khuda ne) kaha: 'Tumhare liye ye nishani hai ke tum teen din tak logon se ishare se guftugu (talk) kar sakoge (aur tumhari zaban baghair kisi zaheri sabab ke logo se baat nahi kar payegi) aur (is azeem ne'mat par shukrane ke taur par) apne Parwardegar ko bahut yad karo aur subah o shaam uski tasbeeh karo."_
(Surah Aal-e-Imran: 41)

📚📖
👉 _* Tafseer:*_
Janabe Zakariya (as) ne jab Allah se nishani maangi to Allah ne 3 din ki Ibaadat baghair kisi se kalam kiye ada karne ka mauqa enayat farmaya. عشی means din ke Akheri lamhat yani Zuhr, إبکار means din ke shuruati lamhat yani Fajr. Ye Ibaadat unko gift mein di gayi.
Lekin Hamare Rasool (sa) logon se door Ghare Hira mein jakar Ibaadat kiya karte apni marzi se. Itni ibaadat ki ke Khuda ko unka ye amal bahut pasand aya balke unki ibaadat ko kam karne ke liye kaha. Imam Sajjad (as) ne dua o Ibaadat ke zariye hi Tableegh ki. Ye the Ale Imraan.
(To be cont'd .....)
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜
----------------------------------------------

_*MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!*_
🙇
_*AL MAHDI (atfs):*_ (21)
Awaiting the Advent

*قَالَ رَسُولُ اللٌّهِ : اِنْتِظَارُ الْفَرَجِ بِالصَّبْرِ عِبَادَةٌ.*
Rasoole Khuda (sa):
"Intezare Faraj (Mahdi: Solution of all problem) Sabr ke sath ek Ibaadat hai."

The Messenger of Allah (sa):
_“Awaiting the Faraj (relief from all problem) with patience is (a form of) worship.”_

(Biharul Anwar, Vol 52, P-145; Da’wat of Rawandi)
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜

*28th Shaban 1437*, 5th June 2016, Sunday,

*BAZM-E-ADAB WELCOMES YOU*
***********************************
       ♦ _*JANABE MARYAM (sa)*_ ♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (312)

*بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ*

*وَإِذْ قَالَتِ الْمَلَائِكَةُ يَا مَرْيَمُ إِنَّ اللَّهَ اصْطَفَاكِ وَطَهَّرَكِ وَاصْطَفَاكِ عَلَىٰ نِسَاءِ الْعَالَمِينَ * يَا مَرْيَمُ اقْنُتِي لِرَبِّكِ وَاسْجُدِي وَارْكَعِي مَعَ الرَّاكِعِينَ*

_"Aur (wo waqt yad karo) jab Farishton ne kaha: 'Aye Maryam! Khuda ne tumko Chuna, Pak kiya aur tamam jahan ki aurton par bartari aur Fazilat di."_

_"Aye Maryam! (is ne'mat ke shukrane ke taur par) apne Parwardegar ke samne khuzu (humble) karo, Sajda baja lao aur rukoo karne salon ke sath rukoo karo."_
(Surah Aal-e-Imran: 42 - 43)

📚📖
👉 _* Tafseer:*_
Is ayat mein Janabe Maryam (sa) ki Fazilat ko bayan kiya hai. H. Esa (as) ki madare girami sab aurton ki Sardar hain. Lekin jo Sardar e Anbiya (sa) ne hame bataya unse bhi badh Sayadatun nisail Alemin (Chief of all women) Janabe Fatema Zahra (sa) hai.
Rasoole Khuda (sa) ne farmaya:
"Fatema (sa) tamam aurton ki Sardar siwai Maryam ki."
(Sunni Book: Fathul Bari, Vol. 8, P-474)

"Ye manna ke Fatema (sa) Janabe Maryam se Afzal hain: Abu Jafar (as) ka aur sabhi Imam ka ye manna hai. Is baat ki Tasdeeq ho chuki hai ke Fatema Zehra (sa) tamam bichhli aur aane wali aurton se bartar hain, kiyonki woh Rasoole Khuda (sa) ka ek hissa hain, aur doosre asbab ki wajah se, woh is wajah se bhi afzal hain kiyonki wohi sababe khilqat e kaynat hain, kiyonki Rasoole Khuda (sa) ka kisi se ma'azena (compare) nahi kiya ja sakta."
(Ruhul Ma'ani, Vol.3, P-155)

Zakariya Ibne Zahid ne Feras se, unhone Al Shobi se, unhone Masrooq se, unhone Aisha se rivayat bayan ki:
Rasoole Khuda (sa) ne apne Akheri lamhat mein farmaya:
"Aye Fatema! Kiya tum is baat se khush nahi ke tum Alemin ki aurton ki Sardar ho, is Ummat ki aurton ki sardar, tamam mo'menat ki Sardar?!
(Al Hakim: ye sahih hadis hai, Bukhari & Muslim ne bhi is ko naql kiya hai.)
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜
----------------------------------------------

_*MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!*_
🙇
_*AL MAHDI (atfs):*_ (22)
_Last Hadis of this series:_

Traits of Those in Waiting for the Imam

*قَالَ الإِمَامُ جَعْفَرُ بْنُ مُحَمَّدٍ الصَّادِقُ : مَنْ سَرَّهُ أَنْ يَكُونَ مِنْ أَصْحَابِ الْقَائِمِ فَلْيَنْـتَظِرْ وَ لْيَعْمَلْ بِالْوَرَعِ وَ مَحَاسِنِ الأَخْلاَقِ وَ هُوَ مُنْـتَظِرٌ. فَإِنْ مَاتَ وَ قَامَ الْقَائِمُ بَعْدَهُ كَانَ لَهُ مِنَ الأَجْرِ مِثْلُ أَجْرِ مَنْ أَدْرَكَهُ.*

Imam Ja’far Sadiq (as):
_"Jo Shakhs chahta ke woh Al-Qaim ke ashab mein shumar ho usko chahiye ke woh Intezar kare, Wara (Taqwe se upar ka level) ke sath amal kare, Mohasine Akhlaq ho, to woh Muntazir mein shumar hoga. Aur agar woh shakhs Qaim ke Zahoor se pahle mar gaya to usko waisa hi ajr milega jaise woh Zahoor ke waqt Hazrat ko dark karta."_

_“A person who would like to be among the companions of al-Qa’im should be in a state of (active) waiting (Intizar), and perform all of his deeds with Wara’ [a level higher than Taqwa] and with the most beautiful etiquette and then one will be counted as being in a state of (true) waiting(Intizar). Then if such a person was to die and al-Qa’im was to make his advent after this, then that person would receive the reward as the one who witnessed his (al-Mahdi’s) advent.”_

(Biharul Anwar, Vol 52, P-140; al-Ghaybah of al-Nu’mani)
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜
----------------------------------------------
*29th Shaban 1437*, 6th June 2016, Monday,

BAZM-E-ADAB WELCOMES YOU*

Note: Ham Qur'an ki Tafseer ka silsela wahi se wapas shuru kar rahe hai jo Ramzan se pahle chal raha tha.
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜
♦ _*Qara' Andazi - Drawing a Lot*_ ♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (343)

*بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ*

*ذَٰلِكَ مِنْ أَنْبَاءِ الْغَيْبِ نُوحِيهِ إِلَيْكَ ۚ وَمَا كُنْتَ لَدَيْهِمْ إِذْ يُلْقُونَ أَقْلَامَهُمْ أَيُّهُمْ يَكْفُلُ مَرْيَمَ وَمَا كُنْتَ لَدَيْهِمْ إِذْ يَخْتَصِمُونَ*

_"Ye ghaib ki khabaren hain jo Ham tumhe wah ke zariye bata rahe hain aur jab woh apni qalmen (qara' andazi ke liye pani mein) phek rahe the ke Maryam ki kifalat aur sarparasti kaun kare aur us waqt (bhi) jab uski sarparasti ka iftekhar aur mansab hasil karne ke liye (Ulema) apas mein masroofe kashmakash the, tum maujood na the (aur ye sab baten tumhe wah ki marefat batayi gayi hain.)"_
(Surah Aal-e-Imran: 44)

📚📖
👉 _* Tafseer:*_

Jaisa ke ham pahle bata chuke hain Janabe Imran ne ye mannat mani thi ke jo pachcha paida hoga to usko Baitul Muqaddas ke hawale kar diya jayega lekin jo bachcha paida hua woh ladki thi aur Janabe Imran apni mannat par qayem rahe, lekin mushkil ye pesh ayi ke iski kifalat wo sarparasti kaun karega. To ye faisla kiya gaya ke wahan ke Ulema ke darmiyan qara' andazi (lot) ke zariye chunao ho. Isliye unhone naam likh kar qalmen pani mein dali aur ye tai hua ke  sab qalam pani mein doob jayengi aur jo qalam pani par tairegi usko select kiya jayega. Is tarah se Janabe Zakariya (as) ka naam select hua.
Is waqea se ye pata chalta hai Qara' andazi (taking a lot) ek deeni tareeqa hai jisko Allah ne Qur'an mein saraha hai. Lekin ye tareeqa mushkil waqt mein hi istemal kiya ja sakta hai jab log mutazabzib hon aur faisla lene se qasir hon. Business ya apne kisi kaam ke liye jis mein income ka zariya ho ye theek nahi.
Hamne tarikh mein ye bhi dekha ke Musalman jo apne Khalifa chunne ke liye pareshan tha usne ye bhi tareeqa istemal nahi kiya nahi to iske sahi hone ka jawaz mil jata. Lekin Jab jab Khalifa ko Allah ne chin liya ho to phir koi pareshani ki baat nahi.
Aajkal ye sahi tareeqa sabhi log is tarah istemal karte hai: Jaise kisi ko Hajj o Ziyarat ko bhejne ke liye, ya kisi ko inaam dene ke liye, jo ke Ramazan mein hamne zyada tar dekha. Ikhtelaf door karne ke liye ye tareeqa sahi hai.
Aise mushkelat bhi hal kiye jate hain jaisa ke ahadis mein aya hai: e.g.
Agar koi kisi bhed (sheep or goat) se bad fe'li kare aur phir use bakriyon ke revad mein chhod de. To agar use pahchana na ja sake to Qara' andazi ke zariye in mein se ek bhed nikal li jaye aur uska gosht khane se parhez kiya jaye kiyonki sare revad ko chhod dena to bade nuqsan ka baes banega aur phir un sab ka gosht khana bhi jaez nahi - yahan Qara' is mushkil ka hal hai.
(Tafseer e Namoona)
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜
----------------------------------------------

_*MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!*_
🙇 💰
Qara' Andazi aur Lottery mein farq hai: Qara' Andazi mushkelat ke Hal ke liye jaez hai, lekin Lottery jo income ke liye ho haram hai.

Imam Muhammad al-Baqir (a.s.):
_"Har tarah ke betting wale khel ya uske alalat ki kharid o furokht Haram hai. Ye amale Shaitan hai jo tumhe uksata hai."_

_“All kinds of games of betting are gambling and the sale, the purchase and the use of all the tools of gambling are Harām. It is only an act that Shaitan instigates you to do.”_
(Tafseer Al Qummi)

*Ahkam Ay. Al Sistani (DZ):*
Q: I work at an exchange office but they also make me sell lottery. Is it permitted to sell lottery in this case?

Ans: Buying and selling lottery tickets are not permissible. Yes, it is permissible to take part in a lottery with the intention to contribute in a charitable project such as building a mosque or a bridge not with the intention of earning a profit or a prize.
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜
----------------------------------------------
*3rd Shawwal 1437*, 8th July 2016, Friday,
🔸🔸🔸🔸🔸🔸🔸🔸🔸🔸

BAZM-E-ADAB WELCOMES YOU*

  ♦ _*ESA: KALMA-E-KHUDA*_ ♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (344)

*بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ*

*إِذْ قَالَتِ الْمَلَائِكَةُ يَا مَرْيَمُ إِنَّ اللَّهَ يُبَشِّرُكِ بِكَلِمَةٍ مِنْهُ اسْمُهُ الْمَسِيحُ عِيسَى ابْنُ مَرْيَمَ وَجِيهًا فِي الدُّنْيَا وَالْآخِرَةِ وَمِنَ الْمُقَرَّبِينَ*

_"Woh waqt (yaad karo) jab Farishton ne kaha: Aye Maryam! Khuda apni taraf se tumhe ek KALMA (aur ba azmat shakhsiyat) ki basharat deta hai jis ka naam Eisa bin Maryam hai, woh Duniya o Akherat mein maqam o Azmat ka malik hoga aur woh muqarrabin mein se hai."_
(Surah Aal-e-Imran: 45)

📚📖
👉 _* Tafseer:*_
Ye ayat Hazrat Eisa (as) ki wiladat ka tazkara kar rahi hai jo ham pahle bayan kar chuke hain.
*Hazrat Eisa (as) ko Kalma kiyon kaha gaya?*
Bibile mein Jesus Christ ko Word of God kaha gaya hai.
Iski bahut si wajah ho sakti hain. Unki ghair mamooli wiladat, ya Khuda ne unki waldah ko ek Kalam ke zariye basharat di, ya ye ke Qur'an mein Kalma se murad Makhlooqe Khuda hai aur H. Esa (as) Khuda ki azeem makhlooqat mein se hain.
*Maseeh kiyon kahte hai?*
Maseeh means Masah مسح karne wala ya Mash shudah means Touch karnewala. Hazrat Esa (as) naqabile ilaaj bimaron ke badan par hath pher kar Hukm e Khuda se use shifayab karne se pahle hi unka naam Maseeh rakh diya gaya. Ya is wajah se Allah ne unhe har napaki aur gunah se masah yani pak rakha.
*Son of God:*
Is ayat mein Allah ne clearly Hazrat Esa ko Maryam ka beta bataya jo ke Christian ke liye jawab hai. Jo ek maa se paida hua ho woh Khuda kaise ho sakta hai.
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜
----------------------------------------------

_*MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!*_
🙇
Imam Sadiq (as):
_"Jo shakhs khuluus se LA ILAHA ILLALAH kahe wo Jannat mein jayega. Khuluus ye hota hai ke ye kalma kehna usay Allah (swt) ki haraam ki huwi cheezo'n se baaz rakhe."_
(Meezan ul Hikmah, v2)

Hazrat Isa (as):
_"Jis tarah ek mareez Khaane ko dekhta hai lekin dard ki shiddat mein oos se lazzat nahi utha sakta, oosi tarah duniya-daar aadmi MAAL KI MOHABBAT ki wajah se Na to Ibaadat ki lazzat utha sakta hai aur Na hi uski mithaas se lutf le sakta hai."_
(Meezan ul Hikmah, v6)
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜

*4th Shawwal 1437*, 9th July 2016, Saturday,

BAZM-E-ADAB WELCOMES YOU*

      ♦ _*BACHPAN SE REHBARI*_ ♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (345)

*بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ*

*وَيُكَلِّمُ النَّاسَ فِي الْمَهْدِ وَكَهْلًا وَمِنَ الصَّالِحِينَ*

_"Aur woh (Hazrat Esa (as)) logon se gahware mein aur adhed umr mein guftugu karega aur woh Saleheen mein se hain."_
(Surah Aal-e-Imran: 46)

📚📖
👉 _* Tafseer:*_
Imam Baqir (as) farmate hain:
"Rehbar ke liye age ya umr ki koi qaid nahi hoti woh chahe Nabi, Rasool ya Imam ho." Hazrat Esa (as) paida  hote hi ne apni waleda ki pakeezgi sabit karne ke liye gahware (cradle) se gawahi di. Jab 2 saal ke the unko Nabuwwat o Risalat aur Kitab o Shariat mili. Hazrat Yahya bhi bachpan se Nabi the.
(Al Hidayatul Kubra, P-360)
Usi tarah Hazrat Ali (as) ne paida hoti hi Pura Qur'an aur sari asmaani Kitaben Sunai.
Imam Ali Naqi (as) aur Imam Mahdi (as) ne 5 saal ki umr mein Imamat shuru ki.
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜

_*MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!*_
🙇
Imam Sadiq (as):
_"Ek martaba H. Isa (as) ne H. Yahya (as) ki qabr pe aakar unko zinda kiya aur kaha ke 'Main chaahta hoon ke tum Tableegh mein meri madad karo'. H. Yahya (as) ne jawab diya 'Jaa'n kani (Dum nikalne) ki shiddat aur takleef main ABHI TAK NAHI bhoola. Tum mujhe phir oosi takleef mein mubtela karna chaahte ho?'"_
(Roohul Hayaat)

♦ _*WILADAT WITHOUT PREGNANCY*_

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (346)

*بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ*

*قَالَتْ رَبِّ أَنَّىٰ يَكُونُ لِي وَلَدٌ وَلَمْ يَمْسَسْنِي بَشَرٌ ۖ قَالَ كَذَٰلِكِ اللَّهُ يَخْلُقُ مَا يَشَاءُ ۚ إِذَا قَضَىٰ أَمْرًا فَإِنَّمَا يَقُولُ لَهُ كُنْ فَيَكُونُ*

_"(Maryam ne) kaha: Parwardegar! Mujh se bachcha kiyonkar hoga jabke kisi shakhs ne mujhe chhua tak nahi. (Jawab me) farmaya: Khuda usi tarah jise chahta hai paida karta hai, jab woh kisi cheez ka faisla kar leta hai to bas kahta hai ho ja to wo ho jati hai."_
(Surah Aal-e-Imran: 47)

📚📖
👉 _* Tafseer:*_
Allah jo karna chahta hai to sirf 'kun fa ya koon' se ho jata hai. Uske liye kisi process ki zaroorat nahi. Isliye Janabe Maryam ko jab tajjub hua to ye sawal kiya aur Khuda ne jawab diya. Khuda ke Qudrat ka koi andaza nahi laga sakta.

Abu Abullah (as):
_"Beshak, Janabe Maryam ne H. Esa (as) ko 9 ghante hamal mein rakha, har ek ghanta ek mahine ke barabar tha."_
(Kafi, Vol 8, P-332, 516)

Abu Muhammad al-Hasan ibn-‘Ali al-Thani (the second) said:
_“Al-Husain was born in al-Madina Tuesday, five days before Jamadi al-’Ula, three years after al-Hijrah. His mother became pregnant with al-Husain fifteen nights after his birthday and she was pregnant during six months and then she bore him. And no baby was born in six months exept him and Jesus the son of Mary."_
(Dala'il Al Imama, 71)
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜
----------------------------------------------

_*MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!*_
🙇
Hazrat Isa (as):
_"Kitne chiraag aise hain jinhe aandhiyo'n ne gul kar diya hai aur kitne Ibaadat-guzaar aise hain jinhe KHUD-PASANDI ne barbaad kar dala hai."_
(Meezan ul Hikmah, v6)

    ♦ _*MOAJZA - MIRACLE*_ ♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (347)

*بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ*

*وَرَسُولًا إِلَىٰ بَنِي إِسْرَائِيلَ أَنِّي قَدْ جِئْتُكُمْ بِآيَةٍ مِنْ رَبِّكُمْ ۖ أَنِّي أَخْلُقُ لَكُمْ مِنَ الطِّينِ كَهَيْئَةِ الطَّيْرِ فَأَنْفُخُ فِيهِ فَيَكُونُ طَيْرًا بِإِذْنِ اللَّهِ ۖ وَأُبْرِئُ الْأَكْمَهَ وَالْأَبْرَصَ وَأُحْيِي الْمَوْتَىٰ بِإِذْنِ اللَّهِ ۖ وَأُنَبِّئُكُمْ بِمَا تَأْكُلُونَ وَمَا تَدَّخِرُونَ فِي بُيُوتِكُمْ ۚ إِنَّ فِي ذَٰلِكَ لَآيَةً لَكُمْ إِنْ كُنْتُمْ مُؤْمِنِينَ*

_"Aur use (Hazrat Esa (as) ko) Rasool ki hasiyat se Bani Israel ki taraf bhejega (jo unse kahega:) 'Mein Parwardegar ki taraf se tumhare liye nishaniyan laya hun. Mein geeli mitti se parinde jaisi moorat banata hun. Phir us mein phookta hun to woh hukm-e-Khuda se parinda ban jata hai. Nez madar zad andhe ko aur baras mein mubtela logo ko shifa deta hun, murdon ko zinda karta hun aur jo kuchh tum khate ho aur apne gharon mein zakheera karte ho, uski tumhen khabar deta hun. Beshak is mein tumhare liye nishani hai agar tum imaan rakhte ho."_
(Surah Aal-e-Imran: 49)

📚📖
👉 _* Tafseer:*_
Har Nabi apne Sath ek Moajza rakhta tha. Ye Nabi ki Nubawwat ko sabit karne ka ek zariya hai.
Imam Ali Reza (as):
"Hazrat Musa (as) ke zamane mein Jadoogar bahut the. Hazrat Musa (as) ne aisa amal anjam diya jiske muqable mein tamam Jadoogar aajiz aa gaye. Hazrat Maseeh (as) ke zamane aur dawat ke mauqe par atba (Doctors) bimaron ke ilaaj mualeje (treatment) mein bahut maharat rakhte the. Janabe Esa (as) ne la ilaaj bimaron ko maaddi wasail ke baghair Shifa dekar apni Haqqaniyat ko sabit kar diya. Paighambar e Islam (sa) ke zamane mein Khutaba, shu'ara aur sukhanwar bahut zyada fasahat o balaghat ke malik the aur un sab ne Qur'ani fasahat o balaghat ke samne ghutne tek diye."
(Bihar, Vol 5, P-19)

Allah har cheez par Qudrat rakhta hai lekin Allah ke har kaam wasilon wa zarae se hote hain. Jaise Uske hukm se Malaeka kaam karte hain jabke Woh khud bhi kar sakta hai lekin Khuda ki Azmat o Buzurgi is mein mein ke Usne Apne kaam ke liye Malaeka ko khalq kiya. To same ikhtiyar Allah apne Auliya, Paighambar wo Imam ko bhi de deta hai. Kar Khuda ki Qudrat se raha hai, kah raha hai mein kar raha hun. To ye shirk nahi. Isi Ayat se sabit hai. To Hazrat Ali (as) murdon ko zinda kar den to tajjub ki kiya baat hai kiyonki ke woh Vali e Khuda the. Imam Sher ke photo ko zinda sher bana den. Imam aasmaan ki taraf hath phailayen to barish hone lage. Jo bhi Moajza dikhata hai wo باذن الله (Khuda ki ijazat se) hota hai. Ise _*'Vilayat-e-Takveeni'*_ kahte hain. Yani Anbiya aur Aimma (as) zaroorat ke waqt izne Parwardegar se Alam e Khilqat mein tasarrufat kar sakte hai aur ye Vilayate Tashreei yani awam par hukumat, qawaneen ki nashro ishaat aur direct Dawat o Hidayat se balatar hai.
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜
----------------------------------------------

_*MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!*_
🙇
Imam Husain (as):
_"Hazrat Isa (as) ko sirf Bani Israil ka Nabi bana kar bheja gaya tha aur unki Nabuwwat Baitul Muqaddas tak mehdood (limited) thi."_
(Tafseer Noor us Saqlain, v2, p86)
Sab Anbiya ka area limited tha lekin hamare Rasool (sa) pure Alemin ke liye aye.

Imam Sadiq (as)
_se puchha gaya, "Aakhir kya wajah hai ke Esa (as) ke as'haab (hawaari) paani ke upar chala karte the jab ke as'haab e Muhammad (saww) mein aisi koi baat nahi hai?" Aap ne farmaya, "Is liye ke as'haab e Esa (as) ko rozgaar kamane ki fikr nahi thi, jab ke as'haab e Muhammad (saww) rozgaar ki fikr mein hamesha pareshaan rehte the."_
(Meezan ul Hikmah, v8, p633)

           ♦ _*SHARIYAT*_ ♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (348)

*بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ*

*وَمُصَدِّقًا لِمَا بَيْنَ يَدَيَّ مِنَ التَّوْرَاةِ وَلِأُحِلَّ لَكُمْ بَعْضَ الَّذِي حُرِّمَ عَلَيْكُمْ ۚ وَجِئْتُكُمْ بِآيَةٍ مِنْ رَبِّكُمْ فَاتَّقُوا اللَّهَ وَأَطِيعُونِ*

_"(Hazrat Esa (as) farmate hai:) Aur mein Tasdeeq karta hun aur gawahi deta hun uski jo Taurait mein se mujhe se pahle tha aur (mein aya hun taake) baaz cheezen jo (zulm o gunah ki wajah se) tum par haram the (jaise baaz chaupahe (cattles) ka gosht aur machhliyan) unhe halal karun aur tumhare Parwardegar ki taraf se tumhare liye nishani laya hun. Isliye ke tum Khuda

se daro aur meri ita'at karo."_
(Surah Aal-e-Imran: 50)

📚📖
👉 _* Tafseer:*_

Uolul Azm Paighambar jo aye nai shariyat le kar aye, jisse pichhli shariyat mansookh (cancel) ho jati thi. Shariyat ka badalne ki bahut si wujuhat hain. Ek ye ke phichhli shariyat log bhol gaye ya logon ne badal di, ya ye ke waqt aur zamane ke mutabiq shariyat hoti hai. Ye aisa nahi hai ke pichhli shariyat mein koi nuqs tha. Ya aisa nahi kuchh correction ke sath naya version ho.
Allah ne Musa (as) ke pairokar yani Bani Israel ke zulm o gunah ki wajah se qanoon o shariyat sakht thi. Unki shariyat mein Unt (Cemal) ka gosht ya kuchh ki charbiyan, kuchh parinde Haram the. Jiska Ayat (4:160) mein zikr hai. Lekin H. Esa (as) ke soft rule rahe. Jo pabandiya Bani Israel par lago thi wo hata di gayi. Ahm baat ye ke Paighambar jo bhi shariyat laye usko follow karna, taake Taqwa ikhtiyar karen. Akheri Shariyat hamare Rasool (sa) ke liye ayi jo taa Qayamat lagu rahegi kiyonki woh Akheri Nabi hain.
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜
----------------------------------------------

_*MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!*_
🙇 🏴🏴🏴🏴🏴🏴🏴🏴🏴
Aaj yaume gham, aaj ke din Janabe Zehra ki Qabr Ale Saud Maloon ne mismar kar di.
Imam Husain (as):
"Jab Hazrat Sayyeda (sa) ki wafat hui to Amirul Mo'menin (as) ne unhe raat ke waqt khamoshi se dafn kar diya aur unki qabr ka nishan mita diya. Phir khade hokar unhone Qabre Rasool (sa) ki taraf rukh karke kaha:
_"Ya Rasoolallah! Aap par meri taraf se Salam ho aur aap ki us beti ki taraf se bhi Salam ho jo abhi aa kar aap ki zaer bani hai aur jo aap ki sarzameen mein dafan hui hai. Jisne aap se jaldi milne ko tarjeeh di hai. Ya Rasoolullah! Aap ki sufiya beti ke gham mein mera sabr qaleel ho chuka hai aur meri tamam tar bahaduri Sayyadatun Nisail Aalameen ke gham mein aa kar jawab de chuki hai."_
(Noorus Saqlain, Ale Imran: P-75)

Aur woh aaj bhi Mazlooma hain, aaj bhi unki qabr par saya nahi.
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜

          ♦ _*HAZRAT ESA (as):♦*_
     ♦ _*Khuda ke Bande hain*_ ♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (349)

*بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ*

*إِنَّ اللَّهَ رَبِّي وَرَبُّكُمْ فَاعْبُدُوهُ ۗ هَٰذَا صِرَاطٌ مُسْتَقِيمٌ*

_"Khuda mera aur tumhara Parwardegar hai pas usi ki Ibaadat karo (na ke meri ya kisi aur cheez ki) yehi seedhi rah hai."_
(Surah Aal-e-Imran: 51)

📚📖
👉 _* Tafseer:*_
Is Ayat mein un logon ki aqeedon ki nafi ki gayi hai jo Hazrat Esa (as) ko Khuda ya Uska ka beta samajhte hain (Jesus the Son of God), jais Nasrani, Christian. Hazrat Esa (as) Khuda ke bande hain aur Khuda ki Ibaadat karte hain. Ye logon ki fitrat hai ke jisko zyada fazilat ka malik dekhte hain hai usko apna Bhagwan, God, Khuda manne lagte hain. Hazrat Esa (as) ki tarah jab logon ne  Hazrat Ali (as) ko murdon ko zinda karte dekha to Nusairiyon ne unko Khuda bana diya. Jiski Imam ne khuda tardeed ki aur dikhaya ke mein khud Us Khuda ki Ibaadat karta hun.

Rasule Khuda (saww)
ne H. Ali (as) se farmaya: _"Tum mein Isa (as) ki shabaahat (samaanta / similarity) paayi jaati hai. Agar mujhe ye andesha na hota ke log tumhare baare mein wo baatein na karne lag jaayein jo ke Nasara e Isa (as) ke mutalliq kahi thi to main tumhare itne fazaael bayaan karta ke tum jahaa'n se bhi guzarte log tumhare qadmo'n ki mitti ko mutabarrik samajh kar uthha lete."_
(Tafseer Noor us Saqlain, v7, p553)
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜
----------------------------------------------

_*MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!*_
🙇
Imam Ali (as):
_"6 Paigambaro'n ke 2 naam hain:
_(1) H. Yusha bin Noon (as) ya Zulkifl,_
_(2) H. Yaqoob (as) ya Israel,_
_(3) H. Khizr (as) ya Hilqqiya,_
_(4) H. Yunus (as) ya Zun Noon,_
_(5) H. Isa (as) ya Maseeh,_
_(6) H. Muhammad (saww) ya Ahmed (saww)."_
(Khisaal, ch6)
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜

*9th Shawwal 1437*, 14th July 2016, Thursday,

♦ _*HAWARI - DISCIPLES*_ ♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (350)

*بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ*

*فَلَمَّا أَحَسَّ عِيسَىٰ مِنْهُمُ الْكُفْرَ قَالَ مَنْ أَنْصَارِي إِلَى اللَّهِ ۖ قَالَ الْحَوَارِيُّونَ نَحْنُ أَنْصَارُ اللَّهِ آمَنَّا بِاللَّهِ وَاشْهَدْ بِأَنَّا مُسْلِمُونَ*

_"Hazrat Esa (as) ne unse Kufr (aur mukhalefat) ko dekha to kaha: 'Kaun Khuda ki taraf (aur uske Deen liye) mera yawar o madadgar bane ga?' Hawareiin (jo unke makhsoos shagird the) kahne lage: 'Ham Khuda ke yawar o madadgar hain, is par imaan laate hain aur aap (bhi) gawah rahen ke ke ham Islam le aye hain."_
(Surah Aal-e-Imran: 52)

📚📖
👉 _* Tafseer:*_
Hawariin حوارين hawari حوارى ki jama (plural) hai aur iska root حور Hoor hai jiske maani hai 'dhona aur safed karna'. Unko ye isliye kaha gaya ke woh log paak dil aur roohe ba safa ke malik the.
Imam Raza (as):
_"Baaz log samjhte hain ke unka ka profession kapde dhona tha lekin hamare nazdeek iski wajah ye hai ke unhone khud ko bhi gunah ki aaloodgi se paak rakha hua tha aur doosron ko bhi paak karne mein koshan rehte the."_
Qur'an aur Bible ke mutabiq Hawareiin ke naam (Disciples of Jesus Christ):
(1) Andrew (2) Bartholomew (3) James the Elder (4) James the Younger (5) John (6) Judas (7) Thaddeus (8) Mathew (9) Peter (10) Phillip (11) Simon the Zealot (12) Thomas.
*Similarities:*
Bahut si baaten hamare Rasool (sa) ke mushabe hain:
Jab Dawate Zul Asheerah mein aap ne sawal kiya kaun hai jo mere is Deeni Mission mein Yawar o madadgar hoga, kisi ne jawab nahi diya siwai Hazrat Ali (as) ke, jabke hamare Rasool (as) ke Janashin ki tadaad misle hawareiin ki tadadad ke barabar 12 hai. Mojezat mein bhi samanta hai.
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜
----------------------------------------------

_*MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!*_
🙇
Rasule Khuda (saww):
_"Ya Ali! Tumhari misaal Isa bin Maryam (as) ki tarah hai, jis se Isaiyo'n ne hadd se zyada pyaar kiya to kaafir ho gaye aur Yahudiyo'n ne bugz kiya to kaafir ho gaye."_
(Aqwaal e Masoomeen (as), p129)

Imam Sadiq (as)
se puchha gaya, _"Aakhir kya wajah hai ke Isa (as) ke as'haab (hawaari) paani ke upar chala karte the jab ke as'haab e Muhammad (saww) mein aisi koi baat nahi hai?" Aap ne farmaya, "Is liye ke as'haab e Isa (as) ko rozgaar kamane ki fikr nahi thi, jab ke as'haab e Muhammad (saww) rozgaar ki fikr mein hamesha pareshaan rehte the."_
(Meezan ul Hikmah, v8, p633)
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜
----------------------------------------------
*10th Shawwal 1437*, 15th July 2016, Friday,

♦ _*ITTEBA - OBEDIENCE*_ ♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (351)

*بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ*

*رَبَّنَا آمَنَّا بِمَا أَنْزَلْتَ وَاتَّبَعْنَا الرَّسُولَ فَاكْتُبْنَا مَعَ الشَّاهِدِينَ*

_"Parwardegar! Jo kuchh Tu ne nazil kiya hai ham us par imaan laye, aur hamne (Tere) Rasool ki pairawi ki hai. Hame gawahon ke zumre mein likh le."_
(Surah Aal-e-Imran: 53)

📚📖
👉 _* Tafseer:*_
Hawareiin ne ita'at ki wajah se dua ki unhe Allah gawah banaye.
Jabke hadith, Ayaat wa rivayaat mein dekhte hain ke Rasool aur Imam hamare Aamaal ke gawah hai.
Rasool e Khuda (sa) ne apne ashab se farmaya:
_"Mera tumhare darmiyan maujood rehna bhi khair hai aur na rehna bhi khair hai"_
Jabir bin Abdullah Ansari ne sawal ki rehna to samajh mein aata hai, lekin na rehna?
Jawab mein farmaya:
_"Jab maujood rahenge is ayaat (8:33) ki bena par un par koi Azaab nahi ayega. Isi ayat ki bena par farmaya Rasool (sa) juda ho jayege tab bhi khair hai kiyonki har Monday aur Thursday logon ke Aamaal Rasool aur Imam ke samne pesh kiye jate hain. Jab Nek Aamaal dekhte hain to Allah ka Shukr ada karte hain aur jab bure Aamaal dikhai dete hain to Allah se uske liye isteghfar karte hain."_
(Basairud Darajat- Shaikh Tusi, Tafseer Ayyashi, Allama Majlisi )

Ab jo log kahte hain ke unhe Rasool (sa) ki zaroorat nahi, direct Allah ko apne Aamaal dikhayenge to woh log Qayamat mein hare hue muqadme ke manind khade honge kiyonki unka koi gawah (witness) nahi hoga. 😊
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜
----------------------------------------------

_*MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!*_
🙇
Rasule Khuda (saww):
_"Jo koi apne rishedaaro'n ke paas Sil e Rahem karne apne Nafs aur apne Maal ke saath jaata hai, to Allah usay 100 shahido'n ka sawaab ataa karta hai aur har qadam par usay 40000 neki deta hai aur 40000 gunah maaf karta hai aur uska martaba 40000 darja buland karta hai aur oos se aisa sulook hota hai jaise usne 100 saal Allah ki Ibadat Sabr aur puri tawajjoh ke saath ki."_
(Anwaru'l Hidayah)
(Family Life Of Islam)
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜
----------------------------------------------
*11th Shawwal 1437*, 16th July 2016, Saturday,
🔹🔹🔹🔹🔹🔹🔹🔹🔹🔹

BAZM-E-ADAB WELCOMES YOU*

       ♦ _*MAKR O FAREB*_ ♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (352)

*بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ*

*وَمَكَرُوا وَمَكَرَ اللَّهُ ۖ وَاللَّهُ خَيْرُ الْمَاكِرِينَ*

_"Aur (Yahoodiyon aur Maseeh ke dushmano ne unki aur unke Deen ki barbadi o naboodi ke liye) sazish ki aur Khuda ne (unki aur unke Deen ki hifazat ke liye) charajoi ki aur Khuda behtar charajoi karne wala hai."_
[Surat Aal-E-Imran 54]

📚📖
👉 _* Tafseer:*_
Makar yani sazish, planning etc. Ye achhe ke liye bhi ho sakti hai aur bure kaam ke liye bhi. Allah ke makr se murad Uski Nabi ki hifazat karna aur dushmano se bachana.

Rasool (sa) ke qatl ki sazish:
Abu Attufail se rivayat:
_"Jab Rasool e Khuda (sa) jange Tubuk ke liye ja rahe the, Uqbah ke maqam par ruke tabhi kuchh naqab posh log aye aur Rasool (sa) par war kiya, Ammar ne jawabi hamla kiya. Rasoole Khuda (sa) ne Huzaifa se kaha jaldi aage badho. Rasool (sa) ne unko bataya ke unki kiya sazish thi, ke woh Rasool (sa) ko wahan se niche dhakel dete._
_Naqab posh hamlawar the: Abu Bakr, Umar, Usman, Talha aur Saad bin Abi Waqas."_
(Tabarani ki rivayat, Majma Al Zawaid, Vol 1, P-132, H-425)
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜
----------------------------------------------

_*MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!*_
🙇
Imam Sadiq (as):
_"5 logo'n ko neend nahi aati,_
_1) Wo shakhs jisne kisi ka khoo'n bahaya ho,_
_2) Wo shakhs jiske paas maal bahut ho magar uske paas koi ameen (amaanat-daar) na ho,_
_3) Wo shakhs jisne maal e duniya ke liye logo'n se jhoot aur fareb ki baatein ki ho'n,_
_4) Wo shakhs jis par logo'n ka qarz bahut zyada ho magar uske paas kuchh maal na ho,_
_5) Wo shakhs jo kisi se mohabbat kare aur uski judaai mutawaqqe (apekshit / expected) ho."_
(Man La Yahzarahul Faqih, v1, p318)
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜
----------------------------------------------
*12th Shawwal 1437*, 17th July 2016, Sunday,
🔹🔹🔹🔹🔹🔹🔹🔹🔹🔹

BAZM-E-ADAB WELCOMES YOU*

⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜
       ♦ _*H. ESA (as)*_ ♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (353)

*بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ*

*إِذْ قَالَ اللَّهُ يَا عِيسَىٰ إِنِّي مُتَوَفِّيكَ وَرَافِعُكَ إِلَيَّ وَمُطَهِّرُكَ مِنَ الَّذِينَ كَفَرُوا وَجَاعِلُ الَّذِينَ اتَّبَعُوكَ فَوْقَ الَّذِينَ كَفَرُوا إِلَىٰ يَوْمِ الْقِيَامَةِ ۖ ثُمَّ إِلَيَّ مَرْجِعُكُمْ فَأَحْكُمُ بَيْنَكُمْ فِيمَا كُنْتُمْ فِيهِ تَخْتَلِفُونَ*

_"(Woh waqt yaad karo) jab Khuda ne Esa (as) se kaha: Mein tumhe le lun ga aur apni taraf utha lun ga aur jo log Kafir ho gaye hain unse pak karunga aur jo tumhari pairavi karte hain unhe in logon se Yaum e Qayamat tak ke liye bartar qarar dunga jo log Kafir ho gaye hain. Phir tumhari bazgasht (return) Meri taraf hai aur jis cheez mein tum ikhtelaf karte ho tumhare darmiyan faisla kar dunga."_
[Surat Aal-E-Imran 55]

📚📖
👉 _* Tafseer:*_
Yahan متوفيك aur وفات ka ek hi root hai. Aam taur par wafat ko Maut ke maani mein lete hain. Lekin iska root hai وفى jiska matlab hai 'kisi cheez ki takmeel karna' 'to complete'. Arab mein ye word wasooli ke maani mein bhi istemal hota hai. Doosri ayaton mein bhi ye word aya hai متوفيك jiske maani ye hain ke Allah ne le liya (yani hisab kitab pura hua- Mahavra).
Yani Hazrat Esa (as) ki aam maani ke mutabiq wafat nahi hui, balke Allah ne unko apne tahveel mein le liya. Aur rivayat ke mutabiq bhi ye musallam Islami Aqeeda hai ke H. Esa (as) abhi tak zinda hai, sirf is zameen se utha liye gaye. Christian ke mutabiq bhi jaiske woh mante hai Good Friday ke din unki wafat hui (ghaib ho gaye) lekin 3 din k baad Easter (Sunday ko) dikhayi diye. Yani k woh zinda hain.
Jaisa ke is Ayat mein hai ke H. Esa (as) ke pairokar kafiron se bartar honge. Lekin jaisa ke Qur'an o rivayat ke mutabiq Imam Mahdi (as) tamam adyan par ghalib ayenge aur aap puri Duniya mein hukumat karenge. H. Esa (as) ka Deen haqeeqat mein jo aaj Christianity hai woh nahi tha balke aslan Tawheedi Deen tha jo ke Islam hai. Isliye Imam Mahdi (as) doosre religions par overpower rehenge jaise tehreef shuda Christianity religion, Jewish, Hindus ...... etc. Aur H. Esa (as) Imam ke peechhe Namaz padhenge. (Bukhari). Qayamat se pahle ek adil hukumat qayem hogi aur Haq o Batil ka faisla hoga aur sab ikhtelaf door ho jayenge.
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜
----------------------------------------------

_*MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!*_
🙇
Rasule Khuda (saww):
_"Jab Mahdi (atfs) zahoor karenge to Khuda Esa (as) ko naazil karega aur ye dono ek jagah jamaa ho jayenge aur jab wajib Namaz ka waqt hoga to Mahdi (atfs) Esa (as) se kahenge, “Aye Rooh e Khuda, aage badhiye (yaani Jamaat padhaiye)”. Esa (as) farmayenge, “Aap Ahlebait (as) par koi bhi sabqat (Lead) nahi kar sakta hain”. Phir Mahdi (atfs) aage badhenge aur Esa (as) aap ke pichhe Namaz padhenge.”_
(Jamaal e Muntazar, p489)
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜
----------------------------------------------
*13th Shawwal 1437*, 18th July 2016, Monday,

BAZM-E-ADAB WELCOMES YOU*

           ♦ _*AAMAAL*_ ♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (354)

*بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ*

*فَأَمَّا الَّذِينَ كَفَرُوا فَأُعَذِّبُهُمْ عَذَابًا شَدِيدًا فِي الدُّنْيَا وَالْآخِرَةِ وَمَا لَهُمْ مِنْ نَاصِرِينَ * وَأَمَّا الَّذِينَ آمَنُوا وَعَمِلُوا الصَّالِحَاتِ فَيُوَفِّيهِمْ أُجُورَهُمْ ۗ وَاللَّهُ لَا يُحِبُّ الظَّالِمِينَ * ذَٰلِكَ نَتْلُوهُ عَلَيْكَ مِنَ الْآيَاتِ وَالذِّكْرِ الْحَكِيمِ*

_"Phir woh log jo Kafir ho gaye hain (aur unhone Haq ko pahchanne ke bawajood usse inkar kar diya hai) unhe Duniya wa Akherat mein sakht Azaab dunga aur unka koi yawar o madadgar na hoga."_
_"Aur woh log jo Imaan laye hain aur unhone nek Aamaal anjam diye hain to Khuda unhe unka pura pura Ajro Sawab dega. Aur Khuda Zalimo ko dost nahi rakhta."_
_"Ye jo kuchh Ham aap ke liye padhte hain, tumhari Haqqaniyat ki nishani aur Hakeemana tazkara hai."_
(Surah Aal-e-Imran: 56 - 58)
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜
----------------------------------------------

_*MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!*_
🙇
Imam Ali (as):
_"Allah ki itni Ibadat karo jitni tumhe Allah ki zarurat hai, Allah ki itni na-farmani karo jitna Allah ke azaab par Sabr kar sakte ho, Duniya ke liye itne aamaal karo jitna tumhe is duniya mein rehna hai, Akherat ke liye itne aamal karo jitna tumhe wahaa'n rehna hai."_
(Aqwaal e Masoomeen (as), p101)
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜

 ♦ _*H. ESA (as): - KHILQAT*_ ♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (355)

*بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ*

*إِنَّ مَثَلَ عِيسَىٰ عِنْدَ اللَّهِ كَمَثَلِ آدَمَ ۖ خَلَقَهُ مِنْ تُرَابٍ ثُمَّ قَالَ لَهُ كُنْ فَيَكُونُ * الْحَقُّ مِنْ رَبِّكَ فَلَا تَكُنْ مِنَ الْمُمْتَرِينَ*

_"H. Esa  (as) ki misal Khuda ke nazdeek H. Adam (as) ki si hai, jinhe Khuda ne mitti se paida kiya. Phir usse se kaha: 'ho ja to woh ho gaya." (Isliye ke baap ke baghair Maseeh ki wiladat hargiz unki uloohiyat (Godhood) ki daleel  nahi ban sakti.)"_
_"Ye cheezen tumhare Parwardegar ki taraf se Haqaeq (Truths) hai lehaza tum taraddod wa shakh (doubt & hesitation) karne walo mein se na bano."_
(Surah Aal-e-Imran: 59 - 60)

📚📖
👉 _* Tafseer:*_
Is Ayat mein Hazrat Esa (as) ki paidaish ke bare mein jo logo ke zehno sawal paida hote hain unka jawab diya gaya hai. Ke jab Allah Hazrat Adam (as) ko bin maa-baap ke paida kar sakta hai to H. Esa (as) ka bin baap ka hona koi shak wali baat nahi. Doosra pahlu ye hai ke jaisa Christian maante hain ke bin baap se matlab wo Khuda ya Khuda ke bete ho gaye, Yani Khuda baap ho gaya. Ye bhi ghalat hai. Agar aisa maanenge to Khuda ko bhi usi khilqat ke process se guzrna hoga, to phir Khuda kaise hua? Ya yeh ke Khuda ne apna roop badal kar H. Esa (as) ke bhes mein aa gaya, to is tarah ka Khuda to mohtaj ho gaya. Khuda ko kiya zaroorat aisa karni ki. Isse is Khuda ki majboori zahir hoti hai. Yahan Allah Ta'ala farma raha hai, wo majboor nahi hai, Wo jo chahta hai, kahta hai aur wo cheez ho jati hai.
Lekin jab itni daleel e dene ke bawajood bhi Christian (Najran ke Nasrani) na maane to Rasoole Akram (sa) ne Ale Imran (yani Ahle Bait) (as) ka sahara liya.
Phir _MUBAHELA_ hua. Yani dono ke beech ye tai hua ke dono group ek maidan mein jama honge aur Khuda (God) se dua karenge k _'jhoto par Allah ki La'anat ho.'_

👉Next Ayat e Mubahela kal mulaheza farmayen.
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜
----------------------------------------------

_*MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!*_
🙇
Allah (swt):
_"Aye Isa (as)! Mujhe is tarah pukaro jaise garq hone wale (doobne waale) ko koi bachaane waala na ho."_
(Sharh Dua e Kumail)

Imam Reza (as):
_"J. Esa bin Maryam (as) ne apne hawaariyo'n se kaha, "Agar tumhara Deen salaamat ho aur tumhare haath mein duniya se kuchh chala jaaye to gham na karo. Duniya-daar duniya ke jaane par gham karte hain, unhe Deen ke chale jaane ka koi gham nahi hota."_
(Amaali - Shaikh Sadooq, p461)

*15th Shawwal 1437, 20th July 2016, Wednesday,

⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜
            ♦ _*MUBAHELA*_ ♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (356)

*بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ*

*فَمَنْ حَاجَّكَ فِيهِ مِنْ بَعْدِ مَا جَاءَكَ مِنَ الْعِلْمِ فَقُلْ تَعَالَوْا نَدْعُ أَبْنَاءَنَا وَأَبْنَاءَكُمْ وَنِسَاءَنَا وَنِسَاءَكُمْ وَأَنْفُسَنَا وَأَنْفُسَكُمْ ثُمَّ نَبْتَهِلْ فَنَجْعَلْ لَعْنَتَ اللَّهِ عَلَى الْكَاذِبِينَ * إِنَّ هَٰذَا لَهُوَ الْقَصَصُ الْحَقُّ ۚ وَمَا مِنْ إِلَٰهٍ إِلَّا اللَّهُ ۚ وَإِنَّ اللَّهَ لَهُوَ الْعَزِيزُ الْحَكِيمُ*

_"Is Ilm o danish ke baad jo (H. Esa (as) ke bare mein) tumhare paas pahuncha hai. Phir bhi koi tumse jhaghre to kah do: "Aao ham apne beton ko bulate hain, tum apne beton ko bulao, ham apni aurton ko bulate hain, tum apni aurton ko bulao aur ham apne nafson ko bulate hain tum apne nafso ko bulao. Phir MUBAHELA karenge aur jhonton par Khuda ki LAANAT karenge."_
_"Ye (H. Esa as ka) haqeeqi qissa hai (aur unki uloohiyat aur Khuda ka beta hone ki sab baaten be buniyad hain.) Aur Khuda e Yagana ke alawa koi Ma'bood nahi aur Khuda to Dana o Hakeem hai."_
(Surah Aal-e-Imran: 61 - 62)

📚📖
👉 _* Tafseer:*_
Mubahela مباهله ka root hai بهل means 'reha karna', 'chhod dena'. Jab Rasoole Khuda (sa) ka Najran ke Christian se debate wa mubahesa hua aur woh apni baat par ade rahe to ye waqea pesh aya. Yani Faisla Allah par chhod diya gaya, ke jhooton par Allah ki Laanat hogi.
Ye waqea laghbagh sabhi kitabon mein darj hai. Pahle ek general rule pesh kiya gaya ke meeting ke hazreen kaun kaun honge. History mein hamne dekha beton mein Hasan wa Husain (as), Aurton mein Janabe Fatema Zehra (sa), Nafs e Rasool Ali (as) ko is kaam ke liye Rasool (sa) ne Khuda ke hukm se chuna. Najran ke Christian ne jab ye manzar dekha ke Rasool (sa) in Ale Imran (Ahle Bait) se farma rahe the ke jab mein dua karun to tum Ameen kahna. Ye dekh un par aisi haibat tari hui ke woh sulah par amada hua aur jizya (tax) dene par razi ho gaye.

Is ayat mein Ahle Bait e Rasool (Ale Imran) (as) ke fazilat milti hai jo ke un logon ne us din pahchan liya. Lekin Musalman aaj tak na pahchan saka. Kuchh mutassib Musalman is waqea se hi sire se inkar kar dete hain. Ye waqea 24 Zilhajj ko pesh aya. Aur is tarah se Rasoole Akram (sa) ko kamyabi hasil hui. Jabke Quran khud farma raha hai: _"Beshak Ye ek sachcha waqea hai."_
Puri detail ki yahan gunjaish nahi hai readers se guzarish hai ke is topic par aur books refer karen.
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜
----------------------------------------------
_*MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!*_
🙇
_"Ek roz Moaiviya ne Saad bin Abi Waqas se kaha:'Tum Abu Turab (Ali as) ko sab o sham (gali) kiyon nahi karte?' Woh kahne laga:_
_'Jab se Ali (as) ke bare mein Paighambar (sa) ki kahi hui 3 baaten mujhe yaad ayi hain, meine is kaam ko chhod diya. In mein se ek ye thi ke jab Ayat e Mubahela nazil hui to Paighambar ne sirf Fatema (sa), Hasan o Husain (as) aur Ali (as) ko dawat di. Iske baad farmaya: اللهم هولاء اهلى (khudya! Ye mere ahl hain)."_
(Sahih Muslim)

Zamakhsari:
"Ye Ayat Ahle Kisa (Ale Imran-Ahle Bait as) ki fazilat ko sabit karne ke liye qavi daleel hai."
(Tafseer e Kashshaf)
----------------------------------------------

2. Musnad Ahmed bin Hambal, Vol 1, P-185
3. Tafseer e Tabari, Vol 3, P-192.
4. Mustadrak Haakim, Vol 3, P-15.
5. Dalailun Nubuwwa Hafiz Abu Naeem, P-297

14. Fusoolul Muhimma - Ibne Sabbagh, P-108.

⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜
             ♦ _*AKHLAQ*_ ♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (357)

*بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ*

*إِنَّ هَٰذَا لَهُوَ الْقَصَصُ الْحَقُّ ۚ وَمَا مِنْ إِلَٰهٍ إِلَّا اللَّهُ ۚ وَإِنَّ اللَّهَ لَهُوَ الْعَزِيزُ الْحَكِيمُ*

_"Ye (MUBAHELA mein H. Esa (as) ki debate ka) haqeeqi qissa hai (aur unki uloohiyat aur Khuda ka beta hone ki sab baaten be buniyad hain.) Aur Khuda e Yagana ke alawa koi Ma'bood nahi aur Khuda to Dana o Hakeem hai."_
(Surat Aal-e-Imran: 62)

📚📖
👉 _* Tafseer:*_
Ayah Mubahela (Dabate) jo ke Christian aur Rasoole Khuda (sa) ke beech hui, is ki kamyabi Ahle Bait (as) (Ale Imran) ki fazilat ki wajah se hai.
Tableegh ke liye kisi mission ya jamaat ki zaroorat nahi. Har fard ek ghair Muslim ke liye Namoona Amal ban sakta hai bashart ye ke uska Akhlaq wa bartao doosron ke sath achha ho. Rasoole Khuda (sa) ne 40 saal tak pahle apne Akhlaq se kafiron ka dil jeeta phir apni Risalat ka ailan kiya, jabke ailan ke baad ki zindagi sirf 23 saal. Phir Rasoolullah (sa) ko na koi daleel ya saboot ki zaroorat padi. Bas unse kaha: kaho 'La Ilaha.....' aur logo ne kah diya. Yahan debate mein bhi last option jo mein Mubahela kiya gaya wo ye ke sirf jhooton par Laanat bhejenge. Christian ye yaqeen ke sath samajh gaye Ahle Bait o Ale Imran (as) ki dua ka qabool na hona na mumkin hai, isliye unhone apni haar maan li.
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜
----------------------------------------------

_*MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!*_
🙇
Imam Sadiq (as):
(Agar mukhalefin apki baat na maane to kiya karen?)
_*"Teen din tak apne Akhlaq ki islah karo."*_
Raavi kahta hai:
_"Means aapne farmaya Roza rakho, Ghusl karo. Phir jis se Mubahela karna chahte ho use sehra (maidan) mein le jao. Phir apne right hand ki ungliyon se uske right hand mein dalo aur apni taraf se shuru karo aur kaho: 'Khuda wanda! Tu saat aasmano aur saat zameeno ka Parwardegar hai aur poshida asrar (hidden) se agah hai aur Rehman o Rahim hai. Mere mukhalif ne agar Haq se inkar kiya hai aur Batil ka dawa kiya hai to aasman se us par bala o musibat nazil farma aur use dardnak Azaab mein mubtela kar de. Is dua ko repeat karo."_
Imam (as) ne iske baad farmaya:
_"Zyada waqt nahi guzrega ke  is dua ka natija ashkar hoga. Khuda ki Qasam mein ne hargiz aisa koi shakhs nahi paya jo tayyar ho ke is tarah uske sath Mubahela kiya jaye."_
(Tafseer Noorus Saqlain, Vol 1, P-351)
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜
----------------------------------------------
*17th Shawwal 1437, 22nd July 2016, Friday,
🔹🔹🔹🔹🔹🔹🔹🔹🔹🔹

BAZM-E-ADAB WELCOMES YOU*

⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜
            ♦ _*TAWHEED*_ ♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (358)

*بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ*

*فَإِنْ تَوَلَّوْا فَإِنَّ اللَّهَ عَلِيمٌ بِالْمُفْسِدِينَ * قُلْ يَا أَهْلَ الْكِتَابِ تَعَالَوْا إِلَىٰ كَلِمَةٍ سَوَاءٍ بَيْنَنَا وَبَيْنَكُمْ أَلَّا نَعْبُدَ إِلَّا اللَّهَ وَلَا نُشْرِكَ بِهِ شَيْئًا وَلَا يَتَّخِذَ بَعْضُنَا بَعْضًا أَرْبَابًا مِنْ دُونِ اللَّهِ ۚ فَإِنْ تَوَلَّوْا فَقُولُوا اشْهَدُوا بِأَنَّا مُسْلِمُونَ*

_"Agar (in wazeh shawahed ke bawajood woh qabool e Haq se) roogardani (neglect) karte hain (to jan lo ke woh Haqeeqat ke mutlashi nahi aur) Khuda fasad karne walon se aagah hai."_
_"Kah do! Aye Ahle Kitab! Aao aisi baat ki taraf jo hamare aur tumhare darmiyan mushtarak (common) kai ke siwai Khuda e Yagana (One God) ke kisi ki Ibaadat na karen aur kisi cheez ko Uska Sharik qarar na den aur ham mein se baaz Khuda ko chhod kar baaz doosron ko Khuda ke taur par qabool na karen. Jab (woh is dawat se)  roogardani karenge to kahiye: 'Gawah raho ke ham Musalman hain'."_
(Surah Aal-e-Imran: 63 - 64)

📚📖
👉 _* Tafseer:*_
Allah ne Christian wa doosre mazhab ko ek common belief par dawat di hai aur wo hai _'Tawheed'._ Means har mazhab Khuda ko ek manta hai. To jab ek manta hai to phir shirk kiyon karta hai. Christian Trinity ka aqeeda rakhte hain yani: One God, Jesus, The Holy Spirit. Ek Khuda 3 alag roop dharan karega to majboor mana jayega. Ya ek se zyada hoga. Jabke Woh Real mein Ek hai, to Zyada ginana Haqeeqat se inkar karna hai.
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜
----------------------------------------------

_*MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!*_
🙇 👋
Imam Sadiq (as):
_"Beshak dushman ke muqable mein Musalmano'n ka ittehad (united) aur unka musta'id (vigilant / chaukas / jaagrut) rehna hi Deen ka sutoon hai."_
(Almustashaar Abdul Haleem Jundi (Misri), p193)
☠
Imam Sadiq (as):
_"7 aadmiyo'n ka azaab sab se zyada shadeed hoga: Qaabil, Namrood, Baani e Yahoodiyat (Founder of Jewism), Baani e Nasraniyat (Founder of Christianity), Firoun aur 2 aadmi is Ummat ke."_
(Khisaal, ch7)
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜
----------------------------------------------
*18th Shawwal 1437, 23rd July 2016, Saturday,
🔹🔹🔹🔹🔹🔹🔹🔹🔹🔹

BAZM-E-ADAB WELCOMES YOU*

⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜
      ♦ _*HAZRAT IBRAHIM (as)*_ ♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (359)

*بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ*

*يَا أَهْلَ الْكِتَابِ لِمَ تُحَاجُّونَ فِي إِبْرَاهِيمَ وَمَا أُنْزِلَتِ التَّوْرَاةُ وَالْإِنْجِيلُ إِلَّا مِنْ بَعْدِهِ ۚ أَفَلَا تَعْقِلُونَ*

_"Aye Ahle Kitab! (Hazrat) Ibrahim (as) ke bare mein kiyon jhagda karte ho (aur tum mein se har ek inhe apne Deen ka pairokar samajhta hai) halanke Taurat aur Injeel to unke baad nazil hui hai, kiya tum aql o fikr nahi rakhte."_
(Surah Aal-e-Imran: 65)

📚📖
👉 _* Tafseer:*_
Christian aur Jews kahte the ke H. Ibrahim (as) bhi unke mazhab se the. To commonsense hai ke H. Esa wa H. Moosa (as) Hazrat Ibrahim (as) ki kayi pusht baad mein aye to jab to unka Deen tha bhi nahi. Kuchh Kafir unki murti bana poojte the.
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜
----------------------------------------------

_*MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!*_
🙇
Imam Sadiq (as)
se raawi ne sawaal kiya ke, _"Kya wajah hai ke main aap se Salmaan e Farsi ka tazkera zyada sunta hoo'n?"_  Aap ne farmaya:
_"Salman e Farsi na kaho balke Salman e Mohammadi kaho. Kya tum jaante ho ke main Salman ko zyada kyun yaad karta hoo'n?"_
Raawi ne kaha, "Nahi".
Imam (as) ne farmaya: _"Unke 3 ausaaf (qualities / khususiyaat) ki wajah se main unko zyada yaad karta hoo'n._
_(1) Wo apni khwaish e nafs par Ali (as) ki khwaish ko muqaddam rakhte the (yaani apni khwaish ko aap ki khwaish par qurbaan kar diya karte the. Wo ye nahi dekhte ke meri khwaish kya hai balke wo ye dekhte the ke Ali (as) ki khwaish kya hai). Yehi manzelat e ita'at o itteba hai,_
_(2) Wo faqr aur ghorba (gareebi aur gareebo'n) se mohabbat karte the aur unko saahebaan e Daulat (maaldaaro'n) par tarjih (preference) dete the,_
_(3) Wo Ilm aur Ulema se mohabbat karte the. H. Salman Allah ke nek bande the jo Deen e Hanif e Ibrahimi par qaaem o daaem the aur wo kabhi mushrik nahi rahe."_
(Amaali - Shaikh Toosi, v1, p348)
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜
----------------------------------------------
*19th Shawwal 1437, 24th July 2016, Sunday,

              ♦ _*JIHALAT*_ ♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (360)

*بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ*

*هَا أَنْتُمْ هَٰؤُلَاءِ حَاجَجْتُمْ فِيمَا لَكُمْ بِهِ عِلْمٌ فَلِمَ تُحَاجُّونَ فِيمَا لَيْسَ لَكُمْ بِهِ عِلْمٌ ۚ وَاللَّهُ يَعْلَمُ وَأَنْتُمْ لَا تَعْلَمُونَ*

_"Tum (Ahle Kitab) to wohi ho jo us cheez ke bare mein guftugu karte the jiske bare mein aagah hote the Ab in cheezon ke bare mein guftugu karte ho jinse aagah nahi ho. Khuda janta hai aur tum nahi jante."_
(Surah Aal-e-Imran: 66)
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜
----------------------------------------------

_*MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!*_
🙇
Imam Ali (as)
ne logo'n ko Kaaba ke gird tawaaf karte dekha aur farmaya:
_"Ye log Jahiliyyat mein bhi isi tarah tawaaf kiya karte the. Unhe hukm diya gaya hai ke Kaaba ka tawaaf kar ke hamare paas aayein aur apni Wilayat aur mohabbat hamare liye zaahir karein aur apni nusrat ko hum par pesh karein, TAB UNKA HAJJ QUBOOL HOGA". Phir aap ne ye Ayat padhi (Ibrahim (as) ne Khana e Kaaba banaate waqt Khuda se Dua ki) LOGO'N KA DIL MERI ZURRIYAT KI TARAF JHUKA DENA, yaani unke dilo'n mein mohabbat de dena. (Surah Ibrahim, Surah 14, Ayat 37)"_
(Al Kaafi, v2, p400)

Imam Ali (as):
_"Jab Aqalmand budhha hota hai to uski Aql jawaan ho jaati hai aur jab Jaahil budhha hota hai to uski Jihaalat (ignorance) jawaan ho jaati hai."_
(Meezan ul Hikmah, v5)

Wilayat ki ma'arefat na hona Jihalat hai.
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜

*20th Shawwal 1437, 25th July 2016, Monday,

BAZM-E-ADAB WELCOMES YOU*

⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜
            ♦ _*DEEN-E-HANIF*_ ♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (361)

*بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ*

*مَا كَانَ إِبْرَاهِيمُ يَهُودِيًّا وَلَا نَصْرَانِيًّا وَلَٰكِنْ كَانَ حَنِيفًا مُسْلِمًا وَمَا كَانَ مِنَ الْمُشْرِكِينَ*

_"Ibrahim (as) na Yahoodi (Jew) the na Nasrani (Christian) balke woh Mukhlis Muwahhid (Staunch believer of One God) aur Musalman (One who submit to God) the, aur woh hargiz Mushrekin mein se nahi the."_
[Surah Aal-e-Imran: 67)

📚📖
👉 _* Tafseer:*_
Allah ne yahan Hazrat Ibrahim (as) ke Deen ka tarruf karaya hai. Unka ek Deen-e-Hanif tha. Hanif حنيف means woh shakhs jo Batil ko chhod kar Haq ki taraf mael (inclined) ho. Hazrat Ibrahim (as) Tawheed parast the aur Qur'an kahta hai ke woh Musalman the. Yani unka aur Rasoole Akram (sa) ka Deen ek hi tha. Hanif ke yehi bhi maani hain ke apni fitrat par palatna, chunke Islam Deen-e-Fitrat hai isliye Deen-e-Hanif bhi hai. Musalman means Allah ke samne mutlaqan Tasleem (Absolute Submission) jis mein zarra brabar bhi shirk na paya jata ho.
Imam Sadiq (as):
_"Ibrahim (as) ek Mukhlis Shakhsiyat the jisne kabhi butparasti nahi ki."_ Yehi Deen-e-Hanif hai.
(Mohd ibn Yaqub Kuleini, Kafi, vol. 2, pg. 15, hadith 1.)
H. Ibrahim (as) se aaj tak pairokar badalte rahe lekin Deen wohi raha. Pairokar (follower) sunte kuchh aur karte kuchh aur the. H. Esa (as) ne kuchh kaha, Christians ne usme tehreef (changes) kiye. Rasoole Akram (sa) ne ek hi baat ki lekin samajhne wale 73 tukdo mein bat gaye. Imam Mahdi (as) jab Zahoor karenge aur wohi Deen-e-Hanif ko pesh karenge to logon ko naya lagega. Yehi Deen Ale Imran ka hai. Khandane Rasoole Khuda aur khandane Abu Talib (Imran) aur unki pichhli naslen Islami shariyat ke pahle isi Shariyat e Ibrahim (as) par amal kar rahi thi. Means Anbiya ke ajdad mein koi bhi Kafir ya mushrik na tha. Ye ek common sense hai ke Rehbar jis baat ko logo ko mana kar raha ho wo khud kaise ho sakta hai. Aise Rehbar bhi qabil e qubool nahi jo pahle khud Kafir hon aur doosron ko Kufr se mana karen.
Isliye ham dua karte bare Ilaha hame usi Deen-e-Hanif par baqi rakh.
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜

_*MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!*_
🙇 🕌
*الإمام الصادق (ع): المسلم من سلم الناس من يده ولسانه ، والمؤمن من ائتمنه الناس على أموالهم وأنفسهم.*
🕌
Imam Sadiq (as):
_"Ek Musalman woh hai jiske haath aur zabaan se log Mehfooz hon, aur Momin woh hai jis par log apni maal o jaan ka bharosa karen."_

_"A Muslim is he whose hand and tongue people feel safe from, whilst a believer (mu'min) is he whom people trust with their belongings and their lives."_
[Ma`ani al-Akhbar, p. 239, no. 1]
🕌
*رسول الله‏ (ص): الإسلام عريان ؛ فلباسه الحياء ، وزينته الوفاء ، ومروءته العمل الصالح ، وعماده الورع ، ولكل شيء أساس وأساس الإسلام حبنا أهل البيت.*
🕌
Rasoole Akram (sa):
_"Islam urya tha, haya uske kapde hain, uski Zeenat Wafa hai, uski qadr uske Aamaal hain, uska sutoon wara' (Taqwe se kahi bala), har cheez ki buniyad hoti hai aur Islam ki buniyad ham Ahle Bait ki Muhabbat hai."_

_"Islam is naked, and its clothing is modesty, its adornment loyalty, its valour good deeds, and its pillars piety. Everything has a foundation, and the foundation of Islam is the love for us, the Ahlul Bait (the household of the Prophet)."_
[al-Mahasin, v. 1, p. 445, no. 1031]

          ♦ _*YAHOODI SAZISH*_ ♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (343)

*بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ*

*وَدَّتْ طَائِفَةٌ مِنْ أَهْلِ الْكِتَابِ لَوْ يُضِلُّونَكُمْ وَمَا يُضِلُّونَ إِلَّا أَنْفُسَهُمْ وَمَا يَشْعُرُونَ*

_"Ahle Kitab (Yahood) ka ek grp chahta tha ke tumhe gumrah kar de lekin (unhe jan lena chahiye ke tumhe gumrah nahi kar sakte) woh apne aap ko gumrah karte hain. Magar samajhte nahi."_
[Surah Aal-e-Imran: 69)

📚📖
👉 _* Tafseer:*_
Is ayat mein dushmano ki sazish se bakhabar kiya hai. Unhe kaha gaya hai ke wo is bejah koshish se dast bardar ho jayen. Maktab e Paighambar mein Musalmano ki tarbiyat is hisab se aur agahi se hui hai ke laut jane ka koi ehtemal nahi.

Imam Baqar (as):
Is ayat ke bare mein farmate hai:
_"Jab Rasoole Akram (sa) Madina tashrif laye to Baitul Muqaddas ki taraf rukh kar ke namaz padhi. Fajr ka waqt. Yahoodiyon ko ye andazi pasand aya. Zuhr ke dauran Qibla change hua. Maghrib ki Namaz Kaabe ki taraf hui. Isliye unke mutabiq Fajr mein jo Imaan laye wo Maghrib mein apna Imaan badal den, is tarah ki sazish kar rahe the."_

Means Yahoodi chahte the jaisa Rasool ka Qibla change hua uski ke sath Imaan bhi change kar den. Subh Imaan ke sath to Sham ko baghair Imaan. Yani Musalman rukh na badlen lekin Rasool ki Jamat mein kuchh aise afraad the unka jism ka rukh badla lekin dil nahi badle jiski wajah se Deen ko kafi nuqsan hua.
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜
----------------------------------------------

_*MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!*_
🙇
Riwayat:
_Rasule Khuda (saww) se puchha gaya ke Momeneen mein sabse afzal Imaan kiska hai? Aap (saww) ne farmaya "Uska Imaan afzal hai jiska Akhlaaq sabse behtar hai"._
(Jadeed Masaael - Ayatullah Sistani)

                  ♦ _*HAQ*_ ♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (364)

*بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ*

*يَا أَهْلَ الْكِتَابِ لِمَ تَكْفُرُونَ بِآيَاتِ اللَّهِ وَأَنْتُمْ تَشْهَدُونَ*
*يَا أَهْلَ الْكِتَابِ لِمَ تَلْبِسُونَ الْحَقَّ بِالْبَاطِلِ وَتَكْتُمُونَ الْحَقَّ وَأَنْتُمْ تَعْلَمُونَ*

_"Aye Ahle Kitab! Kiyon Ayat e Khuda se Kufr karte ho jabke (unki sehet o sadaqat ki) gawahi (bhi) dete ho."_

_"Aye Ahle Kitab! Haq o Batil se kiyon milate ho (aur inhe mushtabah karte go taake log samajh na saken aur gumrah ho jayen) aur Haqeeqat chhupate ho halanke tumhe maloom hai."_
(Surah Aal-e-Imran: 70 - 71)

📚📖
👉 _* Tafseer:*_
Haq ko chhupana nahi chahiye. Kuchh log Batil ko Haq ka libas pahnakar pesh karte hai aur dekhne wala confuse ho jata hai. Aaj ki misal Duniya mein ISIS ya Wahabiyat qatl o gharat ko Islam ke banner ke saye mein pesh kar rahe hain. Kiyonki unhone Haq (Ahle Bait - Ale Imran as) ke raste ko chhud kar Batil Rehmuma ka rasta ikhtiyar kiya hua hai.
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜
----------------------------------------------

_*MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!*_
🙇
Imam Ali (as):
_"Momin ka chiraag hamare Haq ki maarefat hai aur badtareen andhaa-pan hamare fazl se aa'nkhein band kar lena hai."_
(Aqwaal e Masoomeen (as), p167)

🌹 *JUMA MUBARAK*🌹
Rasule Khuda (saww):
_"Juma sayyadul ayyam (tamaam dino'n ka sardaar) hai. Allah Ta'ala is mein hasanaat zyada karta hai, darajaat buland karta hai, Dua qubool karta hai, sakhtiyo'n ko duur karta hai, ummedo'n ko bar laata hai, is roz gunaho'n se azaadi milti hai aur naar e Jahannum se azaad hoga aur jo koi Haq aur Hurmat e Juma ko pehchaante huwe Dua karega to Allah par ye Haq hoga ke wo aatish e dozakh se azaad kar dega."_
(Furoo e Kafi, v2, p210)

           ♦ _*YAHOODI SAZISH*_ ♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (365)

*بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ*

*وَقَالَتْ طَائِفَةٌ مِنْ أَهْلِ الْكِتَابِ آمِنُوا بِالَّذِي أُنْزِلَ عَلَى الَّذِينَ آمَنُوا وَجْهَ النَّهَارِ وَاكْفُرُوا آخِرَهُ لَعَلَّهُمْ يَرْجِعُونَ*

_"Ahle Kitab (Yahood) ki ek jamat ne kaha (jao aur) jo kuchh mo'menin par nazil hua hai (zahiran) din ki ibteda mein us par Imaan le aao aur din ke aakhir mein Kafir ho jao (aur laut aao) shayed wo (tumhare is amal se apne Deen se) bargashta ho jayen (kiyonki woh tumhe Ahle Kitab aur guzishta aasmaani basharton se aagah samajhte hain aur ye sazish inhe mutazalzal karne ke liye kafi hai.)"_
(Surah Aal-e-Imran: 72)

📚📖
👉 _* Tafseer:*_
Yahoodi (Jews) ki aghaze Islam se aaj tak Musalmano ke khilaf tarah tarah ki sazishe karte rahe hain. Is aayaat mein unki ek ahm sazish ka pardah fash kiya hai. Yahoodiyon ka maqsad aaj tak ye nahi raha ke doosron ko Yahoodi banayen balke ye raha ke unka tasallut (control) sab par rahe. Isliye daure Jahilliyat mein poora Arab inka maqrooz rahta tha. Unki sazish ye thi ke kuchh log kuchh waqt ke liye Musalman ban jaye aur maqsad pura hone ke baad wapas apne Deen par laut ayen. Maqsad ye tha ke Musalmano ke darmiyan ghadbadi phailana. Ikhtalefat ko badhawa dena. Isliye ham dekhte hain ke kuchh converted personalities Khalifaon ke darbar mein musheer e khas the. Kuchh to achche ohdon par faiz hue dekha. Aur ye sazish aaj bhi Israel ki taraf se jari hai. Duniya ka Super Power, source of terrorism aaj Israel hai. America uska ghulam hai. IMF, UN Israel par depend hai. Musalmano par musallat hone ke liye wo kuchh ko Musalman/Mulla bana kar unke darmiyan bhej deta hai. Salafism is unka ek purana kamyab product raha hai. Aaj ki zinda misal ISIS hai. ISIS ko dekh khud Musalman mutazalzal ho gaye: aya support karen ya oppose karen - aaj tak ye faisla nahi ho paya. Mimbar par se inke numainde taqreer karen aur aapas mein ikhtelaf ka shikar bane. Jaise Duniya bhar mein Israeli Product hi milta hai. Apko naya Yahoodi Islam bhi Islamic Pack mein milega. Pack ka naam Islamic State, box ke andar khoon mein tadapta Islam milega. Isse pahle Al Qaida ka product launch hua tha jo ab outdated ho gaya. Ab dekhyi is ke baad kaunsa product ayega.
Urdu book 'Hemfre ke etrafat' mein British ke zamane ki tafseel darj hai.
Kuchh proofs ham News section mein pesh kar chuke hai aur dete rahte hain.
Ye bahut mukhtasar khulasa tha warna iske liye kai Volumes chahiye.
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜
----------------------------------------------

_- Yahoodi,_ 🕍

            ♦ _*YAHOODI SAZISH*_ ♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (366)

*بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ*

*وَلَا تُؤْمِنُوا إِلَّا لِمَنْ تَبِعَ دِينَكُمْ قُلْ إِنَّ الْهُدَىٰ هُدَى اللَّهِ أَنْ يُؤْتَىٰ أَحَدٌ مِثْلَ مَا أُوتِيتُمْ أَوْ يُحَاجُّوكُمْ عِنْدَ رَبِّكُمْ ۗ قُلْ إِنَّ الْفَضْلَ بِيَدِ اللَّهِ يُؤْتِيهِ مَنْ يَشَاءُ ۗ وَاللَّهُ وَاسِعٌ عَلِيمٌ * يَخْتَصُّ بِرَحْمَتِهِ مَنْ يَشَاءُ ۗ وَاللَّهُ ذُو الْفَضْلِ الْعَظِيمِ*

_"Aur siwai us shakhs ke jo tumhare Deen ki pairavi karta hai aur kisi par Imaan na rakhi. Kaho ke Hidayat to woh hai jo Khuda ki taraf se ho (aur tumhari ye sazish uske muqable mein be asar hai)(phir woh apne sathiyon se mazeed kahne lage ke ye na samajhna ke) kisi ko tumhari tarah (Aasmani Kitab) di jayegi ya ye tumhare Parwardegar ke darbar mein koi bahes kar sakega (balke Nabuwwat aur Mantiq, ye dono cheezen sirf tumhari qaum aur nasl mein hain) kah do ke Fazl (Nabuwwat, Aql aur Mantiq ki ata kisi mein munhasir nahi hai balke woh) Khuda ke hath mein hai aur Woh jise chahta hai (aur iska ahl samajhta hai) ata karta hai aur Khuda Wase' (Wasee' atyaat wa enayat ka Malik) aur (inke munasib mawaqe se) aagah hai."_
_"Jise Chahta hai apni Rehmat se nawazta hai aur Allah Azeem Enayat o Fazl ka Malik hai."_
(Surah Aal-e-Imran: 73 - 74)

📚📖
👉 _* Tafseer:*_
Ayat ki shuruwat mein Yahoodi apne pairokar se kah rahe hain ke ye raaz (Khufiya planning) khufiya hi rahe. Isse pichhli aur ye Ayat Yahoodiyon ki khufiya sazish ke bare mein hai jisse Allah hame aagah kar raha hai. Mazmoon toolani hai isliye yahan sirf ishaara kafi hai. Interested Hazrat is par zyada tehqeeq kar sakte hain.
Next post mein hamne English mein kuchh isi se related topic par likha hai aur iski links pesh ki hai jisko open karke aap padh sakte hain. Ye aaj ki Yahoodi sazish ke zinda proofs hain.
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜

🙇

(Khisaal, ch7)

            ♦ _*AMAANAT*_ ♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (367)

*بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ*

*وَمِنْ أَهْلِ الْكِتَابِ مَنْ إِنْ تَأْمَنْهُ بِقِنْطَارٍ يُؤَدِّهِ إِلَيْكَ وَمِنْهُمْ مَنْ إِنْ تَأْمَنْهُ بِدِينَارٍ لَا يُؤَدِّهِ إِلَيْكَ إِلَّا مَا دُمْتَ عَلَيْهِ قَائِمًا ۗ ذَٰلِكَ بِأَنَّهُمْ قَالُوا لَيْسَ عَلَيْنَا فِي الْأُمِّيِّينَ سَبِيلٌ وَيَقُولُونَ عَلَى اللَّهِ الْكَذِبَ وَهُمْ يَعْلَمُونَ*
*بَلَىٰ مَنْ أَوْفَىٰ بِعَهْدِهِ وَاتَّقَىٰ فَإِنَّ اللَّهَ يُحِبُّ الْمُتَّقِينَ*

_"Aur Ahle Kitab mein se kuchh aise bhi hain ke agar tum inhe bahut si daulat bataur amanat do to tumhe lauta denge aur kuchh aise bhi hain ke agar unhe ek dinar bhi sipurd karo to woh tumhe hargiz wapas na karenge magar us waqt tak jab tak tum unke sar par khade raho (aur un par musallat raho) ye is wajah se hai ke woh kahte hain ham Ummiyeen (Yahoodiyon ke alawa kisi) aur ke saamne  jawab deh nahi hain aur Khuda par Jhoot bandhte hain halanke jante hain."_

_"Ji haan jo shakhs apne Ahd o Paiman poora kare aur parhezgari ikhtiyar kare (Khuda use dost rakhta hai kiyonki) Khuda parhezgaron ko pasand karta hai."_
(Surah Aal-e-Imran: 75 - 76)

📚📖 💰
👉 _* Tafseer:*_
Yahoodi samajhte the ke unhe Haq pahunchta hai ke woh Amanato mein khayanat karen. Woh kahte the ke woh Ahle Kitab hain, Paighambar un mein se hain, doosre log sab Batil hain isliye doosron ke maal ka ehteram karna koi zaroori nahi. Doosron ka maal ghasb karna jaez samajhte the. Aaj Israel bhi yehi kar raha hai doosron ki zamin par na jaez qabza kiye hue hai. Aghaze Islam mein Arab Yahoodi Business agreement tha (jo ke aaj bhi hai). Lekin Islam ke zuhoor ke baad Yahoodiyon ne Arabo ka Haq ghazb kar liye ye kahte hue ke ye agreement us waqt hua tha jab woh unke mukhalif nahi the. Ab chunke woh mazhab basal chuke hain to ab unka sab maal hazam kar lena jaez hai.
Lekin Qur'an ne sab Yahoodiyon ko aisi sifat se nahi nawaza balke kuchh achhe bhi the.
Sawal ye bhi paida hota hai ke kuchh Musalman hazrat ye bhi kahte hain ke ghair Muslim ya Kafir ki amanat par qabza jamana jaez hai????
Islam mein qataan ye jaez nahi. Doosron ke maal ka ehteram karna lazim wa zaroori hai. Ahadis mulaheza farmayen.
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜
----------------------------------------------

_*MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!*_
🙇 💰
Imam Sajjad (as):
*عليكم بادآء الامانة فوالذى بعث محمدا بالحق نبيالو ان قاتل ابى الحسين بن على بن ابى طالب ائتمننى على السيف الذى قتله به لا ديته اليه.*
💰
_"Amanat ada karna tum sab par lazim hai. Qasam hai us Khuda ki jisne Muhammad (sa) ko Haq ke sath maboos kiya. Agar mere walid Husain bin Ali bin Abi Talib (as) ka qatil wohi talwaar jis se usne shaheed kiya hai mere pas bataur amanat rakhta (aur mein qubool jar leta) to (bhi) mein uski Amanat use ada kar deta."_
(Amali-e-Sadooq, P-149)
💰
Imam Sadiq (as):
*"ان لله لم يبعث نبيا قط الا بصدق الحديث و ادآء الامانة مؤداتا الى البر و الفاجر."*
_"Khuda be kisi Paighambar ko maboos nahi kiya magar ye ke har nek o bad ke sath rast goi (sach bolna) aur Amanat ki adaygi uske programo mein shamil thi."_
(Mishkatul Anwar, Safeenatul Bihar)
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜
----------------------------------------------
*27th Shawwal 1437, 1st August 2016, Monday,

BAZM-E-ADAB WELCOMES YOU*

        ♦ _*JHOOTI QASAM*_ ♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (368)

*بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ*

*إِنَّ الَّذِينَ يَشْتَرُونَ بِعَهْدِ اللَّهِ وَأَيْمَانِهِمْ ثَمَنًا قَلِيلًا أُولَٰئِكَ لَا خَلَاقَ لَهُمْ فِي الْآخِرَةِ وَلَا يُكَلِّمُهُمُ اللَّهُ وَلَا يَنْظُرُ إِلَيْهِمْ يَوْمَ الْقِيَامَةِ وَلَا يُزَكِّيهِمْ وَلَهُمْ عَذَابٌ أَلِيمٌ*

_"Beshak woh log jo apne Ahd aur Qasam ko mamooli qeemat par bech dete hain unka Akherat mein koi hissa nahi hai aur Khuda unse Kalam nahi karega aur Qayamat ke din unki taraf nigahe Rehmat nahi karega aur unhe gunah ki kasafat se paak nahi karega aur unke liye dardnak Azaab hai."_
(Surah Aal-e-Imran: 77)

📚📖
👉 _* Tafseer:*_
Qur'an is baat par zor de raha hai ke jo log mamooli baat par Khuda ki jhooti Qasam khate rahte hain unke liye dardnak Azaab hai. Agar sab sachhe Musalman ho jaye to Court Affidavit Document ki koi zaroorat na ho. Kiyonki use is baat par yaqeen hoga ke jhooti Qasam ka anjaam kiya hoga. Ek Momin ka doosre Momin par bharosa karna farz hai, lekin jab sahi mano mein Momin hon. Jhooti Qasam jab khayega jab dil mein Allah wa Qayamat ke din par yaqeen nahi hoga. Aisa shakhs zahir mein Musalman dikhayi dega lekin dil se munafiq hoga. Usko Duniya se zyada lagao rahega aur har waqt yehi sochega jitna zyada ho sake chhal kapat se doosron ki zamin par qabza karun aur ye bhool jata hai ke Maut anqareeb hai, Khuda se bhi milna hai.
Ye mukhtasar ahadis ka khulasa tha.
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜
----------------------------------------------

_*MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!*_
🙇
Rasoole Akram (sa):
_"Jo shakhs jhooti Qasam kha kar apne Musalman bhai ke maal par qabza kare to jab woh Khuda ke huzoor mein hazir hoga to Allah us par naraaz hoga."_
(Majmaul Bayan)

Imam Baqir (as) ayat (3:77) ke zel mein  farmate hain:
_"Jiska Akherat mein hissa tak na ho to woh Jannat mein Akhir kaise jayga ?"_
(Tafseer Noorus Saqlain)
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜
----------------------------------------------
*28th Shawwal 1437, 2nd August 2016, Tuesday,
🔹🔹🔹🔹🔹🔹🔹🔹🔹🔹

BAZM-E-ADAB WELCOMES YOU*

⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜
      ♦ _*TAURET MEIN TAHREEF*_ ♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (370)

*بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ*

*وَإِنَّ مِنْهُمْ لَفَرِيقًا يَلْوُونَ أَلْسِنَتَهُمْ بِالْكِتَابِ لِتَحْسَبُوهُ مِنَ الْكِتَابِ وَمَا هُوَ مِنَ الْكِتَابِ وَيَقُولُونَ هُوَ مِنْ عِنْدِ اللَّهِ وَمَا هُوَ مِنْ عِنْدِ اللَّهِ وَيَقُولُونَ عَلَى اللَّهِ الْكَذِبَ وَهُمْ يَعْلَمُونَ*

_"In (Yahood) mein kuchh aise log bhi hain jo (Khuda ki) Kitab ki tilawat ke waqt apni zaban yun pherte hain ke tum guman karne lago ke (jo kuchh woh padh rahe hain) Kitab e Khuda mein se hai halanke woh Kitab e Khuda mein se nahi hota (Yahan tak ke woh sarahat se) kahte hain ke ye Khuda ki taraf se hai. Jabke woh Khuda ki taraf se nahi hota aur woh Khuda par Jhoot bandhte hain. Halanke jabke hain."_
(Surah Aal-e-Imran: 78)

📚📖 😏 🤔
👉 _* Tafseer:*_
'Yalwoona' يلؤن yani zaban ko bigadh aur tedha kar ke bolna. Yahoodi is tarah ter kechhte the aur Khud sakhta Tauret ki ayaton ko Khuda ka kalam kahte the. Allah ne inhe jhoota qarar diya.
Jo baat Allah ki taraf se na ho aur use Allah ki taraf mansoob karna ye Allah par tohmat hai. Usi tarah ye bhi hai ke jo fe'l Paighambar ya Imam ne nahi kiya ho use karna ye bhi unke uper tohmat hogi. Tauret mein Yahoodiyon ne raddo badal kar diya aur usko Allah ka Kalam kahne lage. Lekin Qur'an ke nazool ne uski asliyat batayi, lekin Qur'an mein ajtak koi Tehreef nahi hui kiyonki iska muhafiz Allah hai. Haan Rasool (sa) ke bayanat ko Musalmano ne apne hisab se tod madod kar pesh karna shuru kiya. Isliye Ahadis mein sahi aur ghalat mein tashkhees karna mushkil ho gaya. Tauret ki tarah wohi haal hota agar Imam ka wujood na hota. Koi bhi Kitab baghair teacher ke samajh mein nahi aa sakti. Isliye har zamane mein Imam ka wujood raha aur aaj tak hai. Nahi to Deen-e-Islam kab ka mit gaya hota. Deen ka khud wujood hi Imam ke wujood ko sabit kart hai.
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜
----------------------------------------------

_*MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!*_
🙇 👺
Rasule Khuda (saww):
_"Jo kisi Momin ya Momena par Bohtaan (tohmat / slander / allegation) lagaaye ya uski nisbat wo baat kahe jo usme nahi hai, to Khuda usko Aag ki pushht par jagah dega."_
(Jaame ul Akhbaar, p262)
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜

*30th Shawwal 1437, 4th August 2016, Thursday,

       ♦ _*TAWHEED*_ ♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (371)

*بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ*

*مَا كَانَ لِبَشَرٍ أَنْ يُؤْتِيَهُ اللَّهُ الْكِتَابَ وَالْحُكْمَ وَالنُّبُوَّةَ ثُمَّ يَقُولَ لِلنَّاسِ كُونُوا عِبَادًا لِي مِنْ دُونِ اللَّهِ وَلَٰكِنْ كُونُوا رَبَّانِيِّينَ بِمَا كُنْتُمْ تُعَلِّمُونَ الْكِتَابَ وَبِمَا كُنْتُمْ تَدْرُسُونَ * وَلَا يَأْمُرَكُمْ أَنْ تَتَّخِذُوا الْمَلَائِكَةَ وَالنَّبِيِّينَ أَرْبَابًا ۗ أَيَأْمُرُكُمْ بِالْكُفْرِ بَعْدَ إِذْ أَنْتُمْ مُسْلِمُونَ*

_"Kisi shakhs ko zeb nahi deta ke Khuda Aasmani Kitab, hukm aur Nabuwwat use de aur phir woh logon se kahta phire ke Khuda ko chhod kar meri Ibaadat karo, (balke us ke shayane shaan ye hai ke woh kahe) Khuda wale bano  jaisa ke Kitab e Khuda ki Ta'leem hai aur jaise tumne dars padha hai (aur Khuda ke alawa kisi ki parastish na karo)."_
_"Aur na ye ke tumhe hukm de ke Farishton aur Anbiya ko apna Parwardegar bana lo. To kiya woh tumhe Kufr ki taraf dawat deta hai jabke tum Musalman ho chuke ho."_
(Surah Aal-e-Imran: 79 - 80)

📚📖
👉 _* Tafseer:*_
Christian ne Hazrat Esa (as) ko Khuda aur Khuda ka beta bana diya jabke khud H. Esa (as) ne aisa koi dawa nahi kiya balke woh us Khuda ki Ibaadat karte the jo unka Khaliq hai. Kisi Nabi ya Imam ne kabhi Khudai ka dawa nahi kiya. Ayat ka lahja ye hai ke ye common sense hai ke jo Nabi Khuda ki taraf bula raha ho apne aap ko Khuda kaise kahega. Yahoodiyon ne Hazrat Ozair ko Khuda ka beta mana, Jahil Arabo Farishton ko Khuda ki betiya mante the. Musalmano ka ye shewa nahi ki woh kisi shakhs/shakhsiyat ki pooja kare.

Nusairi Hazrat Ali (as) ko Khuda manne lage, aaj bhi Alawi Shia firqa baqaeda unki parastish karta hai (Syria, Iraq, Turkey, Macedonia, Bosnia mein)

(YouTube par unki Ibaadat ke video dekh sakte hain, Misal ke taur par:
*Demal Cemevi Semah (Turkey)*
Cemevi means Ali ki Ibaadatgah
https://youtu.be/GK0eV1wsH4k ).

Jange Naherwan Hazrat Ali (as) ne Nusairiyon se ladi. Nusairi se Ali (as) ne kaha agar tum mujhe Khuda kahoge to qatl kar donga, usne kaha: kar do. Ali (as) qatl kar diya, phir zinda kiya. Usne kaha ab to Pura yaqeen ho gaya. Ali (as) ne kaha lekin mein Khuda ka banda hun, jo kaam karta ho Allah ki ijazat se karta hun. Lekin woh nahi maane aur wasil e Jahannam hue.

Jab Hazrat Ali (as) Anbar (Iraq) pahunche to wahan ke kisan Murawweja tariqe ke mutabiq aapke samne sajde mein gir pade. Ali (as) naraaz aur ghazabnak hue aur farmaya: 'Ye sab kiya hai?'
Woh bole "Badshahon ke samne aise hi pesh aate hain"
Ali (as) ne farmaya:
_"BaKhuda tumhare Chief aur Hukkam ko is amal se koi fayda nahi pahunchta aur tum apne aap ko isse Duniya mein ranj o takleef mein mubtela karte ho aur Akherat mein badbakhti mein giraftar karte ho. Kis qadr nuqsandeh hai wo takleef o mushaqqat ke jis ke baad Azaab e Khuda bhi ho aur kis qadr fayda bakhsh hai aur Araam o azaadi jis ke saath aatish e Jahannam se bhi amaan hasil ho."_

Jo Shia Hazrat ajkal Imam (as) ke age 'jjh' lagane lage hain woh in baaten par ghaur karen. Jo Imam ko had se zyada badhate hain unhe 'Ghulat' kaha jata hai. Jo fazail ko kam kare unhe 'Muqassir' kahte hain. Bas hamare liye beech ka rasta hai. Har kam limit mein hona chahiye. Aaj ki ayat inhi baaten par roshni dalti hai.
(Tafseere Namoona & Noorus Saqlain)
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜
----------------------------------------------

_*MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!*_
🙇
Imam Raza (as) from 7th, 6th, 5th, 4th, 3rd, 2nd, 1st Imam:
Rasoole Khuda (sa):
_"Mujhe mere Haq se buland na karo. Allah ne mujhe Nabi banane se pahle apna Abd (عبد) banaya, phir Nabi (نبى) banaya."_
(Uyoonul Akhbare Raza, Tafseere Noorus Saqlain)

♦ _*AHD O PAIMAN (COVENANT)*_ ♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (372)

*بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ*

*وَإِذْ أَخَذَ اللَّهُ مِيثَاقَ النَّبِيِّينَ لَمَا آتَيْتُكُمْ مِنْ كِتَابٍ وَحِكْمَةٍ ثُمَّ جَاءَكُمْ رَسُولٌ مُصَدِّقٌ لِمَا مَعَكُمْ لَتُؤْمِنُنَّ بِهِ وَلَتَنْصُرُنَّهُ ۚ قَالَ أَأَقْرَرْتُمْ وَأَخَذْتُمْ عَلَىٰ ذَٰلِكُمْ إِصْرِي ۖ قَالُوا أَقْرَرْنَا ۚ قَالَ فَاشْهَدُوا وَأَنَا مَعَكُمْ مِنَ الشَّاهِدِينَ*

_"Wo waqt (yaad karo) jab Khuda ne Anbiya (aur unke pairokaron se) ye takeedi Ahd o Paiman (Covenant) liya ke jab tumhe Kitab o Hikmat de dun iske baad tumhare paas ek Paighambar aye jo uski tasdeeq kare jo tumhare paas hai to us par Imaan le aana aur uski madad karna (phir Khuda ne un se) kaha: 'kiya is cheez ka iqrar karte ho aur us par Takeedi Ahd o Paiman bandhe ho. Unhone kaha: (Ji haan) ham iqrar karte hain. (Khuda ne unse) kaha: (Is Muqaddas Ahd o Paiman par) gawah raho aur mein bhi tumhare saath gawah (Witness) hun."_
(Surah Aal-e-Imran: 81)

📚📖
👉 _* Tafseer:*_
Allah ne har Nabi aur unke pairokar se Ahd liya ke unke baad jo Nabi (ya unke Janasheen) ayen unki Tasdeeq karen aur unki Vilayat ka Iqrar karen. Is tarah har Nabi ka iqrar ka silsila ek ke baad ek Hazrat Muhammad (sa) tak pahunchta hai aur phir Vilayat e Ali (as) ka Iqrar.
Imam Baqir (as):
_"........ Lekin ummaton ne is misaq e Ilahi par amal nahi kiya aur tamam sabqa ummaton be aane wale Nabiyon ki Mukhalefat ki."_
(Tafseer Ayyashi)
Faiz bin Abi Shaiba ki rivayat:
Imam Sadiq (as):
(Is ayat ke zel mein)
_"....... Allah ne Anbiya (as) se Rasoole Khuda (sa) par Imaan lane aur Ameerul Mo'menin (as) ki madad karne ka wada liya tha."_
Ravi ne jab ولتنصرنه (aur unki madad karna) ke bare mein sawal kiya to farmaya:
_"Ji haan Hazrat Adam (as) se lekar Hazrat Esa (as) tak jitne bhi Anbiya aye hain wo Duniya mein laut kar ayenge aur Ameerul Mo'menin (as) ki fauj mein shamil ho kar jang karenge."_
(Tafseer Noorus Saqlain)
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜
----------------------------------------------

_*MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!*_
🙇
Imam Baqir (as):
_"Khuda Wande Aalam ne hamare Shiyo'n se hamari Wilayat ke iqraar liya hai jab ke wo Aalam e Zar mein the. Usne unse oos waqt Apni Rabubiyat aur H. Rasule Khuda (saww) ki Nabuwwat ka bhi iqraar le liya tha."_
(Al Kaafi, v2, p481)

Rasule Khuda (saww):
_"Jo shakhs ye chahta hai ke wo Jannat mein H. Khaleelullah (as) ke ghar ka hamsaya (padosi) ho aur Jahannum ki aag se mehfooz rahe to usko chahiye ke wo Ali ibne Abi Talib (as) se mohabbat kare aur uski Wilayat ka iqraar kare."_
(Amaali - Shaikh Toosi, v2, p365)
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜
----------------------------------------------
*2nd Zilqad 1437, 6th August 2016, Saturday,

BAZM-E-ADAB WELCOMES YOU*

♦ _*AHD O PAIMAN (COVENANT)*_ ♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (373)

Cont'd ......

*بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ*

*فَمَنْ تَوَلَّىٰ بَعْدَ ذَٰلِكَ فَأُولَٰئِكَ هُمُ الْفَاسِقُونَ*

_"Iske baad bhi jo apne Ahd se phir jaye wohi Fasiq (Nafarman) hai."_
(Surah Aal-e-Imran: 82)

📚📖
👉 _* Tafseer:*_
Ahadis o rivayat se jaisa ke hamne kal bataya ke Allah ne Aalam e zar mein har Nabi aur unke pairokar se Ahd liya ke unke baad jo Nabi aur unke Janasheen ayen unki Tasdeeq karen aur unki Vilayat ka Iqrar karen.
Aaj ki ayat mein ye zikr hai ke jisne is Vilayat ka inkar ya nafarmani ki woh Fasiq hai. Usne Ahd Shikni ki. Uska is Deen e Islam se koi wasta nahi.
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜
----------------------------------------------

_*MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!*_
🙇  📝
Imam Baqir (as):
_"Hamare aur Allah ke darmiyaan koi rishtedaari nahi hai. Allah ka qurb (nazdeeki) sirf aur sirf Allah ki ita'at karne mein hai. Jo koi Allah ki ita'at kare aur hamare saath mohabbat rakhe to uske paas hamari Wilayat hai."_
(Aqwaal e Masoomeen (as), p168)
📝
Imam Baqir (as):
_"Wilayat e Ali (as) ka itteba (follow / paalan) karna aur unki Wilayat ko tasleem karna tumhare umoor (affairs) ko pareshaan na hone dega, adl o insaaf ko tumse qaaem rakhega aur aakhir tumko Jannat mein pahu’ncha dega."_
(Irshadaat e Masumeen (as), p81)
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜
----------------------------------------------
*3rd Zilqad 1437, 7th August 2016, Sunday,

              ♦ _*ISLAM*_ ♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (374)

*بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ*

*أَفَغَيْرَ دِينِ اللَّهِ يَبْغُونَ وَلَهُ أَسْلَمَ مَنْ فِي السَّمَاوَاتِ وَالْأَرْضِ طَوْعًا وَكَرْهًا وَإِلَيْهِ يُرْجَعُونَ*

_"Kiya ye log Allah ke Deen ke siwa kuchh aur talash kar rahe hain jabke Aasman aur Zameen ke tamam rahne wale Usi ke samne Ikhtiyar ya Majboori se (Uske Hukm ke) samne sar Tasleem hain. Aur woh Uski taraf laut kar Jayenge."_
(Surah Aal-e-Imran: 83)

📚📖 🕌
👉 _* Tafseer:*_
Is ayat mein 'Islam' ka zikr hai. Poori Duniya ki khilqat Uske samne sar jukhai hai. Ye Kainat ka system Allah ke hukm par chal raha. Allah ki Vilayat (Authority) hai. Jaise Sunrise aur Sunset, Duniya ka rotation aur revolution, Solar System. Taaro (Stars) ka chamakna, Suraj ka chamakna....etc, ye sab Khuda ke hukm ke aage sar kham kiye hain Ikhtiyari ya ghair ikhtiyari taur par. Agar in mein se koi bhi Allah ki na sune to Nabudi aur Halakat ke siwa kuchh nahi. Means ye sab Musalman hain aur Allah ki Vilayat ka iqrar karte hain.. Kiyonke apne aapko Uske aage Submit kar diya hai.
Action do tarah ke hote hain:  (1) Takweeni (2) Tashreeii - Ikhtiyari. Jin Aamaal ya waaqeat mein khilqat ko ikhtiyar nahi wo Takweeni hai. Wo nizam machine ki tarah chalta rahta hai. Agar machine ka koi hissa kam na kare to machine mein kharabi paida hogi, aur nuqsan bhi hoga. Na karne ki yahan koi gunjaish nahi.
Tashreeii wo Aamaal hai jin ka ikhtiyar insaan ko hai kare ya na kare. Allah, Rasool aur Aimmah ki Vilayat ko qabool kare aur unki itteba (following) aur unki Shariyat par Amal kare:  Isko Tashreeii kahte hain. Ye hai Islam (Submission, Tasleem). Is tarah Poori  Kainate Takveen wa Tashreeii mein, jisne Vilayat ka iqrar kiya aur unke Ahkam par amal kiya,  unko kaha jayga Musalman. (Submitted Person).
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (375)

*بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ*

*قُلْ آمَنَّا بِاللَّهِ وَمَا أُنْزِلَ عَلَيْنَا وَمَا أُنْزِلَ عَلَىٰ إِبْرَاهِيمَ وَإِسْمَاعِيلَ وَإِسْحَاقَ وَيَعْقُوبَ وَالْأَسْبَاطِ وَمَا أُوتِيَ مُوسَىٰ وَعِيسَىٰ وَالنَّبِيُّونَ مِنْ رَبِّهِمْ لَا نُفَرِّقُ بَيْنَ أَحَدٍ مِنْهُمْ وَنَحْنُ لَهُ مُسْلِمُونَ*

_"kahdo, ke ham Allah par Imaan laye hain aur (is tarah) us par (bhi Imaan laye hain) jo ham par, Ibrahim (as) par, Ismail (as) par, Ishaq (as) par, Yaqoob (as) par aur Asbaat par nazil hua hai aur us par (bhi Imaan laye hain) jo Moosa (as), Esa (as) aur (doosre) Paighambaro ko Allah Ta'ala ki taraf se diya gaya hai, ham unke darmiyan farq nahi karte aur Uske (farman) ke samne Tasleem hain."_
(Surah Aal-e-Imran: 84)

📚📖
👉 _* Tafseer:*_
Jaisa ke hamne kal bataya Islam Mazhabe Tawheed hai. Sabhi Anbiya ki dawat Tawheed thi. Jab Alame Takveen mein Tawheed hi Tawheed nazar aati hai, to Aalam e Tashreeii mein bhi Anbiya (as) ne Tawheed ki dawat di. Lekin Anbiya ke pairov (followers) ka bhatak jana Rehbar ke dawat mein nuqs ka sabab nahi tha. Zamane ke hisab se ek ke baad doosre Nabi aate rahe. Anbiya mein koi farq nahi tha.
Asbat اسباط sabt سبط se hai yani kisi cheez ka phailao. Yahan Asbat se murad Hazrat Yaqoob ki Aulad jin mein Anbiya bhi the (Bani Israel).
Jaisa ke ayat se zahir hai sab Anbiya Musalman the. Musalman woh hai jo Tawheed par Imaan rakhta hai aur Uske Ahkam par Tasleem ho jata hai.

Imam Moosa Kazim (as):
"Is Ayat (3:83) ka talluq Qaem Ale Muhammad (atfs) se hai. Jab Aap Zahoor karenge to tamam Yahood o Nasara (Jews & Christians), Saebeen wa Zanaoqa, Murtaddeen aur Kuffar ko jama karke unke samne Islam ki dawat pesh karenge aur us waqt jo log khushi se Islam qabool karenge Aap unhe Namaz, Zakat aur doosre Ahkam e Islam par Amal karne ja hukm denge aur jo log inkar karenge to Aap unki gardane uda denge. Phir aisa waqt ayega ke Mashriq o Maghrib (East & West) mein sirf Tawheed parast afraad dikhayi denge."
(Ibne Kabir se rivayat Tafseer Noorus Saqlain)
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜
----------------------------------------------

(Amaali - Shaikh Sadooq, p611)

Kal ki corrected Hadis:
