                ♦ _*ISLAM*_ ♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (376)

*بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ*

*وَمَنْ يَبْتَغِ غَيْرَ الْإِسْلَامِ دِينًا فَلَنْ يُقْبَلَ مِنْهُ وَهُوَ فِي الْآخِرَةِ مِنَ الْخَاسِرِينَ*

_"Aur jo koi ISLAM (aur Hukm e Haq ke samne sar tasleem kham karne) ke alawa apne liye koi aur Deen intekhab kare to wo usse qubool nahi kiya jayega aur aisa shakhs Akherat mein nuqsan uthanewalon mein se hoga."_
(Surah Aal-e-Imran: 85)

📚📖
👉 _* Tafseer:*_
Jaisa ke pahle bata chuke hain puri Kainat ka system Khuda ke hukm ko follow kar raha hai. To jo Allah ke hukm ko follow kare wo Musalman, isliye poori Kainate Takveeni Musalman, sare Anbiya wa Imam  Musalman. Khuda ka pasandeeda Deen ISLAM.  Ab jo koi bhi Islam ke alawa koi aur tareeqa apnai wo Khuda ko follow nahi kar raha hai, isliye woh Akherat mein nuqsan uthayga kiyonki Akherat mein Usi Khuda se mulaqat hogi jisko wo Inkar kar raha tha.
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜
----------------------------------------------

_*MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!*_
🙇 🕌
Rasule Khuda (saww)
se puchha gaya:
_"Ya Rasulallah! Islam kya hai? Uski khususiyat bayaan farmayein"._
Aap (saww) ne farmaya: _"Islam uryiaa'n hai yaani baghair libaas hai uska libaas Taqwa hai, uski zeenat Hayaa aur Parhezgaari uska maalik aur uska kamaal hai. Uska phal (fruit) nek aamal hain aur har cheez ki ek buniyaad hai aur Islam ki buniyaad hum Ahlebait (as) ki mohabbat hai"._
(Amaali - Shaikh Toosi, v1, p221)
🕌
Riwayat:
Kuchh as'haab ne Rasule Khuda (saww) ki khidmat mein arz ki,
_"Ya Rasulallah (saww), kya hum se bhi koi behtar hai? Kyun ki hum ne Islam qubool kiya aur aap ki khidmat mein haazir reh kar Jihaad kiya"._ Aap (saww) ne farmaya: _"Haa'n tum se behtar meri ummat ke wo log hain jo mere baad paida honge aur mujh par Imaan layenge"._
(Hayaat ul Quloob, v2, p914)

              ♦ _*MURTAD*_ ♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (377)

*بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ*

*كَيْفَ يَهْدِي اللَّهُ قَوْمًا كَفَرُوا بَعْدَ إِيمَانِهِمْ وَشَهِدُوا أَنَّ الرَّسُولَ حَقٌّ وَجَاءَهُمُ الْبَيِّنَاتُ ۚ وَاللَّهُ لَا يَهْدِي الْقَوْمَ الظَّالِمِينَ*

_"Khuda in logon ko kiyonkar   Hidayat kare jo Imaan lane, Rasool ki Haqqaniyat ki gawahi dene aur unke liye wazeh nishaniyan aa jane ke baad kufr karen aur Khuda zalimo ko Hidayat nahi karta."_
(Surat Aal-E-Imran 86)

📚📖
👉 _* Tafseer:*_
Ab tak Islam ke bare mein tarruf karaya. Ab Murtad ke bare mein tazkara hoga. Woh Musalman jo kafir ho jaye use _Murtad_ kahte hain. Ye ترديد se bana hai yani rad رد karna means reject karna. Terminologically Kisi Musalman ka doosra mazhab ikhtiyar kar lena. Lekin koi insaan apne aap ko Musalman bhi kahe aur Islam ke arkan par etrazat kare ya Quran ki behurmati kare, murti pooja karne lage ye sab murtad kahlay jayenge. Murtad 2 tarah ke hote hain. Jo Paidaishi Musalman ho, yani uska ka gharana Musalman ho aur woh convert ho jaye to use _Murtad e Fitri_ kahte hain. Lekin jo doosre Mazhab se Musalman hua ho aur phir wapas doosre mazhab mein convert ho jaye ya la mazhab ho jaye use _Murtad e Milli_ kahte hain. Quran Murtad logon ki mazammat kar raha hai.
Iski tafseeli guftugu ki gunjaish nahi hai ham sirf ishara karte hain. Detail mein kitabon mein study karen.
Tarikh mein bahut se Mashhoor Murtad logon ka zikr hai. Jange Ridda mein Rasool ke baad do firqe wujood mein aye Shia aur Sunni. Dono ne ek doosre par Murtad ka ilzam lagay aur kafi khoon baha. Ek doosre par Kufr wa Murtad ka ilzam qatl o gharat ka sabab bhi bana. Sawal ye hai ke inhe qatl karne ki kis ne authority di.
Kuchh misal jin par Murtad ka ilzam laga ya sahi mein Murtad the aur unhe saza di gayi.
(1) Khalifa Bani Abbas Al Mansoor ne Abu Hanifa ko jail mein rakha aur wahi par unko zaher diya gaya (767 AD)
(Yaqubi, Vol 3, P-86, Murujuz Zaban, Vol 3, P269-270. Wikipedia.)
(2) Hallaj (A Sufi) ko Al Muqtadir ne saza di.
(3) Suhrawardi apne Ismaili sathiyon ke sath saza payi.
(4) Ibne Taymiyah (5) Dara Sikho ko Aurangzeb ne suli par chadhaya,....... etc.
Aur bahut lambi list hai.
Abhi haal mein Salman Rushdie, Taslima Nasrin, Bahai, Qadyani etc. Murtad ki misalen hai.
(To be Cont'd .......)
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜
----------------------------------------------

_*MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!*_

Imam (as) ne farmaya:
_"Use qatl kar dena chahiye"_
(Tehzibul Ahkam: Vol 10, P-139)

                        (Cont'd)

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (378)

*بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ*

*أُولَٰئِكَ جَزَاؤُهُمْ أَنَّ عَلَيْهِمْ لَعْنَةَ اللَّهِ وَالْمَلَائِكَةِ وَالنَّاسِ أَجْمَعِينَ * خَالِدِينَ فِيهَا لَا يُخَفَّفُ عَنْهُمُ الْعَذَابُ وَلَا هُمْ يُنْظَرُونَ*

_"Unki (Murtad) is ravish ka yahi badla hai ke un par Allah, Farishton aur tamam insaano ki Laanat hai."_
_"Woh hamesha is Laanat (aur phitkar) mein (mubtela) rahenge unke Azaab mein takhfeef (light) nahi hogi aur unhe muhlat nahi di jayegi."_
(Surah Aal-e-Imran: 87 - 88)

📚📖 🕌
👉 _* Tafseer:*_
Islam ke sabhi firqe Murtad ko ek Mujrim ki hasiyat se mante hain, aur in ke liye sakht saza muayyan ki hai, jis mein sare isteghfar ke raste band hone ke baad final saza qatl hai.
Lekin jaise ke hamne pahle bataya is ke Muslim hukmarano aur khud sakhta rehnomao ne iska political fayda bhi uthaya. Aaj bhi Pakistan, Saudi Arabia, Iran aur doosri Muslim country mein blasphemy rule ke tahet sazai hoti hain. Iske khilaf bahut se non-Muslim Humanitarian log awaz uthate rahte hain.
Kuchh had tak rule sahi hain lekin jahan najaez fayda uthaya jay ghalat hai.
Actual Islamic view dekha jaye to insaan ko Haq nahi kisi ko saza de. Ye Haq sirf Allah ke chune hue numaynde ka hai. Hazrat Ali (as) apni zahir Khilafat ke daur mein saza dete the to mujrim khush hota tha ke aaj mein paak ho gaya. Agar jang mein Ali (as) ki talwar chalti thi to naslon ko dekh leti thi. Ye aam insaan ke bas ke bahar hai, isliye insaan human right violation kar baithta hai.
Murtad aur Taqayya ya Kitman mein farq hai. Murtad janboojh kar mazhab badalta hai. Jabke Islam mein koi jabr nahi (Ayatal Kursi), isliye kisi ko bhi jabran apna Aqeeda manwana sahi nahi. Lekin agar koi kisi Musalman par jabr kare aur apni jan o izzat ki khatir zahiran waqtiya taur par Aqeeda badal de to koi harj nahi aur isko Taqayya kahte hain. Zyadatar Shiyon ne Khalifa Bani Abbas ke zamane mein Taqayya ke istemal kiya. Us waqt Khalifa ne Sadat ka qatle aam kiya, zinda diwaron mein chun diya gaya. Agar koi Ziyarat Imam Husain (as) ko jata to shart ye rahti thi ke agar do admi hain to ek ko shaheed hona padta, ya hath kate jate. Aise halat mein Sadat itne sakht Taqayye mein rahe ke baap apne bete ko apna asli Aqeeda zahir na kar saka. Is tarah jo aaj kuchh Shia Syed hain to kuchh Sunni Syed hain, is ki wajah yehi hai. Sadat Imam ki aulad hoti hai, to Syed hote hue Imam ko na mane ye ajeeb lagta hai lekin zamana guzarta gaya aur aulad sab bhoolti chali gayi.
Doosri baat ye ke rivayaton  ke mutabiq jahan jhoot bolne se kisi ki islah ho jaye ya kisi ki jaan, izzat o abru bach jaye jaez hai.
Aur ye Munafeqat bhi nahi kiyon ke Munafiq Musalman hote hue dil mein kund Aqeeda aur dushmane Islam rehta hai. Jabke Taqayya karne wala dil se Haq Aqeeda lekin zahir mein dushman ki ji huzoori mein rehta hai.
Ye tha Murtad, Munafiq, Taqayya karne wale mein farq.
Allah hame aise haalat se bachaye rakhe aur hame apne Aqeede par sabit qadam rakhe.
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜
----------------------------------------------

(Aasmani Nasihatein, v2, p238)

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (379)
🕌
*بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ*

*إِلَّا الَّذِينَ تَابُوا مِنْ بَعْدِ ذَٰلِكَ وَأَصْلَحُوا فَإِنَّ اللَّهَ غَفُورٌ رَحِيمٌ * إِنَّ الَّذِينَ كَفَرُوا بَعْدَ إِيمَانِهِمْ ثُمَّ ازْدَادُوا كُفْرًا لَنْ تُقْبَلَ تَوْبَتُهُمْ وَأُولَٰئِكَ هُمُ الضَّالُّونَ*
🕌
_"Albatta (Murtad hone baad) is Laanat se wo log mustasna (exempted) hain jo is ke baad TAUBA kar len aur apne tarz e Amal ki islah kar len. Beshak Allah Bakhshnewala, Meherban hai."_
_"Jo log Imaan lane ke baad Kafir ho gaye hain aur phir (apne) Kufr mein badh gaye hain (aur is raah mein israr karte hain) to unki Tauba kabhi bhi (jo majboori ki bena par ho ya marte waqt ki jaye) qubool nahi hogi aur woh (waqean) gumrah hain (aur woh Khuda ki rah bhi kho chuke hain aur Tauba ki bhi.)"_
(Surah Aal-e-Imran: 89 - 90)

📚📖
👉 _* Tafseer:*_
Murtad se mutalliq ayaton ka zikr hua. Iske shane nuzool mein ye waqea darj hai:
Ek shakhs Haris bin Suwaid bin Samit ne Muhazzar bin Ziyad ka qatl kiya. Phir saza se bachne ke liye usne Deen e Islam chhod diya aur bhag kar Mecca chala gaya. Phir kuchh time ke baad wo naadim hua (repented) aur Tauba ki khwahish ki. Rasoolullah (sa) ne uski Tauba qubool ki aur wo baad mein ek achha Musalman sabit hua.'
(Majmaul Bayan, Tafseer e Noorus Saqlain)
Allah Bakhshnewala, Meherban hai, woh Tauba ko qubool karta hai. Lekin jo wapas nahi palat ta aur apne Kufr par musir rahta hai uske liye Tauba ka raasta band ho jata hai.
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜
----------------------------------------------

_*MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!*_
🙇
Rasule Khuda (saww):
_"Tum mein behtareen wo log hain jo khata ke baad Tauba karein."_
(Hadiyat ush Shia, p41)

Rasule Khuda (saww):
_"Tauba ke liye naadim hona (pachhtana / remorse) hi kaafi hai."_
(Hadiyat ush Shia, p8)

Imam Ali (as):
_"Gunaho'n ka tark (avoid) karna Tauba karne se zyada behtar hai."_
(Meezan ul Hikmah, v1, p807)

Imam Ali (as):
_"Jo Tauba karta hai Khuda uski Tauba ko qubool farmata hai aur uske a'aza o jawaareh (organs and limbs) ko hukm hota hai ke uski parda-poshi karein, zameen ke hisso'n ko hukm diya jaata hai ke uske oyuub (aibo'n) ko chhupayein aur gunah qalam-bund karne (likhne) waalo'n ke haafize (memory) se wo gunah hataa diye jaate hain."_
(Meezan ul Hikmah, v1, p808)

                  ♦ _*KUFR*_ ♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (379)

*بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ*

*إِنَّ الَّذِينَ كَفَرُوا وَمَاتُوا وَهُمْ كُفَّارٌ فَلَنْ يُقْبَلَ مِنْ أَحَدِهِمْ مِلْءُ الْأَرْضِ ذَهَبًا وَلَوِ افْتَدَىٰ بِهِ ۗ أُولَٰئِكَ لَهُمْ عَذَابٌ أَلِيمٌ وَمَا لَهُمْ مِنْ نَاصِرِينَ*

_"Jo log Kafir ho gaye aur halate Kufr mein mar gaye, zameen agar sone se pur ho aur woh use (apne gunahon ke kaffare ke taur par) fidya kar de to bhi un se ye hargiz qubool nahi kiya jayega aur unke liye dardnak Azaab hai aur unka koi yawar o madadgar nahi."_
(Surah Aal-e-Imran: 91)
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜

🙇

👉 _Logo'n par zyadati karna,_
👉 _Khairaat karne aur neki karne ki aadat chhor dena,_
👉 _Kufraane Ne'mat karna, Shukr e Khuda na bajaa laana."_

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (380)

*بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ*

*لَنْ تَنَالُوا الْبِرَّ حَتَّىٰ تُنْفِقُوا مِمَّا تُحِبُّونَ ۚ وَمَا تُنْفِقُوا مِنْ شَيْءٍ فَإِنَّ اللَّهَ بِهِ عَلِيمٌ*
(Surah Aal-e-Imran: 92)

*اَلسَّلَامُ عَلَیْكَ یَا غَرِیْبَ الْغُرَبَاۤءِ اَلسَّلَامُ عَلَیْكَ یَا سُلْطَانَ اَبَا الْحَسَنِ عَلِیَّ ابْنَ مُوْسَی الرِّضَا وَ رَحْمَۃُ اللہِ وَ بَرَكَاتُہٗ۔*
📚📖
Mamoon ne Imam Reza (as) ko Madina se Toos (Mashhad - Iran) bulaya.
Nishapur jo Ilm ka Markaz tha Tamam Musalman (Shia aur Sunni) aur Raviyan wa Ulema jama hue aur Imam ka welcome kiya. Un logon ki request par Imam (as) ne unko ek Hadis ka tohfa diya jis ko 'Silselatuz Zahab' (Golden Chain) kaha jata hai. Ye chain Imam se lekar Rasool (sa) tak pahunchti hai aur Gibrael (as) ye Allah ki Hadis farmayi:
*كلمة لا إله إلا الله حصني فمن قالها دخل حصني  ومن دخل حصني أمن من عذابي*

_"Kalma-e-La ilaha illal lah mera Qila hai, jo is mein dakhil ho gaya mere Azaab se bach gaya."_
Imam kuchh der ruke phir farmaya:

*لکن بشرطھا وشروطھا و أنأ من شروطھا*
_*"Lekin kuchh sharten (conditions) hain. Aur mein un sharayt mein se hun."*_

(Means without Ahle Bait (as) Kalma pura nahi ho sakta. Kalma Vilayat ke bina adhoora hai.)

Imam Ali Raza (as) once passed from the city of Nisha Pur on his way to Toos (Toos is present day Mashhad). The Caliph Mamun Rashid had summoned the Imam with the intention of getting him killed. Nishapur was the centre of knowledge, jurisprudence, theology and hadith those days, so some of the famous hadith collectors came out to see the son of the Prophet, they entreated the Imam to come out of his caravan and narrate for them a hadith of the Holy Prophet, which they could write down and remember, they took the chance of meeting the son of the Holy Prophet(saw) as a blessing.

After much insistence the Imam(as) showed the light of his face and narrated a tradition known as Hadis-e-Silsila-Tuz-Zahab (Chain of Gold) because all the narrators in the chain of this hadith are infallibles.

The Imam said “My father Musa Al Kazim heard from his father Jaffar us Sadiq.. who heard from his father Muhammad Al-Baqir, who narrated from his father Zain-ul-Abideen who narrated from his father Sayyed us Shuhada Imam Hussein(as) who narrated from Amir ul Momineen Imam Ali(as) that Rasool Allah said “Gibrael said to me that Allah says .. My kalima La illaha il lallah is my fort.. whoever says it enters my fort.. and whoever enters my fort shall be safe”

The Imam paused for a while, then said the famous words:

*But there are certain conditions for this, and I am one of the conditions.*

Meaning saying that you believed in God and his Prophet was not enough to enter Allah’s fort and find amaan (peace), the Iqrar of Wilayat had become a necessary element for the completion of faith.

About twenty thousand writers have narrated this tradition.
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜
----------------------------------------------

_*MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!*_
🙇
🎸🎧🎼🎹🎷🎺🎤🎧🎻
Imam Reza (as):
_"Jis shakhs ke ghar mein dhol, baa'nsuri ya geet-sangeet ki koi bhi cheez ya shatranj 40 din tak rahe to wo shakhs Allah ke Gazab (gusse) ko daawat deta hai."_
(Greater Sins II)
🙇�
Imam Reza (as):
_"Jab log naye naye gunah karte hain to nayi nayi balaao'n mein mubtela hote hain."_
(Aqwaal e Masoomeen (as), p152)

            ♦ _*NEK TOHFA*_ ♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu
🎁
Start your Day by reading Quran: (381)

*بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ*

*لَنْ تَنَالُوا الْبِرَّ حَتَّىٰ تُنْفِقُوا مِمَّا تُحِبُّونَ ۚ وَمَا تُنْفِقُوا مِنْ شَيْءٍ فَإِنَّ اللَّهَ بِهِ عَلِيمٌ*

_"Neki ka maqam us waqt tak hargiz tumhe hasil na hoga, jab tak Mehboob cheezon mein se kuchh Allah ki rah mein kharch na karo, aur jo kuchh bhi tum kharch karoge to Allah usse ba khabar hai."_
(Surah Aal-e-Imran: 92)

📚📖 🎁
👉 _* Tafseer:*_
Is ayat ke zel kuchh ahadis mulaheza hon:

Imam Sadiq (as):
_"Allah ki rah mein raddi aur nakara (bhangar) cheezen nahi deni chahiye, balke aisi cheez di jaye jo insaan ko khud bhi achhi lagti ho."_
(Rauatul Kafi, Tafseer Noorus Saqlain)
🎁
Hazrat Ali (as) ne ek kapda khareeda, aap ko achha laga to aapne Allah ki rah mein de diya. Aur farmaya:
_"Maine Rasoole Akram (sa) se suna tha ke jo Khuda ki REZA ko apne nafs ki REZA par tarjeeh (prefer) dega to Allah bhi Qayamat ke din use Jannat ke liye tarjeeh dega. Jise koi cheez pasand aa jaye use Allah ki rah mein de de to Allah Ta'ala Qayamat ke din farmayega ke log Duniya mein rahkar ek doosre ke Tohfe (Gift) ke badle mein Tohfe diya karte the. Aaj Mein teri Neki ke badle tujhe Jannat ka Tohfa deta hun."_
(Majmaul Bayan, Abil Tufail se rivayat, Tafseer Noorus Saqlain)
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜
----------------------------------------------

_*MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!*_
🙇 🎁
Imam Sadiq (as) ne Mufazzal bin Umar se farmaya:
_"Mufazzal! Mein tumhare kisi Hadye ka na to zaroorat mand hun aur na hi mujhe iski khwahish hai albatta ham tumhara hadiya (Khums-Sahme Imam) isliye qubool karte hain taake tumhara maal paak ho jaye. Aur maine apne Walid Imam Baqir (as) se suna tha ke hamara manne wala (Shia) agar ek saal tak thoda ya bahut hame hadiya na de to Qayamat ke din Khuda us par Nazare Shafqat nahi karega."_
(Tafseer e Ayyashi)

             ♦ _*HALAL FOOD*_ ♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (382)

*بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ*

*كُلُّ الطَّعَامِ كَانَ حِلًّا لِبَنِي إِسْرَائِيلَ إِلَّا مَا حَرَّمَ إِسْرَائِيلُ عَلَىٰ نَفْسِهِ مِنْ قَبْلِ أَنْ تُنَزَّلَ التَّوْرَاةُ ۗ قُلْ فَأْتُوا بِالتَّوْرَاةِ فَاتْلُوهَا إِنْ كُنْتُمْ صَادِقِينَ*

_"Tamam (Paak) ghizain Bani Israel ke liye Halal thi siwai unke jinhe (Jababe) Israel (Yaqoob as) ne Taurat ke Nuzool se pahle apne liye Haram qarar diya tha. (Misal ke taur par oont (camel) ka gosht jo unke liye nuqsandeh tha). Unse kaho agar tum (apne etraz mein) sachche ho to lao Taurat aur padho (ye ghalat baaten jo tum pichhle Anbiya ki taraf mansoob karte ho, tumhari tehreef shudah Taurat mein bhi nahi hain.)"_
(Surah Aal-e-Imran: 93)

📚📖 🍩🍔🍗🍤
👉 _* Tafseer:*_
Khane peene ke maamle mein Islamic Shariyat ne bahut si Hidayat di hain. Islam mein HALAL FOOD khana hi jaez qarar diya hai.
Qur'an ki is ayat ke mutabiq Asli Yahoodiyon (Ultra Orthodox, Haredi Judaism) mein bhi ye Islami qanoon Taurat mein bhi the. Aaj bhi asl Yahoodi in Ahkam ko follow karte hai.
Iski detail is link ko open karke padhen:

http://en.m.wikipedia.org/wiki/Kosher_foods

e.g.:
Present Taurat 'Safar La Dian', Chap 11 mein hai:
_"Jugali karne wale aur phate hue sum wale janwaron ko na khao aur oont (camel) bawajood ye ke jugali karta hai magar uska sum phata hua nahi hai, wo tumhare liye Haram hai."_

Yahoodiyon mein bhi kai firqe (sects) hai, aaj bhi asli Yahoodi jo Rabbi kahlate hain inhi Ahkam ko follow karte hain. Inke yahan Tauret mein zibha ka tareeqa Islam se milta julta hai, link mein dekhen. Is tarah se zibha kiye hue Halal Food ko wo KOSHER FOOD kahte hain. Ye sab jagah balke India mein bhi milta hai.
Inke barkhilaf Talmud Sect ka tareeqa alag hai.

Isse ye pata chalta hai ke hamara Deen Islam wohi Deen e Haneef hai jo kal tha, jo Hazrat Yaqoob ki Shariyat thi, lekin baad wali qaum ne use tabdeel kar diya.
Qur'an woh Kitab hai jo pichhle Anbiya ki kitabon ki Tasdeeq karti hai.
Hame bhi Halal o Haram khane mein ehtiyat baratni chahiye.
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜
----------------------------------------------

_*MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!*_
🙇 🍗🍖
Imam Sadiq (as):
_"Apni kamaai ko paak karo taake tumhari Dua qubool ho, kyunki Ek Haraam luqma khaane se 40 din tak Dua qubool nahi hoti."_
(Meezan ul Hikmah, v3)
🍛🍲
Imam Sadiq (as):
_"Bachcho'n ke liye Halaal Rizq kamana Allah ki raah mein Jihad karne ke barabar hai."_
(Almustashaar Abdul Haleem Jundi (Misri), p222)
🐐
Imam Kazim (as):
_"Ghar ke kisi paale huwe jaanwar ki qurbaani na ki jaaye."_
(Man La Yahzarahul Faqih, v2, p294)
🦄
Rasule Khuda (saww):
_"Apni Qurbaani ke zibah ke waqt haazir raho, kyun ki jab Qurbaani ke jaanwar ke khoon ka pehla qatra zameen par girta hai to uski barkat se Khuda har gunah aur har lagzish (galati) maaf kar deta hai…"_
(Wasaail ush Shia, v10, p120)
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜

           ♦ _*DEEN E HANEEF*_ ♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (383)

*بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ*

*فَمَنِ افْتَرَىٰ عَلَى اللَّهِ الْكَذِبَ مِنْ بَعْدِ ذَٰلِكَ فَأُولَٰئِكَ هُمُ الظَّالِمُونَ * قُلْ صَدَقَ اللَّهُ ۗ فَاتَّبِعُوا مِلَّةَ إِبْرَاهِيمَ حَنِيفًا وَمَا كَانَ مِنَ الْمُشْرِكِينَ*

_"Iske baad bhi jo log apni ghadhi hui baaten Khuda ki taraf mansoob karte hain (aur woh jan boojh kar aisa karte hain) wohi dar haqeeqat Zalim hain."_
_"Kah do, Allah ne sach farmaya. Tum Millat e Ibrahim ka itteba (follow) karo aur woh Batil se kinara kash the (Haneef) aur woh Mushrekin mein se nahi the."_
(Surah Aal-e-Imran: 94 - 95)

📚📖
👉 _* Tafseer:*_
Jaisa ke silsilewar ham explain kar chuke hain ke puri Takvini Kainat Musalman hai, sare Anbiya bhi Musalman Kiyonki sab baghair chun wa chera Allah ki itteba (follow) kar rahe hain.
Kal hamne Yahoodiyon ki kuchh misalen din jin Halaal Food (Kosher Food) ki jo ke aaj bhi raej hai. Isse ye pata chalta hai ke Pichhle Anbiya ke zamane mein jo Deen tha, khas kar Hazrat Ibrahim (as) ka Deen jisko Deen e Haneef kaha gaya hai woh Islam tha. Deen e Hanif yani jis mein koi butparasti (idol worship) ka inclination (mael) na ho.
To read in detail click on the link:
https://en.m.wikipedia.org/wiki/Hanif

Jahiliyat ke zamane mein Arab apne aap par Ibrahim (as) ke follower hone par fakhr karte the. Kaaba buton se bhara tha, jis mein ek murti Ibrahim (as) ki bhi thi. Imran ke farzand Hazrat Ali (as) ne Hazrat Ibrahim (as) ki sunnat ko follow karte hue Kaaba ko buton se saaf kiya aur sab buton ko toda. Jiska Arabo ne oppose kiya, jaise Nimrod ke chahne walon ne kiya tha.
Is liye Hamare Rasool (saww) aur unke Ahle Bait (as) ne usi sunnat e Ibrahim (as) ko zinda kiya jiski buniyad Tawheed hai. Ibrahim (as) Mushrekin mein se nahi the. Isliye Ale Ibrahim mein Ale Imraan bhi kabhi Mushrik nahi thi. Hazrat Ismail (as) ki nasal Janabe Hashim aur unke baad Abdullah wa Abu Talib (Imran), sab Millate Ibrahim par qaem the. Be'sat ke pahle Shariyat e Ibrahim (as) par ye khandaan amal karta tha aur un mein se koi but parast nahi tha.
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜
----------------------------------------------

_*MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!*_
🙇
Imam Husain (as):
_"Millat e Ibrahim par sirf ham aur hamare Shia hain. Apne aur Shiyon ke alawa mujhe koi bhi Millat e Ibrahim par dikhai nahi deta."_
(Tafseer e Ayyashi & Tafseer e Noorus Saqlain mein Hababa wal Bayya se rivayat)

Riwayat:
_Kuchh as'haab ne Rasule Khuda (saww) ki khidmat mein arz ki, "Ya Rasulallah (saww), kya hum se bhi koi behtar hai? Kyun ki hum ne Islam qubool kiya aur aap ki khidmat mein haazir reh kar Jihaad kiya". Aap (saww) ne farmaya, "Haa'n tum se behtar meri ummat ke wo log hain jo mere baad paida honge aur mujh par Imaan layenge"._
(Hayaat ul Quloob, v2, p914)

Rasule Khuda (saww):
_"In logo'n ko kya ho gaya hai ke jab unke saamne H. Ibrahim (as) ki aal ka zikr kiya jaata hai to ye khush ho jaate hain aur jab unke saamne Aal e Muhammad (as) ka zikr kiya jaata hai to unke chehre khauf-zada ho jaate hain aur unke dilo'n mein nafrat paida ho jaati hai? Mujhe qasam hai Oos Zaat ki Jiske qabza e qudrat mein Muhammad (saww) ki jaan hai, agar koi shakhs Qayamat ke roz 70 Ambiya ke barabar amal lekar bargaah e Khuda mein haazir hoga aur uske dil mein meri aur mere Ahlebait (as) ki Wilayat na hogi to uska koi amal bhi qubool nahi kiya jayega."_
(Amaali - Shaikh Toosi, v1, p367), (Amaali - Shaikh Mufeed, p190)
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜

          ♦ _*MECCA - BEKKAH*_ ♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (384)

*بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ*

*إِنَّ أَوَّلَ بَيْتٍ وُضِعَ لِلنَّاسِ لَلَّذِي بِبَكَّةَ مُبَارَكًا وَهُدًى لِلْعَالَمِينَ*

_"Pahla ghar jo logon (aur Khuda se tazarro wakiya  khushu) ke liye muqarrar kiya gaya hai wo sar zameen e Mekkah mein hai jo ba barkat hai aur Duniya ke liye Hidayat o Rehbari ka sabab hai."_
(Surah Aal-e-Imran: 96)
(Dua-e-Nudba)

📚📖 🕋
👉 _* Tafseer:*_
Khane Kaaba Allah ka woh pahla Ghar hai jo zameen par tameer hua. Tarikh mein hai ke isko sab se pahle Hazrat Adam (as) ne Allah ke hukm se tameer kiya. Lekin Tufan e Nooh (as) ke zamane mein kuchh nuqsan pahuncha. Hazrat Ibrahim (as) ne phir se az sare nau tameer ki. Is mein jo masalah istemal hua wo to badalta raha lekin uska patthar wohi purana hai. Isliye hajre aswad (Black Stone) ko purani yadgar ke taur Mubarak hote hue Allah ne ise bosa, choomne ka hukm diya. Mekkah ko hi Bekkah bhi kaha jata hai. Bekkah بكه means rush, ijtema. Jis jagah par Kaaba hai us area ko Bekkah bhi kaha jata hai jahan sab jama hote hain. Sab khuzu o khushu se khade hote hain, sab mein yaksaniyat, equality pai jati hai, ghuroor toot jata hai.
🕋
Imam Sadiq (as):
_"Kaaba ko Kaaba is liye kaha jaata hai ke ye zameen ke wast (madhya-bindu / centre) mein nasb (sthaapit / installed) hai, mashriq o maghreeb ke faasle barabar hain (equidistant between east and west). Ye chaukor (square) is liye hai ke Islam ke 4 kalemaat par mushtamil hai,_
"Subhanallah, سبحان الله
Alhamdulillah, الحمد لله
La Ilaha Illallah aur لا اله الا الله
Allahu Akbar". الله اكبر
_Isey Masjidul Haraam is liye kehte hain kyun ki isme mushrik nahi daakhil ho sakte, unke liye ye haraam hai. Kaabe ke bilkul upar chauthe aasmaan par Bait ul M'amoor hai, wo bhi chaukor hai."_
(Aqwaal e Masoomeen (as), p151)
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜
----------------------------------------------

_*MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!*_
🙇
Rasule Khuda (saww):
_"(1) Ali ibne Abi Taalib (as) ki taraf dekhna Ibadat hai,_
_(2) Waaledain ki taraf pyaar bhari nazaro'n se dekhna Ibadat hai,_
_(3) Quran ke sahife mein dekhna Ibadat hai,_ 📖
_(4) Khaana e Kaaba ki taraf dekhna Ibadat hai._ 🕋
(Tafseer Noor us Saqlain, v9, p32)
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜

              🕋 ♦ _*HAJJ*_ ♦🕋

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (385)

*بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ*
🕋
*فِيهِ آيَاتٌ بَيِّنَاتٌ مَقَامُ إِبْرَاهِيمَ ۖ وَمَنْ دَخَلَهُ كَانَ آمِنًا ۗ وَلِلَّهِ عَلَى النَّاسِ حِجُّ الْبَيْتِ مَنِ اسْتَطَاعَ إِلَيْهِ سَبِيلًا ۚ وَمَنْ كَفَرَ فَإِنَّ اللَّهَ غَنِيٌّ عَنِ الْعَالَمِينَ*
🕋
_"Is mein (Kaaba) wazeh wa aashkaar nishaniyan hain. In mein se Maqam e Ibrahim hai aur jo shakhs is mein dakhil ho woh Amaan mein hai aur jo log iski taraf jane ki qudrat rakhte hain un par Wajib hai ke woh Khuda ke liye (Uske) Ghar ki ziyarat karen (Hajj karen) aur jo koi Kufr kare (Hajj tark kare, usne apne aap ko nuqsan pahunch aya, to phir) Khuda to tamam jahano se be Niyaz hai."_
(Surah Aal-e-Imran: 97)
(Dua-e-Nudba mein bhi hai)

📚📖 🕋
👉 _* Tafseer:*_
Cont'd:....

Jaisa ke kal bataya ke Duniya mein sab se pahla ghar Allah ka Ghar (Baitullah) hai. Aaj ki ayat mein Allah ne hukm diya ke jo log istateat (capacity) aur qudrat rakhte hain unke liye Hajj wajib hai. Jaise jaise log badhte gaye Mecca ka area Hajiyon ke liye na kafi hota chala gaya. Masjidul Haram ki isliye kai bar tausee (expansion) hui. Iske liye Kaabe ke atraaf ki abadiyon ko demolish bhi karna pada unko rehabilitate hone ke baad. Tarikh mein milta hai Khalifa Mansoor ne jab ye karravai ki to atraf ke log shift hone ko tayyar nahi the. Is maamle mein Imam Sadiq (as) se mashvara kiya gaya. Imam (as) is ayat ke hawale se dalil pesh ki. 'Ye Khuda ka pahla Ghar hai, jo log bhi atraf mein hain wo baad mein wahan base to unka koi Haq nahi banta ke wahan se na haten.'
Isi tarah Khalifa Mahdi Abbasi ke daur mein bhi aisa hi hua aur Khalifa ke vazir Ali Ibne Yaqteen (Imam ke sahabi) ne Imam Musa Kazim (as) ne same sawal kiya aur Imam ne same jawab diya.
Is tarah Imam ki razamandi se Masjidul Haram ko expand kiya gaya. Jabke jin ke ghar demolish hue woh Imam se khafa bhi hue.
(Tafseer Ayyashi, Noorus Saqlain, Namoona)
🕋
Imam Sadiq (as):
_"Mecca ke 5 naam hain:_
_(1) Ummul Qura (2) Makka (3) Bakka (4) Basasa: halak karnewala shaher. Jisne iski taraf rukh kiya halak hua (Abraha) (5) Umme Rahen: Rahmate Khuda ka Markaz."_
(Kitabul Khisal)
🕋
Imam Sadiq (as):
_"Maqame Kaaba: Bakka, aur city: Makka hai."_
(Tafseer Noorus Saqlain)

(To be cont'd ....)
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜
----------------------------------------------

_*MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!*_
🙇 🕋
Imam Sadiq (as):
_"Hajj ke liye kharch kiya gaya ek dirham, Allah ki khushnudi ke liye diye gaye 20 lakh dirham se behtar hai."_
(Hajj - The Islamic Pilgrimage)
🕋
Imam Sadiq (as):
_"Wo jo tandurust aur maaldaar hone ke bawajood Hajj kiye bagair mar jaata hai wo aisa hai jiske baare mein Allah kehta hai ke "Hum ise Qayamat mein andha uthayenge"._
(Jadeed Masaael - Ayatullah Sistani)

       ♦ _*YAHOODI CHAAL*_ ♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (386)

*بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ*

*قُلْ يَا أَهْلَ الْكِتَابِ لِمَ تَكْفُرُونَ بِآيَاتِ اللَّهِ وَاللَّهُ شَهِيدٌ عَلَىٰ مَا تَعْمَلُونَ * قُلْ يَا أَهْلَ الْكِتَابِ لِمَ تَصُدُّونَ عَنْ سَبِيلِ اللَّهِ مَنْ آمَنَ تَبْغُونَهَا عِوَجًا وَأَنْتُمْ شُهَدَاءُ ۗ وَمَا اللَّهُ بِغَافِلٍ عَمَّا تَعْمَلُونَ * يَا أَيُّهَا الَّذِينَ آمَنُوا إِنْ تُطِيعُوا فَرِيقًا مِنَ الَّذِينَ أُوتُوا الْكِتَابَ يَرُدُّوكُمْ بَعْدَ إِيمَانِكُمْ كَافِرِينَ * وَكَيْفَ تَكْفُرُونَ وَأَنْتُمْ تُتْلَىٰ عَلَيْكُمْ آيَاتُ اللَّهِ وَفِيكُمْ رَسُولُهُ ۗ وَمَنْ يَعْتَصِمْ بِاللَّهِ فَقَدْ هُدِيَ إِلَىٰ صِرَاطٍ مُسْتَقِيمٍ*

_"(Aye Paighambar unse) kaho, aye Ahle Kitab! Tum kiyon (didah o danista) Allah ki ayaton ka inkar karte ho halanke tum jo kuchh karte ho Allah uska Shahid e haal (gawah) hai."_
_"Kaho: Aye Ahle Kitab! ye kiya hai ke jo koi Allah par Imaan lana chahta hai tum use Allah ki raah se rokte ho aur use tedhi chaal chalana chahte ho. Halanke tum haqeeqat e haal se be khabar nahi ho. Yaad rakho jo kuchh tum kar rahe ho Allah us se ghaafil nahi hai."_
_"Aye Imaan walo! Agar tum Ahle Kitab mein se kisi giroh (ke jin ka kaam nifaq aur tumhare darmiyan kina o adawat ki aag bhadkana hai) ki baaton par karband ho gaye to iska natija ye niklega ke woh tumhe Imaan se Kufr ki taraf lauta denge."_
_"Ye kaise ho sakta hai ke tum (ab phir) Kufr ki raah ikhtiyar karo. Jabke tumhara haal ye hai ke Allah ki ayaten  tumhe sunayi jaa rahi hain aur is mein Rasool (Teaching & Guidance) ke liye tum mein maujood hai. (aur aaj Rasool ke numainde Imam maujood hain). (Lehaza Khuda se tamassuk rakho, touch mein raho) aur yaad rakho ke jo koi mazbooti se Allah ka ho raha to bila shubha (without doubt) us par seedhi raah khul gayi (na to uske liye laghzish aur na gum gashtagi ka andesha hai. He cannot slip from the right path)."_
(Surah Aal-e-Imran: 98 - 101)

📚📖 👹👺
👉 _* Tafseer:*_
Jaisa ke hum pahle zere ayaat Yahoodiyon ki sazish ke baare mein bata chuke hain. Aaj kal ke halaat ka tazkara bhi kar chuke hain. Aaj ki ayat bhi usi topic par hai aur ayat khud self explanatory hai. Ayat k zail mein ye waqea hai ke ek Shaami Yahoodi Bin Qaes ne dekha ke Aus o Khazraj ye do qabile jo zamana e Jahiliyat mein ek doosre ke kattar dushman dekh 100 saal se jang  kar rahe the, Islam qabool karne ke baat ek saath baithe the. Yahoodiyon ko aisa dekh kar khatra mehsoos hua, aur sazish ke tahet ek yahoodi naujawan ko unke giroh mein shamil kiya taake unke purane ikhtelafat ko taaza karen aur phir se unko alag karde. Ye ikhtelafat jo ke Jahiliyat ki bena par the, jise Qur'an ne Kufr bataya hai. Islam ek doosre ko milata, jodta hai, jabke Jahiliyat/Kufr ikhtelafat paida karte hain, ek doosre ko todte hain.
Ye sazish aaj bhi badi kamyaabi ke sath chal rahi hai. Yahoodiyat (Zionism) bahut hi chaalaki se Musalmano ko todne ka kaam kar rahi. Duniya mein musalmano ke darmiyan ikhtelafat ubhare jate hain. Jis ka natija Musalmano ke beech jang, tanao, nafrat, bombari hoti hai. Inke auzaar (tool) hai, Salafiyat, Al Qaida, ISIS. Logon ko Ulema se door rakhna. Naye naye sawalat o eterazaat qaum mein paida kar ke ladwana.
Ab ye sab hote hue Allah Qur'an ki in ayaton ke zariye Musalmano ko is sazish se aagah aur warning de raha hai, ke kahin ham is sazish ka shikar na ho jayen.
Allah ki Panah!!!
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜
----------------------------------------------

_*MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!*_
🙇 😏
Imam Reza (as):
_"Zaalim hukkam (badshah) ke kaamo'm mein daakhil hona, unki madad karna, unki haajato'n ke liye koshish karna Kufr ke barabar hai. Unki taraf jaan bujh kar nazar rakhna gunahaan e kabira mein daakhil hai jis par aadmi mustahaq e Jahannum hota hai."_
(Guftaar e Dil Nasheen, p185)
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜

                ♦ _*TAQWA*_ ♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (387)

*بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ*

*يَا أَيُّهَا الَّذِينَ آمَنُوا اتَّقُوا اللَّهَ حَقَّ تُقَاتِهِ وَلَا تَمُوتُنَّ إِلَّا وَأَنْتُمْ مُسْلِمُونَ*

_"Aye Imaan walo! Khuda se yun  daro jaisa ke darne ka Haq hai (Taqwa) aur marna to farmabardar (Muslim) ban kar hi marna."_
(Surah Aal-e-Imran: 102)
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜
----------------------------------------------

_*MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!*_
🙇 😟 _*Tafseer:*_
Amirul Mo'menin Ali (as);
_"Amal ki taraf badho aur maut achanak aa jane se daro isliye ke umr ke palat kar aane ki aas nahi lagai ja sakti jabke rizq ke palatne ki umeed ho sakti hai. Jo rizq hath nahi laga kal uski zyadti ki tawaqqo ho sakti hai aur umeed nahi ke  umr ka guzra hua 'kal' aaj palat ayega. Umeed to aane wale ki ho sakti hai. Aur jo guzar jaye usse mayoosi hi ho sakti hai. Allah se daro jitna usse darne ka Haq hai aur jab maut aaye to tumhe Musalman hi hona chahiye."_
(Nahjul Balagha)
😟
Imam Jafar Sadiq (as):
Is ayat ko is tarah explain kiya:
_"Darne ka Haq (Taqwe ka Haq) ye hai ke Uski ita'at (obey) ki jaye aur nafarmani na ki jaye. Usko yaad kiya jaye aur Use faramosh na kiya jaye aur Uska Shukr kiya jaye aur Uska Kufr na kiya jaye."_
(Ma'aniul Akhbar, Noorus Saqlain)
😭
Imam Sajjad (as):
_"Khauf e Khuda ka matlab rona aur aa'nsu bahana nahi hai, kyun ki jab Taqwa na ho jo usay gunaho'n se roke, ye khauf jhoota hai."_
(Uddatud Daee, ch4)
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜

*18th Zilqad 1437, 22nd August 2016, Monday,

          ♦ _*ITTEHAD-UNITY*_ ♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (388)

*بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ*

*وَاعْتَصِمُوا بِحَبْلِ اللَّهِ جَمِيعًا وَلَا تَفَرَّقُوا ۚ وَاذْكُرُوا نِعْمَتَ اللَّهِ عَلَيْكُمْ إِذْ كُنْتُمْ أَعْدَاءً فَأَلَّفَ بَيْنَ قُلُوبِكُمْ فَأَصْبَحْتُمْ بِنِعْمَتِهِ إِخْوَانًا وَكُنْتُمْ عَلَىٰ شَفَا حُفْرَةٍ مِنَ النَّارِ فَأَنْقَذَكُمْ مِنْهَا ۗ كَذَٰلِكَ يُبَيِّنُ اللَّهُ لَكُمْ آيَاتِهِ لَعَلَّكُمْ تَهْتَدُونَ*
👨‍👨‍👦‍👦
_"Aur tum sab milkar mazbooti se *Allah ki Rassi ko tham lo aur tafarraqe mein na pado* aur Khuda ki us Ne'mat ko yaad karo jo Usne tum par ki hain. Jab tum ek doosre ke dushman the, Usne tumhare dilon mein ulfat paida kar di, iske baad tum is Ne'mat ke wajah se bhai bhai ban gaye. Tum aag ke gadhhe ke kinare par khade the, Allah ne tumko isse bacha liya. Is tarah se Allah apni Nishaniyan tumhare liye khol kar bayan karta hai taake tum Hidayat hasil kar sako."_
(Surah Aal-e-Imran: 103)

📚📖 👨‍👨‍👦‍👦
👉 _* Tafseer:*_
Jaise ke Mashhoor hai jab bhi ittehad ki baat hoti hai is ayat ko pesh kiya jata hai. Koi kahta hai Shia-Sunni ittehad, koi Hindu-Muslim unity ki baat karta hai. Tafseel ki gunjayesh nahi hai. Lekin ahadis ke mutabiq Allah k Rassi se murad *'Vilayat e Ahle Bait (as)'* hai. Agar tamam Musalman is Rassi ko tham len to koi tafarraqa baqi nahi rahega.
(Tafseer Ali Ibne Ibrahim)
👨‍👨‍👦‍👦
Imam Baqir (as):
_"Khuda janta tha ke ye log Nabi ke baad ikhtelaf karenge isliye Allah ne Ummat e Mustafa (saww) ke afraad ko ikhtelaf se usi tarah se roka jaisake Usne sabiq (pichhli) Ummaton ko roka tha aur Khuda ne inhe hukm diya ke tum sab mil kar Vilayat e Ale Muhammad (saww) ka Aqeeda rakho aur tafarraqe mein na pado."_
(Tafseer Noorus Saqlain)
👨‍👨‍👦‍👦
Imam Zainul Abedin (as):
_"Hamare gharane (Ahle Bait) ka Imam Masoom hota hai aur Ismat aisi cheez nahi hai jise dekha ja sake aur mehsoos kiya ja sake. Yehi wajah hai ke Imam mansoos hota hai (Appointed by Allah)."_
Sawal kiya gaya Masoom ke kiya meaning hai? Aap ne farmaya:
_"Masoom woh hota hai jo Khuda ki Rassi (حبل الله) ko thame hue ho aur Allah ki Rassi Qur'an hai aur Qur'an  aur Masoom kabhi ek doosre se juda nahi hote. Imam Qur'an ki taraf rehnumai karta hai aur Qur'an Imam ki taraf rehnumai karta hai aur isi cheez ko Allah ne in alfaz se bayan kiya hai (Bani Israel: 9)."_
(Ma'

anil Akhbar, Noorus Saqlain)

⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜
----------------------------------------------

_*MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!*_
🙇 👨‍👨‍👦‍👦
Imam Sadiq (as):
_"Beshak dushman ke muqable mein Musalmano'n ka ittehad (united) aur unka musta'id (vigilant / chaukas / jaagrut) rehna hi Deen ka sutoon hai."_
(Almustashaar Abdul Haleem Jundi (Misri), p193)

Agar sab Musalmano ke Aqaedi ittehad ho jaye to Dushman chahe kitna hi supar power ho, uske samne ghutne tek dega.
Aur ye ittehad Imam Mahdi (atfs) ki daur mein zaroori qayem hoga. Inshallah.
Puri Duniya us waqt ke intezar mein hai.
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜

            ♦ _*TABLEEGH*_ ♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (390)

*بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ*

*وَلْتَكُنْ مِنْكُمْ أُمَّةٌ يَدْعُونَ إِلَى الْخَيْرِ وَيَأْمُرُونَ بِالْمَعْرُوفِ وَيَنْهَوْنَ عَنِ الْمُنْكَرِ ۚ وَأُولَٰئِكَ هُمُ الْمُفْلِحُونَ*

_"Tum mein se ek Jamat aisi ho jo bhalai ki baton ki taraf dawat dene wali ho. Wo Neki ka hukm de, burai se roke aur bila shubha aise hi log kamyabi hasil karne wale hain."_
(Surah Aal-e-Imran: 104)

📚📖
👉 _* Tafseer:*_
Aaj ke ayat Amr bil Maroof aur Nahi Anil Munkar ke bare mein hai. Ye Furoo-e-Deen ke do juz hain, yani wajib hain, jaise Namaz wajib hai. Har shakhs par ye wajib hai fardan fardan ye Wajibe Aini hai means ye zaroori hai, doosre Qur'an ki ayat mutabiq ek group ye kaam kare baqaeda organized way mein jo sab nahi kar sakte: Ye Wajib e Kifai hai. Is tarah bahut se Tableeghi idare qaem ho gaye lekin abhi tak koi bhi idara is kaam mein kamyab nahi hua. Iski bahut si wujuhat hain. Kiyonki in idaron asli maqsad kuchh aur hota hai. Zyadatar ye idare ki hukmaran ke tahet hote hai jo iska fayda uthate hain. Tableegh asl mein Akhlaq se hoti hai. Agar har Musalman ba Akhlaq ho jaye to uske rishtedar wa Khandan, dost, padosi, uski society sab par asar padega aur ghair Muslim ye dekh is taraf attract honge.
Imam Sadiq (as) ke mutabiq jo Tableegh kar raha hai usko Maroof aur Munkar ka pura ilm ho, kiyonki agar use ilm na hoga to dar haqeeqat wo Munkar ki taraf bula raha hai.
Ali (as) Nahjul Balagha mein farmate hain:
_"Allah ne in logo par Laanat ki hai jo logo ko Neki ka hukm dete hain aur khud us par amal na karte hon, doosron ko burai se bachne ki Tableegh karte hon aur khud burai karte hon"_
Jis giroh ka is ayat mein zikr hai tafseer ke mutabiq usse murad Ahle Bait (as) hain jinki puri zindagi is kaam mein masroof rahi. Ale Imran ki ek kadi Imam Husain (as) se jab Maqsad e ravangi e Karbala poochha gaya to yehi jawab diya _'Amr bil Maroof ......, mere jadd ki ummat ki Islah.'_  
Bare Ilaha hame aise bana de ke ghair hame dekh kar imaan le ayen.
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜
----------------------------------------------

_*MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!*_
🙇
Imam Ali (as):
_*"Amr bil Maroof aur Nahi az Munkar* (ye dono) maut ko jaldi qareeb nahi aane dete aur Rozi mein kami nahi hone dete, balke sawaab ko do-guna (double) karte hain aur ajr ko azeem karte hain aur in dono (Amr bil Maroof aur Nahi az Munkar) mein afzal, zaalim haakim (badshah) ke saamne insaaf ki baat kehna hai."_
(Guftaar e Dil Nasheen, p59)

Imam Husain (as):
_"Mera khurooj (Jihad) na to kisi khud-pasandi, na akadd, na fasaad aur na hi zulm ke liye hai. Maine to sirf apne Jad ki ummat ki islaah ke liye khurooj kiya hai. Main *Amr bil Maaruf aur Nahi az Munkar karna* chahta hoo’n aur apne Jad Muhammad Rasulallah (saww) aur apne baap Ali ibne Abi Taalib (as) ki seerat pe chalna chahta hoo'n."_
(Aqwaal 14 Masumeen (as), p89)
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜

            ♦ _*FIRQA BANDI*_ ♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu
💔
Start your Day by reading Quran: (389)

*بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ*

*وَلَا تَكُونُوا كَالَّذِينَ تَفَرَّقُوا وَاخْتَلَفُوا مِنْ بَعْدِ مَا جَاءَهُمُ الْبَيِّنَاتُ ۚ وَأُولَٰئِكَ لَهُمْ عَذَابٌ عَظِيمٌ*

_"Aur dekho! Un logon ki tarah na bano jinhonne (Khuda ke ek hi Deen par ikathe rehne ke bajae) *Tafarraqa paida kiya* aur  (Kitabullah) ki Roshan Daleelon ke bawajood ikhtelaf kiya. Aise hi logon ke liye bahut bada Azaab hai."_
(Surah Aal-e-Imran: 105)

📚📖 💔
👉 _* Tafseer:*_
Jaisa ke kal hamne bataya ittehad sirf ek hi tarah se ho sakta hai ke sab ke sab Musalman Qur'an ki Hidayat ke mutabiq 'Allah ki Rassi' ko tham len. Ahadis ke mutabiq Allah ki Rassi Ahle Bait (as) hain. Lekin Musalmano ne Ahle Bait (as) ka daman chhoda to firqon mein bat gaye aur muntashir ho gaye. Ek mazboot Rassi ko chhod tooti hui boseeda rassiyon ko pakda aur phir un tooti rassiyon mein ulajhte gay. Itne uljhe ke Haqeeqi Rassi ko bhool gaya. Isliye Islam puri Duniya mein phailta to gaya lekin is tarah jaise ek aadmi waste paper ke tokdo ko uda deta hai aur wo udte hue sab jagah phail jate hain. In tukdo mein ek qeemti dastawez bhi hoti hai jise wo la ilme mein phekta hai lekin wo tokda ek haqiqat pasand uthata hai aur apne kam mein lata hai.
Ahle Bait (as) hi ittehad ki buniyad hain warna Ikhtelafat ke siwa kuchh nahi.
Rasoole Khuda (sa) ki maroof peshengoi jisko Islam ke har firqe bayan karte hai:
_"Yahoodi qaum Hazrat Moosa (as) ke baad 71 aur Esai 72 firqon mein bat gayi thi aur meri Ummat 73 firqon mein bat jayengi aur in mein ek hi Jannati hoga."_
(Ref: Shia: Khisal, Ma'ani, Ehtejaj, Amali Sudooq, Asl Sulaim bin Qais. Sunni: Durrul Mansoor, Jameul Usool aur Milal o Nahl.)
Aaj jo Duniya mein ho raha hai uska asl sabab yehi hai. Gulf Muslim Countries sab ek doosre ke samne ladne ko tayyar. Mera Deen asli hai doosre sab Kafir isliye qatl o gharat karo. Sare Musalman ek doosre ko maar kaat ke liye tule hai, jabke Islam to 'Religion of Peace' tha. Nehru ki zabani:
_"Nai tawanai aur jadeed fikr ke jisne unko bedar kiya aur unhe itmenan Nafs aur Qudrat se nawaza wo Deen e Islam tha."_
(Glance at World History, Vol 1, P-317)
Is tarah aur bahut se aqwaal hain. Agar Islam mein itne firqe na hote to puri Duniya mein ye ek mazboot taqat hoti. Lekin kiya karen har ek ki aankh par Ta'assub ki ainak lagi hai.
Intezar hai to bas ek hasti ka  jo puri Duniya mein Adl o Insaaf Qaem karke ek Muttahid aur Haqeeqi Islam ko pesh karega aur woh hain Ahle Bait (as) aur Ale Imraan ki Akheri kadi: Imam Mahdi (atfs).
Jo pahle Imam Ali (as) par muntashir hue the woh 12th Imam par muttahid ho jayenge. Inshallah
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜
----------------------------------------------

_*MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!*_
🙇 💔
*رسول الله‏ (ص) : ما اختلفت امة بعد نبيها إلا ظهر أهل باطلها على أهل حقها.*
Rasooe Khuda (saww):
_"Jaise hi Ummat mein apne Nabi ke baad ikhtelaf shuru hota hai un mein se Ahle Batil ki Ahle Haq par fatha hoti hai."_

_"No sooner does a community differ [between themselves] after their own prophet, than the people of falsehood from amongst them become victorious over the people of truth."_
[Kanz al-`Ummal, no. 929]
💔
Rasule Khuda (saww):
_"Tumhe bataaoo'n, tum mein se badtareen shakhs kaun hai?_ Logo'n ne kaha, "Ya Rasulallah (saww), aap farmaiye". Aap (saww) ne farmaya _"Jo logo'n mein chugal-khori karta firta hai aur dosto'n mein tafarka (phoot) daalta hai"._
(Jadeed Masaael - Ayatullah Sistani)
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜

*20th Zilqad 1437, 24th August 2016, Wednesday,

♦ _*SIYAH AUR SAFED CHEHRE*_ ♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (391)

*بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ*

*يَوْمَ تَبْيَضُّ وُجُوهٌ وَتَسْوَدُّ وُجُوهٌ ۚ فَأَمَّا الَّذِينَ اسْوَدَّتْ وُجُوهُهُمْ أَكَفَرْتُمْ بَعْدَ إِيمَانِكُمْ فَذُوقُوا الْعَذَابَ بِمَا كُنْتُمْ تَكْفُرُونَ * وَأَمَّا الَّذِينَ ابْيَضَّتْ وُجُوهُهُمْ فَفِي رَحْمَةِ اللَّهِ هُمْ فِيهَا خَالِدُونَ*
👱🏿👱🏻
_"(Nifaq dalne walon par wo Azeem Azaab) us Din hoga jab kuchh chehre safed aur kuchh siyah (black) ho jayenge. Wo log jinke chehre siyah ho jayenge (unse kaha jayega) kiya tum Imaan (aur saya e ukhwat mein aane) ke baad kafir ho gaye the to (ab) apne kiye hue Kufr ke Azaab ka maza chakho."_
_"Lekin jinke chehre safed honge wo Khuda ki Rehmat mein honge aur is mein hamesha rahenge."_.
(Surah Aal-e-Imran: 106 - 107)

📚📖 👱🏿👱🏻
👉 _* Tafseer:*_
Jaisa ke hamne pahle bayan kiya ke Rasool (saww) ke rehlat ke baad Ummat 73 firqo mein bat gayi. Iski wajah ye thi ke khud Rasool (saww) ke zamane mein bhi Musalmano mein kuchh sachche the aur kuchh munafeqeen the. Munafeqeen jo ke baad mein khul kar saamne aa gaye. Ye Munafeqeen kaun the ye qare'en (Readers) khud history ki study karen. Yahan Qur'an inke liye bata raha hai ke Qayamat ke din unke chehre siyah honge.
Lekin kaun siyah aur safed hoga kuchh ahadis mulaheza farmayen:
Ameerul Mo'menin Hazrat Ali (as):
_"Roze Qayamat Rasool (saww) ke left ki taraf tareeki (darkness) hogi aur is tareeki se ye nida buland hogi:_
_'Aye ahle moqif! Khush khabri hai uske liye jisne Khuda aur Rasool par Imaan lane ke baad Wasi se Muhabbat rakhi. Aaj sirf wohi Kamyab hoga aur wohi sukoon aur Jannat hasil karega jo Khuda ke huzoor Nabi aur Wasi ke ikhlas ke sath pesh hoga aur jisne in dono ki pairavi ka sharaf hasil kiya hoga."_  
(Roza e Kafi, Noorus Saqlain)
Rasoole Khuda (saww):
_"Qayamat ke din Khuda ki taraf se nida ayegi:_
_'Ye mera Habib Muhammad (saww) aur ye mera Wali Ali (as) hai. Khush khabari hai uske liye jisne usse Muhabbat ki hai aur halakat hai uske liye jisne usse adawat ki hai aur us par Jhoot tarashe hain."_
(Kitabul Khisal)
Ek toolani hadis ka Akheri hissa:
Rasoole Khuda (saww):
_"........  Qayamat ke Din Mein meri ummat se poonchhunga ke tumne mere baad 'Saqlain' (Quran o Ahle Bait as) ke sath kiya sulook kiya tha? Un mein se ek giroh kahega Siqle Akbar (Qur'an) ko hamne phad dala aur Siqle Asghar (Ahle Bait as) se jang ki aur unhe qatl kiya. Mein kahonga siyah chehre liye dozakh mein chale jao. Phir ek giroh kahega hamne Siqle Akbar ki itteba ki aur Siqle Asghar se Muhabbat ki. Mein kahunga apne Roshan o shaad chehre liye Jannat mein chale jao."_
(Tafseer Ali Ibrahim Hazrat Abu Zar Ghaffari (ra) se rivayat)
Ji haan, ye Qayamat ke Din chehro ke colour ka criteria hoga. Ab hame abhi se faisla karna hoga ke ham kis group mein hain: Black ya White face?
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜
----------------------------------------------

_*MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!*_
🙇 👱🏻👱🏿
******* JUMA MUBARAK *******
*وَشِيعَتُكَ عَلَىٰ مَنَابِرَ مِنْ نُورٍ مُبْيَضَّةً وُجُوهُهُمْ حَوْلِي فِي ٱلْجَنَّةِ وَهُمْ جِيرَانِي وَلَوْلاَ انْتَ يَا عَلِيُّ لَمْ يُعْرَفِ ٱلْمُؤْمِنُونَ بَعْدِي. وَكَانَ بَعْدَهُ هُدىٰ مِنَ ٱلضَّلاَلِ وَنُوراً مِنَ ٱلْعَمَىٰ وَحَبْلَ ٱللَّهِ ٱلْمَتِينَ وَصِرَاطَهُ ٱلْمُسْتَقِيمَ*
👱🏻👱🏿
Rasoole Khuda (saww):
_"..... Aur Aye Ali! Agar tum na hote to mere baad Mo'menin ki shanakht (recognition) mumkin na hoti aur haan aisa hi tha. Ali (as) Rasool (saww) ke baad gumrahiyon mein rahnuma aur tarikiyon mein chiraghe baseerat hain. Aur Allah ki mazboot Rassi, aur iska seedha rasta hain......"_
(Dua-e-Nudba ba roze Juma)
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜

                ♦ _*AYAAT*_ ♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (392)

*بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ*

*تِلْكَ آيَاتُ اللَّهِ نَتْلُوهَا عَلَيْكَ بِالْحَقِّ ۗ وَمَا اللَّهُ يُرِيدُ ظُلْمًا لِلْعَالَمِينَ * وَلِلَّهِ مَا فِي السَّمَاوَاتِ وَمَا فِي الْأَرْضِ ۚ وَإِلَى اللَّهِ تُرْجَعُ الْأُمُورُ*
(Surah Aal-e-Imran: 108 - 109)

_"Ye Ayaate Khuda wandi hain jinko Ham aap par Haq ke sath tilawat kar rahe hain. Aur Allah Aalameen ke liye zulm ka irada nahi karta."_
_"Aasmano aur zameeno mein jo kuchh hai wo Allah ki Milkiyat hai aur tamam umoor Allah ki taraf lautai jayenge."_

📚📖
👉 _* Tafseer:*_
Dear readers ham apke ke liye Qurani Ayaat aur unke matalib pesh kar rahe hai jo ke bar Haq hain. Ye silsila 6000 dino tak chalta rahega. Kuchh ilmi baaten aisi hongi jo apni abhi tak suni nahi hogi. Ham jo bhi pesh kar rahe hain direct Kitabon ke hawale se kar rahe hain. Pas touch mein rahen.
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜
----------------------------------------------

_*MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!*_
🙇 🗡
Imam Sadiq (as)
se kisi shakhs ne kaha, "Allah aap ko jazaa e khair ataa farmaye. Kya H. Ali (as) Deen mein pukhta aur qawi (firm and strong) nahi the?" Aap (as) ne farmaya, _"Haa'n, wo qawi the"._ Usne kaha, "Phir qaum kis tarah unpar ghaalib aa gayi aur unhone iska difaa (defend) nahi kiya aur na unko roka". To aap (as) ne farmaya, _"Kitaab e Khuda mein ek Ayat hai jisne unko is baat se roka"._ us shakhs ne kaha, "Wo kaun si aayat hai?" Aap (as) ne farmaya:_
*.....لَوْ تَزَيَّلُوا لَعَذَّبْنَا الَّذِينَ كَفَرُوا مِنْهُمْ عَذَابًا أَلِيمًا.*
[Surat Al-Fath 25]
_Kyun ki Allah Azz Wa Jall ki Momin amaanatein Kaafiro'n aur Munafiqo'n ki sulbo'n (loins) mein maujood the to Ali (as) ke liye ye mumkin nahi tha ke unke aaba (purvaj) ko qatl kare de'n ta waqt ye ke amaanatein paida ho jaayein aur jab amaanatein nikal aayi'n to Ali (as) unpe hamlawar huwe aur unse muqabila kiya. Isi tarah hamare Ahlebait (as) ke QAIM (atfs) ka oos waqt tak zahoor na hoga jab tak Allah ki amaanatein paida na ho jaayein phir wo apne mukhaalifeen par galba haasil kar ke unko qatl karenge"._
(Kamaluddin, v2, p608)
🤔
Imam Sadiq (as):
_"Haram-zade (illegitimate child born out-of-wedlock) ki 4 nishaniyaa'n hain:
_-Ahlebait e Paighambar (saww) se dushmani rakhna,_
_-Zina ka shauq rakhna ke usi se paida huwa hai,_
_-Deen ko haqeer samajhna,_
_-logo'n se bura bartaav rakhna."_
(Hadiyat ush Shia, p276)
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜

*23th Zilqad 1437, 27th August 2016, Saturday,

♦ _*AMR BIL MAROOF & NAHI ANIL MUNKAR*_ ♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (393)
✨
*بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ*

*كُنْتُمْ خَيْرَ أُمَّةٍ أُخْرِجَتْ لِلنَّاسِ تَأْمُرُونَ بِالْمَعْرُوفِ وَتَنْهَوْنَ عَنِ الْمُنْكَرِ وَتُؤْمِنُونَ بِاللَّهِ ۗ وَلَوْ آمَنَ أَهْلُ الْكِتَابِ لَكَانَ خَيْرًا لَهُمْ ۚ مِنْهُمُ الْمُؤْمِنُونَ وَأَكْثَرُهُمُ الْفَاسِقُونَ*
✨
_"Tum behtareen Ummat ho jinhe logon ke liye namoona bana kar laya gaya hai. (kiyonki) Tum logon ko Nekiyon ka hukm dete ho aur Buraiyon se mana karte ho aur Khuda par Imaan rakhte ho aur agar Ahle Kitab bhi Imaan le aate to unke liye behtar hota, un mein chand afraad Imaandar aur unki aksariyat nafarman hai."._
(Surah Aal-e-Imran: 110)

📚📖 ✨
👉 _* Tafseer:*_
Ayat 104 ki topic ko continue karte hue jisko ham explain kar chuke hain. Qur'an ke sab Ahkamaat zaheran umoomi (General) hote hain. Lekin har ayat mein khas mafhoom chhupe hote hain. Rivayat ke mutabiq ek ayat ke 50 batini meaning hote hain. Ye sirf wohi bata sakta hai jinke ghar ye Kitab nazil hui aur woh hain Ahlul Bait (as) (Ale Imran) jo Rasekhuna film Ilm hain.
Is ayat mein Jo Amr bil Maroof aur Nahi Anil Munkar karta hai unko behtreen Ummat qarar diya hai. Pehle ham bayan kar chuke hain jo ye kaam kar raha hai wo kaisa hona chahiye. Sirf Tableeghi Jamaat banane se kam nahi chalta. Jo ye kaam kar raha hai woh in khusoosiyat mein afzal hona chahiye.
Imam Sadiq (as):
_"Is ummat ke tamam afraad Khair e Ummat nahi hain. Kiya Amirul Mo'menin aur Hasnain Karimain (as) ke qatil bhi Khair e Ummat kahlane ke mutaheq hain? Khair e Ummat ki sifat bayan karte hue Allah ne farmaya 'Amre Bil Maroof aur Nahi Anil Munkar.....' Aur Aimma e Ahle Bait (as) hi is ayat ke misdaq hain."_
(Tafseer Ali Ibne Ibrahim, Noorus Saqlain, Manaqib Shahre Ashoob)
Jaisa ke pahle bhi bayan kar chuke hain Rasool (sa) aur unke Ahle Bait (as) ki puri zindagi isi kaam mein guzri aur woh Masoom bhi the, pas Khair e Ummat woh nahi to aur kaun ho sakta hai.
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜
----------------------------------------------

_*MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!*_
🙇 ✨
Imam Ali (as):
_"Amr bil maaruf aur Nahi Anil Munkar (ye dono) maut ko jaldi qareeb nahi aane dete aur Rozi mein kami nahi hone dete, balke sawaab ko do-guna (double) karte hain aur ajr ko azeem karte hain aur in dono (Amr bil Maroof aur Nahi az Munkar) mein afzal, zaalim haakim (badshah) ke saamne insaaf ki baat kehna hai."_
(Guftaar e Dil Nasheen, p59)
✨
Imam Ali (as):
_"Wo jo jismaani, zabaani aur ruhaani tariqe se Amr bil Maaruf aur Nahi anil Munkar karna chhor deta hai, wo ek zinda laash ki tarah hai."_
(Miskhat ul Anwaar)
✨
Janabe Fatima Zehra (sa):
_"Khuda Wande Aalam ne Amr bil Maroof aur Nahi Anil Munkar ko maashre (society) ki islaah (sudhaarne) ke liye qaraar diya hai."_
(Guftaar e Dil Nasheen, p41)
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜
----------------------------------------------
*24th Zilqad 1437, 28th August 2016, Sunday,

         ♦ _*Qatl e Anbiya*_ ♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (394)

*بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ*

*لَنْ يَضُرُّوكُمْ إِلَّا أَذًى ۖ وَإِنْ يُقَاتِلُوكُمْ يُوَلُّوكُمُ الْأَدْبَارَ ثُمَّ لَا يُنْصَرُونَ* *ضُرِبَتْ عَلَيْهِمُ الذِّلَّةُ أَيْنَ مَا ثُقِفُوا إِلَّا بِحَبْلٍ مِنَ اللَّهِ وَحَبْلٍ مِنَ النَّاسِ وَبَاءُوا بِغَضَبٍ مِنَ اللَّهِ وَضُرِبَتْ عَلَيْهِمُ الْمَسْكَنَةُ ۚ ذَٰلِكَ بِأَنَّهُمْ كَانُوا يَكْفُرُونَ بِآيَاتِ اللَّهِ وَيَقْتُلُونَ الْأَنْبِيَاءَ بِغَيْرِ حَقٍّ ۚ ذَٰلِكَ بِمَا عَصَوْا وَكَانُوا يَعْتَدُونَ*

_"Ye (Yahoodi) tumhe satane ke alawa tumhara koi nuqsan nahi kar sakenge aur agar unhone tum se jang  ki to muqable mein peeth dekhayge aur unhe kisi taraf se koi imdad nahi milegi."_
_"Ye jahan bhi rahen un par zillat ki mar pad chuki hai albatta inhe ahd ya logon ke muahede ki panah mil jay to woh mustashna hai. Aur ye Allah ke ghazab mein ghir chuke hain aur muhtaji musallat kar di gayi hai. Ye saza isliye hai ke ye Ayaat e Ilahi ka inkar karte the aur na Haq Anbiya ko qatl kiya karte the. Ye unki nafarmaniyon aur zyadtiyon ka natija hai."_
(Surah Aal-e-Imran: 111 - 112)

📚📖
👉 _* Tafseer:*_
Ayat bazahir Yahoodiyon ke liye nazil hui lekin ye har zamane aur har in logon ke liye hai jinhone  Hadiyan e Bar Haq (Ahle Bait as) ko sataya, un par zulm dhaye, unko Shaheed kiya. Jiska natija ham aaj tak ham dekh rahe hain. Sab se zyada Rasool ki dukhtar Janabe Fatema (sa) ko aziyyat di gayi, jin ki shahadat hi 18 saal ke sin mein ho gayi. Qateleen Rehbaran e Deen par Allah ki Laanat hai.
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜
----------------------------------------------

_*MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!*_
🙇 ✨
Rasule Khuda (saww)
se puchha gaya ke, _"Qayamat ke din kis shakhs ko sabse zyada azaab diya jayega?" Aap ne farmaya, "Us shakhs ko jisne kisi Nabi ko qatl kiya hoga ya kisi aise shakhs ko qatl kiya jo nekiyo'n ka hukm deta ho aur buraaiyo'n se manaa karta ho"._
(Irshadaat e Masumeen (as), p9)
(Note: hamne kal bataya Amr bil Maroof..... karne wale Ahle Bait (as) hain.)
✨
Qatil halalzada nahi ho sakta:
Imam Sadiq (as):
se puchha gaya ke, _"Firon ko Janabe Musa (as) ko qatl karne se kisne roka jaise ke Quran mein hai 'Aur Firon kehne laga mujhe chhor do ke main Musa (as) ka qatl kar daaloo'n' (Surah 40, Ayat 26)?" Imam (as) ne jawaab diya, "Is liye ke Firon halaal-zada tha aur sirf wo jo na-jaayaz aulaad ho (haraam-zada ho) ya zaaniya (fornicator / vyabhichaari) aurat ki aulaad hi Paigambaro'n aur Hujjat e Khuda ko qatl kar sakte hain."_
(Kaamil uz Ziyaraat, p83)
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜

*25th Zilqad 1437, 29th August 2016, Monday,

♦ _*GHAIR MUSLIM NEK AMAAL*_♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (395)

*بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ*

*لَيْسُوا سَوَاءً ۗ مِنْ أَهْلِ الْكِتَابِ أُمَّةٌ قَائِمَةٌ يَتْلُونَ آيَاتِ اللَّهِ آنَاءَ اللَّيْلِ وَهُمْ يَسْجُدُونَ * يُؤْمِنُونَ بِاللَّهِ وَالْيَوْمِ الْآخِرِ وَيَأْمُرُونَ بِالْمَعْرُوفِ وَيَنْهَوْنَ عَنِ الْمُنْكَرِ وَيُسَارِعُونَ فِي الْخَيْرَاتِ وَأُولَٰئِكَ مِنَ الصَّالِحِينَ * وَمَا يَفْعَلُوا مِنْ خَيْرٍ فَلَنْ يُكْفَرُوهُ ۗ وَاللَّهُ عَلِيمٌ بِالْمُتَّقِينَ*

_"Sab Ahle Kitab yaksan (equal) nahi hain. Ahle Kitab mein ek giroh aisa hai jo Deen par qaem hai. Is giroh ke afraad raat ke awqat mein musalsal halate Sajda mein Aayaat e Ilahi ki tilawat karte hain."_
_"Woh Khuda aur Akherat par Imaan rakhte hain.  Amr e bil Maroof aur Nahi anil Munkar karte hain aur Nek kaamon ko anjam dahi mein ek doosre par sabqat le jate hain aur woh Nek logon mein se hain."_
_"Unki kisi bhi Neki ki Naqadri nahi ki jayegi aur Allah Parhezgaron ko bakhoobi Jannewala hai."_
(Surah Aal-e-Imran: 113 - 115)

📚📖
👉 _* Tafseer:*_
Guzishta ayaton mein Yahoodiyon ko condemn kiya jata raha hai. Lekin puri qaum ko ham bura nahi kah sakte. Maloom ho ke Yahoodi Hazrat Moosa (as) ki pairavi karte the. Unke chahne wale unke farma bardar the. Islam ne ye nahi kaha ke sab pairokar ghalat the. Kuchh din pahle hamne Yahoodiyon ke ek firqe Rabbi ki misal di thi with present reference. Jaise kuchh Ahkam un mein aaj bhi Islami Ahkam se milte julte hain jaise Qurbani/Zibah ke Ahkam. Halal Food ko wo Kosher Food kahte hain (Hamare 17 Aug ke msg ko refer karen), aur bhi bahut cheezen hain. Qur'an yahan unki khusoosiyat bata raha hai. Isliye bahut se Yahoodi ya Christian Muslim ho gaye kiyonki jab tak unko Islam ke bare mein jankari nahi thi woh apne amal ke mutabiq Saleheen wa Muttaqi the. Isliye wo Musalman hue. Isliye jis ka dil saaf rahta hai wo sahi raaste par chala aata hai. Aur phir woh Amr e bil Maroof ..... ka nek amal anjam deta hai.
Aaj jo ham zalim wa jabir Yahoodi wa Esaiyat dekh rahe hain wo Zionism aur Judaism hai jiska asl Deen se koi rabt nahi. Jaise Islam mein Salafism.
Jo Deendar log hote hain khwah woh kisi bhi mazhab se talluq rakhte hon jab unhe Islam jaisa seedha rasta nazar aa jata hai wo fauran ye rah apna lete hain..Qur'an in logon ki taarif kar raha hai. Nek Amal koi bhi kare khwah woh Ahle Kitab ho ya Kafir Allah unko uska ajr deta hai kiyonki Allah Adil hai. Lekin rivayat ke mutabiq unka Ajr isi Duniya mein mil jata hai aur Qayamat ki Din woh khali haath hi jayenge. Jabke Momin ka ajr Khuda ke pas reserve hai. Qayamat ke din unko ye silah milega. Ab jo ham dekhte hain Momin is Duniya mein musibat mein aur Kafir asaesh mein ji rahen hai, iski wajah yehi hai. Allah khoob janta hai kis ko kaise rakhna hai.
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜
----------------------------------------------

_*MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!*_
🙇
Imam Sadiq (as):
_"Duniya mein Momin ke Amal ki koi qadr dani nahi hoti. Iski wajah ye hai ke Momin ki Nekiyan Allah ki bargah mein pahunch jati hain aur logon tak unki rasai nahi hoti isi liye logon mein uski Neki ki shohrat nahi hoti aur iske baraks (contrary) agar Kafir koi Neki kare to uski Neki ko Shohrat mil jati hai aur uski wajah bhi yehi hai ke uska amal Khuda ke liye to hota nahi isi liye woh Khuda ki taraf safar hi nahi karta. Woh sirf insaano tak hi mehdood ho kar rah jata hai."_
(Kitab Ilalush Sharaye)

♦ _*GHAIR MUSLIM NEK AMAAL*_♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (396)

*بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ*

*إِنَّ الَّذِينَ كَفَرُوا لَنْ تُغْنِيَ عَنْهُمْ أَمْوَالُهُمْ وَلَا أَوْلَادُهُمْ مِنَ اللَّهِ شَيْئًا ۖ وَأُولَٰئِكَ أَصْحَابُ النَّارِ ۚ هُمْ فِيهَا خَالِدُونَ * مَثَلُ مَا يُنْفِقُونَ فِي هَٰذِهِ الْحَيَاةِ الدُّنْيَا كَمَثَلِ رِيحٍ فِيهَا صِرٌّ أَصَابَتْ حَرْثَ قَوْمٍ ظَلَمُوا أَنْفُسَهُمْ فَأَهْلَكَتْهُ ۚ وَمَا ظَلَمَهُمُ اللَّهُ وَلَٰكِنْ أَنْفُسَهُمْ يَظْلِمُونَ*

_"Jin logon ne Kufr ikhtiyar kiya woh hargiz apne amwal aur aulad ke zariye Allah ke Azaab o saza se nahi bach sakte. Woh Ahle Jahannam hain aur hamesha ke liye us mein rahenge."_
_"Ye log jo kuchh is Duniyavi zindagi mein kharch karte hain unki misal us jalane wali (garm) hawa ke manind hai jo is qaum ki zara'at (khet) par chal pade jis ne apne aap par zulm kiya (aur namunasib waqt par zara'at ki) pas woh use nist o nabood kar de. Khuda ne un  par zulm nahi kiya balke unhone khud apne upar zulm kiya hai."_
(Surah Aal-e-Imran: 116 - 117)

📚📖
👉 _* Tafseer:*_
Jaisa ke kal ki ayat mein un Ahle Kitab ki taarif ki thi jo Nek Amal baja laate hain. Aaj ki aayat Non Muslim Kafiron ke bare mein hai. Kafir woh hota hai jo Allah par yaqeen nahi rakhta. Woh apne maal wa aulad par zyada bharosa karta hai. Lekin Kafir ka hamesha ka maskan Jahannam hai.
Aapne dekha hoga bahut se Non Muslim Nek kaam mein aage aage rehte hain. Bahut dan o dakshina karte hain. Kal ham explain kar chuke hain. Allah ne unki misal aise khet ki di hai jis par agar loo (garm hawa) chal jai to barbad ho jaye. Usi tarah uski Nekiyan bhi barbad ho jati hai. Kiyonki unki Neki insured nahi rahti. Isliye woh barbad ho jate hain.
Usi tarah jaise Musalmano mein kuchh gunah aise hote hain jo Neki ko kha jate hain. Jaise Hasad Imaan ko kha  jata hai.
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜
----------------------------------------------

_*MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!*_
🙇
Rasule Khuda (saww):
_"Yaqeenan Hasad (jealousy) nekiyo'n ko is tarah kha jaata hai jaise aag khushk (dry) lakdi ko kha jaati hai."_
(Hadiyat ush Shia, p34)

Imam Ali (as):
_"Hasad nekiyo'n ko is tarah tabaah kar deta hai jis tarah aag lakdiyo'n ko jalaa deti hai."_
(Aasmani Nasihatein, v2, p180)

Imam Ali (as):
_"Aisi Aag se daro jiski gehraayi bahut zyada hai, garmi bahut sakht hai aur Azaab har roz naya hai."_
(Tajalliyat e Hikmat)

         ♦ _*RAAZ - SECRET*_ ♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (397)

*بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ*

*يَا أَيُّهَا الَّذِينَ آمَنُوا لَا تَتَّخِذُوا بِطَانَةً مِنْ دُونِكُمْ لَا يَأْلُونَكُمْ خَبَالًا وَدُّوا مَا عَنِتُّمْ قَدْ بَدَتِ الْبَغْضَاءُ مِنْ أَفْوَاهِهِمْ وَمَا تُخْفِي صُدُورُهُمْ أَكْبَرُ ۚ قَدْ بَيَّنَّا لَكُمُ الْآيَاتِ ۖ إِنْ كُنْتُمْ تَعْقِلُونَ*

_"Aye Imaan walo! Apno ke alawa kisi ko RAAZDAR na banao. Woh tumhe koi nuqsan pahunche ke bare mein kotahi nahi karenge. Woh tumhari takleef aur ranj par khush hote hain, unke dil ki dushmani aur adawat unke moo se nikal padti hai aur jo kuchh unke dilon mein hai wo us se bhi shadeed tar hai. Hamne Aayaat (aur unse mehfooz rahne ki tadabeer) tumhare liye wazeh kar di hain basharteke tum Aql o khirad se kaam lo."_
(Surah Aal-e-Imran: 118)

📚📖 ✨✨
👉 _* Tafseer:*_
Zindagi mein agar kamyab hona hai to kisi bhi ghair ko apna Raaz fash na karo. Ho sakta hai ke woh tumhara dushman ho aur woh isko tumhare khilaf istemal kar sakta hai. Isse pahle ye dekha zaroori hai hai ke tumhara dost aur dushman kaun hai. Apne ghar ki baaten ghar mein hi agar poshida rahen to isse izzat mein izafa hota hai. Jiska Business Secrets open nahi hota hai uske business mein taraqqi hoti hai.
Khuda ki Qudrat dekhiye ke Usne is tarah ka nizam rakha hai ke koi bhi ek doosre ke man ki baat nahi jaan sakta, khud insaan nahi jaanta ke aage kiya hone wala hai. Agar aisa na hota to sochiye ye Kainat ka nizam chal pata. Isliye har cheez raaz rahne mein bhalai hai.
Ham shiyon ka fariza hai ke Ahle Bait (as) ke Raazon ko fash na karen. Ham jaante hain puri Duniya Ahle Bait (as) ke dushmano se bhari hui hai. Ayat ke mutabiq dushman ye raaz apni makkariyon mein fayda utha sakta hai. Rumooze Ale Muhammad (as) ke baare bahut hadisen warid hui hain. Bahut bar ye bhi kaha gaya hai ke falan hadith sirf apne tak rakho. Kitab Sulaim Ibne Qaes woh kitab hai jisme Al Mohammed (as) ke  raaron mein se ek hai:
Imam Sadiq (as):
_"Hamare jin Shiyon ke pas Kitab Sulaim bin Qaes Al Halali nahi hai uske pas hamare umoor aur unke asbab ki jankari nahi hai jo Asraar e Ale Muhammad (as) mein se hain."_
(Kitab Sulaim, Vol 1,  P-358, Mustadraktul Wasail)

Pas Raaz ko raaz rakhne mein dono fayde hain dunyawi wa Ukhrawi.
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜
----------------------------------------------

_*MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!*_
🙇 ✨✨
Imam Ali (as):
_"Jo apne raazon par qabu rakhta hai uske apne hath on mein control hai."_
[Nahj al-Balagha, Saying 162]
✨✨
Imam Ali (as):
_"Tumhara RAAZ tumhara qaedi hai agar tumne use chhod diya to tum uske qaidi ban jaoge."_
[Ghurar al-Hikam, no. 563]
✨✨
Imam Sadiq (as):
_"Tumhara RAAZ tumhara khoon hai pas ise apne rag ke alawa doosron ki ragon mein dodne na do."_
[Bihar al-Anwar, v. 75, p. 71, no. 15]
✨✨
Imam Ali (as):
_"3 logon ko apna Raazdar na banao:
(1) Aurat (2) Chugalkhor (3) Ahmaq (idiot).
[Ghurar al-Hikam, no. 4662]
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜

*28th Zilqad 1437, 1st September 2016, Thursday,

       ♦ _*DOSTI*_ ♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (398)

*بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ*

*هَا أَنْتُمْ أُولَاءِ تُحِبُّونَهُمْ وَلَا يُحِبُّونَكُمْ وَتُؤْمِنُونَ بِالْكِتَابِ كُلِّهِ وَإِذَا لَقُوكُمْ قَالُوا آمَنَّا وَإِذَا خَلَوْا عَضُّوا عَلَيْكُمُ الْأَنَامِلَ مِنَ الْغَيْظِ ۚ قُلْ مُوتُوا بِغَيْظِكُمْ ۗ إِنَّ اللَّهَ عَلِيمٌ بِذَاتِ الصُّدُورِ*

_"Tum ajeeb log ho ke unhe dost rakhte ho lekin woh tumhe dost nahi rakhte halanke tum Aasmani kutub par Imaan rakhte ho (lekin woh tumhari Aasmani Kitab par Imaan nahi rakhte) aur jis waqt woh tumse milte hain to (jhoot moot) kahte hain ke ham Imaan le aye hain lekin kab woh tanhai mein hote hain to shadeed ghaez o ghazab se apni ungliyan katne lag jate hain. (Unse kahdo ke tum apne ghusse mein jal maro, Khuda seeno mein chhupe hue (asrar) se aagah hai."_
(Surah Aal-e-Imran: 119)

📚📖
👉 _* Tafseer:*_
Qur'an ki ye ayat Musalmano ko tambi kar rahi hai ke Musalman ghaflat mein na rahen. Dushman jo zaheran dost ban kar uski chaplosi karta hai aur woh uska shikar ho jata hai. Dushman ka kaam ye hota ke Musalmano ke darmiyan ghul mil jana aur unse unke raazo ki talash karna. Jo jange Musalmano ne jeeti iska raaz ye tha ke ek to Musalman muttahid rahe aur kisi dushman ko apna dost nahi banaya. Musalmano ki haar ka nateeja bhi yehi tha ke kucch dushman se ja mile. Hazrat Ali (as) wa Imam Hasan (as) ko Dushman se sulah karni padi uski wajah ye thi ke unke zyada tar sathi dushmano se ja mile. Karbala mein sirf 72 shaheed hue, qatil bhi Musalman the.
Isliye main point jis ki taraf ye ayat tanbi kar rahi hai woh ye hai hame ye parakh honi chahiye Dost kaun hai aur dushman kaun. Dono taraf rahna doghlapan hai.
Ajkal baate hoti hain ittehad ki. Ittehad wahan kiya jata hai jahan ham minority mein hain. Ittehad means tum apne Deen par ham apne Deen par (Qur'an). Iska matlab ye nahi ham unse dosti kar len. Eteqad mein koi ittehad nahi ho sakta. Aaj agar Musalman muttehad hote to Dushman unka kuchh nahi bigad sakta tha, lekin aaj Musalman apne doosre Musalman dushman se ladne ke liye Kafiron Yahoodiyon ka sahara le rahe hain.
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜
----------------------------------------------

_*MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!*_
🙇
Imam Ali (as):
_"Apne dost ke dushman ko kabhi dost na banana kyun ki is tarah tum apne dost ko dushman bana loge."_
(Tajalliyaat e Hikmat, p277), (Tuhaful Uqool, p235)

Imam Ali (as):
_"Khabardaar! Kisi *ehmaq* (bewaqoof) ki dosti ikhtiyaar na karna ke tumhe faaida bhi pahu'nchana chahega to nuqsaan pahu'ncha dega; aur isi tarah kisi *bakheel* (kanjoos) se dosti na karna ke tumse aise waqt mein door bhagega jab tumhe uski shadeed zarurat hogi; aur dekho kisi *faajir* ka saath bhi ikhteyaar na karna ke wo tumhe haqeer cheez ke evaz bhi bech daalega; aur kisi *jhoote* ki sohbat bhi ikhteyaar na karna ke wo misle saraab (mirage, mrigtrishna, mrigjall) hai jo door waale ko qareeb aur qareeb waale ko door kar deta hai."_
(Nahjul Balagah, p641)
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜

*29th Zilqad 1437, 2nd September 2016, Friday,

       ♦ _*SABR-O-ISTEQAMAT*_ ♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (399)
✨
*بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ*

*إِنْ تَمْسَسْكُمْ حَسَنَةٌ تَسُؤْهُمْ وَإِنْ تُصِبْكُمْ سَيِّئَةٌ يَفْرَحُوا بِهَا ۖ وَإِنْ تَصْبِرُوا وَتَتَّقُوا لَا يَضُرُّكُمْ كَيْدُهُمْ شَيْئًا ۗ إِنَّ اللَّهَ بِمَا يَعْمَلُونَ مُحِيطٌ*
✨
_"Agar tumhe koi rahat milti hai to unhe bura lagta hai aur agar tumhe koi nakhush gawar hadsa pesh aa jaye to woh khush ho jate hain lekin tum agar (unke muqable mein) sabit qadami aur Parhezgari ikhtiyar karoge to in ki (khain) sazishen tumhe koi nuqsan nahi pahuncha sakti. Khuda us cheez par ahata rakhta hai jo woh anjam dete hain."_
(Surah Aal-e-Imran: 120)

📚📖 ✨
👉 _* Tafseer:*_
Is ayat mein dushman ki kina o adawat ki ek sign bayan ki gayi hai. Tumhari kamyabi se dushman jalta hai aur bure haalaat mein woh khush hota hai. Lekin Sabr o isteqamat wa Parhezgari ikhtiyar karenge to dushman kabhi tum ko nuqsan nahi pahuncha sakta. Isteqamat, hoshyari, Taqwa shart hai baqi Allah tumhara nigheban hai.
Yehi Ta'leemate Ale Imran hai.
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜
----------------------------------------------

_*MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!*_
🙇 ✨
Imam Taqi (as):
_"Jo khwaishaat e nafs ki pairavi karega, wo dushman ki khwaishaat poori karega."_
(Guftaar e Dil Nasheen, p209)
✨
Imam Taqi (as):
_"Bahut se logo'n se dushmani kiye baghair Khuda ki mohabbat haasil nahi ki jaa sakti."_
(Guftaar e Dil Nasheen, p207)
✨
Imam Taqi (as):
_"Faqeeri ki zeenat (beauty) Iffat (paak-damani) hai, Maaldari ki zeenat Shukr karna hai, Balaa ki zeenat Sabr hai, Kalaam ki zeenat Fasaahat (eloquence) hai.'_
(Guftaar e Dil Nasheen)

         ♦ _*JANG-E-UHUD*_ ♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (401)

*بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ*

*وَإِذْ غَدَوْتَ مِنْ أَهْلِكَ تُبَوِّئُ الْمُؤْمِنِينَ مَقَاعِدَ لِلْقِتَالِ ۗ وَاللَّهُ سَمِيعٌ عَلِيمٌ*
_"Aur (yaad karo) woh waqt jab tum subh ke waqt apne ghar walon se Mo'menin ke liye lashkar e Jang Intekhab karne nikle. Khuda Sunne aur Jannewala hai (Jang ke bare mein jo baat cheet ki gayi aur jo afkar baaz ke dimagh mein parvarish pa rahe hain Khuda unhe Janta hai.)"_
(Surah Aal-e-Imran: 121)

📚📖 ⚔
👉 _* Tafseer:*_
Ye ayat Jang e Uhud ke bare mein hai. Jo 3 Hijri mein hui.

Imam Sadiq (as):
"Jab Quraish ko Jange Badr mein shikasht e fash hui (defeated) aur unke 70 afraad qatl aur 70 zakhmi hue aur baqi manda lashkar zaleel o ruswa hokar Makkah pahuncha. Makkah ki aurten apne maqtoolin ke gham mein rone lagi to Abu Sufyan ne kaha ke rona dhona band karo kiyonki rone se dil ka ghubar halka hota hai. (Rona bidat kis ki ravish hai!!!!) Aur agar dil ka ghubar halka ho gaya to tumhare dilon mein Muhammad (saww) ki dushmani bhi kam ho jayegi. Apne ansuon ko ankho mein rehne do aur inhe quwwat mein badlo. Phir ek saal baad Badr ka badla lene ke liye Abu Sufyan ek giran lashkar lekar ravana hua. Uski fauj mein 3000 sawar aur 2000 piyadah the. Aur woh apne sath aurton ko bhi lekar aye aur unse kaha: 'Jab hamari Muhammad (saww) se jang ho to tum apne Badr ke maqtooleen par zor zor se girya karna taake iske zariye se hamare mardon ko ki ghairat wo hamiyat mein mazeed izafa ho aur zyada diljamii se jang kar saken.
Udhar Rasool (saww) ko jab iski khabar mili to jang ki tayyariyan shuro ho gayi. Aap (saww) 700 afraad ko shaher ke bahar maidan e Uhud mein jama hue.
Aap (saww) ne 50 teerandazo (Archers) ko ek Pahad ke darre par (Valley) par appoint kiya aur uske chief Abdullah bin Jubair the. Aur takeed ki ke kisi bhi haalat mein is maqam ko nahi chhodna.
Abu Sufyan ne Khalid bin Walid ko 200 sawaron ke sath us pahad ke pichhe rakha aur farmaya us Darre par nazar rakho.
Rasoole Khuda (saww) ke lashkar ke Alambardar Hazrat Ali (as) hue. ......"
(Majmaul Bayan, Noorus Saqlain, Tafseer Namoona)
(To be cont'd)
🗡🗡🗡🗡🗡🗡🗡🗡🗡🗡
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜

_*MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!*_
🙇 ⚔
Imam Sadiq (as):
_"Jab Musalman Jung mein Rasule Khuda (saww) ke saath jaate aur aisi jagah se guzar hota jahaa'n ghaney darakht hote (dense forest) phir sehra mein nikalte aur ek dusre ko dekhte to phir Musafeha karte."_
(Al Kaafi, v4, p89)
⚔

(Man La Yahzarahul Faqih, v4, p318)

         ♦ _*JANG-E-UHUD*_ ♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (402)

*بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ*

*إِذْ هَمَّتْ طَائِفَتَانِ مِنْكُمْ أَنْ تَفْشَلَا وَاللَّهُ وَلِيُّهُمَا ۗ وَعَلَى اللَّهِ فَلْيَتَوَكَّلِ الْمُؤْمِنُونَ*
_"Aur (yaad karo) woh waqt jab tum mein do girohon ne susti ka muzahera karne ka mukammal irada kiya (aur chaha ke woh raste se palat jayen) aur Khuda unka madadgar tha (ke woh is fikr se baaz aa jayen) aur Ahle Imaan ko sirf Khuda par tawakkal karna chahiye."_
(Surah Aal-e-Imran: 122)


📚📖
👉 _* Tafseer:*_
*Jang e Uhud:* (Cont'd)
Imam Sadiq (as) ki rivayat ka khualasa kal se jari ....

'Jange Uhud shuru hui ek taraf sada e Allah o Akbar aur doosri taraf Quraishi ladkiyon ke musical ashaar. Lashkar e Islam ne mazbooti ke sath se hamla kiya. Musalmano ka padla kuchh der bhari raha. Lashkar e Kuffar ne rahe farar ikhtiyar ki. Musalman maale ghanimat (Booty of war) lootne mein lag gaye. Jab Abdullah bin Jubair ke sathi jo pahadi Darre par the jin ko wahan se hatne ke liye Rasool (saww) ne mana kiya tha, woh bhi wahan se hat kar maal ghanimat ki taraf badhe. Khalid bin Walid jo isi Intezar mein tha wahan se Musalmano par pichhe se hamla kiya. Kamyab Jang nuqsan mein tabdeel ho gayi. Hazrat Ali (as) ma'arke mein date rahe aur Kuffar ko wasil e Jahannam karte rahe. Khalid bin Walid ke hamle se Musalmano ki safen titar bitar hone lagi. Bhagte hue Musalmano se Rasool (saww) mukhatib hue:
_'Kiya tum Khuda aur uske Rasool ko chhod kar bhag rahe ho."_
Janabe Hamza jo bahut bahaduri se lad rahe the, Shaheed hue. Abu Sufyan ki biwi Hinda ne Janabe Hamza ka kaleja chabaya. Dubara us kamini ne unka azu e tanasul aur unke kaan aur hath pair kaate.
Jang ke maidan mein sirf jo bache aur Rasool (saww) ko ghere hue the woh the Hazrat Ali (as), Abu Dujana, Samak bin Kharsha. Jang ke dauran Hazrat Ali (as) ki talwar tooti. Rasool (saww) ne Allah ki taraf se nazil hui talwar 'Zulfiqar' Ali (as) ko pesh ki. Hazrat Ali (as) ne apni Jura'at aur taqat ka bhar poor muzahera kiya aur is jang mein aapko 70 zakhm lage.'
(Majmaul Bayan, Noorus Saqlain, Tafseer Namoona)
Tarikh mein ham dekhte hain Rasool (saww) ki rehlat ke baad jo log is Jang mein bhage the aur Ale Hinda wa Sufyan ko Musalmano ne takhte Khilafat par bithaya aur Ale Imraan,  Khandane Rasool (saww) hamesha inke mazloom rahe.
(Poori tarikh Ahle Sunnat ki mashoor kitab Al milal wan Nahl mein maujood hai)
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜
----------------------------------------------

_*MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!*_
🙇
Riwayat:
Jab Rasule Khuda (saww) Jung e Uhad se laute aur unhone Sayyad ush Shohda J. Hamza ke ghar se girya o zaari nahi suni jab ke doosre shahido'n ke ghar se rone ki awaaz aa rahi thi, to aap ne kaha, _"Kya koi khaatun nahi hai jo Hamza par girya kare?"_ Jab Saad bin Maaz, Usaid bin Hazeer aur doosre Ansaar ne ye suna to wo apne apne ghar gaye aur aurato'n se kaha ke wo pehle J. Hamza ke ghar jaa-kar unpar girya kare phir apne Shahido'n par roye. Shaam ke waqt Ansaar ki khawaateen J. Hamza ke ghar gayi aur aadhi raat tak unpar girya kiya. Jab Rasule Khuda (saww) bedaar huwe to unhone sawaal kiya ke ye rone ki awaaz kyu'n aa rahi hai? Jab unhe haqeeqat bataayi gayi to wo khush huwe aur girya karne waali khawaateen ko ye keh-kar Dua di ke, _"Allah tum se raazi rahe aur tumhari aulaad se raazi rahe."_
(Ye waaqeya Islami taarikh / history ki mash'hoor kitaab Rauzatus Safa, v2 aur Madarijunn Nabuwwah aur Maarijunn Nabuwwah wagairah mein naql kiya gaya hai)
(Understanding Karbala - Allama Syed Saeed Akhtar Rizvi, p155)
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜
----------------------------------------------
*3rd ZilHajj 1437, 6th September 2016, Monday,

           ♦ _*JANG-E-BADR*_ ♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (403)

*بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ*

*وَلَقَدْ نَصَرَكُمُ اللَّهُ بِبَدْرٍ وَأَنْتُمْ أَذِلَّةٌ ۖ فَاتَّقُوا اللَّهَ لَعَلَّكُمْ تَشْكُرُونَ*

_"Khuda ne Badr mein tumhari madad ki (aur tum khatarnak dushman par fatehyab hue) jabke tum unki nisbat natawan (powerless) the pas Khuda se daro aur dushman ke muqable mein hukme Paighambar ki nafarmani na karo) taake tum uski Nemat ka shukr ada karne walon mein shumar ho."_
(Surah Aal-e-Imran: 123)

📚📖 ⚔
👉 _* Tafseer:*_

*Jang-e-Badr*

Badr literary means 'Full' aur 'Perfect' 'Kamil'. Chaudhvi ke Chand ko bhi Badr kahte hai.

Jang e Uhud ke natije mein ye Ayat nazil hui. Jange Uhud ke ikhtetam par Mushrekin ke Lashkar ne Makkah lautne ke bajai Madina ka irada kiya taake Hazrat Muhammad (saww) ko Shaheed kare. Madina taraaj kiya jaye (jo ke unki Aal ne Karbala ke waqea ke baad kiya). Ye khabar jab Rasool (saww) ko pahunchi aur ye ayat Nazil hue. Musalmano ko josh dilaya gaya. Lekin chunke dushman Rasool (saww) haqeeqi ansaar ko janta tha isliye dushman ne ghanimat samjha ke wapas laut jaye.
Islam mein ki pahli Jang Jang-e-Badr hai. Jis mein sirf 313 Musalman the aur Mushrekin ki tadaad 1000 aur kafi asleha (weapons) the. Is comparison mein Jang jeetna mumkin nahi tha lekin Allah ki madad aur Musalmano ka khuloos ki wajah se ye Jang Fatehyab hui.
(To be cont'd.....)
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜
----------------------------------------------

_*MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!*_
🙇
Mufazzal bin Umar ki rivayat:
Imam Sadiq (as):
_"Goya mein dekh raha hun ke Qaem e Ale Muhammad (Imam Mahdi) (atfs) Kufa par tashreef farma hain aur unke ird gird Ashaab e Badr ki tadaad ke mutabiq 313 afraad baithe hue hain."_
(Tafseer Noorus Saqlain, Kamaluddin)
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜
----------------------------------------------
*4th ZilHajj 1437, 7th September 2016, Wednesday,
🔹🔹🔹🔹🔹🔹🔹🔹🔹🔹

BAZM-E-ADAB WELCOMES YOU*

           ♦ _*JANG-E-BADR*_ ♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (404)

*بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ*

*إِذْ تَقُولُ لِلْمُؤْمِنِينَ أَلَنْ يَكْفِيَكُمْ أَنْ يُمِدَّكُمْ رَبُّكُمْ بِثَلَاثَةِ آلَافٍ مِنَ الْمَلَائِكَةِ مُنْزَلِينَ * بَلَىٰ ۚ إِنْ تَصْبِرُوا وَتَتَّقُوا وَيَأْتُوكُمْ مِنْ فَوْرِهِمْ هَٰذَا يُمْدِدْكُمْ رَبُّكُمْ بِخَمْسَةِ آلَافٍ مِنَ الْمَلَائِكَةِ مُسَوِّمِينَ*

_"Jis waqt tum Mo'menin se kahte the ke kiya kafi nahi ke tumhara Parwardegar 3000 Malaeka (Aasmaan se) utar kar tumhari madad kare."_
_"Haan! (Aaj bhi) agar tum Sabr o Isteqamat aur Parhezgari ikhtiyar karo aur jab dushman tum par chadh ayega to Khuda 5000 makhsoos nishan rakhne wale Farishton ke zariye tumhari madad karega."_
(Surah Aal-e-Imran: 124-125)

📚📖 🗡
👉 _* Tafseer:*_

*Jang-e-Badr:*
Jaisa ke hamne kal bataya ke Islam ke woh pahli Jang ji mein Musalman kam aur Kuffar zyada the, Lekin Musalmano ko Kamyabi mili. Is ki wajah is ayat mein bayan ki hai: Sabr o Isteqamat aur Parhezgari. Pichhli Ayat mein bataya tha ke chunki is mein Allah ki madad shamil haal thi.

Imam Moosa Kazim (as):
_"Jo Farishte Badr mein nazil hue the unhone Amame bandhe hue the aur uska ek sira aage latka hua tha aur ek sira pichhe latka hua tha. "_
Imam Baqir (as):
_" Badr mein jo Farishte utre the unhone safed  pagdiya (turban) bandhi hui thi."_
🗡🗡🗡🗡🗡🗡🗡🗡🗡🗡
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜
----------------------------------------------

_*MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!*_
🙇 🗡
Imam Mohd Baqir (as):
_"Jang e Badr mein Rasoole Akram (saww) ki madad ke liye 5000 Farishte nazil hue the aur woh Aasmaan par abhi tak nahi gaye aur jab Qaem e Ale Muhammad (atfs) (Imam Mahdi) ka zahoor hoga to woh unki madad karenge."_

Rasule Khuda (saww):
_"Kaala rang makrooh hai magar 3 kaali cheezein istemaal ki jaa sakti hain:_
(1) Amama,
(2) Moza (socks) aur
(3) Rida (chaadar)."
(Khisaal, p88)
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜

*5th ZilHajj 1437, 8th September 2016, Thursday,

           ♦ _*JANG-E-BADR*_ ♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (405)

*بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ*

*وَمَا جَعَلَهُ اللَّهُ إِلَّا بُشْرَىٰ لَكُمْ وَلِتَطْمَئِنَّ قُلُوبُكُمْ بِهِ ۗ وَمَا النَّصْرُ إِلَّا مِنْ عِنْدِ اللَّهِ الْعَزِيزِ الْحَكِيمِ * لِيَقْطَعَ طَرَفًا مِنَ الَّذِينَ كَفَرُوا أَوْ يَكْبِتَهُمْ فَيَنْقَلِبُوا خَائِبِينَ*

_"Lekin ye sab kuchh to sirf tumhe basharat dene ke liye aur tumhare itminan ki khatir hai warna Kamyabi to faqat Khudai Tawana wa Hakim (Mighty & Wise) ki taraf se hai."_
_"(Ye Wada jo Khuda ne tumhare sath kiya hai) is liye hai taake Lashkar e Kuffar ke ek hisse ko qata  kar de ya inhe zillat ke sath patai taake woh maayoos ho kar (apne ilaqe ko) palat jayen."_
(Surah Aal-e-Imran: 126 - 127)

📚📖 ✨✨
👉 _* Tafseer:*_
Jaisa ke pichhli ayaton ke mein bata chuke hain Jange Badr mein Khuda ki Madad shamil e haal thi kiyonki us Jang mein Nau Musalmano ne pur khuloos wa muttahid hokar Kuffar se muqabla kiya aur unhe zalil wa ruswa kar ke lauta diya.
Jang ki Aur tafseel Sura Anfal mein ayegi.
Do Jango ki misal mein ye pata chala ke ek mein Sabr o Isteqamat thi to Fateh o Kamyabi hasil hui, jahan Musalmano ko Allah Rasool par bharosa nahi raha wahan shikast (defeat) hui.
Kahi bhi agar hame Kamyabi nazar aa rahi hai to samajhye Allah ki madad zaroor shamil e haal hai, aur Allah sab ko madad nahi karta. Jis ko Allah Chahta ya Mehboob rakhta hai usi ki madad karega. Sab cheezon ka talluq hamare Imaan o Amal se hai.
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜
----------------------------------------------

_*MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!*_
🙇 ✨✨
Rasule Khuda (saww):
_"Jab kisi bande par zulm hota hai jiska wo inteqaam nahi le sakta, na hi uska koi naasir o madadgaar hota hai, aur wo zulm hone par apni nigaah aasmaan ki taraf kar ke Allah se Dua maangta hai to Khuda Wande Aalam farmata hai, Labbaik Mere bande, Main duniya mein bhi teri madad karunga aur Aakherat mein bhi."_
(Meezan ul Hikmah, v5, p866)
✨✨
Rasule Khuda (saww):
_"Jo Musalman ki pus e pusht (peethh peechhe) madad kare, Allah uski Duniya o Akherat mein madad karega."_
(Hadiyat ush Shia, p18)
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜

*6th ZilHajj 1437, 9th September 2016, Friday,

BAZM-E-ADAB COMMEMORATE  SHAHADAT OF IMAM MOHAMMAD BAQIR (as)*
