⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜
               ♦ _*TAUBA*_ ♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (406)

*بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ*

*لَيْسَ لَكَ مِنَ الْأَمْرِ شَيْءٌ أَوْ يَتُوبَ عَلَيْهِمْ أَوْ يُعَذِّبَهُمْ فَإِنَّهُمْ ظَالِمُونَ*

_"Kisi qism ka ikhtiyar (Kuffar aur Jang se farar karne wale Musalmano ke faisle ke bare mein) tumhe nahi hai magar ye ke Khuda chahe inhe dar guzar kar de ya saza de kiyonki woh zalim hain."_
(Surah Aal-e-Imran: 128)

📚📖
👉 _* Tafseer:*_
Allah Ta'ala ne bahut jagah farmaya hai _'Use ikhtiyar hai jise chahe bakhsh de aur jise chahe Azaab de'_ ke alfaz irshad farmaye hain aur wazeh nahi kiya ke Woh kis ki maghferat karega aur kis ko Azaab dega. Usko mubham (ambiguous) rakhne mein raaz ye hai ke insaan hamesha umeed aur khauf ki manzelat par rahe. Itni umeed na ho ke Azaabe Ilahi se bekhauf ho jaye aur itna khauf na ho ke Rehmat e Ilahi se maayoos ho jaye aur woh umeed aur khauf ke bain bain rahe.
Imam Sadiq (as):
_"Agar Momin ke khauf aur uski umeed ka wazan kiya jay to dono ka padla barabar hoga."_
(Majmaul Bayan, Noorus Saqlain)
Kuchh log ye safai pesh karte ke Yazid ne bhale hi zulm kiya lekin Allah use maaf bhi kar sakta hai isliye hame uske karnamo ki mazammat nahi karni chahiye.
Ye baat ek ba Aql insaan ke liye ahmaqana hai. Ek shakhs zulm kare aur bakhsh diya jaye kaise mumkin. Ham Allah ko Hakeem o Dana mante hain, Woh insafwar hai. Ayat mein bataya gaya hai ke insaan ko koi ikhtiyar nahi ke khud natija nikal le ye shakhs Jahannam mein nahi jayega ya koi Jannat mein. Allah ne hukm diya hai ke Zalim ki mazammat (condemn) kiya jaye. Agar unke usool par chala jaye ke sab khatakar maaf kar diye jayenge to phir har koi zulm karke yehi kahega. Isliye faisla Allah ke hath par chhodte hain lekin Allah ki Hikmat ko bhi jante hain.
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜
----------------------------------------------

_*MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!*_
🙇
Imam Ali (as):
_"Gunaho'n ka tark (avoid) karna Tauba karne se zyada behtar hai."_
(Meezan ul Hikmah, v1, p807)

Imam e Shafaee (Ahle Sunnat ke Imam) ne ailaan kiya hai ke,
_“Agar Aal e Muhammad (as) ki mohabbat gunah hai to ye ek aisa gunah hai ke jis se main kabhi Tauba nahi kar sakta aur agar Aal e Muhammad (as) ki mohabbat ka naam hi Rafz hai to tamaam duniya ke logo’n mein sabse bada Raafizi main hoon.”_
(Haqeeqat e Tabarra by Allamah Farogh Kazmi, p41)
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜
----------------------------------------------
*7th ZilHajj 1437, 10th September 2016, Saturday,
🔹🔹🔹🔹🔹🔹🔹🔹🔹🔹

BAZM-E-ADAB WELCOMES YOU*

⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜
           ♦ _*ALLAH: MALIK HAI*_ ♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (407)

*بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ*

*وَلِلَّهِ مَا فِي السَّمَاوَاتِ وَمَا فِي الْأَرْضِ ۚ يَغْفِرُ لِمَنْ يَشَاءُ وَيُعَذِّبُ مَنْ يَشَاءُ ۚ وَاللَّهُ غَفُورٌ رَحِيمٌ*

_"Aur jo kuchh Aasmano aur Zameen mein hai woh Allah ki milkiyat (Ownership) hai, Woh jise chahta hai (aur munasib samajhta hai) bakhsh deta hai aur jise chahta hai Azaab deta hai aur Khuda Bakhshnewala, Meherban hai."_
(Surah Aal-e-Imran: 129)

📚📖
👉 _* Tafseer:*_
Ham Allah ke bande hain, hame Allah ne khalq kiya hai. Allah ham par puri tarah se Muheet hai. Woh hamara Malik hai. Agar hame in sab baton par yaqin e Kamil ho jay to kiya ham gunah kar sakte hain. Kiya ham Allah ke siwa kisi aur se sawal kar sakte hain. Ye Insaan ka idhar udhar bhatakna batata hain ke uska Allah par etemaad nahi hai.
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜
----------------------------------------------

_*MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!*_
🙇
Imam Sajjad (as):
_"Hamd hai Us Allah ke liye ke jab chaahoo'n apni haajat ke liye pukaarta hoo'n aur jab chaahoo'n tanhaai mein baghair kisi siraarshi ke Us se raaz o niyaaz karta hu'n, to Wo meri haajat poori karta hai. Hamd hai Us Allah ke liye jiske siwaa main kisi ko nahi pukaarta aur agar Uske ghair se Dua karu'n to Wo meri Dua qubool nahi karega. Hamd hai Us Allah ke liye jiske ghair se main ummeed nahi rakhta aur agar ummeed rakhoo'n bhi to wo meri ummeed poori nahi karega."_
(Dua e Abu Hamza Sumaali)
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜

*8th ZilHajj 1437, 11th September 2016, Sunday,

BAZM-E-ADAB COMMEMORATE SHAHADAT OF MUSLIM BIN AQEEL (as)*

         ♦ _*SOOD - INTEREST*_♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (408)

*بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ*

*يَا أَيُّهَا الَّذِينَ آمَنُوا لَا تَأْكُلُوا الرِّبَا أَضْعَافًا مُضَاعَفَةً ۖ وَاتَّقُوا اللَّهَ لَعَلَّكُمْ تُفْلِحُونَ*

_"Aye Imaanwalo!  Dugna chaugna Sood (Interest/Bayaz) na khao aur Allah ke Azaab se darte raho taake tum nijat hasil kar sako."_
(Surah Aal-e-Imran: 130)

📚📖 💰
👉 _* Tafseer:*_

Pichhli ayaton mein ham is topic par zikr kar chuke hain. Same ham phir repeat kar rahe hain:
Sood aur Tijarat dono brabar nahi hote. Dono mein farq hai:
(1) Aam khareed o furokht mein dono side nafa nuqsan brabar sharik hote hain. Jabke Soodi karobar mein Soodi idare din na din daulat mand hote jate hain aur kamzor aur zyada interest de de kar ghareeb hota chala jata hai.
(2) General Business mein Capitalist (jo maal lagata hai) uske maqsad production aur consumption ki taraf rahta hai.
Jabke Interest Business mein aisa kuchh nahi.
(3) Sood khuri (Interest Business) aam honse Capital (sarmaya) ka ghalat istemal hota hai, jisse Economic Crisis (Iqtesadi gadbad) paida hoti hai. Jabke Business mein Capital ka sahi istemal hota hai.
(4) Sood khuri logon ke economic level ki jang o kashmakash ki wajah se hai.  Lekin Business mein aisa kuchh nahi hai.

'Majmaul Bayan mein hai ke ke Allah ne Sood ko Haram qarar diya kiyonki Sood se Muashara (Society) mein kharabiyan janam leti hain. Jis Samaj mein Soodi Karobar common ho jaye to wahan ko kisi ko Qarza-e-Hasana dena pasand nahi karta aur koi apne maqrooz ko farakh dast hone tak mohlat dene par amaada nahi hota.'
(Noorus Saqlain)

Allah jis kam ko Haram qarar deta wo hamare liye nuqsandeh hota, Woh behtar Jannewala hai. Agar him kisi Haram amal ko achha samajh rahe hain to ye hamari kam ilmi ki bena par hai.
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜
----------------------------------------------

_*MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!*_
🙇 💰
Rasule khuda(saww):
_"Jo shakhs len-den karna chaahta hai usay 5 cheezo'n se bachna chaahiye:_
1] Sood [interest / vyaaj],
2] Qasam khaana,
3] Maal ka aib chhupana,
4] Jo cheez doosro'n ko BECHNI ho uski taarif karna, aur
5] Jo cheez auro'n se kharidna ho uski buraai karna."
(Tehzibul Islam)
💰
Imam Ali (as):
_"Aye saudagaro'n! Pehle Tijaarat [business] ke masle (rules) yaad kar lo phir tijaarat mein mashgool ho, kyun ki is Ummat ke liye Munaafa aur Suud [interest] ka fark chi'nti (ant) ke paao'n ke oos nishaan se bhi zyaada baarik hai jo sakht patthar par bana ho.. "_
(Tehzibul Islam)
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜
----------------------------------------------
*9th ZilHajj 1437, 12th September 2016, Monday,
🔹🔹🔹🔹🔹🔹🔹🔹🔹🔹
BAZM-E-ADAB WELCOMES YOU*

               ♦ _*TAQWA*_ ♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (412)

*بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ*

*وَاتَّقُوا النَّارَ الَّتِي أُعِدَّتْ لِلْكَافِرِينَ*

_"Aur us aag se daro jo Kafiron ke liye tayyar ki gayi hai. "_
(Surah Aal-e-Imran: 131)

📚📖
👉 _* Tafseer:*_
*وَاتَّقُوا اللَّهَ لَعَلَّكُمْ تُفْلِحُونَ*
Is se pahli ayat mein kaha gaya tha ke agar Kamyab hona hai to Taqwa ikhtiyar karo. Taqwa yani Khauf-e-Khuda (Fear of God). Sath hi sath is ayat mein ye bhi bataya ke us Jahannam ki Aag se bhi daro jo Kafiron ke liye banayi gayi hai. Agar kisi pas Khauf e Khuda aur Jahannam ka dar nahi to uske Aamaal wa umoor  asar andaz hote hai. Phir insaan pasti ki taraf jata hai, but parasti karta, shirk karta hai. Ek Khuda ke alawa kai kai Khuda bana deta hai. Ganpati ke ird gird ghoomta hai. Is tarah Haq ko Cover karta hai aur Kafir ban jata hai. Aur Jahannam Kafiron ke liye banayi gayi hai.
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜
----------------------------------------------

_*MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!*_
🙇
Imam Sajjad (as):
_"Khauf e Khuda ka matlab rona aur aa'nsu bahana nahi hai, kyun ki jab Taqwa na ho jo usay gunaho'n se roke, ye khauf jhoota hai."_
(Uddatud Daee, ch4)

Rasule Khuda (saww):
_"Aye Ali (as)! 3 baatein jiske andar na ho uska koi amal durust nahi hoga._
_1) Aisa Taqwa jo usko Khuda ki maasiyato'n se roke,_
_2) Aisa Ilm jis se bewaqoofo'n ki jihaalat ko duur kar sakey,_
_3) Aisi Aql jis se logo'n se milansaari se pesh aaye._
(Guftaar e Dil Nasheen, p25)
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜
----------------------------------------------
*13th ZilHajj 1437, 16th September 2016, Friday,
🔹🔹🔹🔹🔹🔹🔹🔹🔹🔹

BAZM-E-ADAB WELCOMES YOU*

♦ _*ALLAH: SARI KAINAT KA MALIK*_♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (581) 🌏

*بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ*

*وَلِلَّهِ مَا فِي السَّمَاوَاتِ وَمَا فِي الْأَرْضِ ۗ وَلَقَدْ وَصَّيْنَا الَّذِينَ أُوتُوا الْكِتَابَ مِنْ قَبْلِكُمْ وَإِيَّاكُمْ أَنِ اتَّقُوا اللَّهَ ۚ وَإِنْ تَكْفُرُوا فَإِنَّ لِلَّهِ مَا فِي السَّمَاوَاتِ وَمَا فِي الْأَرْضِ ۚ وَكَانَ اللَّهُ غَنِيًّا حَمِيدًا * وَلِلَّهِ مَا فِي السَّمَاوَاتِ وَمَا فِي الْأَرْضِ ۚ وَكَفَىٰ بِاللَّهِ وَكِيلًا * إِنْ يَشَأْ يُذْهِبْكُمْ أَيُّهَا النَّاسُ وَيَأْتِ بِآخَرِينَ ۚ وَكَانَ اللَّهُ عَلَىٰ ذَٰلِكَ قَدِيرًا*

_"Aasmaano aur Zameen ki tamam cheezen Allah ki Milkiyyat hain. Ham ne tum se pahle Ahle Kitab ko aur ab tum ko ye Wasiyyat ki hai ke Allah se Darte raho (Taqwa). Aur agar tum ne Kufr ka ravayya ikhtiyar kiya to yaad rakho ke Aasmaano aur Zameen ki tamam cheezen Khuda ki Milkiyyat hain. Woh Beniyaz aur har Ta'reef ke qabil hai."_
_"Aur Aasmaano aur Zameen ki tamam Ashya Khuda ki Milkiyyat hain aur bataure Karsaaz Khuda Kafi hai."_
_"Agar Chahe to tum logon ko Zameen se hata kar tumhari jagah doosron ko le aaye aur Allah isi par Qadir hai."_
(Surah Nisa: 131 - 133)

📚📖 🌏
👉 _* Tafseer:*_
Poori Kainat ka Maalik Allah hai. Shuru se akhir tak Allah ne ek advice di ke Allah se daro means Taqwa o Parhezgari ikhtiyar karo. Jo zaat aise Lamutanahi hai (Unlimited) aur be payan Qudrat rakhti hai woh apne Bando ko Beniyaz karne se Aajiz nahi ho sakti. Taqwa ikhtiyar karna hamare liye fayde mand hai aur Khuda ko iski zaroorat nahi. Khuda ki nafarmani se khud insaan ko hi nuqsaan hoga. Allah ki Milkiyyat ka takraar is baat ki ahmiyat ko bata raha hai ki itni Azeem Zaat ki nafarmani karoge to tumhara kiya hashr hoga. Is liye zaroori hai ke ham Gunahon se parhez karen.
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜
✍🏻___Syed Shoeb Raza Abdi
----------------------------------------------

_*MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!*_
🙇 🍂
Imam Askari (as):
_"Taqwa e Ilahi ikhtiyaar karo aur (hamare liye) baais e zeenat bano, baais e buraayi na bano."_
(Guftaar e Dil Nasheen, p243)
🍃
Imam Sajjad (as):
_"Khauf e Khuda ka matlab rona aur aa'nsu bahana nahi hai, kyun ki jab Taqwa na ho jo usay gunaho'n se roke, ye khauf jhoota hai."_
(Uddatud Daee, ch4)
🌿
Imam Ali (as):
Yaqeenan aksar log 2 khoobiyo'n ki wajah se Jannat mein daakhil honge aur wo 2 khoobiyaa'n hain: Taqwa aur Husn e Khulq."_
(good manners)
(Hadiyat ush Shia, p35)
☘
Rasule Khuda (saww)
se puchha gaya, _"Ya Rasulallah! Islam kya hai? Uski khususiyat bayaan farmayein"._
Aap (saww) ne farmaya: _"Islam uryiaa'n hai yaani baghair libaas hai uska libaas Taqwa hai, uski zeenat Hayaa aur Parhezgaari uska maalik aur uska kamaal hai. Uska phal (fruit) nek aamal hain aur har cheez ki ek buniyaad hai aur Islam ki buniyaad hum Ahlebait (as) ki mohabbat hai"._
(Amaali - Shaikh Toosi, v1, p221)

                 ♦ _*DUNIYA*_ ♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (582) 🌏

*بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ*

*مَنْ كَانَ يُرِيدُ ثَوَابَ الدُّنْيَا فَعِنْدَ اللَّهِ ثَوَابُ الدُّنْيَا وَالْآخِرَةِ ۚ وَكَانَ اللَّهُ سَمِيعًا بَصِيرًا*

_"Jo Shakhs Duniyavi badla ka khwahish mand ho to use maloom hona chahiye ke Allah ke paas Duniya ka Sawab bhi aur Akherat ka Sawab bhi hai aur Allah Sunnewala aur Dekhnewala hai."_
(Surah Nisa: 134)

📚📖 🌏 _* Tafseer:*_
----------------------------------------------

_*MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!*_
🙇 🌏
*Q: Duniya ko Duniya kiyon kahte hai?*
Amirul Momenin Ali (as) ne ek Yahoodi sawal ka Jawab diya:
_"Ye lafz ' *دنو*' se derived hai jiske maani hain 'Qareeb' aur chunke Duniya qareeb hai isi liye use Duniya kaha jata hai jabke Aamaal ki jaza wa saza ka Din takhir se aata hai isi liye is Din ko 'Yaum e Akherat *يوم آخرت*' kaha jata hai."_
(Ilalus Sharai, Noorus Saqlain)
🌏
Rasoole Akram (as):
_"Ye lafz ' *دناءت*' se derived (mushtaq) hai aur Duniya ka ghar chunke intihai ghatiya hai, isi liye isko 'Duniya' kaha jata hai. Agar Duniya ko Akherat ke sath paida kiya jata to Ahle Duniya bhi Ahle Akherat ki tarah se fana hote. ' *آخرت*' ki wajah tasmiyyah ye hai ke woh Duniya ke baad takhir se qaem hogi. Iske saalon ki kaifiyat bayan nahi ki ja sakti aur iske dino ko shumar nahi kiya ja sakta aur Ahle Akherat par Maut taari na hogi."_
(Noorus Saqlain)
🌏
Imam Sadiq (as):
_"Duniya baik waqt 'Talib' bhi hai, 'Matloob' bhi hai. Jo Duniya ko Talab karta hai to Maut us Talibe Duniya ko Talab karti hai, yahan tak ke use Duniya se bahar nikal leti hai aur jo Akherat ko talab karta hai to Duniya bhi use talab karti hai aur woh Duniya mein rah kar apne hisse ka rizq khata hai."_
(Man La Yahzarul Faqih, Chap Nawadir)
🌏
Imam Jafar Sadiq (as):
_"Jo Shakhs apne dil ko Duniya se lagayega to us ke evaz woh 3 baaton mein mubtela ho jayega:_
_(1) Kabhi na khatam hone._
_(2) Poori na hone wali Aarzoo._
_(3) Kabhi hasil na hone wali khwahish."_
(Noorus Saqlain)
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜
✍🏻___Syed Shoeb Raza Abdi
----------------------------------------------
*28th Jamadi us Sani 1438, 28th March 2017, Tuesday,
🔹🔹🔹🔹🔹🔹🔹🔹🔹🔹

BAZM-E-ADAB WELCOMES YOU*

               ♦ _*ADAALAT*_ ♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (583) ⚖

*بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ*

*يَا أَيُّهَا الَّذِينَ آمَنُوا كُونُوا قَوَّامِينَ بِالْقِسْطِ شُهَدَاءَ لِلَّهِ وَلَوْ عَلَىٰ أَنْفُسِكُمْ أَوِ الْوَالِدَيْنِ وَالْأَقْرَبِينَ ۚ إِنْ يَكُنْ غَنِيًّا أَوْ فَقِيرًا فَاللَّهُ أَوْلَىٰ بِهِمَا ۖ فَلَا تَتَّبِعُوا الْهَوَىٰ أَنْ تَعْدِلُوا ۚ وَإِنْ تَلْوُوا أَوْ تُعْرِضُوا فَإِنَّ اللَّهَ كَانَ بِمَا تَعْمَلُونَ خَبِيرًا*

_"Aye Imaan Walo! Insaaf ke Alambardar bano. Allah ke liye Gawah bano agarche tumhare Gawahi khud tumhare liye ya tumhare Waledain ke liye ya tumhare Rishtedaron ke liye nuqsan deh hi kiyon na ho. Fareeq e Maamla khwah Maldaar ho ya Ghareeb, Allah tum se zyada unka Khairkhwah hai. Lehaza Khwaheshat ki pairavi na karo taake Insaaf kar sakoge. Agar tum ne lagi lipti baat kahi ya Sachchai se pahlu bachaya to jaan lo ke tumhare Aamaal ki Allah ko sab Khabar hai."_
(Surah Nisa: 135)

📚📖 ⚖
👉 _* Tafseer:*_
Agar aap Allah ko Haazir o Naazir jaante hain to Allah ka hukm hai ke Insaaf qaem karo. Adaalat ke maamle mein yahan apno ki paasdari se door rahne ki nasihat ki gayi hai. Agar Adaalat mein tarafdari barti gayi to Insaaf barqaraar nahi rakha ja sakta. Hazrat Ali (as) ne Adaalat ki bahut si misalen pesh ki: Jaise do Auraten is baat par lad rahi thi ke ye bachha unka hai. Ali (as) ne faisla sunaya ke bachche ko kaat kar adha adha dono de diya jaye. Ek Aurat ne kaha ke bachcha doosri Aurat ko de diya jaye lekin kaata na jaye. Ali (as) ne farmaya ke yehi iski Maa hai. Is tarah ke bahut waqeat kitabo mein darj hain refer karen.
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜
✍🏻___Syed Shoeb Raza Abdi
----------------------------------------------

_*MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!*_
🙇 ⚖
Imam Jafar Sadiq (as):
_"Qayamat ke Din 3 qism ke afraad tamam makhlooq mein se Khuda ke zyada qareeb honge yahan tak ke Allah Hisaab se farigh ho jaye.: Woh Shakhs hai jo:_
_(1) Qudrat rakhte hue bhi apne se kamzor par zulm na kare._
_(2) Do Afraad ke darmiyan chale magar woh kisi ek ki taraf joo barabar bhi mael (incline) na ho._
_(3) Har haal mein Haq baat kahe khwah usse uska fayda hota ya nuqsan._"
(Kitabul Khisaal)
⚖
Imam Sadiq (as):
_"Jhooti gawaahi dene wala Dozakh ke alawa kahi'n aur nahi jayega."_
(Amaali - Shaikh Sadooq, p450)

               ♦ _*IMAAN*_ ♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (584) 💐

*بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ*

*يَا أَيُّهَا الَّذِينَ آمَنُوا آمِنُوا بِاللَّهِ وَرَسُولِهِ وَالْكِتَابِ الَّذِي نَزَّلَ عَلَىٰ رَسُولِهِ وَالْكِتَابِ الَّذِي أَنْزَلَ مِنْ قَبْلُ ۚ وَمَنْ يَكْفُرْ بِاللَّهِ وَمَلَائِكَتِهِ وَكُتُبِهِ وَرُسُلِهِ وَالْيَوْمِ الْآخِرِ فَقَدْ ضَلَّ ضَلَالًا بَعِيدًا*

_"Aye Imaan walo! (Waqai) Imaan le aao Khuda par, Uske Paighambar par, Uski Kitab par jo us par nazil hui aur un (Aasmani) Kutub par jo isse pahle bheji gayi hain aur jo Shakhs Khuda, Uske Malaeka (Angels), Uski Kutub, Uske Rusul aur Roze Akherat ka inkar kare woh bahut door ki Gumrahi mein mubtela hai."_
(Surah Nisa: 136)

📚📖  _* Tafseer:*_
_*MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!*_
🙇 🍀
Imam Ali (as):
_"Imaan zabaan se iqraar aur dil se maarefat aur aa'za se amal karne ke majmu'e ka naam hai."_
(Uyoon Akhbaar ar Reza, v2, p77)
🌻
Imam Reza (as):
_"Imaan Islam se ek darja afzal hai, aur TAQWA Imaan se, aur YAQEEN Imaan se, aur Adam ki Aulad ko Yaqeen se afzal koi cheez nahi di gayi."_
(Bihaar ul Anwaar v78, p338)
(Guftaar e Dil Nasheen)
🌼
Imam Sadiq (as):
_"Imaan ke hote huwe koi amal nuqsaan nahi pahu'nchata aur kufr ke hote huwe koi amal fayda nahi pahu'nchata."_
(Irshadaat e Masumeen (as), p82)
🌺
Rasule Khuda (saww):
_"Ali (as) ki mohabbat Imaan hai aur Ali (as) ka bugz kufr hai."_
(Hadiyat ush Shia, p123)
🌷
Rasule Khuda (saww):
_"Kisi shakhs ke dil mein Imaan us waqt tak daakhil nahi ho sakta jab tak wo mere Ahlebait (as) ke saath Allah aur uske Rasul (saww) ki khaatir mohabbat na rakhta ho."_
(Amaali - Shaikh Toosi, v1, p133)
🌹
*Imam Mohd Baqir (as):*
_"Jo shakhs har *Jumeraat* ko apne Naakhun kaate to uski Aulad ki bhi aa'nkh nahi aayegi (even his children will not suffer from eye pain / conjunctivitis)."_
(Wasaail ush Shia, v5, p 61)

✍🏻___Syed Shoeb Raza Abdi

              ♦ _*MURTAD*_ ♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (585)

*بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ*

*إِنَّ الَّذِينَ آمَنُوا ثُمَّ كَفَرُوا ثُمَّ آمَنُوا ثُمَّ كَفَرُوا ثُمَّ ازْدَادُوا كُفْرًا لَمْ يَكُنِ اللَّهُ لِيَغْفِرَ لَهُمْ وَلَا لِيَهْدِيَهُمْ سَبِيلًا * بَشِّرِ الْمُنَافِقِينَ بِأَنَّ لَهُمْ عَذَابًا أَلِيمًا*

_"Yaqeenan woh log jo Imaan laye phir Kufr ikhtiyar kiys, phir Imaan laye, phir Khufr ikhtiyar kiya, phir Kufr mein badhte chale gaye, to Allah unko hargiz Ma'af mahi karega aur na kabhi unko seedhi raah dikhayega. Aap Munafeqeen ko dardnak Azaab ki Basharat de den."_
(Surah Nisa: 137 - 138)

📚📖
👉 _* Tafseer:*_
Tarz o Ravish ka taghayyur (change), har rang o roop ki ye tabdeeli aur taloon mizaji ka ye aalam dar asal Islami Usoolon ki sahih taur par tehqeeq na karne ka nateeja hai aur ya Munafeqeen aur Ahle Kitab mein se mutassib Kuffar ki sazish hai taake haqeeqi Momenin ko mutazalzal (shaky) kiya ja sake kiyonki unke za'am mein unki aamad o raft haqeeqi Momenin ke Imaan ko davan dol kar degi. Isliye inke liye dardnak Azaab hai. Haqeeqat mein woh kaun hain, Rivayato mein mulaheza farmayen.
🍀
Usoole Kafi mein hai ke ye Ayat Hazrat Ali (as) ke un siyasi hareefon ke mutalliq nazil hui jo ibteda mein Nabi e Akram (saww) par Imaan laye aur jab unke saamne Vilayet e Ali (as) pesh ki gayi to unhone inkar kar diya. Phir jab Maqam e Ghadeer mein Rasool e Akram (saww) ne "Man kunto Maula...." Ka Ailan kiya to woh Imaan le aye. Phir jab Rasool e Khuda (saww) ki Aankhen band hui to unhone inkaar kar diya. Iske baad woh gumrahi mein badhte hi gaye aur yun unke dil Imaan se khaali ho gaye.'
(Noorus Saqlain)
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜
✍🏻___Syed Shoeb Raza Abdi
----------------------------------------------

_*MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!*_
🙇 🌷
Imam Ali (as):
_"Allah ne Apni makhlooq ko paida nahi kiya jab tak ke us se Apni Wahdaniyat aur is Zurriyat e Zakiya ki Wilayat aur unke Dushmano se bara'at ka Ahad (promise) nahi le liye. Aur Arsh qaem nahi huwa jab tak ke uspar Noor se *La Ilaha Illallah Muhammadan Rasulallah Aliyyun Waliyullah* na likha gaya."_
(Aqwaal e Masoomeen (as), p232)

                 ♦ _*DOSTI*_ ♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (586) 👬

*بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ*

*بَشِّرِ الْمُنَافِقِينَ بِأَنَّ لَهُمْ عَذَابًا أَلِيمًا * الَّذِينَ يَتَّخِذُونَ الْكَافِرِينَ أَوْلِيَاءَ مِنْ دُونِ الْمُؤْمِنِينَ ۚ أَيَبْتَغُونَ عِنْدَهُمُ الْعِزَّةَ فَإِنَّ الْعِزَّةَ لِلَّهِ جَمِيعًا*

_"Aap (saww) Munafeqeen ko dardnak Azaab ki basharat de den."_
_"Jo Ahle Imaan ko chhod kar Kafiron ko apna Sarparast banate hain. Kiya ye Munafiq izzat ki talab mein unke paas jaate hain jabke tamam tar Izzat to Allah ke liye hai."_
(Surah Nisa: 138 - 139)

📚📖 👬
👉 _* Tafseer:*_
Ye Ayat tamam Musalmano ko tanbeeh karti hai ke woh apni izzat o aabroo ke liye chahe woh iqtesadi (financial) ya saqafati (cultural) pehloo ko ho ya siyaasi hawale se Dushmanan e Islam ki dosti talash na karen balke woh Zaate Ilahi par Bharosa karen jo tamam Izzaton ka sarchashma hai. Dushmanan e Islam ki apni bhi koi izzat nahi to woh doosron ko kiya denge aur agar unki ba zahir kuchh izzat ho bhi to woh qabil e etemad nahi hain kiyonki jab bhi inke mafad ka taqaza hua woh fauran apne Mukhlis tareen ittehadiyon ko bhi chhod kar apni rah len ge aur unki ye haalat hogi jise kabhi shanasai hi na thi.
Daur hazir ki tareekh bhi aise waqeaat se bhari padi hai. Aur aaj kal bhi aisa hi ho raha hai India mein haal hi election mein ye zyada dekha gaya. Jab Musalmano ke aise haalat ho jate hain ke Kafiron se dosti karne lagte hain aur gunah badh jate hain to Allah un par ek zalim badshah muayyan kar deta hai.
(Tafseer e Namoona)
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜
✍🏻___Syed Shoeb Raza Abdi
----------------------------------------------

_*MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!*_
🙇 👬
Imam Askari (as):
_"Tumhara behtareen Dost wo hai jo tumhari galtiyo'n ko bhool jaaye aur tumhare ehsaanaat ko yaad rakkhe."_
(Insaan ke Kamaal mein Akhlaaq ka Kirdaar)
👬
Rasule Khuda (saww):
_"Dosti aur dushmani wiraasat mein muntaqil (transfer) hoti hai."_
(Hadiyat ush Shia, p11)
👬
Imam Sadiq (as):
_"Logo'n mein nek Dost 3 tarah ke tajrube se banao:_
_(1) Gaiz o gazab mein dekho ke wo haqq se khaarij to nahi hota hai,_
_(2) Daulat ke zariye se aazmao,_
_(3) Safar saath kar ke dekho."_
(Imam Jafar Sadiq (as) - Almustashaar Abdul Haleem Jundi (Misri), p208)

  ♦ _*MEHFIL-E-GUNAH (CLUB)*_ ♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (587) 🤓

*بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ*

*وَقَدْ نَزَّلَ عَلَيْكُمْ فِي الْكِتَابِ أَنْ إِذَا سَمِعْتُمْ آيَاتِ اللَّهِ يُكْفَرُ بِهَا وَيُسْتَهْزَأُ بِهَا فَلَا تَقْعُدُوا مَعَهُمْ حَتَّىٰ يَخُوضُوا فِي حَدِيثٍ غَيْرِهِ ۚ إِنَّكُمْ إِذًا مِثْلُهُمْ ۗ إِنَّ اللَّهَ جَامِعُ الْمُنَافِقِينَ وَالْكَافِرِينَ فِي جَهَنَّمَ جَمِيعًا*

_"Allah tum ko is Kitab mein pahle hi Hukm de chuka hai ke jab tum suno ke Allah ki Ayaat ke khilaf Kufr baka ja raha hai aur unka Mazaq udaya ja raha hai to unke sath mat baitho, yahan tak ke woh doosri baaton mein masroof na ho jayen warna tum bhi un jaise qarar paoge. Yaqeen jano ke Allah Kuffar aur Munafiqon ko Jahannam mein ek jagah jama karne wala hai."_
(Surah Nisa: 140)

📚📖 🤓
👉 _* Tafseer:*_
Yahan Quran ka Mazaq means Deen ka mazaq, Shariyat ka mazaq hai. Aisi Majlis ya Club mein sharik hona jaez nahi.
(1) Majlis e Gunah (Club) mein shirkat irtekabe gunah ke manind hai, chahe sharik hone wala khamosh baithta rahe, Burai par razamandi yaani gunah ko support karna hai.
(2) Nahi Munkir agarche nahi anjaam de sakte lekin aisi Majlison se door rahna behtar hai.
(3) Gunah ki Mehfilon mein shirkat karne wale ka Gunah bhi Gunah karne wale ke barabar hai.
(4) Lekin agar Tauheen e Deen na ho to Non-Muslim ki Majlis mein sharik hone mein koi harj nahi, Mubah kam hai.
(5) Gunehgaron ki Mehfil mein ek Musalman sharik ho aur Gunah par aitraz na kare to ye Munafiqat hai. Kam se kam use na pasandgi ka to izhaar karna hi chahiye.
Saqeefa ke bare mein kuchh aise information milte hain ke jahan kuchh badkar Arab jama hote the. Deen ke Khilaf wahan sazishen hui jiska natija Musalman aaj tak bhugat raha hai.
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜
✍🏻___Syed Shoeb Raza Abdi
----------------------------------------------

_*MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!*_
🙇 🤓
Imam Sadiq (as):
_"Allah Ta'ala ne Bani Adam ke aa'za (parts) par Imaan farz kiya aur har hisse ke liye Imaan ka alaihda taqaza muqarrar kiya. Allah ne Kaan par ye farz kiya ke jis cheez ke sunne se Allah ne mana kiya hai woh use na sune aur unki taraf tawajjah na kare. Isi liye Allah Ta'ala ne is Ayat mein farmaya (4:140)."_
(Usoole Kaafi)
🤓
Imam Reza (as):
_"Jab dekho ke koi shakhs Haq ka inkaar kar raha hai aur usko jhutla raha hai aur Ahle Haq par aitraz kar raha hai to tum uske paas se uth kar chale jao. Uske saath na baitho."_
(Tafseer e Ayyashi)

           ♦ _*MUNAFEQEEN*_ ♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (588) 🤓

*بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ*

*الَّذِينَ يَتَرَبَّصُونَ بِكُمْ فَإِنْ كَانَ لَكُمْ فَتْحٌ مِنَ اللَّهِ قَالُوا أَلَمْ نَكُنْ مَعَكُمْ وَإِنْ كَانَ لِلْكَافِرِينَ نَصِيبٌ قَالُوا أَلَمْ نَسْتَحْوِذْ عَلَيْكُمْ وَنَمْنَعْكُمْ مِنَ الْمُؤْمِنِينَ ۚ فَاللَّهُ يَحْكُمُ بَيْنَكُمْ يَوْمَ الْقِيَامَةِ ۗ وَلَنْ يَجْعَلَ اللَّهُ لِلْكَافِرِينَ عَلَى الْمُؤْمِنِينَ سَبِيلًا*

_"Yaqeen Jano ke Allah Kuffar aur Munafiqon ko Jahannam mein ek jagah jama karne wala hai."_
_"Ye Munafiq tumhare halaat ka intezar kar rahe hain. (Dekh rahe hain ke tumhara anjam kiya hota hai). Agar tumhe Allah ki tarah se fatah (Victory) naseeb hui to woh aa kar kahenge ke kiya ham tumhare sath na the? Aur agar Kuffar ka pallah bhari raha ke kiya ham tumhare khilaf ladne par qadir na the. Phir bhi ham ne tum ko Musalmano se bachaya? Allah tumhare aur unke darmiyan Qayamat ke Din Faisla karega. Allah Kafiron ke liye Musalmano par ghalib aane ki hargiz sabeel nahi rakhega."_
(Surah Nisa: 141)

📚📖 🤓
👉 _* Tafseer:*_
Guzishta Ayat mein Islam Mukhalif Majlis mein shamil hone ke liye mana kiya tha. Phir hame Shaqeefa ki Majlis yaad aa gayi, kiya woh anti thi ya pro-Islam thi. Agar Pro-Islam hoti to Rasool e Akram (saww) ke hukm se hoti aur sabhi Sahaba us mein sharik hote lekin doosre sabhi sahaba Rasoole Akram (saww) ke Dafn o Kafan mein mashghool the.
Pas agar Musalman koi Anti-Islamic Activities karen to unhe Munafiq (Hypocrite) kaha jayega. Yahan is Ayat mein Allah ne Munafiqon ki kartooton ka zikr karna shuru kiya hai. Inhe is Ayat mein thali ka Baigan bataya hai. Agar Musalman jeete to unke sath aur agar Kuffar jeete to unke sath. Allah Qayamat ke Din sab ki poll khol dega. Munafeqeen ki kuchh aur sifat agli Ayat mein zikr hoga.
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜
✍🏻___Syed Shoeb Raza Abdi
----------------------------------------------

_*MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!*_
🙇 🤓
Imam Reza (as):
_"Allah Kafiron ke liye Musalmano par ghalib aane ki hargiz sabeel nahi rakhega.": is Ayat ka mafhoom ye hai ke Allah Kafiron ko Daleel o Hujjat ke zariye se Anbiya par kabhi ghalba nahi dega."_
🤓
Rasule Khuda (saww):
_"Aye Ali (as)!...Khuda ki qasam! Aap se mohabbat wo rakkhega jo Momin hoga aur bugz wo rakkhega jo Munafiq (hypocrite) hoga."_
(Amaali - Shaikh Mufeed, p33)
🤓
Imam Kazim (as):
_"Kitna bura wo shakhs hai jo 2 chehre aur 2 zabaan waala ho - yaani Munafiq ho; saamne apne biradar e Momin ki taarif kare aur peethh pichhe geebat kare."_
(Guftaar e Dil Nasheen)

           ♦ _*MUNAFEQEEN*_ ♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (589) 🤓

*بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ*

*إِنَّ الْمُنَافِقِينَ يُخَادِعُونَ اللَّهَ وَهُوَ خَادِعُهُمْ وَإِذَا قَامُوا إِلَى الصَّلَاةِ قَامُوا كُسَالَىٰ يُرَاءُونَ النَّاسَ وَلَا يَذْكُرُونَ اللَّهَ إِلَّا قَلِيلًا * مُذَبْذَبِينَ بَيْنَ ذَٰلِكَ لَا إِلَىٰ هَٰؤُلَاءِ وَلَا إِلَىٰ هَٰؤُلَاءِ ۚ وَمَنْ يُضْلِلِ اللَّهُ فَلَنْ تَجِدَ لَهُ سَبِيلًا*

_"Munafeqeen Khuda ko dhoka dena chahte hain jabke Khuda unko Dhoke mein rakhne wala hai aur jab Munafiq Namaz ke liye uthte hain to nihayat susti ke sath uthte hain. Ye log Namaz mehez logon ke dikhawe ke liye padhte hain aur Khuda ko bahut kam yaad karte hain."_
_"Ye Munafiq Islam aur Kufr ke darmiyan hairan o sargardan hain, na poore is taraf hain na poore us taraf hain aur jisko Khuda Gumrahi mein chhod de uske liye aap ko koi raasta na milega."_
(Surah Nisa: 142 - 143)

📚📖 🤓
👉 _* Tafseer:*_
Is Ayat mein Munafeqeen ki kuchh aur sifat bayan ki gayi hain:
(1) Woh apni chaal mein khud phans jate hain. Woh dhoka dena chahte hain jabke khud hi dhoka kha jate hain.
(2) Chunke woh Khuda aur Uske Azeem Waadon par Imaan nahi rakhte isliye sab Ibadaat dikhawe ke liye karte hain.
(3) Chunke woh Khuda se door ho jaate hain isliye Khuda se attachment toot jata hai, isliye unki ibadaat, Namaz sab ek formalities hoti hain. Namaz zyada padhte hain par khuloos nahi rahta.
(4) Agar Khuda ka koi zikr karen to woh dil se nahi balke adatan hota hain.
(5) Ye log dhobi ke gadhe ke tarah hain na ghar ka na ghat ka. Na to Musalman ka kirdar rakhte na hi khul kar kufr ka ailan karte hain. Ye Muallaq insaan hain.
Isliye Khuda ne unhe chhod diya hai unhe kabhi nijaat nahi milegi. Kiyonki woh Ahle Bait (as) ke Dushman hain.
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜
✍🏻___Syed Shoeb Raza Abdi
----------------------------------------------

_*MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!*_
🙇 🤓
Imam Sadiq (as):
_"Hazrat Luqman ne apne bete se farmaya:_
_Munafiq ki 3 Nishaniyan hain:_
_(1) Uski zaban uske dil ki mukhalif hoti hai._
_(2)  Uska fe'l (act) uske qaul (saying) ka mukhalif hona._
_(3) Uska batin uska zahir ka mukhalif hota hai."_
(Kitabul Khisal)
🎷🤓
Imam Sadiq (as):
_"Susti karne wale (Lazy) ki 3 Nishaniyan:_
_(1) Jab akela hoga to Masti karega._
_(2) Jab log uske paas maujood honge to wo chusti karega._
_(3) Har kaam mein chahega ke log uski ta'reef karen."_
(Kitabul Khisal)
🕌🤓
Imam Baqir (as):
_"Kasmasate hue, ungte hue aur bojhalpan ikhtiyar karke Namaz ke liye khada na hona kiyonki ye Munafiqat ki Alamat hai."_
(Ilalush Sharaye)

      ♦ _*SARPARAST, WALI*_ ♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (590) 🌷

*بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ*

*يَا أَيُّهَا الَّذِينَ آمَنُوا لَا تَتَّخِذُوا الْكَافِرِينَ أَوْلِيَاءَ مِنْ دُونِ الْمُؤْمِنِينَ ۚ أَتُرِيدُونَ أَنْ تَجْعَلُوا لِلَّهِ عَلَيْكُمْ سُلْطَانًا مُبِينًا*

_"Imaan Walo! Momenin ko chhod kar Kuffar ko apna Wali aur Sarparast (ya sahara) na banao. Kiya tum chahte ho (aisa karke) apne khilaf Bargahe Ilahi mein ek wazeh Daleel qaem kar lo."_
(Surah Nisa: 144)

📚📖 🌷
👉 _* Tafseer:*_
Guzishta Ayaat mein Munafeqeen ki kuchh khusoosiyat bayan ki gayin, ab Allah hame nasihat kar raha hai ke in logon se door rahen, inko na apna dost banayen, na Wali ya Sarparast. Na inko apna Sahara banaye, na Madadgar. Kiyon ham idhar udhar jaye jabke ham Allah ne hame Ahle Bait (as) jaise Sarparast se nawaza. 14 Masoomeen (as) ke alawa hamara kaun hajat rawa ho sakta hai. Aur Hazrat Abbas (as) Babul Hawaij ko hamare liye shafe qarar diya. Ham Babul Hawaij ke samne sawali bante hai. Beshak Hamara Maula Mushkil kusha, jiska farzand Bawaij, yehi hamari zindagi ke sahare hain.
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜
✍🏻___Syed Shoeb Raza Abdi
----------------------------------------------

_*MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!*_
🙇 🌷🌷🌷🌷🌷🌷🌷🌷🌷
*اَلسَّلاَمُ عَلَیْکَ یَابْنَ اَمِیْرِ الْمُؤْمِنِیْن اَلسَّلاَمُ عَلَیْکَ اَیُّہَا الْعَبْدُ الصَّالِحُ الْمُطِیْعُ لِلّٰہِ وَ لِرَسُوْلِہٖ اَشْہَدُ اَنَّکَ قَدْ جَاہَدْتَ وَ نَصَحْتَ وَ صَبَرْتَ حَتّٰی اَتٰیکَ الْیَقِیْن*
*لَعْنَ اﷲُ الظَّالِمِیِن لَکُمْ مِنَ الْاَوَّلِیْنَ وَالْآخِرِیْنَ وَ اَلْحِقْہُمْ بِدَرَکِ الْجَحِیْمِ.*

_"Salam ho yabna Ameerul Momenin, Salam ho aye Abde Saleh (Nek Bande), Allah o Rasool (saww) ke Mutee wa farmabardar, Mein gawahi deta hun ke Aap ne Jihad aur Sabr kiya yahan tak ke Yaqeen (Maut) ke aa gayi."_
_"Allah ki Laanat ho jisne Aapko qatl kiya Awwl o Akhir, Jaheem unka mustaqil thikana ho."_
🌷🌷🌷🌷🌷🌷🌷🌷🌷🌷
Hazrat Abbas (as) ki is Ziyarat mein Aap ko in Alqaab se nawaza gaya hai:
Abdus Saleh, Allah o Rasool ke Mutee, jaise ke Aap ne Imam Husain (as) ke sath apne wafadari nibhai. Sabr: Kisi Shuja ko Imam ki ita'at mein Dushman par war na karna Sabr ki inteha thi.
Hazrat Khizr (as) ko Quran mein Abd e Saleh se khitab kiya, jinka Ilm Musa (as) ki Ilm se zyada tha, na H. Musa (as) unke Ilm ke saamne Sabr kar paye, har baat mein kiyon.....ye 2 Nabi the. Hazrat Abbas ko bhi usi Alfaz se khitab kiya gaya aur Hazrat Khizr ki woh sifaat payi jaati hain. Agar Hazrat Abbas (as) ki mulaqat H. Khizr se hoti to unhe kahna nahi padta
( *قَالَ إِنَّكَ لَنْ تَسْتَطِيع مَعِيَ صَبْرًا* ) [Surat Al-Kahf 67]
Hazrat Abbas Ilm o Shuja'at ke markaz the.
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜
----------------------------------------------
*7th Rajab 1438, 5th April 2017, Wednesday,

             ♦ _*MUNAFEQEEN*_ ♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (591)

*بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ*

*إِنَّ الْمُنَافِقِينَ فِي الدَّرْكِ الْأَسْفَلِ مِنَ النَّارِ وَلَنْ تَجِدَ لَهُمْ نَصِيرًا * إِلَّا الَّذِينَ تَابُوا وَأَصْلَحُوا وَاعْتَصَمُوا بِاللَّهِ وَأَخْلَصُوا دِينَهُمْ لِلَّهِ فَأُولَٰئِكَ مَعَ الْمُؤْمِنِينَ ۖ وَسَوْفَ يُؤْتِ اللَّهُ الْمُؤْمِنِينَ أَجْرًا عَظِيمًا*

_"Yaqeenan Munafiq Dozakh ke sab se past tabqe mein honge aur tum unka koi Madadgar na paoge."_
_"Albatta un mein se jo Tauba kar len aur apni Islah kar len aur Khuda se poori tarah wabasta ho jayen air apne Deen ko Allah ke liye khalis kar den to aise afraad Momin ke saath honge aur anqareeb Allah Ahle Imaan ko Ajre Azeem ata karega."_
(Surah Nisa: 145 - 146)

📚📖 👽
👉 _* Tafseer:*_
Guzishta Ayaat mein Munafeqeen ki khusisiyat ka bayan hua. Aaj ki Ayat mein zikr hai ke unko iska kiya badla milega. Musalman ya to Momin hoga ya Munafiq. Momin ke liye Ajre Azeem hai jabke Munafiq ke liye Jahannam ka sab se nichla tabqa hai.
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜
✍🏻___Syed Shoeb Raza Abdi
----------------------------------------------

_*MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!*_
🙇 👽
Hazrat Ali (as):
_"Aye girohe Mardum! Mere baad aise Rahnuma honge jo Dozakh ki dawat denge aur Qayamat ke Din unki Madad na ki jayegi."_
_"Aye Girohe Mardum! Unse Allah bhi bari hai aur mein bhi unse la talluq hun."_
_"Aye Girohe Mardum! Woh aur unke Madadgar aur unke Pairokar aur unke itteba karne wale (followers) Dozakh ke nichle tabqe mein honge aur Takabbur karne walon ke liye intihai bura tikhana hain."_
(Ehtejaj e Tabarsi)

♦ _*SHUKR-E-NEMATE ILAHI*_ ♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (592) 🙏🏻

*بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ*

*مَا يَفْعَلُ اللَّهُ بِعَذَابِكُمْ إِنْ شَكَرْتُمْ وَآمَنْتُمْ ۚ وَكَانَ اللَّهُ شَاكِرًا عَلِيمًا*

_"Khuda tumhe Azaab de kar kiya karega agar tum Uska Shukr karo aur Imaan ki Raah par chalne lag jao. Khuda bada Qadardan aur sab ke haal se Waqif hai."_
(Surah Nisa: 147)

📚📖 🙏🏻
👉 _* Tafseer:*_
Guzishta Ayaat mein Khuda ke Azaab ka zikr hua. Ye Dardnak Azaab inteqami nahi taake Woh Gunehgar Bando se inteqam le balke ye insaan ke Imaan o Aamal ka natija hai. Agar ham Uski Nematon ka Shukr karen aur Khuda par Imaan le ayen to Khuda ko Azaab ki zaroorat hi kiyon pade.
Is Ayat mein 'Shukr' ko 'Imaan' par muqaddam rakha hai. Ye isliye ke jab tak Insaan Uski Nematon ko pahchan na le aur Shukr Guzari ke maqam tak na pahunch jaye us waqt tak khud Use nahi pahchan sakta. Kiyonki Uski Nematen Ma'arefat ka zariya hain. Wujoob e Ma'arefat e Ilahi ke liye Wujoob Shukre Mun'im (منعم) zaroori hai aur Shukr Guzari Insaani Fitrat hai, Nemat Bakhshne wale ka Shukr ada karna Wajib hai, lehaza is Nematen ata karne wale ki Ma'arefat bhi Wajib hai.
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜
✍🏻___Syed Shoeb Raza Abdi
----------------------------------------------

_*MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!*_
🙇 🙏🏻
Imam Sajjad (as):
_"Wo gunah jo nemato'n ko badal dete hain wo ye hain: Logo'n par zyadati karna, Khairaat karne aur neki karne ki aadat chhor dena, Kufraane Ne'mat karna, Shukr e Khuda na bajaa laana."_
(Irshadaat e Masumeen (as), p86)
🙏🏻
Imam Sadiq (as):
_"Ne'mat ka Shukr ye hai ke moharramaat se (haraam cheezo'n se aur haraam kaamo'n se) bacha jaaye aur poora shukriya ye kehna hai AL HAMDU LILLAHI RABBIL AALAMIN."_
(Al Kaafi, v3, p347)
🙏🏻
Rasule Khuda (saww):
_"Agar Allah ne tujhe khush-haal (prosperous) banaya hai to Uska Shukr adaa karo, aur agar bad-haal (destitute) ho to Astagfaar karo."_
(Rizq)
🙏🏻
Imam Sadiq (as):
_"Allah ki sabse mehboob makhlooq wo hai jo kisi bhi Ne'mat ke ataa hone par Shukr kare aur Musibat ke waqt Sabr kare."_
(Miskhat ul Anwaar)
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜

*9th Rajab 1438, 7th April 2017, Friday,

   ♦ _*MAZLOOM KI AWAAZ*_ ♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (593) 🤷🏻‍♂🙋🏻‍♂

*بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ*

*لَا يُحِبُّ اللَّهُ الْجَهْرَ بِالسُّوءِ مِنَ الْقَوْلِ إِلَّا مَنْ ظُلِمَ ۚ وَكَانَ اللَّهُ سَمِيعًا عَلِيمًا * إِنْ تُبْدُوا خَيْرًا أَوْ تُخْفُوهُ أَوْ تَعْفُوا عَنْ سُوءٍ فَإِنَّ اللَّهَ كَانَ عَفُوًّا قَدِيرًا*

_"Allah buland awaaz se kisi ki badgoi pasand nahi karta magar jab koi Mazloom ho to use uski ijaazat hai aur Allah Sunnewala aur sab kuchh Jannewala hai."_
_"Agar tum kisi khair ko zahir karo ya use makhfi (hidden) rakho ya kisi Burai se darguzar (ignore) karo to Allah Gunahon ka Ma'af Karnewala aur Sahibe Ikhtiyar hai."_
(Surah Nisa: 148 - 149)

📚📖 🙋🏻‍♂🤷🏻‍♂
👉 _* Tafseer:*_
Khuda ko pasand nahi ke koi kisi ki badgoi kare ya logon ke oyoob (defects) bayan kiye jayen kiyonki Khuda Sattarul Oyoob (Aibo ko Chhupanewala) hai, logon ki izzat o aabru ka khayal rakhna hamara farz hai. Lekin jo zalim hai uske aibon ko chhupana nahi chahiye.
Tafseer e Ali ibne Ibrahim ke mutabiq Ayat ka mafhoom ye hai ke Mazloom ko Zaalim ka shikwa karne ki ijaazat hai kiyonki Allah Ta'ala ko ya pasand nahi ke Insaan Zulm o Burai ka Shikwa kare albatta Mazloom ko aisa karne ki ijaazat hai. Use Zaalim ke khilaf buland Awaaz se wa waila karne ka Haq hai.
Ek aur Hadis mein hai ke agar tumhare paas koi Shakhs aaye aur tumhare saamne khushamad karte hue tumhari taarifen kare jo tum mein maujood nahi hain to uski baat ko qubool na karna aur use jhutlana, usne tum par zulm kiya hai.
(Noorus Saqlain)
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜
✍🏻___Syed Shoeb Raza Abdi
----------------------------------------------

_*MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!*_
🙇 🙋🏻‍♂🤷🏻‍♂
Imam Mohd Baqir (as):
_"Madad hasil karne ke liye Mazloom ko ijaazat hai ke woh Zaalim par Sab o Shitam (gaali ya bura bhala kahna) kar sakta hai lekin iske liye shart ye hai ke woh aise maamle ke liye madad hasil karne ka khwahishmand ho jiski madad Deeni aitbar se bhi jaaez ho."_
(Majmaul Bayan, Noorus Saqlain)
🤷🏻‍♂
Imam Jafar Sadiq (as):
_"Agar koi shakhs kisi ka Mehmaan ho aur Mezbaan achchi Mehmaan nawazi na kare to us Mehmaan ko ye Haq hasil hai ke woh uski Bukhilana (Kanjoos) Mezbaani ko bayan kare."_
(Noorus Saqlain)
🌻🌻🌻🌻🌻🌻🌻🌻🌻🌻
*Imam Muhammad Taqi (as):*
_"Agar Ulema apni nasihat ko chhupa le'n, yaani sargardaa'n (bhattakte / aawara) aur gumraah insaan ki hidayat na karein ya (ma'anvi / spiritually) murda insaan ko dekh kar usay zinda na karein to unhone apne saath khayaanat ki."_
(Guftaar e Dil Nasheen, p207)
🌻
Imam Taqi (as):
_"4 baatein insaan ko amal par ubhaarti hai: Sehet, Maaldaari, Ilm, Taufeeq."_
(Guftaar e Dil Nasheen, p205)
🌻
Imam Taqi (as):
_"Jis ne'mat ka shukriya adaa na kiya jaaye wo oos gunah ke misl hai jo baksha na jaaye."_
(Aqwaal 14 Masumeen (as), p207)
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜

*10th Rajab 1438, 8th April 2017, Saturday,

♦ _*KUCHH PAR IMAAN, KUCHH SE INKAAR*_ ♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (594) 🚩

*بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ*

*إِنَّ الَّذِينَ يَكْفُرُونَ بِاللَّهِ وَرُسُلِهِ وَيُرِيدُونَ أَنْ يُفَرِّقُوا بَيْنَ اللَّهِ وَرُسُلِهِ وَيَقُولُونَ نُؤْمِنُ بِبَعْضٍ وَنَكْفُرُ بِبَعْضٍ وَيُرِيدُونَ أَنْ يَتَّخِذُوا بَيْنَ ذَٰلِكَ سَبِيلًا * أُولَٰئِكَ هُمُ الْكَافِرُونَ حَقًّا ۚ وَأَعْتَدْنَا لِلْكَافِرِينَ عَذَابًا مُهِينًا*

_"Beshak jo log Allah aur uske Rasoolon ka inkaar karte hain aur woh Allah aur Uske Rasoolon ke darmiyan tafreeq (difference) paida karna chahte hain aur kahte hain ke ham baaz par Imaan rakhte hain aur baaz ka inkaar karte hain aur woh chahte hain ke Imaan o Kufr ke darmiyan mein ek raah nikal len."_
_"Ye log pakke Kafir hain aur Ham ne Kafiron ke liye ruswa karnewala Azaab tayyar kar rakha hai."_
(Surah Nisa: 150 - 151)

📚📖 🚩
👉 _* Tafseer:*_
Ye Ayat dar asal Yahoodi aur Esaiyon ki haalat bayan kar rahi hai. Yahoodi Hazrat Esa (as) ko nahi maante the jabke Esaayi Rasoole Khuda (saww) ko nahi maante. Jabke Allah ka Hukm hai 1,2400 Paighambar par Imaan rakhna aur unke Ausiya par bhi. In mein koi farq nahi. Musalman ka matlab hi ye hai ke jo kuchh Allah ne hukm kiya hai sab ke aage apna sar kham karna, Allah ke saamne tasleem ho jana. Yahan common minimum program se kaam nahi chalega. Kisi ek ka bhi inkaar Kufr hai. Aur inkaar karne walon ke liye ruswa kun Azaab hai.
Tafseer e Ali bin Ibrahim mein is Ayat ke zimn mein likha hai ke isse woh log murad hain jo kuchh Anbiya ko manne ka daawa karte the aur kuchh Anbiya par Imaan nahi rakhte the aur is Ummat mein jo log Rasoole Khuda par Imaan rakhen aur Amirul Momenin (as) ki Imamat ka inkar karen to woh bhi ma'anavi taur par unke hi bhai hain.
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜
✍🏻___Syed Shoeb Raza Abdi
----------------------------------------------

_*MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!*_
🙇 🚩
Imam Ali (as):
_"Momin aur kaafir ke darmiyaan sirf Namaz ka farq hai. Lihaaza, jo Namaz ko chhor kar Imaan ka daawa kare, uska amal usay jhootlayega aur khud uske khilaaf gawaahi dega."_
(Tajalliyat e Hikmat, ch Namaz)
🚩
Imam Ali (as):
_"(Khud ko) Astagfaar / Tauba se muattar (khushbudaar) kar lo, tumhe gunaho'n ki badbu ruswaa (badnaam) nahi karegi."_
(Kashkool, Book 2, p88)
🚩
Imam Askari (as):
_"Momin ke liye kitni buri baat hai ke aisi cheez ki taraf raghbat (khwaish) rakhe jo uski zillat o ruswaayi ka sabab ho."_
(Guftaar e Dil Nasheen, p237)
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜

*11th Rajab 1438, 9th April 2017, Sunday,

      ♦ _*MO'JEZA KA DEMAND*_ ♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (596) 📚

*بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ*

*يَسْأَلُكَ أَهْلُ الْكِتَابِ أَنْ تُنَزِّلَ عَلَيْهِمْ كِتَابًا مِنَ السَّمَاءِ ۚ فَقَدْ سَأَلُوا مُوسَىٰ أَكْبَرَ مِنْ ذَٰلِكَ فَقَالُوا أَرِنَا اللَّهَ جَهْرَةً فَأَخَذَتْهُمُ الصَّاعِقَةُ بِظُلْمِهِمْ ۚ ثُمَّ اتَّخَذُوا الْعِجْلَ مِنْ بَعْدِ مَا جَاءَتْهُمُ الْبَيِّنَاتُ فَعَفَوْنَا عَنْ ذَٰلِكَ ۚ وَآتَيْنَا مُوسَىٰ سُلْطَانًا مُبِينًا*

_"Aye Nabi! Ye Ahle Kitab agar aaj Aap se ye mutaleba kar rahe hain ke Aap Aasmaan se un par koi Kitab naazil karayen. Isse badh chadh kar unhone Moosa se mujremana mutaleba kiya tha aur unhone kaha tha ke hamen Khuda ko ailaniya (openly) dikha do. Isi sarkashi ki wajah se Bijli ne unhen apni giraft mein le liya tha. Phir unhone hamari wazeh (clear) Nishaniyon ke aa jane ke baad Gausala (Calf) ko Ma'bood (Deity) bana liya tha. Hamne isse bhi darguzar (Ma'af) kiya tha aur Hamne Moosa (as) ko khuli hui Daleel ataa ki thi."_
(Surah Nisa: 153)

📚📖 📕
👉 _* Tafseer:*_
Yahoodiyon ka mutaleba nek niyyati nahi tha. Kabhi kabhi sawal ka maqsad jawab nahi, balke tanz hota hai. Unhe ne demand kiya ke kiyon ek poori Kitab ek sath nazil ho jaye. Jabke Tauret unko ek sath hi di ja chuki hai. Allah ne to unka ek mutaleba pahle hi poora kar chuka tha, lekin woh sahi raah par to kiya aate, ek Gausala ki pooja karne lage. Unka mutaleba tha ke ham Khuda ko direct apni Aankh se dekhna chahte hain. Allah ne unki ye maang poori ki. Sawal ye hain ke kiya Allah ne apne Aap ko dikhaya. Allah ke Jism/Body se mubarrah hai. Sirf Matter/Maddah ko hi ham dekh sakte hai. Allah Matter nahi hai, na koi Body rakhta hai. To phir unhone kiya dekha? Rivayaton se pata chalta hai ke woh Noor ki tajalli Hazrat Ali (as) ki thi. Jab woh is tajalli ko Khuda samajh kar bardasht nahi kar paye to Haqiqat ko kaise bardasht karte. Lekin is ke baad bhi unhone ne ek bachhre ki pooja ki.
Isi tarah aaj kal ye bhi sawal kiya jata hai ke Ahle Bait (as) ke bare mein Qur'an mein zikr kahan hai? Jab hamare Nabi (saww) ne khud unke bare mein clear Ayaten bata di phir bhi samajh mein nahi ayen to koi kare.
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜
✍🏻___Syed Shoeb Raza Abdi
----------------------------------------------

_*MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!*_
🙇 📚🏞
Imam Ali (as)
se puchha gaya ke Suraj ki raushni mein jo intehaai baareek baareek zarraat (kann / particles) dikhayi dete hain wo kya hain? Aap ne farmaya:
_"H. Musa (as) ne Allah se deedaar ki darkhwaast ki thi. Allah ne farmaya ke tum pahaad par nazrein jamaao, agar pahaad apni jagah qaem raha to tum Mujhe dekh loge aur agar pahaad apni jagah par qaem na raha to tum Mujhe nahi dekh sakoge kyun ki tumhari nigaah kamzor hai, tum Mere deedaar ki taab (tolerance) nahi laa sakte. Iske baad Allah ne pahaad par jalwa giraya. Pahaad ke 3 hisse ho gaye, ek hissa uddkar aasmaan ki taraf gaya, doosra hissa zameen ke nichhe dha'ns gaya, aur tumhein ghar ke kamro'n mein jo bareek zarraat dikhayi dete hain ye oosi pahaad ka gubaar (dhuul / dust) hai"._
(Tafseer Noor us Saqlain, v3, p445)
📚
Rasule Khuda (saww):
_"Jo koi bhi ye chahta hai ke Ilm e Adam (as) aur parhezgaari e Nuh (as) aur burdbaari (forbearance / sahahsheelta) e Ibrahim (as) aur azmat e Musa (as) aur Ibadat e Isa (as) par nazar kare to wo Ali ibne Abi Talib (as) par nigaah kare."_
(Maula Ali Ki Shaan Mein 1000 Ahadees, h270, p188)

♦ _*AHD O PAIMAN (COVENANT)*_ ♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (597) 📜✍🏻

*بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ*

*وَرَفَعْنَا فَوْقَهُمُ الطُّورَ بِمِيثَاقِهِمْ وَقُلْنَا لَهُمُ ادْخُلُوا الْبَابَ سُجَّدًا وَقُلْنَا لَهُمْ لَا تَعْدُوا فِي السَّبْتِ وَأَخَذْنَا مِنْهُمْ مِيثَاقًا غَلِيظًا*

_"Aur Hamne un logon par Toor ko utha kar un se Ita'at ka Ahd liya tha aur Hamne unse kaha tha ke Sajdah rez ho kar Darwaze mein dakhil ho jao aur Hamne unse kaha tha ke Hafte ke roz (Saturday) zyadti na karna aur Hamne unse pukhta Ahd (Covenant) liya tha."_
(Surah Nisa: 154)

📚📖 📜✍🏻
👉 _* Tafseer:*_
Yahoodiyon se Kohe Toor ke saye mein Ahd liya gaya. Ye same zikr Ayat (Baqarah: 63) mein ho chuka hai. Tafseer e Majmaul Bayan aur Al Manar mein hai Toor ka pahad apni jagah se ukhad gaya aur unke sar par musallat ho gaya. Jabke doosri Tafseer hai ke pahad mein zalzalah aya. Aur ye pahad ka tukda unke sar par ruka raha jab tak unhon Ahd na le liya. Is tarah Allah ne itni sakhti ke sath Ahd liya. Is Ayat ke zel mein ham detail zikr kar chuke hain.
Mufassir Tabarsi, Ibne Zaid ka qaul bayan karte hain.
"Jis waqt Hazrat Moosa (as) kohe Toor se wapas aye aur apne sath Tauret laye to apni Qaum ko bataya ke mein Aasmaani Kitab le kar aya hun jo Deeni Ahkam aur Halal o Haram par mushtamil hai. Ye woh Ahkam hai jinhen Khuda ne tumhare liye Amali Program qarar diya hai. Ye unke liye mushkil Ahkam the. Yahoodi nafarmani aur sarkashi par tul gaye. Khuda ne bhi Farishton ko ma'moor kiya ke woh Kohe Toor ka ek bahut bada tukda unke saron par la kar khada kar den. Isi asna mein Hazrat Moosa (as) ne unhe khabar di ke Ahd o Paiman (Covenant) baandh lo, Ahkam e Khuda par amal karo, sarkashi o baghawat se Tauba karo, tum se ye Azaab tal jayega warna sab halak ho jayege. Is par unhone sar tasleem kham kar diya. Tauret ko qubool kiya aur Khuda ke huzoor mein Sajdah kiya. Jab har lamha woh Kohe Toor ke apne saron par girne ke muntazir the lekin bil Akhir unki Tauba ki wajah se Azaab e Ilahi tal gaya."
Yahi mazmoon Sura Baqarah: 93, Aaraaf: 171 mein bhi aya hai.
Khuda ne Hukm diya tha ke Saturday ko Holiday karen. Chunke woh darya kinare rahte the, us din Machhli (fish) ka shikar ki manadi ki.
Lekin Yahoodiyon ne baad mein ye Ahd tod diya, aur Azaab ke mustaheq hue.
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜
✍🏻___Syed Shoeb Raza Abdi
----------------------------------------------

_*MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!*_
🙇 📜✍🏻
Imam Ali (as):
_"Allah Ta'ala ne Hazrat Musa (as) ko 4 baato'n ki Wasiyyat ki:_
_(1) Jab tak tere gunah maaf na ho, doosro'n ke aib talaashne mein mashgool na hona,_
_(2) Jab tak Mere Khazane khatm na ho, apni Rozi ki fikr mat karna,_
_(3) Meri Haakimiyat (rule) ke hote huwe kisi gair ki haakimiyat ko tasleem na karna aur_
_(4) Jab tak Shaitan mar na jaaye uske Makr o Fareb se ghaafil na rahna."_
(Khisaal, p118)

                ♦ _*AHD SHIKNI*_ ♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (598) 📜🗡

*بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ*

*فَبِمَا نَقْضِهِمْ مِيثَاقَهُمْ وَكُفْرِهِمْ بِآيَاتِ اللَّهِ وَقَتْلِهِمُ الْأَنْبِيَاءَ بِغَيْرِ حَقٍّ وَقَوْلِهِمْ قُلُوبُنَا غُلْفٌ ۚ بَلْ طَبَعَ اللَّهُ عَلَيْهَا بِكُفْرِهِمْ فَلَا يُؤْمِنُونَ إِلَّا قَلِيلًا*

_"Akhirkar unki Ahd Shikni (Covenant Breaking) ki wajah se aur is wajah se ke unhone Allah ki Ayat ka inkaar kiya aur bahut se Anbiya ko Na-Haq qatl kiya, aur ye kaha ke hamare dilon par parde pade hue hain, halanke dar haqiqat unke Kufr ki wajah se Allah ne unke dilon par Mohr laga di hai, lehaza un mein se bahut kam afraad Imaan late hain."_
(Surah Nisa: 155)

📚📖 📜🗡
👉 _* Tafseer:*_
Kal ham ne Ayat ke zel mein bayan kiya tha ke Hazrat Moosa (as) ke zariye Allah ne Yahoodiyon se Ahd liya ke woh Ahkam Ilahi par amal karenge. Lekin baad mein woh palat gaye aur is Ahd par amal na karke isko ko tod diya jiska Natija ye hua ke unke Kufr ki wajah se Rehnooma e Deen ko qatl kiya. Allah ne Azaab ke taur par unke dilon par Mohr laga di. Ye Yahoodiyon ka zikr hai, lekin dekha jaye to Rasoole Akram (saww) ki rehlat ke baad khud Musalmano ne bhi yehi tarikh dohrai. Is Ayat ke misdaq woh log bhi hain jinhone Rahnuma e Islam ko Shaheed kiya. Isliye Duniya mein Momin kam hi nazar aate hain.
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜
✍🏻___Syed Shoeb Raza Abdi
----------------------------------------------

_*MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!*_
🙇 📜🗡
*رسول الله (ص): لا دين لمن لا عهد له .*
_"Jo Shakhs Ahd qaem nahi rakh sakta uska koi Deen nahi."_
[Nawadir al-R`awandi, p. 5]
📜🗡
Rasoole Khuda (saww):
_"Jab woh Ahd Shikni karte hain Allah apne Dushman ko un par musallat kar deta hai."_
[Bihar al-Anwar, v. 100, p. 46, no. 3]
📜🗡
Rasoole Khuda (saww):
_"Beshak, Jo apne muaede mein wafa nahi karta ya Ahd Shikni karta hai, ya aisa waada karta hai jo uski salahiyat ke bahar ho, ya us mein se kuchh baghair nek niyyat ke ghatata hai, to phir mein Roze Qayamat unka gareban pakdunga."_
[Kanz al-`Ummal, no. 10924]

✝ _*SALEEB (CRUCIFICATION)*_ ✝

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (599)

*بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ*

*وَبِكُفْرِهِمْ وَقَوْلِهِمْ عَلَىٰ مَرْيَمَ بُهْتَانًا عَظِيمًا * وَقَوْلِهِمْ إِنَّا قَتَلْنَا الْمَسِيحَ عِيسَى ابْنَ مَرْيَمَ رَسُولَ اللَّهِ وَمَا قَتَلُوهُ وَمَا صَلَبُوهُ وَلَٰكِنْ شُبِّهَ لَهُمْ ۚ وَإِنَّ الَّذِينَ اخْتَلَفُوا فِيهِ لَفِي شَكٍّ مِنْهُ ۚ مَا لَهُمْ بِهِ مِنْ عِلْمٍ إِلَّا اتِّبَاعَ الظَّنِّ ۚ وَمَا قَتَلُوهُ يَقِينًا * بَلْ رَفَعَهُ اللَّهُ إِلَيْهِ ۚ وَكَانَ اللَّهُ عَزِيزًا حَكِيمًا*

_"Aur unke Kufr aur Maryam (sa) par Azeem buhtaan lagane ki wajah se."_
_"Aur unke is qaul ki wajah se ke ham ne Maseeh Esa bin Maryam Rasoolullah ko qatl kar diya hai. Halanke unhone fil waqae use qatl nahi kiya aur na Saleeb par chadhaya gaya (Crucified) balke Maamla un par Mushtaba kar diya gaya jin logon ne Esa (as) ke mutalliq ikhtelaf kiya woh dar asl Shak mein mubtela hain inke pas is ke mutalliq koi Ilm nahi hai. Unhone mehez guman hi ki pairavi ki hai. Unhone Yaqeenan Maseeh ko qatl nahi kiya tha ."_
_"Balke Khuda ne use apne taraf utha liya. Allah Zabardast Taqat Rakhne wala aur Hakeem hai."_
(Surah Nisa: 156 - 158)

📚📖 ✝
👉 _* Tafseer:*_
Guzishta Ayaton Ahd Shikni ka zikr hua tha. Ahd Shikni ke wajah Ahle Kitab ne Anbiya ka qatl kiya. Lekin is Ayat mein zikr ye hai ke unhone Hazrat Esa (as) ko qatl karne ki koshish ki lekin Allah ne H. Esa (as) ko utha liya. Ahadis mulaheza ho:
✝
Imam Baqir (as):
"Jis Raat Allah Ta'ala ne Hazrat Esa (as) ko uthana tha us Raat Aap (as) ne apne Hawariyun (Disciples) ko jama hone ka hukm diya. Isha ke waqt woh jama hue aur unki tadaad 12 thi. Aap (as) ne unhe ghar mein dakhil kiya. Kuchh der ke liye Aap chale gaye aur baad mein us ghar ke kone ke chashme se Aap baramad hue aurAap ke sar se paani ke qataraat tapak rahe the.
Aap (as) ne Hawariyun se farmaya:
" Allah ne meri taraf Wahi ki hai ke Woh mujhe is waqt apni taraf utha raha hai aur Woh mujhe Yahoodiyon se Paak karne wala hai. Tum mein ek shakhs ko meri shabeeh bana diya jayega. Woh qatl ho jayega aur use Saleeb par chadha diya jayega. Woh mere sath Jannat mein mere darje mein hoga."
"Tum mein se ek Subah hone se pahle 12 martaba mera inkaar karega."
"..... Mere baad tumhare 3 giroh banenge. Un mein se 2 giroh Khuda par iftera karne wale (Buhtaan) honge aur unka thikana Dozakh mein hoga aur ek giroh Sham'oon ki pairavi karega aur woh Khuda ke mutalliq sachchi baten karega aur woh giroh Jannat mein jayega."
"Iske baad Allah ne unko us ghar ke ek kone se apni jaanib utha liya. Hawariyun ne Aap ko Aasmaan ki taraf jate hue dekha."
✝
Rasool e Akram (saww):
_"Hazrat Esa (as) Baitul Muqaddas aye aur unhone is shaher mein rah kar 33 baras tak Tableegh e Deen karte rahe......"_
(Noorus Saqlain)
✝
Rasule Khuda (saww):
_"Hawaariyo'n ne H. Isa (as) se puchhha, "Hum kin logo'n ke saath baithhein?" Aap (as) ne farmaya, "Jinki soorat se zikr e Khuda yaad aaye, jinki guftagu se tumhara Ilm zyada ho, jinke Ilm se Akherat ki taraf raghbat ho"._
(Al Kaafi, v1, p85)
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜
✍🏻___Syed Shoeb Raza Abdi

(Usoole Kaafi)

✝ _*SALEEB (CRUCIFICATION)*_ ✝

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (600) ✝

*بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ*

*وَبِكُفْرِهِمْ وَقَوْلِهِمْ عَلَىٰ مَرْيَمَ بُهْتَانًا عَظِيمًا * وَقَوْلِهِمْ إِنَّا قَتَلْنَا الْمَسِيحَ عِيسَى ابْنَ مَرْيَمَ رَسُولَ اللَّهِ وَمَا قَتَلُوهُ وَمَا صَلَبُوهُ وَلَٰكِنْ شُبِّهَ لَهُمْ ۚ وَإِنَّ الَّذِينَ اخْتَلَفُوا فِيهِ لَفِي شَكٍّ مِنْهُ ۚ مَا لَهُمْ بِهِ مِنْ عِلْمٍ إِلَّا اتِّبَاعَ الظَّنِّ ۚ وَمَا قَتَلُوهُ يَقِينًا * بَلْ رَفَعَهُ اللَّهُ إِلَيْهِ ۚ وَكَانَ اللَّهُ عَزِيزًا حَكِيمًا*

_"Aur unke Kufr aur Maryam (sa) par Azeem buhtaan lagane ki wajah se."_
_"Aur unke is qaul ki wajah se ke ham ne Maseeh Esa bin Maryam Rasoolullah ko qatl kar diya hai. Halanke unhone fil waqae use qatl nahi kiya aur na Saleeb par chadhaya gaya (Crucified) balke Maamla un par Mushtaba kar diya gaya jin logon ne Esa (as) ke mutalliq ikhtelaf kiya woh dar asl Shak mein mubtela hain inke pas is ke mutalliq koi Ilm nahi hai. Unhone mehez guman hi ki pairavi ki hai. Unhone Yaqeenan Maseeh ko qatl nahi kiya tha ."_
_"Balke Khuda ne use apne taraf utha liya. Allah Zabardast Taqat Rakhne wala aur Hakeem hai."_
(Surah Nisa: 156 - 158)

📚📖 ✝
👉 _* Tafseer:*_
Guzishta post is Ayat ke zel mein Ahadees post ki thi.
Christian ye maante hai ke Good Friday ke Din Hazrat Esa (as) (Jesus Christ) is Duniya se gaye aur Easter ke Din (Sunday) phir zahir ho gaye. Unka Aqeeda hai ke H. Esa (as) qatl hue, unhone ne logon Gunah ke evaz qurbani di, aur puri Duniye ke insano ko gunahon se pak kar diya. Is kaam ke liye Khuda ko Jesus ke roop mein zameen par aana pada. 3 God ka Aqeeda un mein paya jata hai jise Trinity kahte hain.
Islam unke Aqaed ko radd karta hai. Khuda itna Majboor nahi ke usko logon ki hidayat ya Kaffare ke liye bhes badalna pade.
Woh kahte hain:
God is One, The God, The Son of God (Jesus Christ) The Holy Spirit.
Trinity Hindu Aqeede mein payi jati jise kahte hain Trimurty. Ye sab batil Aqaed hain.
Aql is baat ko tasleem nahi kar sakti ke Jo Ek hai woh 3 kaise ho sakta hai. Is Topic ko doosri Ayat ke zel mein discuss karenge.
Aaj ki Ayat mein Quran jawab de raha hai ke Hazrat Esa (as) ka qatl nahi hua balke woh zinda hain. Khuda ka koi beta nahi (Sura Tauheed). Agar Hazrat Esa (as) logon ke liye fidya (atonement) ban gaye to iska matlab ye hua ke ab sab Christian azadi ke saath gunah kar sakte hain, ya phir ghadi ghadi Hazrat Esa (as) ko fidya dena hoga. Bible jis mein ye Aqaed ka zikr hai ke Hazrat Esa (as) qatl hue,  woh baad mein Hawariyon ne likhi. Asl Injeel to Christian ke pas hai hi nahi, jo hai woh bhi English translation hai. In kitabon mein tehreef mumkin hai. Jin mein se ek Injeel Barnabas hai jo Bible mein shamil nahi.
Tafseer Ali bin Ibrahim mein marqoom hai ke Hazrat Esa (as) ki Rahme Maadar mein tasveer kashi ki gayi. Woh Baap ke Sulb mein nahi rahe the aur jab unhe zameen se uthaya gaya to inhone oon (wool) ka Jubba pahna hua tha.
(Noorus Saqlain)
Islam ka jo Aqeeda hai wohi Hazrat Esa (as) ka hai. Woh ek Nabi the, jinko Allah ne logon ki Hidayat ke liye maboos kiya tha.  Woh Chauthe Aasmaan par abhi tak zinda hain aur Imam Mahdi (atfs) ke zahoor ke baad Hazrat Esa (as) bhi zahir honge.
(To be cont'd.)
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜
✍🏻___Syed Shoeb Raza Abdi
----------------------------------------------

_*MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!*_
🙇 ✝
Imam Baqir (as):
_"Yahoodi Hazrat Esa (as) ki talaash mein wahan aye. Unhone us jawan ko jo shabeeh Esa (as) ban chuka tha wahan se giraftar kar liya aur jis ke mutalliq Aap (as) ne farmaya tha ke woh Subah hone se pahle 12 martaba unka inkaar karega usne bhi Aapka 12 martaba inkaar kiya aur yun Aapki dono peshingoiyan (forecast) sahih sabit hui."_
(Noorus Saqlain)
✝
Imam Husain (as):

(Tafseer Noor us Saqlain, v2, p86)

             ♦ _*MASHWARAH*_ ♦

As-salamu alaikum wa  Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (437)

*بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ*

*فَبِمَا رَحْمَةٍ مِنَ اللَّهِ لِنْتَ لَهُمْ ۖ وَلَوْ كُنْتَ فَظًّا غَلِيظَ الْقَلْبِ لَانْفَضُّوا مِنْ حَوْلِكَ ۖ فَاعْفُ عَنْهُمْ وَاسْتَغْفِرْ لَهُمْ وَشَاوِرْهُمْ فِي الْأَمْرِ ۖ فَإِذَا عَزَمْتَ فَتَوَكَّلْ عَلَى اللَّهِ ۚ إِنَّ اللَّهَ يُحِبُّ الْمُتَوَكِّلِينَ*

_"Rehmat-e-Ilahi ke sabab tum un logon ke liye bahut NARM MIJAZ waqae hue ho. Warna agar tum tundkhu (Harsh) aur Sang Dil hote to ye sab tumhare gird o pesh se chhat jate (dispersed). Unke qasoor maaf kardo, unke liye maghferat talab karo aur kaam mein unse mashwara karo aur jab tum pukhta irada karlo to Allah par bharosa rakho. Yaqeenan Allah Ahle Tawakkal se Muhabbat rakhta hai."_
(Surah Aal-e-Imran: 159)

📚📖
👉 _* Tafseer:*_
Is Ayat mein kai Topic hain. Pahli baat ye ke Hamare Rasool (saww) Rahmatul lil Alemin the. (Merciful for Whole World). Jab Fateh Mekkah hua to unhe apne Dushman Abu Sufiyan ka ghar ko jai aman qarar diya aur Kuffar e Makkah se inteqam nahi liya. Ek Yahoodi Aurat jo aap (saww) par kachhra pekhti thi, uske bimar hone par uski ayadat ke liye gaye. Aise bahut waqeaat hain jiski yaha gunjaish nahi hai. Rasool (saww) sabko sath lekar chalte the. Ashaab se Mashwara bhi karte the. Jaise Jange Ahzab mein unhone Janabe Salman e Farsi ke mashware par Khandak khudwai. Agar Rasool Khuda (saww) sakht mijaz hote to log unke tarah aane ke bajay door bhagte. Unke Janesheen ki bhi yehi ravish rahi. Hazrat Ali (as) ne apne qatil Ibne Muljim ko pani pilane ka hukm diya.
Hazrat Ali (as) ne Nahjul Balagha mein farmaya:
_"Khud pasandi se badhkar wahshat nak aur koi tanhai nahi aur Mashwara karne se badhkar aur koi mazboot pusht panahi nahi hai."_
Isliye Ali (as) ne Khalifa e duwwum ke Shura ke ineqaad par usme hisaa liya jabke maloom tha ke is mein jana bekar hai. Kiyonki faisla pahle se hi tai tha. Isliye Ali (as) Munafeqin ke sath bhi aise rahe ke aaj log use  Ali (as) ke ittehaad se tashbeeh dene lage. Jabki ke kuchh ka manna hai unhone apne mukhalif ki rehnumai qubool kar li ho. Ye nazaryat unki logon ke sath itna ghul mil jane ki wajah se paida hue.
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜
----------------------------------------------

_*MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!*_
🙇 📋
Imam Ali (as):
_"Buzdil se mashwera na karna woh tumhare liye nikalne ka raasta tang kardega aur Bakheel (Kanjus) se Mashwara na karna woh tujhe tere maqsad tak pahuchne nahi dega aur Harees (Lalchi) se mashwara na karna woh tumhare liye hirs (Lalach) ko bayes e zeenat bana kar pesh karega."_
(Kitabul Khisal, Noorus Saqlain)
📋
Imam Zainul Abedin (as):
_"Mashwara karne wale ka tujh par ye Haq hai: Agar tumhe raye (Suggestion) ka ilm ho to Mashwara do aur agar tum khud raye dene ke qabil nahi ho to uski us shakhs ki taraf rehnumai karo jo raye ko janta ho aur jab tum kisi se Mashwara le lo to phir tum par Mashwara dene wale ka ye Haq hai ke uski jo raye tumhare muwafiq na ho us mein use mutahham na karo aur agar uski raye  tumhe muwafiq mehsoos ho to Allah ki Hamd karo."_
(Risalatul Huqooq, Noorus Saqlain)
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜

              ♦ _*ISTEKHARA*_ ♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (438)

*بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ*

*فَبِمَا رَحْمَةٍ مِنَ اللَّهِ لِنْتَ لَهُمْ ۖ وَلَوْ كُنْتَ فَظًّا غَلِيظَ الْقَلْبِ لَانْفَضُّوا مِنْ حَوْلِكَ ۖ فَاعْفُ عَنْهُمْ وَاسْتَغْفِرْ لَهُمْ وَشَاوِرْهُمْ فِي الْأَمْرِ ۖ فَإِذَا عَزَمْتَ فَتَوَكَّلْ عَلَى اللَّهِ ۚ إِنَّ اللَّهَ يُحِبُّ الْمُتَوَكِّلِينَ*

_"Rehmat-e-Ilahi ke sabab tum un logon ke liye bahut NARM MIJAZ waqae hue ho. Warna agar tum tundkhu (Harsh) aur Sang Dil hote to ye sab tumhare gird o pesh se chhat jate (dispersed). Unke qasoor maaf kardo, unke liye maghferat talab karo aur kaam mein unse MASHWARA karo aur jab tum pukhta irada karlo to Allah par bharosa rakho. Yaqeenan Allah AHLE TAWAKKAL se Muhabbat rakhta hai."_
(Surah Aal-e-Imran: 159)

📚📖
👉 _* Tafseer:*_
1) Istikhara: Musalmano ki Kamyabi.

*قالَ رَسُولُ اللهِ صلّى اللهُ عَلَيْهِ و آله:*
*مِنْ سَعادَةِ أبْنِ آدَمَ أسْتِخارَتُهُ اللهَ وَرِضاهُ بِما قَضَى اللهُ وَ مِنْ شَقْوَةِ أبْنِ آدَمَ تَرْكُهُ أسْتِخارَةَ اللهَ وَ سَخَطُهُ بِما قَضَى اللهُ.*

Rasool e Khuda (saww):
_"Bani Adam ki sa'adat ke liye ye hai ke woh Allah se behtari ki khwahish kare (Istekharah kare) aur jo Allah ne qaza ki hai us par razi ho aur Bani Adam ki Shaqawat ye hai ke woh Istekhara ko tark kare aur Allah ki qaza par razi na ho."_
(Biharul Anwaar, Vol 77, P-159, H 1532)
⛓
Jaise ke pahle hamne bataya Islam ne Mashwara (Consultation) ki takeed ki hai. Lekin jab Ishteshara (Consultation) fail ho jaye to phir Allah se Istekhara kare. Istekhara yani ye dekhna ke Allah ke is amr mein kiya marzi hai. Jab insaan apne kaam me tazabzub (hasitation) ka shikar ho jata hai. Jab uski aql kaam nahi karti hai tab Allah se apne Behtari ke liye dua ki jati hai: yani karna behtar hai ya na karna. Ye na to toss hai, Na hi coincidence hai. Ye Allah se Dua hai. Ya yun kahen ke ham Allah se mashwara le rahe hain. Lekin ye last step hain. To jab Istekhara kar le to us par amal bhi kare, karna hai ya na karna. Aisa nahi ke ham har chhote mote kaam me ye karte rahen. Jab logo se Isteshara aur apni Aql fail ho jaye tab akheri naubat Istekhara ki aati hai. Iske liye Allah par Tawakkul zaroori hai.
Istekhara Qur'an aur Tasbeeh se kiya jata hai jiski Imam (as) ne taleem di hai. Iske liye qare'een Dua ki kitab refer karen. Istekhara karne ke liye behtar waqt bhi makhsoos hain.
(Refer Istekhara: Mafatihul Janal Hashiya, P-920)
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜
----------------------------------------------

_*MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!*_
🙇 ⛓🎛
*اَلإِمَامُ عَلَيٌّ{ عَليهِ السَّلامْ } فِي وَصِيَّتِهِ إِلى إِبْنِهِ { عَليهِ السَّلامْ } :*

*...وَ أَكْثَرِ الإِسْتِخارَةَ، إِذا أَمْضَيْتَ فَاسْتَخِرْ.*
Imam Ali (as):
(Apne farzand se wasiyat ki:)
_"(Apne sare umoor mein) har waqt Allah se istekhara karo behtar anjam ke liye."_
(Nahjul Balagha, Hikmat 31, Ghurarul Hakam, Hikmat 3988)
⛓🎛
*اَلإمَامُ الْباقِرُ{ عَليهِ السَّلامْ }:*
*كُنَّا نَتَعَلَّمُ الإسْتِخَارَةَ كَمَا نَتَعَاَّمُ السُّورَةَ مِنْ اللهِ عَزَّ وَ جَلَّ.*

Imam Baqir (as):
_"Ham (Ahle Bait as) Istekhara (Allah se Behtari ka sawal karna) ki ta'leem dete hain jaise ham Kitabe Khuda Azza wa Jal ke Surah ki Ta'leem dete hain."_
(Wasaelus Shia, Vol 7, P-66, Hadis 10101)
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜

   ♦ _*TAUFEEQ & KHIZLAAN*_ ♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (439)

*بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ*

*إِنْ يَنْصُرْكُمُ اللَّهُ فَلَا غَالِبَ لَكُمْ ۖ وَإِنْ يَخْذُلْكُمْ فَمَنْ ذَا الَّذِي يَنْصُرُكُمْ مِنْ بَعْدِهِ ۗ وَعَلَى اللَّهِ فَلْيَتَوَكَّلِ الْمُؤْمِنُونَ*

_"Agar Allah tumhari madad karne wala ho to koi taqat tum par ghalib nahi aa sakti aur agar woh tumhe chhod de to iske baad tumhari madad karne wala kaun ho sakta hai? Ahle Imaan ko Allah par Tawakkal karni chahiye."_
(Surah Aal-e-Imran: 160)

📚📖 🙏🏻
👉 _* Tafseer:*_
Kitab "Al Tawheed" mein Abdullah bin Fazl Hashmi se manqool hai:

*وما توفيقى الا بالله و آية آل عمران: ١٦٠*
Imam (as) se Ayat (Ale Imran:160) ke zel mein raavi ne Taufeeq ke bare mein Sawal kiya.
Imam Jafar Sadiq (as) ne jawab diya:
_"Agar banda Allah ke Farman ki aita'at kare aur uska fe'l Amre Ilahi ke mutabiq ho to is surat mein Bande ko *"Muwaffaq موفق" (Taufeeq yaftah)* kaha jayga. Aur agar Banda Khuda ke kisi Hukm ki nafarmani ka irada kare aur Allah us ke aur Uski tajweez karda nafarmani ke darmiyan hael ho jay aur Banda nafarmani to chhod de to is nafarmani ka chhoot jana bhi Taufeeq e Ilahi ka samar (fruit) qarar diya jayega. Aur agar Khuda Bande aur nafarmani ke darmiyan hael na ho aur Banda uska murtakib na ho jaye to Allah ne use chhod diya hai aur uski madad nahi ki hai aur use Taufeeq nahi di hai aur Taufeeq na milne ko *"Khizlan خذلان"* kaha jata hai."_
(Noorus Saqlain)

Insaan jo bhi amal karta hai uski quwwat o hasiyat ke mutabiq karta hai lekin agar uske amal mein Khuda ki madad shamil ho jaye uske liye ye Taufeeq hai. Misal ke taur par agar koi shakhs Namaz padhna chahta hai aur aisi jagah par ho jaha pani na ho, to agar usko aisi jagah mein Wuzu ya Ghusl ke liye pani muhayya ho jaye to ye Taufeeq hai. Ya kisi insaan ke mind mein koi naya Idea click ho jaye jisse usko Kamyabi mile etc. Agar koi Theatre mein film dekhne ke liye nikle lekin raaste mein itni rukawate aa jayen ke woh wahan pahunch hi na paye aur is gunah se bach jaye to ye uske liye Allah ki Taufeeq hai. Ye Taufeeq har kisi ko nahi milti, sirf usi ko milti hai jisko Allah chahta hai. Is ke liye bhi hame Allah ko razi rakhna aur Taufeeq ke liye dua karni chahiye. Aur jis Bande se Allah na khush ya naraaz ho jata hai use chhod deta hai yani ab use koi gunah karne se bacha nahi sakta. Ise Khizlaan kahte hain. Hame Khizlaan  se bachna hoga ke ye naubat aane na paye. Extra help ko Taufeeq kahte hain. Bare Ilaha hame Nek raaste par chalne ki Taufeeq ata farma.
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜
----------------------------------------------

_*MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!*_
🙇 🙏🏻
Imam Taqi (as):
_"4 baatein insaan ko amal par ubhaarti hai:_
_Sehet, Maaldaari, Ilm, *Taufeeq.*"_
(Guftaar e Dil Nasheen, p205)
🙏🏻
Rasule Khuda (saww):
_"Jis shakhs ko Parwardigaar ne mere Ahlebait (as) ki maarefat aur mohabbat ki *Taufeeq* de di goya uske liye tamaam khair jamaa kar diya."_
(Aqwaal e Masoomeen (as), p167)
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜

*15th Muharram 1438, 17th October 2016, Monday,

              ♦ _*KHAYANAT*_ ♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (440)

*بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ*

*وَمَا كَانَ لِنَبِيٍّ أَنْ يَغُلَّ ۚ وَمَنْ يَغْلُلْ يَأْتِ بِمَا غَلَّ يَوْمَ الْقِيَامَةِ ۚ ثُمَّ تُوَفَّىٰ كُلُّ نَفْسٍ مَا كَسَبَتْ وَهُمْ لَا يُظْلَمُونَ*

_"Khayanat karna Nabi ke liye zeba nahi hai aur jo koi Khayanat kare to Khayanat ki hoi cheez lekar woh Qayamat ke Din hazir hoga. Phir har Shakhs ko uske Aamal ka pura badla diya jayega aur Be-insafi nahi ki jayegi."_
(Surah Aal-e-Imran: 161)

📚📖
👉 _* Tafseer:*_
Ye Ayat Jang-e-Uhud ke baad nazil hui thi jab Musalman bhag kar Maale Ghaneemat (War Booty) jama karne mein lag gaye ye soch kar ke shayad Paighambar e Khuda (saww) unko unka hissa de ya nahi. Ji haan ye isi tarah ke Musalman the jin ki ye soch thi aur baade Rasool inhone Islam ki bagdod sanbhali. Jabki us waqt Kafir bhi Rasool (saww) ko Ameen manta tha. Jab Rasool e Khuda (saww) ne Makkeh se Madina Hijrat ki to Hazrat Ali (as) ko apne bistar par sulaya aur takeed ki ke Makkeh walon ki jitne Amanate hain woh unko lauta kar phir ayen. Yani Dushman ki Amanaton mein bhi khayanat nahi ki. Hamen bhi apni Nabi (saww) ke naqse qadam par chalna chahiye aur khayanat karne se bachen.
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜
----------------------------------------------

_*MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!*_
🙇 ⚖
Imam Sadiq (as):
_"Momin Momin ka bhai, uski aa'nkh aur uska Rehbar hai, na uske saath khayaanat karta hai, na Zulm karta hai, na Milaawat karta hai aur na Waada-khilaafi karta hai."_
(Guftaar e Dil Nasheen)
⚖
Imam Sadiq (as):
_"Jo apne biradare Momin ko bure kaam ki taraf jaata dekhe aur rok sakne ke bawajood usay na roke to usne jaise uske Haq mein khayanat ki."_
(Bihaar 15/52)
(Insaan ke Kamaal mein Akhlaaq ka Kirdaar)
⚖
Imam Sadiq (as):
_"Imam ke Maal mein Khayanat karna Khayanat ka Akheri darja hai aur jabke Yateem ka Maal khana aur Sood (Interest) khana isse chhote darje ki Khayanat hai."_
(Tafseer e Ayyashi, Noorus Saqlain)
⚖
Imam Sadiq (as):
_"Jo shakhs hum logo'n ki mohabbat ki thhandak apne dil mein mehsoos kare usay chahiye ke wo apni Maa ko bahut bahut Duaein de is liye ke usne uske Baap ki amaanat mein khayaanat nahi ki."_
(Elal ush Sharaaye, p108), (Man La Yahzarahul Faqih, v3, p307)
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜

*16th Muharram 1438, 18th October 2016, Tuesday,

           ♦ _*ALLAH KI RAZA*_ ♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (441)

*بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ*

*أَفَمَنِ اتَّبَعَ رِضْوَانَ اللَّهِ كَمَنْ بَاءَ بِسَخَطٍ مِنَ اللَّهِ وَمَأْوَاهُ جَهَنَّمُ ۚ وَبِئْسَ الْمَصِيرُ * هُمْ دَرَجَاتٌ عِنْدَ اللَّهِ ۗ وَاللَّهُ بَصِيرٌ بِمَا يَعْمَلُونَ*

_"Bhala woh Shakhs jo Khuda ki khushnoodi ka taabe' ho woh us shakhs ki tarah ho sakta hai jo Khuda ki nakhushi mein giraftar ho aur jiska thikana dozakh ho jo ke bahut bura thikana hai."_
_"Un logon ke Khuda ke haan mukhtalif darje hain. Khuda unke Aamaal ko dekh raha hai."_
(Surah Aal-e-Imran: 162-163)

📚📖
👉 _* Tafseer:*_
Allah Ta'ala sawal kar raha hai ke jisse Allah Razi hai aur jisse Razi nahi hai dono barabar kaise ho sakte hai? Ab jisse Allah Razi nahi hai uske liye har waqt dua karna ke Allah inse Razi ho jaye kaise namumkin hai kiyonke woh to dozakhi hai. Ye bhi achhe woh bhi achhe kaise ho sakte hain? Allah doosri jagah par bhi yahi sawal kar raha hai ke Janne aur na jaane wale (Zumar:9), Beena aur nabeena (Anaam:50), Andhera aur Ujala (Raad:16) kya barabar ho sakte hain? Isliye hame Achchho ke sath hi rahna hai faqat.
Allah jinse Razi hai yani Rehbarane Deen, Ale Imran, Ahle Bait e Athaar (as) unke liye Woh doosri Ayat mein farma raha hai:
*جَزَاؤُهُمْ عِنْدَ رَبِّهِمْ جَنَّاتُ عَدْنٍ تَجْرِي مِنْ تَحْتِهَا الْأَنْهَارُ خَالِدِينَ فِيهَا أَبَدًا ۖ رَضِيَ اللَّهُ عَنْهُمْ وَرَضُوا عَنْهُ ۚ ذَٰلِكَ لِمَنْ خَشِيَ رَبَّهُ*
[Surah Al-Bayyinah: 8]
_"Unki jaza unke Parwardegar ke yaha bahisht e Jaodani ke baghat hain, jiske darakhton ke niche nehren jari hain. Woh hamesha hamesha usi mein rahenge. KHUDA BHI UNSE RAZI HAI AUR WOH BHI KHUDA SE RAZI HAIN, aur ye (baland maqam) us shakhs ke liye hai, jo apne Parwardegar se dare."_
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜
----------------------------------------------

_*MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!*_
🙇 📈 📊
Imam Jafar Sadiq (as):
_"Ammar! Khuda ki qasam Allah ke haan momenin ke mukhtalif darajat hain aur hamari Ma'arefat o Muhabbat ki wajah se Allah unki Nekiyon ko kai gunah zyada kar deta hai aur unke darajat buland karta hai, jabke Ali Ibne Abi Talib (as) aur ham Aimma (as) ke huqooq ke munkaron ka Akheri thikana dozakh hai aur woh Khuda ke ghazab mein giraftar hain."_
(Tafseer e Ayyashi, Rivayat by Ammar bin Marwan)
📈📊
Imam Jafar Sadiq (as):
_"Allah ki Raza ke taqazo par mukammal taur par chalne wale Aimma (as) hain. Ammar! Ahle Imaan ke liye Khuda ke haan darajat hain aur hamari Vilayat o Marefat ki wajah se Allah Ta'ala  unke Aamal ko kai gunah badha deta hai aur unke Darajat e Aliya mein izafa karta hai."_
(Usool e Kafi, Rivayat by Ammar As Sabati)

              ♦ _*NABUWWAT*_ ♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (442)

*بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ*

*لَقَدْ مَنَّ اللَّهُ عَلَى الْمُؤْمِنِينَ إِذْ بَعَثَ فِيهِمْ رَسُولًا مِنْ أَنْفُسِهِمْ يَتْلُو عَلَيْهِمْ آيَاتِهِ وَيُزَكِّيهِمْ وَيُعَلِّمُهُمُ الْكِتَابَ وَالْحِكْمَةَ وَإِنْ كَانُوا مِنْ قَبْلُ لَفِي ضَلَالٍ مُبِينٍ*

_"Yaqeenan Allah ne Ahle Imaan par Ehsaan kiya hai ke un mein se ek Paighambar maboos (raised) kiya jo unke saamne Tilawat e Ayaat karta hai aur unko Mushriko ki kasafaton (dirtyness) se paak karta hai aur unhe Kitab o Hikmat ki Ta'leem deta hai. Agarche isse pahle woh khullam khulla gumrahi mein the."_
(Surah Aal-e-Imran: 164)

📚📖
👉 _*�Tafseer:*_
Allah ne Mo'menin par Rasool bhej kar Ehsaan kiya. Mo'menin par isliye ke wohi Allah ka Ehsaan man sakte hain. Ye Allah ka Fazl o Karam hai ke usne hamare pas Nabi bhej kar hamari Hidayat ka intezam kiya. Kiyonke Allah Adil hai, insaaf karne wala hai usne Badkaro ke liye Jahannam aur Nekokaron ke liye Jannat banayi. Eqaab bila bayan (yani Azab baghair nasihat ke) Zulm hai. Aur Allah Zalim nahi hai. Isliye Allah ne khilqat e Duniya se Qayamat tak Hidayat ka silsila rakha. Jaisa ke Quran mein hai
*إِنَّمَا أَنْتَ مُنْذِرٌ ۖ وَلِكُلِّ قَوْمٍ هَادٍ*
[Surah Ar-Ra'd: 7]
124000 Anbiya bheje jisme First Adam (as) hai aur Last Hazrat Muhammad Mustafa (saww) aur 12 Imam ka silsila aaj tak jari hai. Agar ye Hidayat ka silsila na hota to sirf Jahiliyat hoti. Rasool ke faraez mein se ya hai ke woh Qur'an ki Ta'leem deta hai (Baghair teacher ke book kafi nahi hai), Tazkiya e Nafs karta hai (Isse pahle ham Najis the), Kitabat o Hikmat Ta'leem deta hai (Isse pahle ham Jahil the). Ya yun kaha jaye agar Anbiya na hote to Duniya mein Insaani wujud namumkin tha, aur sab zulmat ka shikar rahte. Hamari ham jins mein se ek Nabi ko bhej kar Allah ne ham par itna bada Ehsaan kiya.
*رَبَّنَا لَا تُزِغْ قُلُوبَنَا بَعْدَ إِذْ هَدَيْتَنَا وَهَبْ لَنَا مِنْ لَدُنْكَ رَحْمَةً ۚ إِنَّكَ أَنْتَ الْوَهَّابُ*
[Surah Aal-E-Imran: 8]
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜
----------------------------------------------

_*MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!*_
🙇

Imam Mahdi (atfs):
_"Khuda Wande Aalam ne Muhammad (saww) ko aalameen ke liye Rehmat bana kar maboos kiya aur unke zariye ne'mato'n ko tamaam kiya aur unpar silsila e Nabuwwat ko khatm kiya aur tamaam logo'n ki taraf Rasul (saww) bana kar bheja."_
(Guftaar e Dil Nasheen, p247)
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜
----------------------------------------------
*18th Muharram 1438*
20th October 2016, Thursday,

               ♦ _*MUSIBAT*_ ♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (443)

*بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ*

*أَوَلَمَّا أَصَابَتْكُمْ مُصِيبَةٌ قَدْ أَصَبْتُمْ مِثْلَيْهَا قُلْتُمْ أَنَّىٰ هَٰذَا ۖ قُلْ هُوَ مِنْ عِنْدِ أَنْفُسِكُمْ ۗ إِنَّ اللَّهَ عَلَىٰ كُلِّ شَيْءٍ قَدِيرٌ * وَمَا أَصَابَكُمْ يَوْمَ الْتَقَى الْجَمْعَانِ فَبِإِذْنِ اللَّهِ وَلِيَعْلَمَ الْمُؤْمِنِينَ*

_"Bhala ye kiya baat hai ke jab tum par Musibat aayi halanke (Jang e Badr mein) isse dugna Musibat tumhare hath se un par pad chuki hai to tum chilla uthe aur kahne lage ke ye aafat kahan se aa gayi. Kah den ke ye tumhari shaamat e Aamaal hai. Beshak Allah har cheez par Qadir hai."_
_"Aur jo Musibat tum par dono Jamat ke muqable ke din nazil hui woh Khuda ke Hukm se nazil hui taake Allah Mo'mino ko achhi tarah maloom kar le aur Munafeqeen ko bhi zahir kar de."_
(Surah Aal-e-Imran: 165 - 166)

📚📖 ⚔🗡
👉 _* Tafseer:*_
Jang e Badr mein 70 Kafir qatl hue the, 70 Giraftar hue the. Qaidiyon ke mutalliq bhi ye faisla hua ke unhe bhi qatl kar dita jaye. Ansaar ne Rasoole Khuda (saww) se arz kiya: "Ya Rasoolullah! Aap unhe qatl na karen aur ye qaedi hamen gift kar den ham unse Fidya lekar azad kar denge. Jibrael Ameen (as) Allah ka paigham lekar nazil hue aur farmaya ke unke liye Qaidiyon se Fidya lene ko mubah (permissible) kiya jata hai aur unhe ikhtiyar diya jata hai ke Fidya lekar Qaidiyon ko riha kar den lekin shart (condition) ye hai ke jitno se Fidya lenge utne hi afraad ainda saal jang mein qatl kiye jayege. 70 Qaidiyon ke Fidye ke badle 70 insaano ki Shahaadat qubool kana padegi.
Rasool e Akram (saww) ne ye shart pesh ki, unhone Shart qubool ki aur kah ke hamare afraad Shaheed hokar Jannat mein chale jayenge.
Phir 1 Saal baad Jang e Uhud hui aur 70 Musalman Shaheed hue to Sahaba ne Rasool (saww) se farmaya ke ham par ye Musibat kahan se aa padi? Rasool (saww) ne phir yaad dilaya ke ye Jang e Badr ki shart ki wajah se.
(Tafseer Noorus Saqlain)
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜
----------------------------------------------

_*MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!*_
🙇 😪
Imam Sadiq (as):
_"Musibat o aazmaish pehle hamare paas aati hai phir tumhare paas pahu'nchti hai aur narmi aur aasani bhi pehle hamare paas aati hai phir tumhare paas jaati hai."_
(Amaali - Shaikh Toosi, v1, p194)
😢
Imam Ali (as):
_"Musibat ke waqt ghabra jaana musibat se badh-kar musibat hoti hai."_
(Meezan ul Hikmah, v1, p68)
👋🏻
Rasule Khuda (saww):
_"Musibat ke waqt Musalman ka raan par haath marna uske ajr (sawaab) ko dho deta hai."_
(Furoo e Kafi, v1, 332)
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜

*19th Muharram 1438, 21st October 2016, Thursday,

   ♦ _*Bahana bazi - Excuses*_ ♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (444)

*بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ*

*وَلِيَعْلَمَ الَّذِينَ نَافَقُوا ۚ وَقِيلَ لَهُمْ تَعَالَوْا قَاتِلُوا فِي سَبِيلِ اللَّهِ أَوِ ادْفَعُوا ۖ قَالُوا لَوْ نَعْلَمُ قِتَالًا لَاتَّبَعْنَاكُمْ ۗ هُمْ لِلْكُفْرِ يَوْمَئِذٍ أَقْرَبُ مِنْهُمْ لِلْإِيمَانِ ۚ يَقُولُونَ بِأَفْوَاهِهِمْ مَا لَيْسَ فِي قُلُوبِهِمْ ۗ وَاللَّهُ أَعْلَمُ بِمَا يَكْتُمُونَ*


_"Aur (Ye musibat isliye ayi) taake Munafeqeen ko bhi zahir karde. Jab unse kaha gaya ke aao Allah ke raaste mein jang karo ya Kafiron ke hamlo ko hi roko to kahne lage ke agar hamko ladai ki khabar hoti to ham zaroor tumhare sath rahte. Ye us Din Imaan ki nisbat Kufr se zyada qareeb the."_
_"Woh moo se aisi baaten kahte hain jo unke dilon mein nahi hoti aur jo kuchh ye chhupate hain Allah usse khub Waqif hai."_
(Surah Aal-e-Imran: 167)

📚📖 😏
👉 _* Tafseer:*_
Jang e Uhud ke silsile se zikr jari hai. Is jang mein 3 group ke log the:
(1) Sabit Qadam afraad jo akheri dam tak date rahe.
(2) Bhagode: jo tazabzub ka shikar ho gaye.
(3) Munafeqin: Ye log tarah tarah ke excuse aur bahana bana ke pahle hi Madina laut gaye aur Jang se moo moda. Ye the Abdullah ibne Abi Saloob aur uske 300 sathi.
Is wajah se Musalmano ko is jang mein nuqsan pahuncha. Ayat mein in logon ki bahane baziyon ka zikr hai.
Aaj ham kahte k ham Imam Mahdi (as) ke Zuhoor ka intezar kar rahe hain, aaj agar unka zahoor ho jaye to kitne log unka sath denge? Rivayat ke mutabiq zahoor ke waqt sabse pahle unke sathi honge sirf 313. Zahoor mein takhir ka matlab ye hai ke abhi to itne afraad nahi hain. Isliye sirf zabani iqraar se hamari sabit qadami sabit nahi hoti.
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜
----------------------------------------------

_*MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!*_
🙇 😶😏
Imam Jafar Sadiq (as):
_"Jiska Yaqeen Zaeef ho to woh asbab (excuses) se talluq qaem karega aur apne liye use jaez qarar dega aur aadaat ki pairavi karega aur logo ke ghair haqeeqi aqwaal ke peechhe chalega aur umoore Duniya mein bhar poor koshish karega aur woh hamesha Duniya ko jama karne aur bukhl karne mein masroof hoga. Aisa shakhs agar zaban ki had tak ye kahta hua dikhai dega ke ata' karnewala aur rokne wala Allah hi hai aur Bande ko wohi kuchh milta hai jo uske muqaddar mein maqsoom mein likha hua hai aur jadd o jahad se Rizq mein koi izafa nahi hota. Lekin uska fe'l aur qalb uske zabani dawon ki tardeed kar raha hota hai. Allah Ta'ala ne aise hi logon ke mutalliq farmaya:"_
*يَقُولُونَ بِأَفْوَاهِهِمْ مَا لَيْسَ فِي قُلُوبِهِمْ ۗ وَاللَّهُ أَعْلَمُ بِمَا يَكْتُمُونَ*
(3:167)
(Misbahus Shari'ah, Noorus Saqlain)
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜
----------------------------------------------
*21th Muharram 1438, 23rd October 2016, Sunday,
🔹🔹🔹🔹🔹🔹🔹🔹🔹🔹

BAZM-E-ADAB WELCOMES YOU*
