                  ♦ _*MAUT*_ ♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (445)

*بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ*

*الَّذِينَ قَالُوا لِإِخْوَانِهِمْ وَقَعَدُوا لَوْ أَطَاعُونَا مَا قُتِلُوا ۗ قُلْ فَادْرَءُوا عَنْ أَنْفُسِكُمُ الْمَوْتَ إِنْ كُنْتُمْ صَادِقِينَ*

_"(Munafeqin:) ye khud to Jang se bach kar baith hi rahe the magar unhone apne Shohada bhaiyon ke liye kaha ke agar unhone hamara kahna mana hota to qatl na hote. Aap kah den ke tum agar sachche ho to apne aap se Maut ko taal do."_
(Surah Aal-e-Imran: 168)

📚📖
👉 _* Tafseer:*_
Jang e Uhud jari:
Munafeqin ne kaha jo momin Shaheed hue woh agar unka sath dete to bache rahte. Lekin Momenin ne Jang mein Rasool ka sath diya aur Munafeqin se doori ikhtiyar ki. Munafeqin aur Momenin mein kabhi ittehad nahi ho sakta. Momin ke liye Maut Shahed ke manind hai jaisa ke Janabe Qasim (as) ne Karbala mein kaha tha, Munafiq to Maut se darta hai. Quran mein bahut jagah Islam Dushmano ke liye Allah ne yehi farmaya ke na woh Maut ki tamanna karte hain, na Maut se bhag sakte hain. Karbala ke Shaheedo ko Maut ki parva nahi thi, muqabala Munafeqin se tha. Unke kahna man lete to unko aman mil jati. Lekin woh sab Allah wale the, apne Iman ko Duniya ke badle nahi bechte. Maut ek aisi cheez hai jiska maza sab ko chakhna hai. Ab ye insaan par hai ke Izzat ke sath Jame Shahadat nosh farmaye ya phir zillat ke bistar se is Duniya s kooch kare.
🗡🛌🗡🛌🗡🛌🗡🛌🗡🛌🗡
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜
----------------------------------------------

_*MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!*_
🙇 🛌 ⚰
Imam Husain (as):
_*"Zillat ki zindagi se Izzat ki Maut behtar hai."*_
(Meezan ul Hikmah, v3)
🗡⚔ 🌍
Imam Askari (as):
_"Momin ke liye kitni buri baat hai ke aisi cheez ki taraf raghbat (khwaish) rakhe jo uski zillat o ruswaayi ka sabab ho."_
(Guftaar e Dil Nasheen, p237)
🗡🛌⚰
Imam Ali (as):
_"Duniya Momin ka qaid-khana, Maut uska tohfa aur Jannat uski manzil hai. Duniya kaafiro'n ki Jannat hoti hai aur maut use is (jannat) se judaa karne waali aur Aag uski manzil hoti hai."_
(Tajalliyat e Hikmat, Duniya)
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜
----------------------------------------------
*22nd Muharram 1438, 24th October 2016, Monday,

      ♦ _*HAYAT-E-SHUHADA'*_ ♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (446)

*بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ*

*وَلَا تَحْسَبَنَّ الَّذِينَ قُتِلُوا فِي سَبِيلِ اللَّهِ أَمْوَاتًا ۚ بَلْ أَحْيَاءٌ عِنْدَ رَبِّهِمْ يُرْزَقُونَ * فَرِحِينَ بِمَا آتَاهُمُ اللَّهُ مِنْ فَضْلِهِ وَيَسْتَبْشِرُونَ بِالَّذِينَ لَمْ يَلْحَقُوا بِهِمْ مِنْ خَلْفِهِمْ أَلَّا خَوْفٌ عَلَيْهِمْ وَلَا هُمْ يَحْزَنُونَ * يَسْتَبْشِرُونَ بِنِعْمَةٍ مِنَ اللَّهِ وَفَضْلٍ وَأَنَّ اللَّهَ لَا يُضِيعُ أَجْرَ الْمُؤْمِنِينَ*

_"Aur jo log Allah ki rahein Qatl (Shaheed) hue hain unhe hargiz murda na samjho balke woh to dar asl zinda hain apne Rab ke pas rizq paa rahe hain."_
_"Jo kuchh Allah ne apne Fazl se unhe diya hai woh us par khush hain aur woh unke liye Basharat talab hain jo unke peechhe rah gaye hain aur abhi unse nahi mile. Unke liye koi khauf nahi hai aur na hi ghamgeen honge. Woh Allah ki Nemat aur Fazl paakar Basharat talab hain aur yaqeenan Allah Ahle Imaan ke ajr ko zae nahi karta."_
(Surah Aal-e-Imran: 169 - 171)

📚📖
👉 _*�Tafseer:*_
Jaisa ke hamne pichhli bayan mein arz kiya tha Shaheed marta nahi balke zinda rahta hai. Lekin Allah ke pas rahta hai (عند ربهم). Allah unhe waise hi rizq muhayya karta hai jaise is Duniya mein. Woh ba Hayat hain. Isliye Imam Husain (as) aur Shuhadaye Karbala sab Allah ke pas zinda hain. Jo kuchh bhi agar ham unse mangte hain wo sunte hain aur Allah se hamari shifarish karte hain.
Nabi Akram (saww):
_"Jao Allah ki rah mein Jihad karo. Agar tum Jihad mein qatl hue to tum Khuda ke haan zindagi paa loge aur Khuda tumhe Rizq dega..."_
(Noorus Saqlain)
Imam Sadiq (as):
_"Muhabbat e Ale Muhammad (as) par Marnewala Shaheed hai."_

Karbala mein Shahadat Muhabbat e Ale Muhammad (as) par mabni thi. Karbala mein 72 Shaheed Ale Muhammad (as) ke liye Shaheed hue. Rasool (saww) ki Hadis e Saqlain ke Mutabiq Islam ko mutamassik e Quran o Ahle Bait (as) bataya. Iske alawa jisne koi aur raah ikhtiyar ki woh bhatak gaya. Yazeed Ibne Moaviya (LA) is Islam ka mazaq uda raha tha. Uske sath Musalmano ki aksariyat thi. Imam Husain (as) aur unke sathiyon ne 'fi Sabeelillah' Islam ke liye Qurbani di aur is Vilayati Islam ko zinda kiya.
Iske alawa jo bhi Muhabbate Ahle Bait (as) ki khatir marta hai woh bhi Allah ki raah mein jihad karne ke maanind hai aur Shaheed marta hai. Woh bhi Allah ke pas zinda aur Usse Rizq pata hai.
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜
----------------------------------------------

_*MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!*_
🙇 ⚜⚰
Rasool e Khuda (saww):
_"Allah Shaheed Rooh ko Jannat ke sabz parindo ke poton mein rakh deta hai jahan woh hasbe khwahish Jannat mein parwaz karte hain aur Jannat ke phal khate hain. Phir Arsh e Ilahi se Mu'llaq qandeelon mein aa kar rihaish karte hain."_
(Noorus Saqlain)
🗡⚰
Woh kaun hain jo apne baad aane walo ke liye Basharat talab hain?
Imam Baqir (as):
_"Khuda ki Qasam woh hamare Shia hain. Jab woh Maut ke baad Jannat mein dakhil hote hain aur Khuda ki tarafa se unhe Ne'mat o Fazl ata' hota hai to unhe yaqeen ho jata hai ke woh Haq par the aur Khuda ke Deen se puri zindagi wabasta rahe. Us waqt woh apne un Momin bhaiyon ke liye Basharat talab hote hain jo abhi tak unse mulhaq nahi hue hote. Un par na koi khauf hota aur na woh ghamgeen honge."_
(Roza e Kafi, Buraid e Ajli se manqool)
⚰🗡
Imam Ali (as):
_"Hamara har marne wala Shia, Siddiq aur Shaheed hokar marta hai kyun ki usne hamare Amr ki tasdeeq ki hai aur hamari wajah se kisi se mohabbat ki aur hamari wajah se kisi se nafrat ki. Is amal ke zariye Allah ki reza ka talab bana to aisa shakhs Khuda aur Rasul (saww) par sahi Imaan rakhne wala hai aur Allah Ta’ala ne farmaya hai WO LOG JO ALLAH AUR USKE RASOOLO’N PAR IMAAN LAAYE WO ALLAH KE NAZDEEK SIDDIQ AUR SHAHEED HAI.. (Surah Hadeed, Surah 57, Ayat 19)"_
(Guftaar e Dil Nasheen, p101)
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜

*23rd Muharram 1438, 25th October 2016, Tuesday,

        ♦ _*ZAKHMI MUJAHEDEEN*_ ♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (447)

*بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ*

*الَّذِينَ اسْتَجَابُوا لِلَّهِ وَالرَّسُولِ مِنْ بَعْدِ مَا أَصَابَهُمُ الْقَرْحُ ۚ لِلَّذِينَ أَحْسَنُوا مِنْهُمْ وَاتَّقَوْا أَجْرٌ عَظِيمٌ * الَّذِينَ قَالَ لَهُمُ النَّاسُ إِنَّ النَّاسَ قَدْ جَمَعُوا لَكُمْ فَاخْشَوْهُمْ فَزَادَهُمْ إِيمَانًا وَقَالُوا حَسْبُنَا اللَّهُ وَنِعْمَ الْوَكِيلُ * فَانْقَلَبُوا بِنِعْمَةٍ مِنَ اللَّهِ وَفَضْلٍ لَمْ يَمْسَسْهُمْ سُوءٌ وَاتَّبَعُوا رِضْوَانَ اللَّهِ ۗ وَاللَّهُ ذُو فَضْلٍ عَظِيمٍ.*

_"Ye Sahebane Imaan hain jinhone zakhmi hone ke baad bhi Khuda aur Rasool ki Dawat par Labaik kahi. Unke Nek kirdar Muttaqi afraad ke liye Ajre Azeem hai."_
_"Ye woh Ahle Imaan hain jab unse baaz logon ne kaha ke koi logon ne tumhare liye Azeem lashkar jama kar liya hai lehaza unse daro to unke Imaan mein aur Izafa ho gaya aur unhone kaha ke hamare liye Khuda Kafi hai aur Woh Behtareen karsaz hai. Akhirkar woh Khuda ki Nemat o Fazl ke sath wapas laut aye. Unko kisi tarah ka koi Nuqsan na pahuncha aur unhone Raza e Ilahi ka itteba kiya aur Allah Fazl e Azeem ka Malik hai."_
(Surah Aal-e-Imran: 172 - 174)

📚📖
👉 _* Tafseer:*_
*Jang e Uhud:*
Ye pahle bhi bayan kar chuke hain ke jang ke ikhtetam par Abu Sufyan tezi se Mecca ki taraf ravana hua, jab Roha pahuncha to bahut pasheman hua aur phir Madina ki taraf lautne ka irada kiya taake baqi manda musalmano ko nabood kare. Ye ittela jab Paighambar e Islam (saww) ko pahunchi to Aap ne hukm diya ke doosri Jang ke liye tayyar ho jayen. Aap ne ye bhi hukm diya ke zakhmi bhi lashkar mein shamil hon. Ek sahabi ka bayan hai ke woh apne zakhmi bhai ko apne kandhe par le kar chal raha tha. Madina se 8 Mile door Hamra Al Asad par padao dala. Ye sun kar ke Musalman abhi bhi jang ke liye tayyar hain dushman  himmat har gaya. Abu Sufyan ke jasoos ne bataya ke Rasool (saww) muqable ke liye ek bada Lashkar jama hai aur tumhara peechha kar raha hai. Isliye Kuffar Mecca wapas laut gaye. Musalmano ne tab kaha Allah hamare liye Kafi hai.
(Majmaul Bayan, Noorus Saqlain, Al Munar)
In Ayaat mein Allah ne in logon ki madah sarai ki hain aur Ajr ke haqdar bataya hai.
Aise hi log Karbala mein the jahan woh sirf Allah par bharosa kiye hue the. Jab ek Karbalai Yazeedi ke samna aata to is Yazeedi ko apne samne ek lashkar nazar aata. Abu Sufyan ka Madina ko taraaj o nabood karne ka us waqt to maqsad pura nahi hua lekin uske pote Yazeed ne ye kaam bhi kar dikhaya. Karbala ke waqae ke baad Madine par hamla hua, Kaaba ko jalaya gaya. Tafseelat ke liye Books refer karen.
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜
----------------------------------------------

_*MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!*_
🙇
Imam Baqir (as):
_"Karbala mein Imam e Aali Maqaam (Imam Husain) (as) ko shaheed kar diya gaya aur aap ko talwaar aur naize ke 320 se zyada zakhm lagaaye gaye. Ye tamaam zakhm aap ke jism e mubarak ke saamne waale hisse mein aaye, aap ne dushman ko pusht nahi dikhaayi thi."_
(Azadaari - 40 Hadith)
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜

*24th Muharram 1438, 26th October 2016, Wednesday,

BAZM-E-ADAB COMMEMORATE SHAHADAT of IMAM ALI IBNUL HUSAIN AL SAJJAD (as)*

             ♦ _*AFWAH E SHAITANI*_ ♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (448)

*بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ*

*إِنَّمَا ذَٰلِكُمُ الشَّيْطَانُ يُخَوِّفُ أَوْلِيَاءَهُ فَلَا تَخَافُوهُمْ وَخَافُونِ إِنْ كُنْتُمْ مُؤْمِنِينَ*

_"Woh to Shaitan hi tha jo apne doston se dara raha tha lehaza tum unse mat daro. Agar tum Momin ho to sirf Mujhse hi daro."_
(Surah Aal-e-Imran: 175)

📚📖 👹👺🙏🏻
👉 _* Tafseer:*_
Jaisa ke zikr Jange Uhud ka jari hai. Hamne kal bataya tha ke Hamra Al Asad mein jab Musalman ye afwah sun kar uth khade hue ke Kuffare Quraish phirse ek badi taqat ke sath unse ladne aa rahe hain. Ye faqat Shaitan ke sathi the jo unhe dara rahe the.
Qur'an ne hame kai jagah bataya ke ye insaan ka dushman hai aur unko nuqsan pahuchata hai. (Anaam:112, Jin:13).
Isliye agar hamare dil mein ghair e Khuda ka khauf hota hai to Imaan kamzor hota hai. Agar aap ko Shaitani taqat aur Khuda ki Taqat ka andaza ho jaye to aap kabhi bhi Shaitan se darne ke bajai Allah se uske shar se mahfooz rahne ki dua karenge.
Ab dekha jaye to logon ko Bhoot paret, Jinnat, Rakshash se zyada dar laga rahta hai. Ya yeh ki kisi ne totka to nahi kar diya. Ya kisi ne kisi ki Rozi bandh di, kisi ki kokh bandh di etc. Musibatzadah aur guruba inke shar se mahfooz rahne ke liye idhar udhar bhatakte rahte hain. Koi kisi Baba ka shikar ho jata hai. Ya kisi rusoomat, andhwishwas, superstitions ka shikar ho jate hain. Asl mein ye log Jahiliyat ka shikar hote hain. Ye Deen se la Ilmi ke sabab hota hai.  
Ham pahle bhi bata chuke hai Musibat o Bala ki wajah. Har musibat khud ya to uske aamaal ka natija hoti hai ya Khuda ka Azaab. Ab agar ye sab Khuda ki taraf se hai to aap kisi surat mein taal nahi sakte, siwai iske ke aapko Khuda ko raazi karna hoga, Khuda ko dost rakhna hoga, Khuda se hi darna hoga. Uske batai hue Ahkam par chalna hoga. Agar aap Khuda ke sath hain to aapko darne ki koi zaroorat nahi, lekin agar Shaitan ke sathi aur usko dost rakhte hain to aap apni safety bhool jayen.
Lekin is baat ka bhi khayal rahe ke jin Shakhsiyat se  Allah Razi hai unke baghair aap Allah ke pas jayenge to koi sunwai nahi hogi.
Ham pahle bhi explain kar chuke hain Allah sirf Ahle Bait e Athaar (as) se hi Razi hai to inka daman na chhode. Ahle Bait (as) ke sath rahenge to Deen aur Duniya sab bakhair hogi.
*اهْدِنَا الصِّرَاطَ الْمُسْتَقِيمَ * صِرَاطَ الَّذِينَ أَنْعَمْتَ عَلَيْهِمْ غَيْرِ الْمَغْضُوبِ عَلَيْهِمْ وَلَا الضَّالِّينَ*
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜
----------------------------------------------

_*MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!*_
🙇
(Bamunasebat Shahadat Imam Sajjad (as) zere ayat unke Aqwaal)
👹👺
Imam Sajjad (as):
_"Aye Rab! Tu Shaitan ki aarzu puuri na hone de balke Tu uske evaz meri zabaan ko Apni Hamd mein masruuf kar de."_
(Dua e Makaarimul Akhlaaq)
😭😰😢
Imam Sajjad (as):
_"Khauf e Khuda ka matlab rona aur aa'nsu bahana nahi hai, kyun ki jab Taqwa na ho jo usay gunaho'n se roke, ye khauf jhoota hai."_
(Uddatud Daee, ch4)
🙏🏻
Imam Sajjad (as):
_"Aye Maabud! Mujhe Rozi mein izafa, watan mein aman aur mere maal aur meri aulaad ke baare mein aa'nkho'n ki thhandak ataa farma aur Apni ne'mato'n mein mujhe khusoosi hissa, badan mein sehat o tandurusti, badan mein tawanaayi aur Deen mein salamati inayat farma aur mujhe aise amal ki taufeeq de de ke main Teri bandagi aur Tere Rasul H. Muhammad (saww) ki farma-bardaari mein rahu'n. Jab tak Tu mujhe zinda rakhe, mujhe Apne oon bando'n mein qaraar de jinka hissa Tere yahaa'n oon bhalaayio'n mein bahut zyada hai jo Tu ne naazil ki aur naazil karta hai, Maah e Ramzan mein, Shab e Qadr mein aur jo Tu har saal naazil karta hai; yaani wo Rehmat jise Tu phailaata hai, wo aaraam jo Tu deta hai, wo sakhti jise Tu duur karta hai; aur gunah jo Tu maaf farmata hai."_
(Dua e Abu Hamza Sumaali)
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜

*25th Muharram 1438, 27th October 2016, Thursday,

                ♦ _*KUFR*_ ♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (449)

*بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ*

*وَلَا يَحْزُنْكَ الَّذِينَ يُسَارِعُونَ فِي الْكُفْرِ ۚ إِنَّهُمْ لَنْ يَضُرُّوا اللَّهَ شَيْئًا ۗ يُرِيدُ اللَّهُ أَلَّا يَجْعَلَ لَهُمْ حَظًّا فِي الْآخِرَةِ ۖ وَلَهُمْ عَذَابٌ عَظِيمٌ*

_"(Aye Paighambar) jo log aaj Kufr ki raah mein badi daud dhoop kar rahe hain unki sargarmiyan tumhe aazurdah na karen, ye Allah ka kuchh bhi na bigad sakenge. Allah ka unke liye irada ye hai ke unke liye Akherat mein koi hissa na rakhe aur unke liye Azaab e Azeem hai."_
(Surah Aal-e-Imran: 176)
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜
----------------------------------------------

_*MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!*_
🙇 🌱🌾🌿
*رسول الله‏ (ص): أركان الكفر أربعة: الرغبة، والرهبة، والسخط، والغضب.*
Rasool e Khuda (saww):
_"Kufr ke 4 Piller hain:_
_- Raghbat (Desire)_
_- Darr (Fear)_
_- Bechaini (Discontentment) aur_
_- Gussa (Anger)."_
[al-Kafi, v. 2, p. 289, no. 2]
🕌🌿🌿
*الإمام علي (ع): بني الكفر على أربع دعائم: الفسق، والغلو، والشك، والشبهة.*
Imam Ali (as):
_"Kufr ki imarat 4 sutoono par khadi hoti hai:_
_- Fisq (Corruption)_
_- Al Ghulu (Extremism)_
_- Shak (Doubt) aur_
_- Subha (Suspicion)."_
[al-Kafi. v. 2, p. 391, no. 1]
🕌🌾🌾
*الإمام الصادق (ع) ـ لما سئل عن منزلة رجل إن حدث كذب، وإن وعد أخلف، وإن ائتمن خان ـ: هي أدنى المنازل من الكفر وليس بكافر.*

_"Jab poochha gaya ke us shakhs ki kiya manzelat hai jo Jhoot bolta hai, Wada khilafi karta hai, Amanat mein khayanat karta hai._
Imam Sadiq (as) ne farmaya :
_"Ye Kufr ki adna (low) manzilen hain jabke woh Kafir nahi hai."_
[al-Kafi, v. 2, p. 290, no. 5]
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜
----------------------------------------------
*27th Muharram 1438, 29th October 2016, Saturday,

BAZM-E-ADAB WELCOMES YOU*
***********************************
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜
         ♦ _*IMAAN V/s KUFR*_ ♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (450)

*بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ*

*إِنَّ الَّذِينَ اشْتَرَوُا الْكُفْرَ بِالْإِيمَانِ لَنْ يَضُرُّوا اللَّهَ شَيْئًا وَلَهُمْ عَذَابٌ أَلِيمٌ*

_"Jo log Imaan ke evaz Kufr ke kharidar bane hain woh yaqeenan Allah ko koi nuqsan nahi pahuncha sakte aur unke liye dardnak Azaab hain."_
(Surah Aal-e-Imran: 177)

📚📖
👉 _* Tafseer:*_
Ayat ke maani clear hain aur hamne kal bataya ke Kufr kise kahte hain. Kafi logo milenge jo apna Imaan bech kar Duniya kharidte hai.
Karbala mein Kufiyon aur fauje Yazidiyon ne apne Imaan ko Yazid ke hatho bech diya tha. بيع Bay means bechna istrah بيعت Bay'at. Yazeed Imam Husain (as) ko Bayat se kharidna chahta jisme woh nakaam raha. In Yazidiyon ke liye dardnak Azaab hai.
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜
----------------------------------------------

_*MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!*_
🙇
*Char Musibaten, Char hal*
Imam Sadiq (as):

1. *Khauf:* Mujhe us par tajjub hai jo Khauf mein mubtela ho kar
*حَسْبُنَا اللَّهُ وَنِعْمَ الْوَكِيلُ*
[Surah Aal-E-Imran 173]
ki panah mein kiyon nahi aa jata. Kiyonki Allah Ta'ala ne farmaya hai.
(فَانْقَلَبُوا بِنِعْمَةٍ مِنَ اللَّهِ وَفَضْلٍ لَمْ يَمْسَسْهُمْ سُوءٌ وَاتَّبَعُوا رِضْوَانَ اللَّهِ ۗ وَاللَّهُ ذُو فَضْلٍ عَظِيمٍ)
[Surah Aal-E-Imran 174]

2. *Gham:*Gham mein mubtela hone wala shakhs
*لَا إِلَٰهَ إِلَّا أَنْتَ سُبْحَانَكَ إِنِّي كُنْتُ مِنَ الظَّالِمِينَ*
[Surah Al-Anbiya' 87]
ki panah mein kiyon nahi aa jata? Kiyonki Allah Ta'ala ne Qissa Yunus (as) mein bayan kiya ke jab unhone Machhli ke shikam (pet) mein ye Kalemat kahe the to _"Hamne unki darkhwast qubool ki aur unhe Gham se nijat di  aur Ham usi tarah se Ahle Imaan ko nijaat diya karte hain."_

3. *Dhoka khana:* Jiske khilaf log heela o makro fareb mein masroof hon to aisa shakhs
(فَسَتَذْكُرُونَ مَا أَقُولُ لَكُمْ ۚ وَأُفَوِّضُ أَمْرِي إِلَى اللَّهِ ۚ إِنَّ اللَّهَ بَصِيرٌ بِالْعِبَادِ)
[Surah Ghafir: 44]
ka sahara kiyon nahi leta? Kiyonki Allah ne ye Kalemat kahne walon ka natija ye bayan kiya hai:
_"Allah ne use Makr karne walon ki buraiyon se bacha liya tha."_

4. *Nazr lagna:* Duniya aur Zeenat e Duniya talab karne wala shakhs
*مَا شَاءَ اللَّهُ لَا قُوَّةَ إِلَّا بِاللَّهِ ۚ*
[Surah Al-Kahf 39]
ki panah mein kiyon nahi aa jata? Kiyonki jisne ye Kalemat jahe the Allah Ta'ala ne uske Kalemat ke baad ye jumle naql kiye:
*إِنْ تَرَنِ أَنَا أَقَلَّ مِنْكَ مَالًا وَوَلَدًا*
[Surat Al-Kahf 39]
_"Agar tum mujhe Maal o Aulad ke lihaz se apne se kam dekh rahe ho to Allah anqareeb mujhe tere Baugh se ataa karega."_
(Kitab Al Khisal, Noorus Saqlain)
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜
----------------------------------------------
*28th Muharram 1438, 30th October 2016, Sunday,
🔹🔹🔹🔹🔹🔹🔹🔹🔹🔹

BAZM-E-ADAB WELCOMES YOU*

⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜
        ♦ _*KAFIRON KO DHEEL*_ ♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (451)

*بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ*

*وَلَا يَحْسَبَنَّ الَّذِينَ كَفَرُوا أَنَّمَا نُمْلِي لَهُمْ خَيْرٌ لِأَنْفُسِهِمْ ۚ إِنَّمَا نُمْلِي لَهُمْ لِيَزْدَادُوا إِثْمًا ۚ وَلَهُمْ عَذَابٌ مُهِينٌ*

_"Ham jo Kafiron ko jo dheel de rahe hain use woh apne liye behtari tasawwur na karen. Ham to unhe isliye dheel de rahe hain taake woh gunahon mein mazeed izaafa kar len, unke liye zaleel karne wala Azaab hai."_
(Surah Aal-e-Imran: 178)

📚📖
👉 _* Tafseer:*_
Aksar sawal hota hai ke Kafir itne gunah aur zulm karne ke bawajood itne aish o araam mein kaise rahte hain. Allah un par Azaab kiyon nahi bhejta. Allah ki Adalat par sawal uthta hai. Is baat ka Allah ne is ayat mein jawab diya hai. Jaise ke mashoor hai Allah ke yahan der hai andher nahi. Allah ki lathi mein awaz nahi hoti. Kyonki Kafir ko Duniya pasand hai isliye Allah uske kuchh Nek Amaal ka badla isi Duniya mein de deta aur uske liye Akherat mein kuchh nahi bachta. Ham Allah ki Adalat ko nahi samajh sakte. Imam (as) hi samjha sakte hain.

Imam Mohd Baqir (as) se poochha gaya: Kafiron ke liye Maut behtar hai ya Zindagi behtar hai?
Imam (as) ne farmaya:
_"Maut Momin wa Kafir dono ke liye behtar hai."_
Wajah:
_"Allah ne Ahle Imaan ke liye farmaya:_
*وَمَا عِنْدَ اللَّهِ خَيْرٌ لِلْأَبْرَارِ*[3:198]
_"Jo kuchh Khuda ke pas hai woh Nekokaron ke liye ziyada behtar hai."_
Aur Kafiron ke liye farmay: [3:178]
(Tafseer e Ayashi, Noorus Saqlain)

_*Khutba Zainab (sa):*_
Duniya e Islam ki Sher Dil Khatoon Janabe Zainab e Kubra (sa) ne Yazeed ke Darbar mein is ayat (3:178) ke hawale se is tarah istedlal pesh kiya:
_"Tu aaj khush hai aur ye khayal karta hai ke chunke toone wasee wa areez (large) Duniya ham par tang kar rakhi hai aur Aasmaan ke kinaron ko ham par band kar diya hai aur qaidiyon ki tarah hame dayar badayar phiraya ja raha hai isliye ke ye teri qudrat o taqat ki nishani hai aur ya Khuda ke haan teri qudrat o manzelat hai aur hamare liye Uske haan koi rah nahi. Ye sab tera ishtebah (mistake) hai. Ye mauqa aur azaadi Khuda ne tujhe isliye di hai taake teri pusht (back) bare gunah (Sin load) se bhari ho jai aur dardnak Azaab tere intezar mein hai. Khuda ki Qasam agar hawadis e zamana mujhe ek Qaidi Aurat ki shakl mein tere paye takht mein le ayen hain to isse ye khayal mat kar ke meri nazar mein tumhari koi thodi si bhi hasiyat ya qadr o waqa'at hai. Mein tujhe chhota, past (low), har lihaz se haqeer aur malamat, sarzanish aur phitkar ka mustahaq samajhti hun. Jo kuchh tujh se ho sakta hai kar le. Khuda ki Qasam tu hamare Noor ko khamosh nahi kar sakta. Tu wah ye Javedan (Live inspiration) aur hamare Aeen e Haq ko mahv (erase) nahi kar sakta. Tu Nabood ho jayega aur ye taab nak Sitara yun hi chamakta rahega."_
(Tafseer e Namoona)
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜
----------------------------------------------

_*MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!*_
🙇
Imam Ali (as):
_"Duniya Momin ka qaid-khana, Maut uska tohfa aur Jannat uski manzil hai. Duniya kaafiro'n ki Jannat hoti hai aur maut usay is (jannat) se judaa karne waali aur Aag uski manzil hoti hai."_
(Tajalliyat e Hikmat, Duniya)
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜

*29th Muharram 1438, 31st October 2016, Monday,

BAZM-E-ADAB WELCOMES YOU*

            ♦ _*PAAK - NAPAAK*_ ♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (452)

*بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ*

*مَا كَانَ اللَّهُ لِيَذَرَ الْمُؤْمِنِينَ عَلَىٰ مَا أَنْتُمْ عَلَيْهِ حَتَّىٰ يَمِيزَ الْخَبِيثَ مِنَ الطَّيِّبِ ۗ وَمَا كَانَ اللَّهُ لِيُطْلِعَكُمْ عَلَى الْغَيْبِ وَلَٰكِنَّ اللَّهَ يَجْتَبِي مِنْ رُسُلِهِ مَنْ يَشَاءُ ۖ فَآمِنُوا بِاللَّهِ وَرُسُلِهِ ۚ وَإِنْ تُؤْمِنُوا وَتَتَّقُوا فَلَكُمْ أَجْرٌ عَظِيمٌ*

_"Allah Ahle Iman ko usi haalat mein nahi rahne dega jis mein tum log us waqt paye jate ho. Woh PAAK logo ko NAPAAK logon se alag kar dega. Allah ka ye tariqa nahi ke woh tumhe ghaib par muttela (inform) karde. Isliye ke wo apne Rasoolon mein se jisko chahta hai muntakhab kar leta hai. Tum Allah aur uske Rasoolon par Imaan rakho. Agar tum ne Imaan aur Taqwa Ikhtiyar kiya to tumhare liye Ajre Azeem hai."_
(Surah Aal-e-Imran: 179)

📚📖 ⚔
👉 _* Tafseer:*_
Jange Uhud ke zel mein Ayaton ki tafseer jari hai.
Jange Uhud ke pahle sirf ek Dushman-e-Islam tha: Kuffar. Lekin is jang mein Munafeqin ka giroh zahir hua. Munafeqin woh khatarnak Dushman tha jisko pahchanna mushkil tha. Allah ko ilm tha, bata bhi sakta tha. To phir Allah ne unka parda fash kiyon nahi kiya. Ya phir agar Allah chahta to sabhi Kuffar o Munafeqin ko ek lamhe mein khatm kar deta. Allah chahta tha ke uske bande jadhho jahd mein lage rahen, khud koshish kare. Allah ne apne Makhsoos Anbiya ko Ilme Ghaib se nawaza. Sab insaan agar ilme ghaib rakhte to nuqsaan ke alawa aur kuchh na hota. Isliye bahut si cheezon ka raaz mein rahna faydemand hain. Yahan tak bahut si hadithon ko Imam ne bayan karne se mana kiya kiyoki log hazam nahi kar payenge. Allah ye Ilme Ghaib apne Hikmat ke mutabiq Uske muntakhab shuda Hadi o Rehbar Anbiya o Imam ko ataa karta hai. Chunke Allah Ahle Imaan wa Muttaqeen ko chahta hai, Woh chahta hai wo napaak logon se door rahen jiska Woh intezam karta hai. Agar Jange e Uhud na hoti to pata nahi chalta kaun munafiq hain. Allah har kisi ka Imtehan leta hai. Usi tarah Karbala ne Paak aur NaPaak ko alag kar ke dekha diya. Agar Karbala ka waqea nahi hota to Najis Yazid Paleed nahi pahchana jata.
Maqtal Abi Makhnaf mein Abdullah se manqool hai ke Ibne Saad ka ghoda sawar dasta Imam Husain (as) ke pas se guzra to Aap (as) ne ye Ayat (3:178-179) padhi.
In ayat ki tilawat se har aqalmand ko rahti Duniya tak ye dars diya hai ke Yazeedi afwaj ki zahiri quwwat ko dekh kar unhe Ahle Haq nahi samjha sakta. Ye zahiri dabdaba Khuda ki taraf se baes e Imtehan hain. Jaisa ke Janabe Zainab (as) ne bhi apne khutbe mein yehi kaha tha.
(Noorus Saqlain, Tafseer e Namoona)
(U r receiving this tafseer written by myself.)
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜
----------------------------------------------

_*MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!*_
🙇 ⚔
Rasule Khuda (saww):
_"Tum mein bad-tareen log Chugal-khori karne wale, Dosto'n ke darmiyaan judaai daalne wale aur paak-daaman logo'n par aib lagaane waale log hote hain."_
(Meezan ul Hikmah, v5)

                ♦ _*ZAKAT*_ ♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (453)

*بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ*

*وَلَا يَحْسَبَنَّ الَّذِينَ يَبْخَلُونَ بِمَا آتَاهُمُ اللَّهُ مِنْ فَضْلِهِ هُوَ خَيْرًا لَهُمْ ۖ بَلْ هُوَ شَرٌّ لَهُمْ ۖ سَيُطَوَّقُونَ مَا بَخِلُوا بِهِ يَوْمَ الْقِيَامَةِ ۗ وَلِلَّهِ مِيرَاثُ السَّمَاوَاتِ وَالْأَرْضِ ۗ وَاللَّهُ بِمَا تَعْمَلُونَ خَبِيرٌ*

_"Jin logon par Allah ne Apna Fazl kiya hai aur woh Bukhl (Kanjoosi) se kaam lete hain to woh is khayal mein na rahen ke ye Bakheeli unke liye achhi hai. Ye Bakheeli unke Haq mein bahut buri hai. Jo kuchh woh Kanjoosi se jama kar rahe hain wohi Qayamat ke Din unke gale ka Tauq (Coller) ban jayga aur Zameen aur Aasmano ki Milkiyat Allah ke liye hai aur Khuda tumhare Aamaal se achhi tarah Ba Khabar hai."_
(Surah Aal-e-Imran: 180)

📚📖
👉 _* Tafseer:*_
Imam Jafar Sadiq (as):
_"Jo bhi Shakhs apne Maal ki Zakat ada nahi karega to Qayamat ke Din Allah us Maal ko Dozakh ka sanp (Snake) bana dega jo uske gale mein Tauq ki tarah chimta hua hoga aur woh Hisab se farigh hone tak uske gosht ko nochta rahega. Isi haqeeqat ko is Ayat ke zariye se Irshad farmaya hai. Ye Ayat Mane'een e Zakat (Tax Evaders) ke mutalliq hai."_
(Al Kafi, Noorus Saqlain)
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜
----------------------------------------------

_*MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!*_
🙇 💰
*الإمام علي (ع): زكاة القدرة ، الإنصاف.*
Imam Ali (as):
_"Qudrat ka Zakat Insaaf hai."_
[Ghurar al-Hikam, no. 5448]
💰
*الإمام علي (ع): زكاة الجمال ، العفاف.*
_"Khoobsurti ka Zakat Iffat (Chastity) hai.'_
[Ghurar al-Hikam, no. 5449]
💰
*الإمام علي (ع): زكاة اليسار ، بر الجيران وصلة الأرحام.*
_"Sarwat (Prosperity) ki Zakat Padosi se achha bartao aur Silah Rahem"_
[Ghurar al-Hikam, no. 5453]
💰
*الإمام علي (ع): زكاة الصحة ، السعي في طاعة الله‏.*
_"Sahet (Health) ka Zakat Allah ki ita'at ki koshish karna."_
[Ghurar al-Hikam, no. 5454]
💰
*الإمام علي (ع): زكاة الشجاعة ، الجهاد في سبيل الله‏.*
_"Bahaduri, Shuja'at ki Zakat Allah ki raah mein Jihad hai."_
[Ghurar al-Hikam, no. 5455]
💰
*الإمام علي (ع): عليك بالصوم ؛ فإنه زكاة البدن.*
_"Roza wajib hai kiyonki woh Badan ki Zakat hai."_
[Bihar al-Anwar, v. 78, p. 99, no. 1]
💰
*الإمام الصادق (ع): إن لكل شيء زكاة ، وزكاة العلم أن يعلمه أهله.*
Imam Sadiq (as):
_"Har cheez ki Zakat hai, aur ILM ki Zakat unki Ta'leem (Teaching) hai jo iske laeq hain."_
[Bihar al-Anwar, p. 247, no. 77]
💰
*الإمام الصادق (ع): المعروف زكاة النعم ، والشفاعة زكاة الجاه ، والعلل زكاة الأبدان ، والعفو زكاة الظفر ، وما أديت زكاته فهو مأمون السلب.*
_"Ne'mat ki Zakat achha adab hai, Uncha Maqam ki Zakat Shafa'at hai, Bimari badan ka Zakat hai, Fatah (Victory) ki Zakat Afv (Maaf karna-Forgiveness), aur jo kuchh Zakat tum doge uske chhin jane se mahfooz rahoge."_
[Bihar al-Anwar, p. 268, no. 182]
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜

*1st Safar 1438, 2nd November 2016, Wednesday,

       ♦ _*DAULAT AUR GHAREEBI*_ ♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (454)

*بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ*

*لَقَدْ سَمِعَ اللَّهُ قَوْلَ الَّذِينَ قَالُوا إِنَّ اللَّهَ فَقِيرٌ وَنَحْنُ أَغْنِيَاءُ ۘ سَنَكْتُبُ مَا قَالُوا وَقَتْلَهُمُ الْأَنْبِيَاءَ بِغَيْرِ حَقٍّ وَنَقُولُ ذُوقُوا عَذَابَ الْحَرِيقِ * ذَٰلِكَ بِمَا قَدَّمَتْ أَيْدِيكُمْ وَأَنَّ اللَّهَ لَيْسَ بِظَلَّامٍ لِلْعَبِيدِ*

_"Allah ne un logo ka qaul sun liya jinhone kaha ke Allah Faqir (Poor) hai aur ham Ghani (Rich) hain. Unki ye baten Ham likh lenge. Isse pahle unhone Paighambaron ko jo nahaq qatl kiya hai wo bhi unke Nama e Aamaal mein sabt (recorded) hai. Ham unse kahenge ke bhadakti hui Aag ka maza chakho."_
_"Ye tumhare apne hathon ki kamai hai. Allah apne bandon par Zulm Karne wala nahi hai."_
(Surah Aal-e-Imran: 181 - 182)

📚📖 💰💶💷
👉 _* Tafseer:*_
Qur'an ki ayaton ko sirf Imam hi explain kar sakte hai:
Imam Jafar Sadiq (as):
_"Khuda ki Qasam jin logon ne (Yahoodi) ye baat kahi thi unhone Allah ko to nahi dekha tha aur na hi unhone Khuda ki Ghurbat ka mushaheda kiya tha jisse unhe pata chalta ke Khuda Gharib hai. Asl baat ye hai ke unhone Auliya e Khuda wandi ko Ghurbat o Iflas mein dekha tha aur unhone apni daulat mandi aur sarwat (Wealth) ko dekh kar ye jumle kahe the ke Allah Gharib hai aur ham daulat mand hain. Unki guftugu ka maqsad ye tha ke agar Khuda ke pas Daulat hoti to woh apne pyare bande ko bhi Daulat mand bana deta. Chunke Khuda ke Pyare Gharib hain isse sabit hota hai ke Khuda bhi Gharib hai jabke ham daulat o sarwat rakhne wale log hain. Al gharz unhone apni daulat ke zariye se Khuda par fakhr kiya."_
(Tafseer Ali bin Ibrahim)
💰
Imam Mohd Baqir (as):
_"Jo log aapko daulat mand aur Imam (as) ko Gharib tasawwur karte hain woh bhi is Ayat e Quran e Majid ke zimn mein Shamil hain."_
(Manaqib Ibne Shahre Ashoob, Noorus Saqlain)
💰
Imam Ali (as):
_"Khuda ki Qasam! Jin logon ke pas zindagi ki taro taza o Shadab Ne'maten thi phir unke hathon se nikal gayi - ye unke Gunahon je murtakib hone ki padash (result) hai kiyonki Allah apne bando par Zulm karne wala nahi hai."_
(Nahjul Balagha)
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜
----------------------------------------------

_*MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!*_
🙇 💰
Rasule Khuda (saww):
_"Tum mein se behtar wo hai jo Faqr (gareebi) par raazi ho jaaye, logo'n se kinara-kash ho jaaye aur Deen aur Taqwa ki fikr kare."_
(Hadiyat ush Shia, p24)
💰
Imam Sadiq (as):
_"Allah par bharosa rakhne waale gareeb ki khuddari, kisi maaldaar ki zarurat-mand ko ki huwi khairaat se behtar hai."_
(Islamic Morals)
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜
----------------------------------------------
*2nd Safar 1438, 3rd November 2016, Thursday,

 ♦ _*QATIL SE RAZAMAND SHAKHS BHI QATIL HAI*_ ♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (455)

*بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ*

*الَّذِينَ قَالُوا إِنَّ اللَّهَ عَهِدَ إِلَيْنَا أَلَّا نُؤْمِنَ لِرَسُولٍ حَتَّىٰ يَأْتِيَنَا بِقُرْبَانٍ تَأْكُلُهُ النَّارُ ۗ قُلْ قَدْ جَاءَكُمْ رُسُلٌ مِنْ قَبْلِي بِالْبَيِّنَاتِ وَبِالَّذِي قُلْتُمْ فَلِمَ قَتَلْتُمُوهُمْ إِنْ كُنْتُمْ صَادِقِينَ*

_"Jo log kahte hain ke Allah ne ham se Ahd liya hai ke ham us waqt tak kisi Rasool par Imaan na layen jab tak woh aisi Qurbani pesh na kare jise Aag kha jay. Aap kah den ke mujh se pahle bahut se Rasool Mo'jezat aur tumhari azmaish ke mutabiq sadaqat ki nishani lay the. Agar tum apne dawa mein sachche ho to tumne unhe qatl kiyon kiya tha."_
(Surah Aal-e-Imran: 183)

📚📖
👉 _* Tafseer:*_
(Quran ki Tafseer Imam ki zabani:)
Imam Jafar Sadiq (as):
_"Bani Israel jab koi Qurbani pesh karte the aur un mein se Khuda ko jo Qurbani manzoor hoti thi Aasmaan se us par Aag ka shola gir kar use bhasm kar deta tha aur jis par Aag ka shola nahi girta tha to Qurbani na manzoor shumar hoti thi. Allah Ta'ala ne Ummat e Islamiya ke liye Aatish e Qurbani ke badle mein Ehram rakha aur logon ko sharminda hone se bacha liya."_
(Al Kafi, Noorus Saqlain)
✋🏻
Imam Sadiq (as):
_"Khuda Qadariya par Laanat kare, Khuda Khwarij par Laanat kare, Khuda Murji'ah par Laanat kare, Khuda Murji'ah par Laanat kare"_
Raavi ne poochha Murj'ah par do bar Laanat kiyon ki?
Aap (as) ne farmaya:
_"Ji haan! Ye wo bad bakht hain jo hamare qatilon ke Momin hone ka Aqeeda rakhte hain. Qayamat tak unke kapdon par hamare khoon ke chhinte jame rahenge. Allah Ta'ala ne ek qaum ke nazaryat ki tarjumani karte hue farmaya: Ayat (3:183). Jin logon ne Rasoole Khuda (saww) se ye baat kahi thi unhone to kisi Rasool ko qatl nahi kiya tha magar Khuda ne unhe mukhatab karke farmaya ke tumne Rasoolon ko kiyon qatl kiya tha? Jabke Aatish e Qurbani ki farmaish karne walon aur Anbiya ke qatilon ke darmiyan poore 500 saal ka fasla tha. Allah Ta'ala ne unhe Anbiya ka qatil is liye qarar diya ke woh apne buzurgon ke fe'l (action) par raazi the. Is tarah se firqa Murji'ah ke afraad bhi hamare qatilon ke fe'l par raazi hain lehaza ye bhi hamare qatil hain."_
(Usool e Kafi, Noorus Saqlain)
✋🏻
Imam Sadiq (as):
'Jab Ahle Kitab ne Rasool e Akram (saww) se kaha ke hamne to Anbiya ka qatl nahi kiya to Aap (saww) ne farmaya:
_"Agar tum qatil nahi ho to Anbiya ke Qatilon par Laanat karo aur unse bezari ka Ailan karo"_ lekin unhone aisa na kiya.'
✋🏻
Imam Sadiq (as) ne Mohd bin Arqat se poochha ke tum Kufa mein rehte ho. Usne kaha haan. Aap (as) ne farmaya tumhe wahan Imam Husain (as) ke qatil dikhai diye?
Usne arz kiya: 'Mein aap par qurban jao, is waqt qateleen e Imam Husain (as) mein se koi nahi hai.'
Aap (as) ne farmaya:
_"Iska matlab to ye hua ke tumhari nazar mein qatil sirf wohi hai jisne direct kiso ko qatl kiya ho. Kiya tum ne Khuda ka farman nahi suna: (3:183)"_
(Yani jo Imam Husain (as) ke qatil se raazi hai woh bhi unka qatil shumar kiya jayga jabke usne khud qatl nahi kiya.)
(Noorus Saqlain)
Isi liya ham ziyarat e Waresa mein padhte hai:
*لَعَنَ اللهُ اُمةً قَتـَلَتـك وَلَعَنَ الله اُمةً ظَلَمَتـكَ وَلَعَن اللهُ اُمةً سـَمِعت بـِذلِك فَرَضِيت بـِهِ*
_(Allahi ki Laanat us Ummat par jis ne Aap ko qatl kiya, Allah ki Laanat ho us Ummat par jis ne Aap par Zulm kiya, Allah ki Laanat ho us Ummat par jisne suna aur is par raazi raha.)_
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜
----------------------------------------------

_*MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!*_
🙇
Imam Ali (as)
se ek naastik (atheist) ne kaha ke kya wajah hai ke Allah ne Ambiya (as) ki lagzisho'n (minor faults) ka Quran mein tafseeli) (detailed) zikr kiya hai? Imam (as) ne farmaya,:
_"Allah jaanta tha ke Ambiya (as) ke karamaat aur Mojezaat dekh kar bahut se log bhatak jayenge aur wo unhe Khuda kehne lag jayenge. Isi liye Allah ne unki lagzisho'n ka tazkera kiya hai taaki logo'n ko maalum ho ke wo Khuda nahi the jaisa ke Allah ne H. Musa (as) ki khwaish e Deedar (Allah ko dekhne ki khwaish) ka tazkera kiya hai aur unki behoshi ka zikr kiya hai to isme bhi Allah ki yehi maslehat hai."_
(Tafseer Noor us Saqlain, v3, p442)
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜
----------------------------------------------
*3rd Safar 1438, 4th November 2016, Friday,

BAZM-E-ADAB WELCOMES YOU*

♦ _*TAKZEEB E PAYAMBAR (saww)*_ ♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (456)

*بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ*

*فَإِنْ كَذَّبُوكَ فَقَدْ كُذِّبَ رُسُلٌ مِنْ قَبْلِكَ جَاءُوا بِالْبَيِّنَاتِ وَالزُّبُرِ وَالْكِتَابِ الْمُنِيرِ*

_"Phir agar iske baad bhi Aapki takzeeb (deny) karen to is takzeeb se mat ghabhrayen kiyonki Aap se pahle bhi Rasoolon ki takzeeb ho chuki hai jo Mo'jezat aur Sahife aur Roshni bakhshne wali Kitaben layen the."_
(Surah Aal-e-Imran: 184)

📚📖
👉 _* Tafseer:*_
Kal ki Ayat (3:183) mein Aatish e Qurbani ka zikr tha. Tafseer Al Munar ke mutabiq Yahoodiyon ne sawal kiya tha ke Rasool (saww) aisa Mo'jeza dekhayen: ke koi Janwar zabah ho aur Aag mo'ajzana taur par Aasmaan se aakar use jala de balke unka maqsad ye tha ke unke mazhabi Ahkamat mein Qurbani ki ek qism Jali hui Qurbani thi. Iske mutabiq woh ek Janwar zabah karte the aur khas rusoom ke mutabiq use Aag laga dete the. (Iski detail Bible ki Torah Chapter Safar Ladiyan (Leviticus) ki pahli Fasl mein hai).
Baqi Is Ayat ke asal maani Imam ki zabani kal bayan kiye the.
Is ayat mein Allah Paighambar (saww) ko tasalli de raha hai ke in logon ne Pichhle Paighambaron ko bhi jhutlaya jo Zuboor wa Injeel laye the (Zubur wa Muneer). To ye koi nai baat nahi. To jaisa un logon ne kiya, hamre Rasool (saww) ke sath bhi waisa hi hua. Ummat sirf Rasool e Khuda (saww) ko nahi balke unki Aal (progeny) ko bhi jhutlaya. Isi Takzeeb ka natija Waqae Karbala hai.
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜
----------------------------------------------

_*MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!*_
🙇 ✨✨
*الإمام الصادق (ع): الكذب على الله‏ وعلى رسوله (ص) من الكبائر.*
_"Alah aur uske Rasool (saww) ki Takzeeb Gunah e Kabirah hai."_
[al-Kafi, v. 2, p. 339, no. 5]
✨✨
Imam Sadiq (as):
_"Jab bhi Surah Masad (Tabbat Yadaa Abi..) (Surah No.111) ki tilawat karo to Abu Lahab ko bad-dua zaroor karna kyun ki ye aisa  jhoota hai ke Rasule Khuda (saww) aur jo kuchh Allah ki taraf se Rasul (saww) par naazil hone waali Wahi ki takzeeb kiya  (jhutlaaya) karta tha."_
(Sawaabul Aamaal o Iqaabul Aaamal, p275)
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜

*4th Mahe Safar 1438, 5th November 2016, Saturday,

                ♦ _*MAUT*_ ♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (457)

*بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ*

*كُلُّ نَفْسٍ ذَائِقَةُ الْمَوْتِ ۗ وَإِنَّمَا تُوَفَّوْنَ أُجُورَكُمْ يَوْمَ الْقِيَامَةِ ۖ فَمَنْ زُحْزِحَ عَنِ النَّارِ وَأُدْخِلَ الْجَنَّةَ فَقَدْ فَازَ ۗ وَمَا الْحَيَاةُ الدُّنْيَا إِلَّا مَتَاعُ الْغُرُورِ*

_"Har Nafs ko MAUT ka zaeqa chakhna hai. Qayamat ke Din tumhe tumhare Aamaal ka poora badla diya jayega aur Kamyab woh hai jo wahan Aatish e Dozakh se bach jaye aur Jannat mein dakhil kar diya jaye jabke Dunyavi Zindagi to dhoke ka saz o saman hai."_
(Surah Aal-e-Imran: 185)

📚📖
👉 _* Tafseer:*_
Maut ka Topic bahut wasee hai jiski yahan gunjaesh nahi lekin in short bayan karte hain.
Yahan Nafs se murad Jism o Jaan hai. (Body & Soul). Nafs ke rivayaton mein alag definition hain.
*Nafs* insaan ka mukammal jazbaat, rujhaan, khwahushaat, aarzoo aur tajarbaat ka majmua hai. Isse ek admi doosre aadmi mein farq nazar aata hai. Nafs mujarrad hai. Ye do tarah ki hai Nafs e Lawwama aur Nafs e Ammarah. Pahli Nafs Neki taraf khechti hai jabke doosri burai ki taraf khechti hai. Sura Yusuf mein Nafs e Ammara ka zikr hai.
Imam Ali (as):
_"Nafs ek jangli ghode ki tarah hai aur jab tum us par sawari kar rahe ho to ek second ki be tawajjohi (Laparwahi) tumhe utha ke pekh degi."_
*Rooh* Quran ki ayat (17:85) ke mutabiq Amr e Ilahi hai. Ye bhi Allah ki makhlooq hai.  Lekin Allah ne Rooh ko beinteha qudrat di lekin is Jism ke sath qaid kar diya.
Pas jo power Allah ki taraf se aata hai use Rooh kahte  hain. Jibrael (as) ko Roohul Amin kahte hain. Aimma ke muhafiz Roohul Quds hai. Misl ke taur par tak current aa raha hai hamne switch on kiya bulb jalne laga. Hamara switch aur supply Allah ke pas hai.
Insaan ke jismani paidaish se pahle woh Alam e Arwah mein tha. Alam e Zar mein iska imtehan liya gaya, jo is imtehan mein paas hua Duniya mein Momin ban kar ubhra. Is tarah us Alam mein do group hue Illieen (Highest Person) and Asfaleen (Lowest Category). Ab sawal uthta hai ke jab faisla pahli hi ho gaya to phir jaza wa saza kaisi? Allah Bandon ka Khaliq hai us Duniya mein ya is Duniya mein Allah jo imtehan leta hai ham uska jawab apne ikhtiyar se dete hain. Allah ne insaan ko amal ke maidan mein khud mukhtar banaya hai. Jabke ham is Duniya mein Alam e Zar ki baten ek khwab ki tarah bhool gaye. Agar hamne us Alam mein sahi jawab diya tha lekin ham ek Kafir ke gharane mein paida hue to Nafs e Lawwah mere uper havi ho jaygi aur ho sakta hai mein convert ho jaon. To ye Duniya ki zindagi hamara final imtehan hai. Topic bahut vast hai har sentence explanation chahta hai. Readers se guzarish ke Books ke zariye mazeed maloomat hasil karen.
This topic will be Cont'd ......
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜
----------------------------------------------

_*MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!*_
🙇 ✨✨
Rasule Khuda (saww):
_"Tamaam Roohein Aalam e Arwaah mein badi taadad (sankhya) mein rehti. Agar wahaa'n ek doosre se taaruf (introduction) huwa hai to yahaa'n unme aapas mein mohabbat hai aur agar wahaa'n ek doosre se (muta'arif) parichit nahi huwi to yahaa'n unke darmiyaan ikhtelaaf hoga."_
(Man La Yahzarahul Faqih, v4, p296)

Imam Baqir (as):
_"Har shakhs ke sone ke waqt uska Nafs aasman mein chadh jaata hai aur uski Rooh uske badan mein baaqi rehti hai aur dono ke darmiyaan aisa rishta baaqi rehta hai jaisa ke suraj aur uski shua (kiran / rays) mein. Phir agar Allah ne uski Rooh qabz kar lene ka izn de diya to Rooh Nafs ki daawat qubool kar leti hai aur agar Allah Rooh ki waapasi ka izn de deta hai to Nafs Rooh ki daawat maan leta hai aur palatt aata hai. Pus, jo kuchh Nafs aasmaan mein Aalam e Malakoot mein dekhta hai, uski taaweel (interpretation) ho sakti hai aur jo kuchh wo aasmaan aur zameen ke darmiyaan dekhta hai wo Shaitan ke takhayyulaat (imaginations) hote hain, unki koi taaweel nahi ho sakti."_
(Irshadaat e Masumeen (as), p115)
✨✨
Imam Baqir (as):
_"Khuda Wande Aalam ne hamare Shiyo'n se hamari Wilayat ke iqraar liya hai jab ke wo Aalam e Zar mein the. Usne unse oos waqt Apni Rabubiyat aur H. Rasule Khuda (saww) ki Nabuwwat ka bhi iqraar le liya tha."_
(Al Kaafi, v2, p481)

               ♦ _*MAUT*_ ♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (458)

*بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ*

*كُلُّ نَفْسٍ ذَائِقَةُ الْمَوْتِ ۗ وَإِنَّمَا تُوَفَّوْنَ أُجُورَكُمْ يَوْمَ الْقِيَامَةِ ۖ فَمَنْ زُحْزِحَ عَنِ النَّارِ وَأُدْخِلَ الْجَنَّةَ فَقَدْ فَازَ ۗ وَمَا الْحَيَاةُ الدُّنْيَا إِلَّا مَتَاعُ الْغُرُورِ*

_"Har Nafs ko MAUT ka zaeqa chakhna hai. Qayamat ke Din tumhe tumhare Aamaal ka poora badla diya jayega aur Kamyab woh hai jo wahan Aatish e Dozakh se bach jaye aur Jannat mein dakhil kar diya jaye jabke Dunyavi Zindagi to dhoke ka saz o saman hai."_
(Surah Aal-e-Imran: 185)

📚📖
👉 _* Tafseer:*_
(Cont'd .....)
Abhi tak hamne bataya ke ham kiya hain. Pas har Nafs ko Maut ka maza chakhna hai. Iska taste lena hai. Yahan Ayat mein na Insaan aur na log istemal hua balke Nafs. Nafs ke bare mein hamne kal bataya tha. Isse pahle ye bhi bata chuke hain ke jo shakhs qatl hua usne Maut ka maza nahi chakha. Isliye jo bhi Shaheed hua hai usne abhi tak Maut ka maza nahi chakha isliye unko bhi Maut ayegi aur uska maza chakhenge, yani woh phir se is Duniya mein ayenge, isko Raja'at kahte hain.
Jab koi marta hai ham kahte hain 'Inteqal' ho gaya, means uska is Duniya se transfer ho gaya. Pas insaan ka Jism marta hai, ya Rooh ki power Supply band ho jati hai. Uska is Duniya se check out hota hai. Ab is Judai ka uska Nafs ehsaas karta hai. Material World se uska transfer ek doosre Aalam mein hota hai. Insaan ke liye Adam عدم  nahi hai. Woh extint فناء (fana) nahi hota. Jaisa ke har jagah Quran mein hai هم فيها خالدون ( _Woh Hamesha rahenge_). Pas is Aalam se Aalam e Barzakh mein qadam rakhta hai jahan uska Aqeede ke taalluq se imtehan hota hai. Agar is mein pas ho gaya to ta Qayamat aish karta hai. Isliye jab murde ko dafn karte hain to Tilqeen padhi jati hai اسمع و افهم (Sun aur samajh). Iska ka matlab murda sunta aur samajhta hai. Akhri bar usko Aqeedat ka lesson Revise karaya jata hai. Jab Qabr mein usse Farishte Sawal karte hain to Hazrat Ali (as) uske sarahne hote hain. Isliye Vilayat e Ali ibne Abi Talib (as) zaroori hai. Agar wo Aqaid mein kamzor hai to ta Qayamat Azaab mein mubtela rahega. Qamayat ke din Aamaal ke bare mein sawal hoga. Agar us mein bhi pas ho gaya to hamesha Jannat mein rahega warna Jahannam mein.
Bare Ilaha hame in imtehanat mein Kamyabi ataa farma.
(Next Topic Imtehan)
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜
----------------------------------------------

_*MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!*_
🙇 ✨🛌⚰
Imam Ali (as):
_"Duniya Momin ka qaid-khana, Maut uska tohfa aur Jannat uski manzil hai. Duniya kaafiro'n ki Jannat hoti hai aur maut usay is (jannat) se judaa karne waali aur Aag uski manzil hoti hai."_
(Tajalliyat e Hikmat, Duniya)
✨🛌⚰
Imam Baqir (as):
_"Malekul Maut ki nigaah karne ki soorat ye hai ke jaise log baithe ho'n aur unhe saktah (laqwah / paralysis) ho jaaye aur wo baat karne ke qaabil na rahein. Ye haalat hoti hai jab Malekul Maut unko dekhta hai."_
(Furoo e Kafi, v1, p354)
✨🛌⚰
Imam Sadiq (as):
_"Jab kisi marne waale ki maut ka waqt aata hai to Khuda Wande Aalam uski aql aur sun'ne aur dekhne ki quwwat ko wasiyyat karne ke liye lauta deta hai. Ab uski marzi par munhasir hai ke wasiyyat kare ya na kare. Yehi wo raahat hai jise Raahat ul Maut kaha jaata hai. Ye har Musalman par laazim hai."_
(Wasaail ush Shia, v2, p124)
✨🛌⚰
Rasule Khuda (saww):
_"Jo bhi mareez Surah Yaseen ko Sakraat e Maut ya Ehtezaar ke waqt padhe to khaazin e Jannat Rizwan uske paas Jannat ka sharbat lekar aata hai aur usay bistar par wo jaam pilaata hai. Chunaanche marne wale ki maut waqe' hoti hai to wo seyr o sairaab (kha-pi kar peyt bhara) hota hai aur jab usay maboos kiya jayega tab bhi wo seyr o sairaab hoga aur wo Ambiya (as) ke hauzo'n mein se kisi bhi hauz ka mohtaaj nahi hoga aur wo seyr o sairaab haalat mein Jannat mein daakhil hoga."_
(Tafseer Noor us Saqlain, v7, p159)
✨🛌⚰
Rasool e Khuda (saww) ne farmaya ke Allah Ta'ala farmata hai:
_"Mein Apni Izzat ka Halaf utha chuka hun aur Apne Jalal ki Qasam kha chuka hun ke Mera jo bhi banda Ali (as) se Muhabbat rakhega Mein use Dozakh se bacha lunga aur use Jannat mein dakhil karunga aur jo bhi shakhs usse bughz rakhega aur uski Vilayat se inheraf karega to mein usse Bughz rakhunga aur Dozakh mein dakhil karunga jo ke bahut bura thikana hai."_
(Amali e Sudooq, Noorus Saqlain)
✨🛌⚰
Rasule Khuda (saww):
_"Jo Ali (as) se mohabbat rakhega, uske paas Khuda Wande Aalam Malekul Maut oos shaan se bhejega jis shaan se wo Ambiya (as) ke paas aate the, Khuda Wande Aalam oos (Ali (as) se mohabbat karne waale) se Munkir Nakeer ke khauf ko duur karega, uski Qabr ko munawwar aur uske chehre ko raushan karega aur wo J. Hamza ke saath hoga."_
(Shiane Ahlebait (as), p17)

Rasule Khuda (saww):
_"Meri aur mere khandaan ki mohabbat 7 jagah par faida-mand hai jab ke har ek jagah par sakht-tareen khauf hai:_ 1) Maut ke waqt,
2) Qabr mein,
3) Qabr se baahar nikalne ke waqt,
4) Naama e Aamal ke waqt,
5) Hisaab ke waqt,
6) Mizaan par, aur
7) Puul e Siraat par.
(Amaali - Shaikh Sadooq, p19)

         ♦ _*IMTEHAAN - TEST*_ ♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (459)

*بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ*

*لَتُبْلَوُنَّ فِي أَمْوَالِكُمْ وَأَنْفُسِكُمْ وَلَتَسْمَعُنَّ مِنَ الَّذِينَ أُوتُوا الْكِتَابَ مِنْ قَبْلِكُمْ وَمِنَ الَّذِينَ أَشْرَكُوا أَذًى كَثِيرًا ۚ وَإِنْ تَصْبِرُوا وَتَتَّقُوا فَإِنَّ ذَٰلِكَ مِنْ عَزْمِ الْأُمُورِ*

_"Musalmano! Tumse tumhare maal aur Jaan ka IMTEHAN (Test) liya jayega aur tumhe Ahle Kitab aur Mushrekin se bhi nagawar baten sunna padengi aur agar tumne Sabr o Taqwa ka muzahera kiya to ye yaqinan bade hausle aur dil gurde ka kaam hai."_
(Surah Aal-e-Imran: 186)

📚📖
👉 _* Tafseer:*_
Jaise ke hamne pichhli ayaton ke zel mein bataya ke Maut o Hayat kiya hai. Hamne dekha ke Maut ke baad Insaan ka Sawab o Azaab ka silsila shuru ho jata hai. Isliye hame ye samjhna hoga ke zindagi ka maqsad kiya hai. Quran ki Ayat ke Mutabiq Ham sirf Ibadat ke liye paida hue hain.
*(وَمَا خَلَقْتُ الْجِنَّ وَالْإِنْسَ إِلَّا لِيَعْبُدُونِ*  (Surah Zariyat: 56)
Ibaadat means Allah ko Malik maante hue Uski Ghulami karna. Ibaadat hi hamara Imtehan hai. Hamara Alam e Zar mein Prelium Exam hua tha. Ab is Duniya mein usse sakht Imtehaan se guzarna hoga. Jaan o Maal se Imtehan liya jayega. Is tarah gharib ko uski ghurbat se Imtehan, Amir ko uski Amiri se Imtehan, Aulad se Imtehan. Aur jaisa ka is Ayat mein hai:
*وَاعْلَمُوا أَنَّمَا أَمْوَالُكُمْ وَأَوْلَادُكُمْ فِتْنَةٌ وَأَنَّ اللَّهَ عِنْدَهُ أَجْرٌ عَظِيمٌ*
[Surah Al-Anfal: 28]
( _Amwal aur Aulad tumhare liye Test hai_)
Doosre mazahib ki tana mezi baten sunna, ye bhi Imtehan. Jab Insaan par Musibat padti hai to shikwa shikayat karne lagta hai. Allah ki Adalat par sawal uthata hai. Ye log jald hi fail ho jate hain. Har Insaan se Imtehan liya gaya chahe Nabi ya Imam kiyon na ho. Hazrat Ibrahim (as) ko aag mein dala gaya, apne bete par chhuri chalana - ye unka Imtehan tha, Hazrat Ayyub (as) se Imtehan liya gaya. Sab se Sakht Imtehan Imam Husain (as) aur unke Ayaal o Ashaab se Karbala mein liya gaya. Lekin is Imtehan mein wohi paas hua jis ne Sabr kiya aur Taqwa o Burdbari Ikhtiyar ki. Karbala mein Sabr o Taqwa apne Aala manzilen paar kar chuka tha. Yahan tak ke Allah ne pukara _"Aye Nafse Mutmainnah, aaja Mere pas aaja, Mein tujhse Razi, tu Mujhse Razi."_
Isliye Imtehan se koi nahi bach sakta. Har Insaan ko iski alag alag muddat rakhi gayi hai. Insaan apne Ikhtiyar se Imtehan deta hai. ls mein kahi bhi Jabr nahi hai. Usko alternative options diye jate hain, ab uski marzi hai kis ko select karta hai. Uski puri Zindagi ek sawalon ka majmua ho jati hai. Ab ye uske uper hai ke kis sawal par woh kaise deal karta hai. Is Examination Hall ko apna Permanent ghar nahi samjh lena chahiye. Usko jo permanent Resort milega woh isi exam ka silah hoga. Jannat wa Jahannam hi hamara permanent thikana hai.
Bare Ilaha hame in sare Imtehanaat mein kamyabi ata farma.
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜
----------------------------------------------

_*MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!*_
🙇 ✨✨
Rasule Khuda (saww):
_"Yaqeenan, balaa (musibat) zaalim ke liye Azaab hai aur Momin ke liye Imtehaan hai."_ (Jaame'al Akhbaar p.113)
(Anecdotes of Reflection)
✨✨
Allah (swt):
_"Balaa o Musibat se maayus Mat ho; Jaise Sona aag mein pighla kar parkha jaata hai waise Momin balaa'on mein parkha jaata hai."_
(Al-Hadith Al-Qudsi)
✨✨
Imam Kazim (as):
_"Tum oos waqt tak hargiz Momin nahi ho sakte jab tak balaa ko ne'mat aur aish ko musibat khayaal na karo, is liye ke balaa mein Sabr karna behtar hai oos gaflat mein jo aish mein hoti hai."_
(Jaame ul Akhbaar, p199)
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜

*7th Safar 1438, 8th November 2016, Tuesday,

       ♦ _*NASHR E AHADIS*_ ♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (460)

*بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ*

*وَإِذْ أَخَذَ اللَّهُ مِيثَاقَ الَّذِينَ أُوتُوا الْكِتَابَ لَتُبَيِّنُنَّهُ لِلنَّاسِ وَلَا تَكْتُمُونَهُ فَنَبَذُوهُ وَرَاءَ ظُهُورِهِمْ وَاشْتَرَوْا بِهِ ثَمَنًا قَلِيلًا ۖ فَبِئْسَ مَا يَشْتَرُونَ*

_"Aur jab Allah ne Ahle Kitab se Ahd liya tha ke tum Uske Ahkam logo ke samne bayan karoge aur unhe nahi chhupaoge magar unhone ise pase pusht dal diya aur unhone ise thodi si qeemat par bech diya. Kitna bura karobar hai jo ye kar rahe hain."_
(Surah Aal-e-Imran: 187)

📚📖 📝
👉 _* Tafseer:*_
Imam Baqar (as):
_"Allah Ta'ala ne Ahle Kitab se wada liya tha ke woh Khatemul Anbiya par Iman layenge aur unki aamad ka ailan karte rahenge lekin Ahle Kitab ne Khudai Misaq ko pase pusht dal diya."_
(Tafseer Ali bin Ibrahim)
Agarche ye Ayat Ahle Kitab ke Ulema ke bare mein hai, lekin haqiqat mein tamam mazhabi Ulema ko is mein tanbi ki gayi hai ke unki zimmedari hai ke Farameen e Ilahi aur Ma'arif e Deeni wazeh karne ki koshish kare aur Allah Ta'ala ne un sab se is silsile mein takeedi Ahd o Paiman liya hai.
Raavi Hasan bin Ammar ka bayan hai ke Zohri ne hadis bayan karna chhod diya tha to use ye hadis sunai jise sun kar usne 40 hadis sunai:
Hazrat Ali (as):
_"Allah Ta'ala ne Ahle Jihalat se llm o Danish ke husool ka Ahd lene se pahle Ulema se Ahd liya ke wo inhe Ilm sikhain."_
📝
Rasool e Khuda (saww):
_"Jo Shakhs Ilm o Danish ko uske Ahl (aur zarooratmand) se chhupayga Qayamat ke Din Khuda unke moo mein (Jahannam ki) Aag ki lagam dega."_
(Tafseer Abul Futuh Raazi, Tafseer Majmaul Bayan. Nahjul Balagha)
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜
----------------------------------------------

_*MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!*_
🙇 📝
Imam Sadiq (as):
_"Hamari Ahadees naql o bayaan karnewala aur unhe logo'n ke darmiyaan parchaar (propagate) karnewala aur hamare Shiyo'n ke aqeede ko mazbuut karnewala 1000 Aabid se behtar hai."_
(Nawaadirul Ahadees, v1, p70)

♦ _*GUNAH PAR KHUSH NUMAI*_ ♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (461)

*بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ*

*لَا تَحْسَبَنَّ الَّذِينَ يَفْرَحُونَ بِمَا أَتَوْا وَيُحِبُّونَ أَنْ يُحْمَدُوا بِمَا لَمْ يَفْعَلُوا فَلَا تَحْسَبَنَّهُمْ بِمَفَازَةٍ مِنَ الْعَذَابِ ۖ وَلَهُمْ عَذَابٌ أَلِيمٌ*

_"Tum un logon ko Azaab se mehfooz na samjho jo apne kartooto par khus hain aur chahte hain ke aise kamo ki ta'reef inhe hasil ho jo unhone kiye hi nahi hain. Un logo ke liye dardnak Azaab hai."_
(Surah Aal-e-Imran: 188)

📚📖
👉 _* Tafseer:*_
Gunah do tarah ke hote hain:
(1) Admi Gunah karke pasheman hota hai. Aise log ki Tauba bhi qubool hone ke chances rahte hain.
(2) Admi Gunah ko Achha kaam samajh kar karta hai. Woh Gunah ko Gunah nahi samjhta.
Ayat is doosre giroh ko mukhatab hai.
Ajkal bahut se aise Gunah aam ho jate hai jis karna koi buri baat nahi maani jati. Jaise Western Countries mein Wine, Drinks, nudity aisi comon ho gayi ke koi bura nahi samajhta. Yahan par Film bini, Music, Najis Khaana, bepurdagi, Namaz tark karn, Sood khori common hai. Jo jan boojh kar raha hai uske Tauba nahi hai. Us par ye ke us Gunah ki tareef hoti hai. Yazeed aur Qatilaan e Imam Husain (as) achha samajh kar apna kaam kar rahe the. ISSI Daesh jo qatlo gharat kar raha usko Islam jawaz pesh karke kar raha tha. Ek insaan ki Kalma padh kar qurbani karna Islami kaam samajh kar rahe the. Pas insaan apne Gunahon par parda dalne ke liye Gunah ko Islami rang de deta hai. Kishore aur Islambhai mein jhagda hota kiyon Islambhai kuchh jagah uski qabza li. Ab Islambhai chilla chilla kar logo jama karenge ke Islam khatre mein hai. Isi liye aajkal sab mar kaat ka naam de diya Jihad.
Bar Ilaha hame aise Gunahon se mehfooz rakh.
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜
----------------------------------------------

_*MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!*_
🙇 ✨✨
Imam Ali (as):
_"Gunaho'n ka tark (avoid) karna Tauba karne se zyada behtar hai._"
(Meezan ul Hikmah, v1, p807)
✨✨
Imam Ali (as):
_"Gunah ek aisi bimari hai jiski dawaa Astagfaar (Tauba) hai aur oos gunah ko Na dohrana uski shifa hai."_
(Tajalliyat e Hikmat, ch Gunah)
✨✨
Rasule Khuda (saww):
_"Agar Gunahaan e Kabeera se insaan parhez karta ho to ek Namaz se doosri Namaz tak jitne gunah e sagheerah honge to Namaz unka kaffara ho jaayegi."_
(Irshadaat e Masumeen (as), p16)
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜

*9th Mahe Safar 1438, 10th November 2016, Thursday,

       ♦ _*WUJOOD E KHUDA*_ ♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (462) ☝🏻

*بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ*

*وَلِلَّهِ مُلْكُ السَّمَاوَاتِ وَالْأَرْضِ ۗ وَاللَّهُ عَلَىٰ كُلِّ شَيْءٍ قَدِيرٌ * إِنَّ فِي خَلْقِ السَّمَاوَاتِ وَالْأَرْضِ وَاخْتِلَافِ اللَّيْلِ وَالنَّهَارِ لَآيَاتٍ لِأُولِي الْأَلْبَابِ*

_"Aasmaan aur Zameen ki Milkiyat Khuda ke liye makhsoos hai. Allah har cheez par Qurat rakhta hai."_
_"Yaqeenan Aasmaanon aur Zameen ki paidaish mein aur Raat aur Din ke bari bari aane mein un Aqalmando ke liye bahut Nishaniyan hain."_
(Surah Aal-e-Imran: 189 - 190)

📚📖 ☝🏻
👉 _*�Tafseer:*_
Puri Kainat ka Malik o Khaliq Allah hai. Isko sabit karne ke liye Quran ne bahut se misalin di hain aur Ahle Aql walon ko ghaur o fikr karne ki takeed ki hai. اختلاف ka root hai خلف (succeeding) yani pai dar pai aana.
Kuchh ka nazarya hai ke ye Duniya by chance ittefaqan wujud mein aa gayi.
Is Duniya ke munazzam system ko dekhne se hi pata chalta hai ke iska koi Khaliq hai aur Woh Allah hai. Kisi bhi accident ko dekhen to us mein koi nazm dikhai nahi dega. Ek Shayr ki shayri ko dekh kar pata chalta hai Shayr kitna azmat wala. Ek machine ko dekh kar Engineer ki qabiliyat ka pata chalta hai. Isi tarah makhlooq (creatures) ko dekh kar Khaliq (Creator) ka pata chalta hai. Allah ne Uoolul Albab (Intellectuals) se mukhatib kiya.
Jitni bareeki ham makhlooq mein payenge utna hamare liye Khuda ki Azmat badhegi, ubudiyat mein izafa hoga, aur hame faqre zaati hoga.
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜
----------------------------------------------

_*MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!*_
🙇 ☝🏻
Imam Sadiq (as):
_"Agar Allah raat aur din mein se kisi ko taweel (lambe) arsey tak qaaim kar deta to phir Rizq Rozi ka haasil karna mushkil ho jaata. Isi liye Kaaenaat ke Khaliq ne din ko raushan aur raat ko sukoon ka zariya banaya hai."_
(Tafseer Noor us Saqlain, v3, p252)
☝🏻
Imam Sadiq (as):
_"Juma ka din bhi (afzaliyat mein) uski raat ke jaisa hai. Lihaza, agar ho sakey to Shab e Juma Namaz padhne aur Dua karne mein basar karo, kyun ki Allah isme Nekiyo'n ko do-guna (double) karta hai aur buryaiyo'n ko mitata hai aur Wo bada Wus'at aur Karam wala hai."_
(Wasaail ush Shia, v5, p67)
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜

*10th Mahe Safar 1438, 11th November 2016, Friday,

♦ _*ALLAH KI KOI KHILQAT BEKAR NAHI*_ ♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (463)

*بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ*

*الَّذِينَ يَذْكُرُونَ اللَّهَ قِيَامًا وَقُعُودًا وَعَلَىٰ جُنُوبِهِمْ وَيَتَفَكَّرُونَ فِي خَلْقِ السَّمَاوَاتِ وَالْأَرْضِ رَبَّنَا مَا خَلَقْتَ هَٰذَا بَاطِلًا سُبْحَانَكَ فَقِنَا عَذَابَ النَّارِ*

_"(Ye Aqalmandon ke liye Nishaniyan hain) jo uthte-baithte aur lete har haal mein Khuda ko yaad karte hain aur Aasmano aur zameen ki takhleeq mein ghaur o fikr karte hain aur zabane haal se kahte hain. Parwardegar! Tu ne ye sab batil paida nahi kiya. Tu abas (useless) kaam karne se Paak o Pakeeza hai. Hame Dozakh ke Azaab se bacha le."_
(Surah Aal-e-Imran: 191)

📚📖
👉 _* Tafseer:*_
Allah ne Aqalmand un logon ko bataya hai jo Kainat ki khilqat par ghaur o fikr karte hain. Ye sab dekh kar yehi pata chalta hai ke jitni bhi cheezen Allah ne paida ki wo fuzool ya bekar nahi hai. Tonsil jo pahle ke Doctor bekar samajh kar nikal dete the ab kahte hain ye bekar nahi. Waise hi Appendix. Is tarah scientific research se yehi pata chala har cheez ka kuchh na kuchh function hai. Jitna ham is kaynat par ghaur o fikr karenge uboodiyat mein zyada izafa hoga. Allah bekar k kaam nahi karta. Isliya ham Ushi ki panah mein hain Ushi se Dua karte hain.

Imam Raza (as):
_"Jab mein apne jism ko dekhta hun to woh har lihaz se mukammal dikhai deta hai. Is mein koi kami aur beshi dikhai nahi deti aur us mein quwwat e mudafeat (defensive power) bhi maujood hai aur mufa'at jazb karne ki bhi us mein salahiyat maujood hai. Lehaza is jism ki Imarat ko dekh kar mujhe maloom ho gaya ke Imarat ka koi me'mar (Builder) bhi hai. Isliye meine Uska Iqrar kiya. Alawa az een jab meine aflak ki gardish aur badalon ke chalne aur hawaon ki amad o raft aur Suraj Chaand aur Sitaron ki gardish aur doosri ajeeb o ghareeb nishaniyan dekhin to mujhe yaqeen ho gaya ke is nizaam ko Chalane wala Maujood hai."_
(Uyoonul Akhbar Al Reza)
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜
----------------------------------------------

_*MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!*_
🙇 🙏🏻
قال على عليه السلام:
*ايهاالناس سلونى قبل ان تفقدونى فلا بطرق السمآء اعلم منى بطريق الارض.*
_"Logo! Mujhse poochh lo qabl iske ke ke tum mujhe na pao, Mein Zameen ke raaston se Aasmaan ke raston ko behtar janta hun."_
(Nehjul Balagha)
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜
----------------------------------------------
*11th Mahe Safar 1438, 12th November 2016, Saturday,

                ♦ _*DOZAKH*_ ♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (464)
🙏🏻
*بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ*

*رَبَّنَا إِنَّكَ مَنْ تُدْخِلِ النَّارَ فَقَدْ أَخْزَيْتَهُ ۖ وَمَا لِلظَّالِمِينَ مِنْ أَنْصَارٍ*

_"Aye hamare Parwardegar! Tu ne jise Dozakh mein dala use tu ne ruswai mein dal diya aur zalimo ka koi madadgar nahi hoga."_
(Surah Aal-e-Imran: 192)

📚📖 🙏🏻🔥🔥
👉 _* Tafseer:*_
*(Ayaat Ale Imran: 190 - 194)*
Rivayat: ....... Jab Bilal ne Subah ki Namaz ke liye pukara to Aap (saww) ke ashkon se tar batar dekha to poochha ke Aap (saww) is qadr kiyon girya kar rahe hain? Lutfe Ilahi to Aap (saww) ke shamile haal hai.'
Rasoole Khuda (saww) ne farmaya:
_"Kiya mein Allah ka Shukr guzar banda na bano, mein kiyon girya na karun Allah Ta'ala ne kal raat mujh par hila dene wali aur pareshan kar dene wali aayat nazil ki hain._
Phir Aap (saww) ne ye 5 aayaat ki tilawat ki aur aakhir mein farmaya:
_"Wai ho us par jo inhe padhe lekin in mein ghaur o fikr na kare."_
(Tafseer Abul Fath Raazi)
Beshak hame Dozakh se darna chahiye aur Nek aamaal ki taraf uboodiyat ka raasta ikhtiyar karna chahiya, phir kis tarah uska khas banda dua mangta hai ye bataya hai Khuda ne. Ye 5 Duaiyyah ayaten hain.
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜
----------------------------------------------

_*MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!*_
🙇 🔥🔥
Imam Ali (as):
_"…Ahle Dozakh ki kaal-kothdi mein kabhi thandi hawa ka guzar nahi hoga. Unki zindagi khatm na hogi aur unhe nit-naye tariqe se azaab diya jaayega. Na to Dozakh ki aag khatm hogi aur na hi Ahl e Dozakh ki zindagi tamaam hogi."_
(Tafseer Noor us Saqlain, v7, p559)
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜

*12th Mahe Safar 1438, 13th November 2016, Sunday,

          ♦ _*MUNADI KI NIDA*_ ♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (465)

*بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ*

*رَبَّنَا إِنَّنَا سَمِعْنَا مُنَادِيًا يُنَادِي لِلْإِيمَانِ أَنْ آمِنُوا بِرَبِّكُمْ فَآمَنَّا ۚ رَبَّنَا فَاغْفِرْ لَنَا ذُنُوبَنَا وَكَفِّرْ عَنَّا سَيِّئَاتِنَا وَتَوَفَّنَا مَعَ الْأَبْرَارِ*

_"Parwardegar! Hamne ek Munadi (Caller) ki Nida (Call) suni jo Imaan ki taraf nida de raha tha ke apne Rab par Imaan lao, ham Imaan laye. Malik! Hamare gunah maaf kar de aur hamare andar jo buraiyyan maujood hain unhen door kar de aur hamara khatema Nek logon ke sath kar."_
(Surah Aal-e-Imran: 193)

📚📖 🗣
👉 _* Tafseer:*_
In Ayaton ke zariye Duaiya Kalemat jari hain. Is Dua mein ham Iqraar kar rahe ke tere Munadi ki baat maan li. Pas to woh Munadi kaun tha ?
Har Nabi o Rasool Munadi hota hai aur logon ko Imaan ki dawat deta hai. Is Ayat mein Allah Ta'ala ne Ahle Imaan ki usi Dua ko naql kiya hai.
Imam Jafar Sadiq (as):
_"Ameerul Momenin (as) ne bachpan mein Aasmaani Nida suni thi ke tum Rasool par Imaan lao. Chunache unhone is Nida par Labaik kahi thi."_
(Tafseer e Ayyashi)

Imam Raza (as):
(Unhone Rasool (saww) se, unhone Jibrael (as) se, unhone Mikaeel se, unhone Israfeel se, usne Allah Ta'ala se suna):
_"Mein Allah hun, Mere alawa koi Ma'bood nahi hai. Meine apni Qudrat se Makhlooq ko paida kiya aur Meine un mein se apne Anbiya (as) ka intekhab kiya aur phir Bazm e Anbiya mein se Muhammad (saww) ko apna Habib aur Khalil aur Safi muntakhab kiya aur use apni makhlooq ki taraf Rasool bana kar rawana kiya. Meine apne Habib ke liye Ali (as) ka intekhab kiya aur Meine use apne Habib ka Bhai, Wasi, Vazir banaya aur unka Khalifa namzad kiya. Chunanche Muhammad (saww) aur Ali (as) Aasmaan o Zameen ki makhlooq par Meri Hujjat hain. Mein Muhammad (saww) ki Nubawwat aur Ali (as) ki Vilayat ke iqraar ke baghair kisi ka amal qubool nahi karunga."_
(Uyoonul Akhbar Al Reza, Noorus Saqlain)
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜
----------------------------------------------

_*MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!*_
🙇 🗣
Imam Reza (as)
se sawaal kiya gaya ke Allah Ta'ala ne Firoun ko kyun garq kiya (paani mein duboya) jab ke wo Allah par Imaan le aaya tha aur Uski Tauheed ka iqraar kar chuka tha? Aap ne farmaya:
_"Iski wajah ye hai ke wo azaab ko aa'nkho'n se dekhne ke waqt Imaan laya tha aur oos waqt ka Imaan qaabil e qubool nahi hai."_
(Uyoon Akhbaar ar Reza, v2, p167)
✨✨
Rasule Khuda (saww):
_"Kisi shakhs ke dil mein Imaan oos waqt tak daakhil nahi ho sakta jab tak wo mere Ahlebait (as) ke saath Allah aur uske Rasul (saww) ki khaatir mohabbat na rakhta ho."_
(Amaali - Shaikh Toosi, v1, p133)
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜
----------------------------------------------
*13th Safar 1438, 14th November 2016, Monday,
🔹🔹🔹🔹🔹🔹🔹🔹🔹🔹

                ♦ _*WA'DA*_ ♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (453)

*بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ*

*رَبَّنَا وَآتِنَا مَا وَعَدْتَنَا عَلَىٰ رُسُلِكَ وَلَا تُخْزِنَا يَوْمَ الْقِيَامَةِ ۗ إِنَّكَ لَا تُخْلِفُ الْمِيعَادَ*

_"Khuda wanda! Jo wa'de Tu ne hamse apne Rasoolon ke zariye se kiye hain unko hamare sath poora kar aur Qayamat ke Din hame ruswa na karna. Beshak Tu Wadakhilafi nahi karta."_
(Surah Aal-e-Imran: 194)

📚📖 🙏🏻
👉 _* Tafseer:*_
Imam Sajjad (as):
_'Aye Maabud! Ye Tera farmaan hai aur Tera kehna durust aur Tera waada sachcha hai ke Allah se uska fazl maango. Beshak, Allah tum par bahut meherbaan hai. Aye mere Sardaar! Ye baat Teri shaan ke khilaaf hai ke Tu maangne ka hukm de to ataa na farmaaye. Tu Apni mamlekat ke baashindo'n ko bahut bahut ataa karne waala hai aur Apni meherbaani aur narmi se unki taraf mutawajjeh hai."_
(Dua e Abu Hamza Sumaali)
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜
----------------------------------------------

_*MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!*_
🙇 🙏🏻
Imam Baqir (as):
_"Har wo gunah jis par Allah ne azaab e Jahannum ka waada farmaya hai wo gunah e kabeera hai."_
(Irshadaat e Masumeen (as), p63)
🙏🏻
Rasule Khuda (saww):
_"Agar koi shakhs ye pasand kare ke uski zindagi meri zindagi ho aur uski maut meri maut aur usko Allah meri Jannat mein jagah de jiska Allah ne waada farmaya hai aur…apni Yad e Qudrat se banaya aur 'Kun Fayakun' farmaane se usay paida kiya, to aise shakhs pe laazim hai ke H. Ali (as) se aur unke baad unki aulaad se mohabbat rakhe."_
(Shiane  Ahlebait (as), p16)
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜

*14th Mahe Safar 1438, 15th November 2016, Tuesday,

      ♦ _*AAMAAL KA AJR*_ ♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (467)

*بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ*

*فَاسْتَجَابَ لَهُمْ رَبُّهُمْ أَنِّي لَا أُضِيعُ عَمَلَ عَامِلٍ مِنْكُمْ مِنْ ذَكَرٍ أَوْ أُنْثَىٰ ۖ بَعْضُكُمْ مِنْ بَعْضٍ ۖ فَالَّذِينَ هَاجَرُوا وَأُخْرِجُوا مِنْ دِيَارِهِمْ وَأُوذُوا فِي سَبِيلِي وَقَاتَلُوا وَقُتِلُوا لَأُكَفِّرَنَّ عَنْهُمْ سَيِّئَاتِهِمْ وَلَأُدْخِلَنَّهُمْ جَنَّاتٍ تَجْرِي مِنْ تَحْتِهَا الْأَنْهَارُ ثَوَابًا مِنْ عِنْدِ اللَّهِ ۗ وَاللَّهُ عِنْدَهُ حُسْنُ الثَّوَابِ*
[Surat Aal-E-Imran 195]

(Jab Sahebane Aql ne dua ki)
_"Jawab mein unke Rab ne farmaya ke Mein tum mein se kisi ka amal zaye karne wala nahi hun khwah Mard ho ya Aurat, tum sab ek doosre ke ham jinse ho. Lehaza jin logon ne hijrat ki aur jinhone unke gharon se nikala gaya aur Meri rah mein Jinhen aziyaten di gayin aur Mere liye lade aur maare gaye unke Mein qusoor maaf karunga aur unhen aise Baghaat mein jagah doonga jinke niche nehren baihti hongi. Ye Allah ke haan unki jaza hai aur Allah ke paas behtareen jaza hai."_
(Surah Aal-e-Imran: 195)

📚📖
👉 _* Tafseer:*_
Pichhli Ayaton mein Ahle Aqlo fahem logon ke Imaan o Aamal, dua ka tazkara hua. Parwardegar ne unki dua qubool ki. Allah Adil hai, Insaafwar hai. Kisi ka koi Nek amal zaye nahi ho sakta.
Is ayat mein Amal aur Roohani irteqa ke ru se Aurat aur Mard ko ham jins bataya hai, dono ki hasiyat Allah ki nazar mein barabar hai. Ye un nazaryat ke bar aks (contrary) hai jo Aurat ke amal ko Mardon se alag jante hain. Christian mein kuchh alag nazaryat hain. Woh kahte hain ke sirf Janabe Maryam (as) ki Rooh hamesha rahegi baqi nahi.
(Kitab wirde sadak Mark)
Jabke Islam ke mutabiq Alam e Barzakh mein Aurat aur Mard ki Rooh ki ek hi haisiyat hogi.
Rasool (saww) ke zamane mein Hijrat ke waqt Musalmano ki Economic Condition Jews ke muqable kamzor thi phir unho ne bahut se jihad kiye, ghar chhoda. Imam Husain (as) ne Islam ke khatir apne ahl o ayal ke sath ghar Medina chhoda, Hajj ko Umre se badla, Kafir Yazid se Jihad kiya aur Shaheed hue. Allah iska Insaaf karega.
Ab Kafir kiyon zyada kamyab hote hain aur aish ki zindagi basar karte hai iska jawab ham de chuke hain. Momin ka zindagi ka maqsad Akherat hai jabke Kafiron ka ye Mukhtasar Duniya.
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜
----------------------------------------------

_*MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!*_
🙇 👰🏻 _*AURAT:*_
Imam Sadiq (as):
_"Shaaista (saaleh / nek) aurat 1000 na-shaaista (na-saaleh) mard se behtar hai. Khuda Wande Aalam uspar Jahannum ke 7 darwaze band kar deta hai aur Jannat ke 8 darwaze khol deta hai taaki wo jis darwaze se chaahe daakhil ho."_
(Aasmani Nasihatein, v1, p109)
👰🏻
Rasule Khuda (saww):
_"Jo aurat zindagi ki mushkilaat mein sabr o tahammul kare, Khuda Wande Aalam usay Shaheed ka sawaab ataa karta hai."_
(Aasmani Nasihatein, v1, p117)
👰🏻
Imam Sadiq (as)
ke paas sawaal aaya ke bhala iski kya wajah hai ke kamzor aurat ke liye Islam mein ek hissa hai aur taaqat-war mard ke liye 2 hisse hain? Aap ne farmaya, _"Aurat ko Diyyat (khoon-baha / blood-money) mein hissa (share) nahi dena padta, uspar kisi ka nafqa (ghar-kharch) waajib nahi hai aur uspar Jihad bhi nahi hai; ye tamaam cheezein mardo'n ke zimme hain is liye aurat ke liye ek hissa hai aur mard ke liye 2 hisse hain."_
(Tafseer Noor us Saqlain, v2, p307)
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜

*15th Mahe Safar 1438, 16th November 2016, Wednesday,

BAZM-E-ADAB WELCOMES YOU*

             ♦ _*DUNIYA*_ ♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (468)

*بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ*

*لَا يَغُرَّنَّكَ تَقَلُّبُ الَّذِينَ كَفَرُوا فِي الْبِلَادِ * مَتَاعٌ قَلِيلٌ ثُمَّ مَأْوَاهُمْ جَهَنَّمُ ۚ وَبِئْسَ الْمِهَادُ*

_"Munkareen ki Duniya ke Mulkon mein chalat phirat tumhe kisi dhoke mein na dal de. Ye mahez chand roza zindagi ka thoda sa lutf hai. Phir unka thikana Dozakh hoga aur woh badtareen thikana hai."_
(Surah Aal-e-Imran: 196 - 197)

📚📖 🌍
👉 _* Tafseer:*_
Sawal ye hota hai ke ham Duniya ki taraf attract hote hain aur us taraf hamari dilchaspi zyada badhti jati hai. Munkarin, Kaferin ko ham dekhte hain ke woh bahut aish ki zindagi guzar rahe hain.
Allah is ayat mein yahi jawab de raha hai ke tum isse dokha na khana. Agar ham Kafiron ko Kamiyab dekh rahe hai to ye sirf limited hai. Agar koi chori karke, dhoka de kar, chalaki se kamyab ho raha hai to woh ye mehnat sirf is mukhtasar zindagi ke liye kar raha hai. Yehi cheez poore Mulk ke liye bhi sadiq aati hai. Jo log sari umr hukumat ke liye ladte rahe aur is duniya se chale gaye. Yazid adhi Duniya mein raaj karta tha, sochiye ab uska thikana kahan hain? Aap kahenge Jahannam. To itna sab kuchh usne jo kiya uska silah ye mila. Isliye hamne dekha sab hukmuran chale gaye apne sath kiya le gaye. Ye sirf Duniya hai. Momin ka asl maqsad sirf aur sirf Akherat hai, ye Fani Duniya sirf Imtehan gah hai. Isko permanent samajh kar dokha na khayen.
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜
----------------------------------------------

_*MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!*_
🙇 🌍
Imam Ali (as):
_"Duniya Momin ka qaid-khana, Maut uska tohfa aur Jannat uski manzil hai. Duniya kaafiro'n ki Jannat hoti hai aur maut usay is (jannat) se judaa karne waali aur Aag uski manzil hoti hai."_
(Tajalliyat e Hikmat, Duniya)
🌍
Allah (swt):
_"Akherat talab kar aur Duniya ko tark kar, kyun ki Akherat ka Ek zarra (atom) behtar hai is Duniya aur uski tamaam cheezo'n se."_
(Al-Hadith Al-Qudsi)
🌍
Allah (swt):
_"Teri Maut teri khwaaishaat pe ha'nsti hai, Meri Akherat teri Duniya pe ha'nsti hai, Meri Daulat teri Laalach pe ha'nsti hai.."_
(Al-Hadith Al-Qudsi)
🌍
Allah (swt):
_"Kitne Maaldaar log is Duniya se gaye apna Maal yahin chhorkar aur Akherat mein gaye Tanha, Gareeb aur apne kartuut pe sharminda?"_
(Al-Hadith Al-Qudsi)
🌍
Imam Ali (as):
_"Jise Akherat ka yaqeen hota hai, wo Duniya ki laalach mein mubtela nahi hota."_
(Tajalliyat e Hikmat, ch Duniya
🌍
Imam Ali (as):
_"Jo apni Akherat sa'nwaar lega, Allah uski Duniya sa'nwaar dega."_
(Tajalliyat e Hikmat, ch Akherat)
🌍
Imam Ali (as):
_"Duniya Daulat se haasil ki jaati hai aur Akherat Amal se."_
(Tajalliyat e Hikmat, ch Duniya)
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜
----------------------------------------------
*16th Mahe Safar 1438, 17th November 2016, Thursday,
🔹🔹🔹🔹🔹🔹🔹🔹🔹🔹

BAZM-E-ADAB COMMEMORATE SHAHADAT OF IMAM REZA (as)*
***********************************
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜
      ♦ _*MUTTAQEEN KA AJR*_ ♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (469)

*بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ*

*لَٰكِنِ الَّذِينَ اتَّقَوْا رَبَّهُمْ لَهُمْ جَنَّاتٌ تَجْرِي مِنْ تَحْتِهَا الْأَنْهَارُ خَالِدِينَ فِيهَا نُزُلًا مِنْ عِنْدِ اللَّهِ ۗ وَمَا عِنْدَ اللَّهِ خَيْرٌ لِلْأَبْرَارِ*

_"Is ke bar aks (On the contrary) jo log apne Rab se darte rahe (Muttaqi) unke liye aise Baghat hain jin ke neeche Nehren baihti hongi, woh us mein hamesha rahenge. Allah ki taraf se ye unke liye samane ziyafat (hospitality) aur jo kuchh Allah ke paas hai wo Nek logon ke liye bahut behtar hai."_
(Surah Aal-e-Imran: 198)

📚📖 ✨✨
👉 _* Tafseer:*_
Jaisa ke hamne kal bataya Kafiron ki ye mukhtasar Duniya aish bhari hoti hai aur woh iske liye koshish karta hai Lekin ye Duniya Muttaqi wo Momin ke liye Imtehan ki jagah is liye woh yahan aish ki nahi sochega balke woh koshish karega ke is Imtihan mein paas ho jay. Is ayat mein Allah ne Mutteqeen ke liye itne ajr rakhen hain. Balke Akherat mein ye log Allah ke guest honge.
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜
----------------------------------------------

_*MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!*_
🙇 ✨✨
Imam Baqir (as):
_"Arafaat aur Al-Mash'ar mein thhaherne waale har muttaqi aur gair-muttaqi shakhs ki Dua qubool hogi. Muttaqi ki Duniya aur Aakherat dono ke liye maangi gayi Dua qubool hogi jab ke gair-muttaqi ki sirf Dunyavi haajat ki Dua qubool hogi."_
(Al Kaafi, v4, p262)
(Hajj - The Islamic Pilgrimage)
✨✨✨
Rasule Khuda (saww):
_"Jiski aa'nkhein khauf e Khuda se behne lagein uska sawaab ye hai ke uske har qatra e ashk ke badle Ohad ke pahaadd ke barabar Ajr uske naama e aamaal mein daal diya jayega."_
(Meezan ul Hikmah, v1, p665)
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜
----------------------------------------------
*17th Mahe Safar 1438, 18th November 2016, Friday,

BAZM-E-ADAB WELCOMES YOU*

            ♦ _*REAL AHLE KITAB*_ ♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (470)

*بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ*

*وَإِنَّ مِنْ أَهْلِ الْكِتَابِ لَمَنْ يُؤْمِنُ بِاللَّهِ وَمَا أُنْزِلَ إِلَيْكُمْ وَمَا أُنْزِلَ إِلَيْهِمْ خَاشِعِينَ لِلَّهِ لَا يَشْتَرُونَ بِآيَاتِ اللَّهِ ثَمَنًا قَلِيلًا ۗ أُولَٰئِكَ لَهُمْ أَجْرُهُمْ عِنْدَ رَبِّهِمْ ۗ إِنَّ اللَّهَ سَرِيعُ الْحِسَابِ*

_"Ahle Kitab mein kuchh aise bhi hain jo Allah par Imaan rakhte hain aur woh us Kitab par Imaan rakhte hain jo tumhari taraf bheji gayi hai aur is Kitab par bhi Imaan rakhte hain jo unki taraf bheji gayi hai. Allah ke aage jhoke hue hain aur Allah ki Aayaat ka mamooli raqam par sauda nahi karte, unka Ajr unke Rab ke paas hai. Yaqeenan Allah chukane mein jaldi karne wala hai."_
(Surah Aal-e-Imran: 199)

📚📖 ⛪
👉 _* Tafseer:*_
Allah Ta'ala ne jahan Ahle Kitab ki mazammat ki wahin is ayat mein kuchh ki madah kar raha hai. Ye Ayat Najjashi (jo Christian se Musalman ho gaya tha) ki wafat par nazil hui. Jin Ahle Kitab ne Islam qubool kiya jabke unhone zaheran ailan nahi kiya unki madah kar raha hai. Unki khusoosiyat (characteristic) is tarah bayan kar raha hai:
(1) Allah par Imaan,
(2) Quran par Imaan,
(3) Wo Aasmani Kitaben jo Ahle Kitab par nazil huin.
(4) Farman e Khuda ke saamne sare Tasleem, Khuzoo wa Khushoo.
(5) Ayaat e Ilahi ko kisi qeemat par na bechna.
Jin mein ye sifaat hain unke liye Ajr o Sawab hai.
(Detail ayat Baqarah: 202 ke zel mein mulaheza farmayen.)
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜
----------------------------------------------

_*MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!*_
🙇 _*IMAAN:*_
Imam Hasan (as):
_"Jo hum kaano'n se sune aur uski tasdeeq (accept) karein wo Imaan hai aur jo aa'nkho'n se dekhein aur qubool karein wo Yaqeen hai."_
(Jaame ul Akhbaar, p49)
⛪
Imam Reza (as)
se sawaal kiya gaya ke Allah Ta'ala ne Firoun ko kyun garq kiya (paani mein duboya) jab ke wo Allah par Imaan le aaya tha aur Uski Tauheed ka iqraar kar chuka tha?
Aap ne farmaya,
_"Iski wajah ye hai ke wo azaab ko aa'nkho'n se dekhne ke waqt Imaan laya tha aur oos waqt ka Imaan qaabil e qubool nahi hai.,,,"_
(Uyoon Akhbaar ar Reza, v2, p167)
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜
----------------------------------------------
*18th Mahe Safar 1438, 19th November 2016, Saturday,

*BAZM-E-ADAB WELCOMES YOU*

⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜
     ♦ _*4 RAAHEN KAMYABI KI*_ ♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (471)

*بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ*

*يَا أَيُّهَا الَّذِينَ آمَنُوا اصْبِرُوا وَصَابِرُوا وَرَابِطُوا وَاتَّقُوا اللَّهَ لَعَلَّكُمْ تُفْلِحُونَ*

_"Aye Sahebane Imaan! SABR se kaam lo aur Pamardi ka muzahera (preserve & endure) karo aur HAQ ki khidmat ke liye kamar basta raho. Allah se darte raho (TAQWA) taake tum kamyab ho sako."_
(Surah Aal-e-Imran: 200)
(Last Ayat of Surah)

📚📖
👉 _* Tafseer:*_
Is Aayat mein kai baaton ka hukm hai jo ke ham rivayton se samjhenge:

*اصْبِرُوا*
Imam Sadiq (as):
 _"Gunehgar se Sabr karo"_.
_"Faraez par Sabr karo."_
_"Masaeb par Sabr karo"_
_"Hamari Muhabbat ki wajah se jo nagawar baten sunna paden un par sabr karo."_
Imam Baqir (as):
_"Khuda ki Nafarmani tarke Sabr ka muzahera karo."_
Rasool e Akram (saww):
_"Ghareebi wa Beemari mein Sabr."_

*وَصَابِرُوا*
Imam Sadiq (as):
_"Pamardi se Faraez par qayem raho."_
_"Faraez par Pamardi."_
_"Masaeb par Pamardi se muqabila karo"_
_"Apne Imam ke sath hokar Dushmano ke muqabile Pamardi ka muzahera karo."_
Imam Baqir (as):
_"Taqayyah se kaam lo."_
Imam Raza (as):
_"Haram se parhez karo."_

*وَرَابِطُوا*
Imam Sadiq (as):
_"Rahe Haq ke liye kamar basta raho. Khuda ka rasta ham hain. Ham Khuda se rabte ka qareebi zariya hain jis ne hamse moo moda usne Nabi e Karim se moo moda aur usne Khuda ke hukm se roogardani ki."_
_"Apne Imam se rabta (contact) qayem rakho."_
_"Apne Rehbaron se contact mein raho."_
Imam Baqir (as):
_"Apne Aimma se rabta rakho."_
Hazrat Ali (as):
_"Namazon se marboot (connected) raho."_

*وَاتَّقُوا اللَّه*
Imam Sadiq (as):
_"Khuda se darte raho. (Taqwa) means Amre bil Maroof aur Nahi Anil Munkar ko baja lao. Aur Nahi Anil Munkar baja late waqt ye bhi khayal rakho ke Ummat ne ham par jo zulm rawa rakhe hain aur hame qatl kiya hai ye bhi badtareen Munkar hai."_

*لَعَلَّكُمْ تُفْلِحُونَ*
Imam Sadiq (as):
_'Agar tum ne in Hidayaat par amal kiya to Jannat jane ke qabil ban jaoge."_
_"Taake falah paa sako."_
*Conclusion:*
(1) SABR - PATIENCE
(2) SABIR - STEADFASTNESS
(3) RABTA - CONNECTION
(4) TAQWA - PIETY
Upar 4 par amal karenge to
KAMYABI - SUCCESS hai.
(Ref: Tafseer Ali ibne Ibrahim, Noorus Saqlain, Majmaul Bayan)
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜
----------------------------------------------

_*MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!*_
🙇
Allah (swt):
_"Aye Insaan! Jo raabeta (connection) tere aur Mere darmiyaan hai wo teri taraf se Dua karna aur Meri taraf se Dua ko qubool karna hai."_
(Ahaadis e Qudsi)
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜
